/ /dpal rdo rje nag po chen po'i zab mo'i chos skor rnams byung ba'i tshul legs par bshad pa bstan srung chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba bzhugs so// stod cha/Volume
I, ff. 1a-208b (1979 ed.)

rgya gar skad du/ shrI tsakre shwa ra na ya ka wa ra sanggu ru tsa badzra mahA ka la sa pa ri wA ra ye ma ma a bi yo ga hri da yA pa tsa ya kritra karma bista ra bha wa tu/
bod skad du/ dpal 'khor lo'i dbang phyug 'dren mchog bla ma dam pa dang rdo rje nag po chen po 'khor dang bcas pa la bdag 'bral med snying gi dkyil nas gsol ba 'debs so
'phrin las rgyas par gyur cig rgyud rgyal ston mdzad gar dgu'i nyams ldan he ru ka /

de dang gnyis med rigs kun bdag po bla ma yi/ /bka' nyan gtso bo srid gsum bza' byed nag po che/ /lcam dral bran g.yog pho nyar bcas pas bdag skyongs shig /bstan srung gang
gi zab mo'i chos tshul rnams/ /'phags pa'i yul du dar zhing rgyas mdzad pa'i/ /grub thob yongs kyi rgyan gyur bram ze che/ /mchog sred la sogs skyes mchog rnams la 'dud/
/gzhan yang lo chen blo gros grags pa sogs/ /gangs can

mun sel skad gnyis smra rnams dang / /yongs rdzogs bstan dang khyad par chos skyong 'di'i/ /mnga' bdag gyur pa sa skya'i bla chen rgyal/ /de sras rje btsun mched dang chos
rje pa/ /khu dbon dam pa kun grags bdag nyid che/ /mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs sogs bstan srung rnams/ /bran du 'khol ba'i skyes chen mchog rnams bsngags/ /khyad par snyigs
dus dpal ldan sa skya pa'i/ /bstan dang bstan 'dzin dgon gnas chos grwar bcas/ /nyams gso gsar du spel ba'i mdzad 'phrin can/ /sngags 'chang chos rje'i rnam thar bsam

bzhin dad/ /gang gi rigs dang chos las 'khrungs pa'i sras/ /nus mthu'i mnga' bdag bsod nams dbang po dang / /yab rjes sbas pa'i sangs rgyas bka' drin can/ /sngags 'chang grags
pa'i mtshan gyis bdag la srungs/ /phyi nang gsang ba'i dregs pa rgyud gsum po/ /dbyer med rang sems brjod bral gnyug ma'i ngang / /zung 'jug gdod ma'i mgon po mus pa
rje/ /brtan g.yo'i bdag po gang de spyi bos mchod/ /gzhan yang lugs 'di'i chos kyi drin nos pa'i/ /nyams rtogs mnga' bdag dbang phyug rab brtan dang / /deng sang gangs ljongs
bstan 'dzin kun gyi rgyan/ /ngag dbang chos grags bdag gi gtsug na mdzes/ /sngon gyi skyes chen tshul khrims 'bar de nyid/ /slar

yang sprul pa'i skur bstan spyan snga rje/ /la sogs bla ma rnams kyi zhabs zung la/ /yan lag mchog gis gus pas rab btud nas/ /bstan srung kun gyi gtso bo nag po che'i/ /zab
las ches zab chos tshul rgya mtsho rnams/ /'phags pa'i yul dang bod 'dir byung ba'i tshul/ /legs par bshad pa'i bstan bcos 'chad la spro/ /snyan brgyud zab mo yi ger bri
ba la/ /chos bdag mkha' 'gros gnang ba'i skabs phye la/ /bdag cag dpon slob rnams kyi 'di phyi'i don/ /'bad med lhun gyis grub pa'i dge legs stsol/ /ces mchod par brjod
cing bshad par dam bca' ba dang / 'phrin las 'chol ba'i tshig sngon du btang nas 'dir rdo rje 'chang chen po'i ye

shes kyi rnam 'phrul bstan srung rgya mtsho'i ded dpon/ rig pa 'dzin pa'i dam tshig gi gnyer kha ba/ ma ga dha rdo rje gdan gyi sgo skyong chen po/ 'phags yul gyi paN grub
rnams kyis yun du bsten zhing ches cher bsngags pa brjod pa/ bod yul bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras rnams kyi thun mong ma yin pa'i bka' srung dam pa
dpal rdo rje nag po chen po'i zab mo'i chos skor rnams byung ba'i tshul legs par bshad pa bstan srung chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba 'di 'chad pa la don gnyis te/
yid ches shing khungs btsun par bya ba'i phyir man ngag gi byung tshul bstan pa/ de las byung ba'i gdams pa dngos bstan pa'o/ /dang po la chos skyong gi chos skor spyir
bstan pa/ bye brag tu nag po chen po 'di'i chos skor byung tshul lo/ /dang po ni/ ji ltar yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che dang dpag bsam gyi shing la bdag 'dzin bsam

pa med kyang / gsol ba btab na 'dod dgu thams cad lhun grub tu 'byung ba ltar/ zung 'jug sku bzhi'i bdag nyid khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid chos sku de bzhin nyid
kyi ngang las ma g.yos bzhin du gzugs sku nyid kyi rnam 'phrul grangs las 'das pas/ gdul bya nam mkha'i mtha' klas pa'i khams dang bsam pa dang bag la nyal gyi rim pa
bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang mthun par chos kyi rnam grangs dpag med cig gsungs pa thams cad kyi don gyi bcud phyung ba/ zung 'jug rdo rje 'dzin pa'i go 'phang sgrub pa'i sgo
gcig pu ni bla med rdo rje theg pa yin te/ dpal kha sbyor las/ chos kyi phung po brgyad khri dang / /bzhi stong gi ni cho ga yis/ /lus kyi de nyid mi shes pas/ /de dag
thams cad 'bras med 'gyur/ /zhes dang / bye brag tu rtsa ba'i rgyud las/ gzhan pa'i sems kyi skad cig kyang / /dngos grub 'dod pas mi gnas so/ /zhes gsungs pa'i

phyir/ de lta bu'i lam zab mo sgrub pa dang / phan bde'i 'byung gnas bstan pa rin po che yun ring du gnas pa la phyi rol bdud la sogs pas thabs sna tshogs kyi sgo nas bar chad
byed pa yin te/ mdo las/ rin chen chos kyang dkon la rtag tu 'tshe ba mang / /zhes gsungs pas/ de'i bar chad bsrung ba dang / bstan pa yun ring du gnas pa'i phyir/ chos
skyong srung ma'i chos skor rnams gsungs pa yin te/ mgon po khros pa'i rgyud las/ gang du rdo rje theg pa yi/ /gsang ba 'dus pa'i yang dag las/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa srung
byed pa/ /snying po 'bras bu lam byed pa'i/ /'dren pa ye shes bstan pa bsrung / /'di nyid gsang ba'i bsgrub pa gang / /zhes dang / de'i lan du/ shes rab snying rje zung
'jug pa'i/ /ting 'dzin gang du bsgom gyur pa/ /bla med dkon mchog bstan pa la/ /rgol ba ngan pa bzlog par mdzad/ /thub

pa mchog gi bstan pa la/ /'dzin dang skyong dang srung ba gsum/ /lnga brgya dus kyi snyigs ma la/ /bdag tu gnyer zhing srungs zhing brtson/ /zhes dang / dus gsum sangs rgyas
thams cad kyi/ /bstan pa srung zhing bka' la gnas/ /dam tshig 'dzin pa'i zhing skyong pa/ /mgon po sa bcu'i dbang phyug gtso/ /dpal ldan rig 'dzin thams cad la/ /mchog
tu gyur pa'i las sgrub pa/ /dpal ldan nag po chen po ni/ /'dis ni lha min ma lus pa'i/ /g.yul las rgyal bar byed pa yin/ /zhes dang / bcom ldan tshe lo brgya ba'i dus/ /de
nyid bstan pa'i snyigs ma yi/ /lnga brgya pa yi dus kyi mthar/ /shin tu gdug cing rtsub pa dang / /mi bsrun pa yi dus kyi tshe/ /de tshe mgon po'i bstan pa 'byung / /zhes
sogs rgyas par gsungs so/ /de ltar srung ma la'ang 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa gnyis las/ 'jig rten pa'i

srung mas ni/ tshe 'dir dngos grub phra mo tsam sgrub par nus kyang skye ba phyi ma log pa'i lam la sbyor ba dang / mi dga' ba cung zad tsam la brten nas lus srog la rgol ba
sogs nyes dmigs che zhing / gnas skabs dang mthar thug gi don mtha' dag sbyin pa'i nus pa kho rang rnams la'ang med pas/ bsten kyang dgos pa chung ba yin te/ bod kyi mkhas
pa dag gis/ rang yang 'khor ba'i btson rar bcings pa yi/ /'jig rten lha yis su zhig skyob par nus/ /zhes gsungs/ des na 'jig rten las 'das pa'i srung ma zhig cis kyang
bsten dgos/ de la'ang yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid kyis rgyud sde rnams nas chos skyong rnam grangs bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig gsungs
pa thams cad mdor bsdus te rnam grangs kyi tshul du smos na/ drang nges kyi sgo nas dbye ba/ rgyud kyi sgo nas dbye ba/ phyi nang gi

sgo nas dbye ba/ go 'phang gi sgo nas dbye ba/ rigs kyi sgo nas dbye ba dang lngar 'dus/ dang po la/ nges don gyi mgon po/ drang don gyi mgon po dang gnyis/ dang po ni/ shrI
ni gnyis med ye shes te/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ sems nyid lhan cig skyes pa'i ye shes spros pa'i mtha' thams cad dang bral ba 'di nyid do/ /de'ang gang gnyis su med na stong
pa dang snying rje zung du 'jug pas na gnyis med do/ /de skad du'ang mngon par 'byung ba'i rgyud kyi le'u dang po las/ ma zhes pa ni sems pa'i snying rje dang / hA zhes
pa shes rab dang sbyor ba ste/ shes rab nyid do/ /kA la ni gnyis tshogs pa las 'dus te/ thabs dang shes rab kyi snying rje chen po la sbyar ba'o/ /zhes gsungs/ 'di nyid
la mtshon bya don gyi chos skyong ngam/ gnas lugs bde chen gyi chos skyong zhes kyang grags/ gnyis pa ni/ gdul bya rnams la snang bar gyur pa'i

gzugs kyi sku chos nyid mi 'gyur ba mtshon pas sku mdog nag po/ chos thams cad stong nyid du ro gcig pas zhal gcig pa/ bden gnyis thugs su chud pas phyag gnyis pa la sogs par
shar ba rnams so/ /'di la ni kun rdzob gzugs kyi mgon po zhes kyang bya/ mtshon byed brda'i chos skyong zhes kyang bya ste/ mgon po khros pa'i rgyud las/ nam mkha'i khams
kyi mthas gtugs pa/ /smon lam rnam par sbyong byed cing / /snying rje'i don brtson sems kyis ni/ /dpa' bos srid pa sbyong bar mdzad/ /sna tshogs gzugs can nor bu bzhin/
/zhes gsungs so/ /gnyis pa rgyud kyi sgo nas dbye ba la gsum ste/ dregs pa pho rgyud/ mo rgyud/ gnyis med kyi rgyud do/ /dang po ni/ mgon pos gtso byas nag po stong la
sogs pa rnams so/ /gnyis pa ni lha mos gtso byas pa'i ma mo bye ba

rnams so/ /gsum pa ni/ bla ma he ru ka 'khor khrag 'thung sha za bye ba 'bum sde rnams so/ /de dag la rgyud ces bya ste/ gang las 'phros pa'i gzhi gsal stong zung 'jug sems
can nas rdo rje 'dzin pa'i bar rgyun ma chad par gnas pa'i phyir te/ 'dus pa phyi ma las/ rgyud ni rgyun chags zhes bya'o/ /zhes gsungs/ gsum pa phyi nang gi sgo nas dbye
ba la gsum ste/ phyi'i mgon po/ nang gi mgon po/ gsang ba'i mgon po/ de skad du'ang mgon po khros pa las/ phyi nang gsang ba'i mgon po che/ /bde ba chen pos rol pa yi/
/ye shes gsang ba bsam mi khyab/ /tshe 'di nyid du 'grub 'gyur zhes/ /bcom ldan rdo rje can gyis gsungs/ /zhes sogs gsungs pa'i dang po ni phyi rol gyi 'dzam bu gling gi
dur khrod brgyad dang yul nyi shu rtsa bzhi la sogs pa na bzhugs pa'i chos skyong gtso 'khor gyi rnam

par snang ba rnams yin te/ khros pa'i rgyud las/ dur khrod gnas pa'i mgon po dang / /nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i zhing skyong bcas/ /phyi rol yul du rgyu ba rnams/ /de dag rim pas
bshad par bya/ /zhes dang / yul ni nyi shu rtsa bzhi yi/ /drag po'i zhing skyong nyi shu yi/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'khor lo yi/ /sa gsum rnam par khyab nas gnas/ /zhes gsungs
so/ /gnyis pa ni/ rdo rje'i lus kyi rtsa gsum 'khor lo lnga/ de dag gi nang na gnas pa'i khams dwangs ma rlung dang bcas pa rnams yin te/ mgon po mngon byung gi le'u
so gcig pa las/ a wa dhu ti dang / la la na dang / ra sa na rnams 'dus pa las mgon po'o/ /la la na shes rab kyi rang bzhin du shes pa'o/ /ra sa na khams bde ba'i rang bzhin
du shes pa'o/ /a wa dhU ti ni bde ba chen po'i rang bzhin can ma zhes pa ste/

khams dkar po bskyed pa dang / khams gsum pa bskyed pa'o/ /zhes gsungs/ de dag la gnad du bsnun tshul yang / le'u zhe bzhi par/ steng 'og gi rlung yang dag par bsnan te/ lte
ba'i dbus su bsgoms na zla ba drug gis nges par 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /zhes dang / dgang ba dang / dbyung ba dang / bum pa can rim pa ji lta ba dran par byas nas/ zla ba
phyed kyis mkha' spyod 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /zhes dang / le'u zhe brgyad pa las/ shes bya thams cad lte ba'i rtsa 'khor du mnan na 'gro ba rnams kyis bde ba the tshom med
par thob pa ni/ yul rnams ye shes kyi mes bsregs pas sgyu mar snang ba'o/ /zhes gsungs/ khros rgyud las/ dkyil 'khor lha lus nyid yin no/ /gzhan du lha dang dkyil 'khor ni/
/btsal bas rnyed par mi 'gyur zhes/ /'dren pa dpa' bos rtag tu gsungs/ /zhes dang / rtag tu sgrub pa po

rnams kyi/ /lus la yang dag gnas nas ni/ /dngos grub ster byed stobs mchog byed/ /ces gsungs so/ /gsum pa ni/ rang sems lhan cig skyes pa'i ye shes skye 'gag gnas gsum dang
bral ba gsal stong zung du 'jug pa'i bdag nyid can 'di nyid do/ /de skad du yang khros rgyud las/ sku gsung thugs kyi gsang ba las/ /drag po kun gyi srog gyur pa/ /zhes
dang / dwangs snyigs las ni rgyu 'bras kyi/ /gnas pa khyad par rten 'brel gyi/ /'khrul dang 'khrul pa ma yin pa/ /khams gsum kun la dbang byed pa/ /zhes gsungs so/ /bzhi
pa go 'phang gi sgo nas dbye ba la gsum ste/ ye shes kyi mgon po/ chos skyong gi mgon po/ 'jig rten gyi mgon po'o/ /dang po ni/ chos sku skye ba med pa la skye ba'i cho 'phrul
du snang ba mgon po rigs lnga la sogs pa rnams so/ /gnyis pa ni/

mthong lam nas sa phyed dang bcu gsum gyi bar ci rigs su gnas pa'i tshul 'dzin pa 'dod khams dbang phyug la sogs pa rnams so/ /gsum pa ni/ lha chen brgyad/ phyogs skyong bcu
la sogs pa 'jig rten pa'i tshul can rnams so/ /de dag kyang khros rgyud las/ 'jig rten chos dang ye shes kyi/ /mgon po'i khyad par mngon du 'byung / /zhes pas bstan no/
/'di la bdag gi bla ma mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags kyi gsung las/ de yang ye shes kyi mgon po ni rgyal ba rigs lnga la sogs pa longs sprul gyi cha
byad can gyi sangs rgyas rnams so/ /chos skyong gi mgon po ni/ sa la gnas pa'i byang sems mtha' dag dang / khyad par du ni gur mgon lcam dral la sogs pa 'das pa'i tshul
bzung ba'i chos skyong rnams so/ /'jig rten pa'i mgon po ni don la 'das pa yin kyang rnam pa 'jig rten pa'i tshul bzung ba'i

pu tra ming sring la sogs pa nas bzung ste/ dkar phyogs la dga' ba'i yi dwags mthu bo che'i bar yan chad do/ /'o na mgon po 'di nyid bcu gsum rdo rje 'dzin pa'i sa la bzhugs
pa yin pas ye shes kyi mgon po nyid yin no snyam na/ don la de ltar yin mod/ 'on kyang ye shes kyi mgon po ston pa sangs rgyas rnams kyi bka' nyan zhing bstan pa bsrung
ba'i tshul bzung bas na chos skyong mgon por bzhag go /gnad 'di go dgos so/ /las mgon rnams la ltos te ye shes kyi mgon po zhes pa'i tha snyad du thob pas/ de'i dbang du
mdzad nas yig cha 'ga' zhig las mgon po 'di la ye shes kyi mgon po zhes bshad pa yang yod do/ /rnam dbye phyed par gyis shig pu tra sogs kyi las mgon rnams la 'jig rten
pa'i mgon por bshad pa ni sgrub thabs gsang ba yid bzhin nor bu

sogs na yod pa yin te/ de nyid las 'jig rten pa rnams mos pho bskul ba yin pas/ thog mar mo'i bod pa/ oM ro ru sogs bzla bar bshad pa des rtogs nus pa yin no/ /zhes gsungs
so/ /lnga pa rigs kyi sgo nas dbye na lnga ste/ sku'i mgon po/ gsung gi mgon po/ thugs kyi mgon po/ yon tan gyi mgon po/ 'phrin las kyi mgon po'o/ /de skad du yang mgon po
khros pa las/ gdod nas grub pa'i dur khrod gnas/ /mkha' 'gro'i dbang phyug mgon po che/ /sku gsung thugs dang 'phrin las dang / /ye shes yon tan rigs kyi lha/ /zhes gsungs/
de yang dang po ni/ bde mchog khros pa mgon po phyag bzhi pa ste/ 'di ni mgon po mngon par 'byung ba dang / mgon po khros pa dang / khrag mtsho khol ma'i rgyud sogs
bod du 'gyur ba'i bcu gnyis tsam nas bstan cing / klu sgrub yab sras/ padma badzra/

slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pa sogs las brgyud de/ bla ma tsa mi dang / dpal chen sga lo la sogs pas gangs can gyi ljongs su spyan drangs te dar zhing rgyas par mdzad do/ /gnyis
pa ni/ spyan ras gzigs khros pa myur mdzad ye shes kyi mgon po phyag drug pa ste/ 'di ni mngon byung dang / khros rgyud le'u brgyad pa rnams las bstan cing / grub chen
sa ra ha dang / sha wa ri ba/ rwa hu la/ gupta badzra/ mnga' bdag mai tri pa rnams las brgyud de/ bla ma shangs pa dhu gu pa zhes grags pa mkhas grub chen po khyung po
rnal 'byor gyis bod yul du rgyas par mdzad do/ /gsum pa ni/ rnam snang chen po'i thugs kyi sprul pa rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po ste/ 'di ni 'og tu rgyas par 'chad
do/ /bzhi pa ni/ gtsug tor gdugs dkar gyi gzungs dang / mtshon bya mngon rol sogs nas bstan

pa'i legs ldan dang / beng la sogs pa ste/ padma 'byung gnas dang / dhi paM ka ra dang / padma lcags kyu sogs nas brgyud pa'o/ /lnga pa ni/ nag po gcer bu'i rgyud dang / gsang
ba thugs kyi dpe nag po sogs nas gsungs pa'i trag shad dang / stag zhon te/ slob dpon padma/ shintaM garbha/ ba ling ta a tsarYa sogs las brgyud pa'o/ /de ltar chos skyong
de dag gi bsgrub tshul gyi don bsdus na gsum ste/ ma ltar du bsgrub pa bkra shis/ sring ltar du sgrub pa snying nye/ bran ltar du sgrub pa las myur ro/ /dang po la
gnad gsum ste/ bca' ba rten gyi gnad/ bsgom pa lha'i gnad/ bzlas pa sngags kyi gnad do/ /gnyis pa la gzer gsum ste/ yid ches pa snying stobs bskyed pa'i gzer/ dam tshig bsrung
ba 'khu ldog med pa'i gzer/ thams cad sems kyi rnam 'phrul du shes pa'i sgrub pa gnad du tshud pa'i

gzer ro/ /gsum pa la ngar gsum ste/ bsgom pa ting nge 'dzin gyi ngar/ bzlas pa sngags kyi ngar/ bsad pa rdzas kyi ngar ro/ /de ltar chos skyong gi man ngag zab mo rnams nyams
su blangs pa la brten nas gnas skabs las bzhi'i dngos grub 'bad med du 'grub cing / mthar thug rdo rje 'dzin pa'i go 'phang tshe 'dir sgrub pa'i mchog kyang yin te/ khros
rgyud le'u dang po las/ phyi nang gsang ba'i mgon po che/ /bde ba chen po'i rol pa yis/ /ye shes gsang ba bsam mi khyab/ /tshe 'di nyid du 'grub 'gyur zhes/ /bcom ldan
rdo rje can gyis gsungs/ /zhes dang / ji srid las kyi sbyor ba yis/ /mgon po 'khor bcas mnyes gyur nas/ /las dang dngos grub sna tshogs pa/ /myur du 'grub par the tshom
med/ /ces dang / le'u nyer lnga pa las/ he ru ka yi go 'phang gnas/ /'di la the

tshom mi bya ste/ /zhes sogs rgyas par gsungs so/ /gnyis pa bye brag tu nag po chen po 'di'i chos skor byung tshul la drug ste/ sngon byung gi lo rgyus/ rgyud nas bstan tshul/
'phags yul rgya gar du bshad srol byung tshul/ bod kha ba can gyi yul du dar tshul/ khyad par rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras la bka' babs tshul/ de las snying por gyur
pa'i lam srol nges bzung ste bshad pa'o/ /dang po la gsum ste/ mgon po'i lo rgyus/ lha mo'i lo rgyus/ las mkhan gyi lo rgyus so/ /dang po ni/ sngon de bzhin gshegs pa gtsug
tor can gyi bstan pa la ri mo mkhan gyi rigs las byung ba'i dge slong bde ba'i 'khor lo zhes bya ba kha dog nag cing yid gtum pa bden pa bzhi'i bslab pa la gnas pa zhig
de bzhin gshegs pa de'i nye 'khor du byung / de yang mngon par shes pa cung zad dang ldan pas bdag ni mngon par shes pa dang ldan pa'o snyam du

mngon pa'i nga rgyal byed do/ /de la de bzhin gshegs pas dge slong khyod log pa'i nga rgyal de lta bu byed par mi rigs te/ dper na 'dod khams kyi dbang phyug chen po des lha
thams cad las bdag stobs che'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal gyis ri rab klad la bskor/ rgya mtsho chen po dbugs kyis rngub/ dga' bo dang nyer dga' la sogs pa'i klu chen po rnams
rgyan du byas/ nyi zla thod du bcings/ lha phran zas su za'o/ /de lta bu'i stobs dang ldan zhing / bdag ni 'jig rten 'di na stobs che ba yin no snyam pa'i nga rgyal byed
mod kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs ni nam mkha' dang mnyam la/ de'i stobs ni rtswa'i rtse mo'i rdul phran tsam du zad do/ /dge slong khyod kyang de dang 'dra bas mngon
pa'i nga rgyal ma byed cig ces gsungs pas/ dge slong de sems shin tu dman par gyur nas/ bdag ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor du gnas pa la dgos pa ci

zhig yod snyam pas lho phyogs kyi nags tshal zhig tu song nas gnas pa'i tshe/ de na dbang phyug chen po'i rten gcig yod pa la dge slong des zhag nyi shu rtsa gcig tu mchod
pa dang / skor ba la sogs pa byas nas gsol ba btab pa'i tshe/ rmi lam du dbang phyug chen pos dge slong khyed bdag gi sras su gyur te 'jig rten 'di na stobs che ba'i dngos
grub sbyin no zhes lung bstan to/ /de nas de bzhin gshegs pas dge slong de dbang phyug chen po la skyabs su song nas lam log par zhugs pa dgongs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa
dge slong gcig tu sprul nas nags tshal der dge slong de'i mdun du byon nas/ dge slong khyod 'dir ci zhig byed ces gsungs pas/ des smras pa/ bdag bcom ldan 'das kyi 'khor
du ma chud nas dbang phyug chen po la skyabs su song ba gcig yin no byas pas/ sprul pa'i dge slong gis smras pa/ yang dag lam ni rnyed gyur nas/ /'khrul pa'i

lam la 'jug byed pa/ /dper na gsal ba'i mig thob nas/ /rab rib skyon gyis bgos pa bzhin/ /dge slong khyod ni de lta bu'o/ /zhes smras pas/ dge slong de lhag pa'i bsam pa dang
ldan pas 'o na da ni bdag gis ci zhig bgyi zhes gsol ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dge slong des gsungs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa ni thabs mkhas la thugs rje chen po dang
ldan pa yin pas de'i spyan sngar bshags pa dang gso sbyong la sogs pa gyis shig /ces gsungs nas de nyid du mi snang bar gyur to/ /de nas dge slong des de bzhin gshegs pa'i
zhabs drung du phyin nas bshags pa dang gso sbyong byas bdag tshe 'di nyid kyis 'bras bu mthar phyin pa thob par lung bstan du gsol/ zhes zhus pas/ de bzhin gshegs pas
gsungs pa/ khyod rten log pa la skyabs su song ba'i mthus skye ba mang du brgyud pa'i dbang phyug chen po'i bu

drag po nag po zhes bya bar skye ba len/ de yang dag pa'i rten las log pas na nag po yin la/ dbang phyug chen pos 'jig rten na stobs che ba'i dngos grub byin pas na drag po
zhes bya'o/ /chen po ni srid pa gsum la dbang byed pas so/ /de'i mthar las kyi srin por skye ba blangs nas/ bskal pa bzang po 'di la rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid kyis btul te/
sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa bsrung bar sems bskyed nas/ byang chub sems dpa' nag po chen po zhes bya bar gyur nas/ des sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa bsrung ba'i bya ba rdzogs pa'i
'og tu rdo rjes brgyan pa zhes bya ba'i zhing khams su sangs rgyas thal ba'i dbang po zhes bya bar mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas par 'gyur ro/ /zhes lung bstan to/ /de
nas skye ba mang po brgyud pa'i mthar sangs rgyas 'od srung gi bstan pa la blon po'i bu zhig tu skyes te/ de rgyal po'i bu dang lhan cig tu yul phyogs 'ga' zhig tu sgra
slob tu phyin pas/ rgyal bus

ni sgra shin tu mkhas pa shes/ blon po'i bus ni ji ltar bslabs kyang ma shes/ de nas khong gnyis yul phyogs su log nas 'ong pa'i lam bar du byi'u gcig skad mang po 'byin pa
la rgyal po'i bus blon po'i bu la/ byi'u 'di ci skad zer ba yin dris pas ma shes/ rgyal bu nyid kyis/ khyed gnyis la lam du 'jigs pa mi 'ong phyin pas chog zer bar 'dug
zer/ de nas chu klung zhig gi 'gram na mar 'ong tsa na shing a mra'i me tog gcig chus khyer nas byung bas/ sbrul gcig na re/ bu lding zhes zer ro/ /rgyal bus de ji skad zer
ba yin shes sam byas pas/ blon po'i bu na re/ bdag gis ma shes rgyal bus mkhyen nam zer ro/ /rgyal bu na re/ a smra'i me tog smin pa ni/ /dri ma med pa'i chu yis khyer/
/zhes zer ba yin byas pa dang / blon po'i bu'i bsam pas/ nged gnyis sgra mnyam por slob tu 'ongs pa las kho ni

shin tu mkhas par 'dug ngas ni ci yang mi shes pas yul du 'grogs nas 'gro ba ngo tsha snyam nas/ bas mtha' nags tshal zhig gi gseb tu rgyal bu'i ske la smyug ma'i tshal pa
brgyab ste bsad do/ /de'i tshe rgyal bu na re/ nga'i pha ma la a pra shri pra zhes bya ba'i 'phrin 'di smros la ber ka 'di gtod cig zer nas shi bar gyur to/ /de nas blon
po'i bus yul du phyin te/ rgyal bu'i pha ma la smras pa/ khyed kyi rgyal bu shi ber ka 'di yin/ 'phrin a pra shri pra zhes zer ro byas/ de nas rgyal pos mchod gnas paNDi
ta lnga brgya yod pa la 'phrin 'di ji skad zer ba yin dris pas/ sgra de shes pa gcig kyang ma byung / der rgyal pos smras pa/ paNDi ta 'di tsam gyi nang nas mi shes pa mi
srid pas/ sang tshun chod la mi smra na thams cad gsod do zhes zer ro/ /de'i dus su de rnams kyi nang nas paNDi ta gcig gi bsam pa la/ paNDi ta lnga brgya'i nang nas

shes pa gcig kyang ma byung pas/ da shes pa mi 'ong bros na thar ba srid dam snyam nas nags tshal chen po zhig gi gseb tu bros pa dang / nags de'i gseb na mi ma yin ma smad
gnyis 'dug pas/ ma na re/ sang ni paNDi ta mang po gsod/ de rnams kyi sha khrag mang po bzar yong ngo zer ro/ /bu mo na re/ de rnams gsod pa'i rgyu mtshan ci yin zer bas/
mas sngar gyi rnam thar bshad do/ /bu mo na re/ sgra de sus shes zer ba la/ ma na re/ yul 'di skad bya ba na paNDi ta 'di skad bya ba yod des shes zer zhing 'dug pa thos
so/ /de nas paNDi ta des paNDi ta de la 'drir phyin pas/ paNDi ta des smras pa/ snying dang 'dra ba'i grogs po yis/ /nags tshal dgon par khrid nas ni/ /thor tshugs rdog
pas mnan byas te/ /ske la smyug ma'i tshal pa brgyab/ /ces bya ba yin zer ro/ /de nas paNDi ta des rgyal po'i rtsar

phyin te/ de skad smras pas/ rgyal pos blon po'i bu bsad do/ /de'i tshe des dmod bor ba dus nam zhig gi tshe nga nus pa dpag tu med pa dang ldan par gyur nas sems can thams
cad kyi srog dbugs la dbang byed par gyur cig ces smon lam btab bo/ /de nas de nyid skye ba mang du brgyud pa'i rjes su/ dzambu'i gling rgya gar gyi yul phyogs gcig na/
mang pos bkur ba'i rgyal po'i khab grong khyer sum brtsegs zhes bya ba'i pho brang gcig yod pa de dang nye ba'i byang phyogs nyi ma phyed kyi sa na/ dur khrod chen po so
si'i gling bya ba de na/ ro zas dang / ro gos thams cad gzhan bdag med par ce spyang gis za ba zhig yod pa la dur khrod der dus re zhig gi tshe dge slong legs ldan nag po
zhes bya ba pha ma med pa'i khye'u mdog nag po gcig tu gyur to/ /des chos nyid skye ba med pa'i don ni ma rtogs/ lus dka' thub kyi sgo nas sdom pa bsrung zhing

gnas pa la dur khrod der gnas pa'i ma mo mkha' 'gro rnams kyis mi sha phul ba gsol/ de nas rim bzhin ro sha ro gos/ ro zas thams cad la longs spyad pas/ grong khyer gsum brtsegs
pa'i mi kha cig na re/ dur khrod na srin phrug mi zan gcig 'dug zer/ phal cher na re/ dge slong dur khrod pa 'di bsod snyoms mi byed pa la dpyad na/ 'o skol gyis ro
bskyal ba thams cad za ba 'dra zhing / nam zhig mi gson po brkus nas bzar 'ong bas 'di gsod dgos zer nas/ grong khyer gsum brtsegs pa'i dmag dpung thams cad der phyin pa
dang / dge slong gis gsod par shes nas/ nga ni srin po min/ chos rtse gcig tu yid la byed pa'i phyir dur khrod 'dir bsgom pa yin byas kyang ma phan par mtshon bsnun to/
/der dge slong zhe sdang gi mtshams sbyar nas 'chi ba'i tshe dmod pa 'di ltar bor te/ ngas

dur khrod 'dir lo dgu'i bar du tshul khrims bsrung / dka' thub byas nas sems can gyi don byed par sems bskyed pa la/ khyed rnams kyis bar chad byas te bsad pas/ nga shi ma
thag tu gnod sbyin chen po ma rung ba zhig tu gyur nas/ spyir sems can thams cad kyi srog dbugs sdud par gyur cig khyad par du grong khyer gsum brtsegs kyi rgyal po rgyal
srid dang bcas pa thams cad kyi gshed mar gyur cig ces smon lam btab bo/ /de nas dge slong de'i bden pa'i mthu dang / sngar dbang phyag chen po la skyabs su song zhing /
des dngos grub byin pa'i stobs kyis/ sangs rgyas kyis sngar lung bstan pa bzhin du dge slong de shi ma thag ri rab kyi zom du lha dbang phyug chen po dang / lha mo u ma
gnyis kyi bur skyes so/ /de yang ji ltar byung zhe na/ ri rab kyi byang shar mtshams na shing yongs 'du sa brtol zhes kyang bya/ dpag bsam gyi shing zhes kyang bya/ a shwattha
zhes kyang bya/ rtsa ba

rgya mtsho chen po nas skyes te lha min gyi yul nas song ba/ rtse mo 'dod khams kyi lha yul du slebs pa la bya khyung gis tshang bcas pa/ lo ma la 'dod yon lnga rang byung
du 'byung ba/ 'bras bu la rin chen sna bdun lo tog ltar smin pa/ yal ga g.yur za ba'i bar nas lha dang / lha mo dang / gza' dang / rgyu skar dang / nyi zla'i tshogs kyis
brgyan pa/ rtsa ba'i ngos na khrus kyi rdzing bu bdun yod/ de re re la shing rta re re/ shing rta re re la bu mo bdun bdun/ de re re la g.yog mo bdun re/ de re re la rma
bya bdun re yod pa/ shing de'i phyogs mtshams thams cad na sman rnam pa sna tshogs dang / lo tog gi rigs sna tshogs rang byung du skye ba/ tsandan gor shi sha dang / sbrul
gyi snying po dang / ga pur la sogs pas brgyan pa'i rdzing bu lnga brgyas bskor ba/ de lta bu'i shing de ni lha dang lha ma yin thun mong gi bsod nams las skyes so/ /de
dus

na shing de'i rtse mo 'dod khams kyi lha yul na yod pas/ lo ma dang 'bras bu lha rnams kyis bdag gir byas shing longs spyad pas/ ri rab sked pa 'od ma'i snang ba zhes bya ba'i
gnas na/ lha ma yin gyi rgyal po gsum brtsegs dang / thag bzang ris dang / dhe ra na ke shu dang / rnam par snang byed dang / rab sil dang / sgra gcan 'dzin la sogs pa
bye ba dung phyur tsam shin tu mi sdug pa'i cha byad du byas nas rab tu rngam pa'i nga ro dang / 'jigs shing dregs pa'i mtshon cha sna tshogs thogs nas ri rab kyi steng
chos bzang zhes bya ba'i gnas su lhags nas/ ri rab kyi steng na lha ba su de ba dang / mahA de ba dang / brgya byin nyid la sogs pa lha'i tshogs rnams la/ lha ma yin rnams
kyis smras pa/ ri rab rtser gnas sum cu rtsa gsum lha/ /shing 'di lha dang lha min thun mong la/ /da lta khyed cag lha rnams dbang byed na/ /da ni nged cag lha min

bdud la blang / /zhes smras pa dang / lha rnams kyis smras pa/ dpag bsam shing la 'dod yon bsam yas kyang / /bsod nams dbang gis lha la yongs su grub/ /gzhan la yod na med
cing skam par 'gyur/ /de bas khyed la ljon shing nged mi ster/ /zhes smras pa la/ lha ma yin rnams kyis smras pa/ thun mong las grub bde ldan ljon pa'i shing / /lha yis dbang
byas nged la mi ster na/ /'jig rten dregs pa'i mtshon cha'i char phab nas/ /lha dang lha min g.yul chen 'gyed par bya/ /zhes smras te slar song nas lha ma yin gyi dmag
drangs so/ /de yang glang po che sa bsrungs kyi mgo sum cu rtsa gnyis la gnod sbyin sum cu rtsa gnyis zhon/ dbus kyi mgo bo la lha ma yin gyi dbang po thags bzang ris
zhon/ glang po che'i sna la ral gri kA ma la nag po btags nas lha ma yin gyi dmag bye

ba dung phyur gyis bskor te rdzu 'phrul gyis nam mkha' la 'ongs nas mtshon cha'i char chen po me lce 'khrugs pa ltar 'bebs shing lhags pas/ chos bzang zhes bya ba'i mdun sar
lha rnams 'tshogs te 'thab par rtsom pa la/ dang por lha rnams kyis khro ma shes par rtsub 'gyur gyi khang pa na/ khro bo lang ka ta nag po khros pa'i kha chu'i rdzing
bu bdun 'khyil ba las 'thungs so/ /der lha rnams zhe sdang skyes te/ shin tu khro bar gyur nas lha'i bzo bo bi shwa karmas nub gcig la gser khrab bye ba dgu 'bum brdungs/
lha mahA kro dhas nub gcig la ral gri dang / 'khor lo dang / tho ba dang / lcags kyu dang / dgra satwa dang / mdung rtse gsum pa bye ba phrag dgu khri dgu 'bum brdungs/
dus der glang po che rab tu brtan pa'i mgo sum cu rtsa gnyis la nye dbang sum cu rtsa gnyis zhon/ dbus kyi mgo bo la lha'i dbang po brgya byin nyid zhon/ lha

dmag bye ba dung phyur gyis go mtshon thogs te dpung gis mtha' brten/ glang po che'i sna la spu gri btags nas lha dang lha ma yin g.yul bkye zhing phan tshun mtshon brgyab
pas/ lha ma yin gyi khrag bo ba rnams bdud dmag khri tsam du 'phel/ lha ma yin gyis mtshon brgyab pa'i lha'i khrag las dmag ma 'phel bar shi'o/ /der lha thams cad ni pham/
lha ma yin rnams rab tu rgyal ba'i dus na/ dpal phyag na rdo rjes lha rnams rab tu rgyal ba'i phyir thugs ka nas hU~M yig mthing nag 'bar pa zhig sprul te/ lha biShNu rA
dza'i dpral ba'i dbus su thim pas lcags kyi mdzer pa chen po gcig tu gyur/ mdzer pa de brdol ba'i nang nas bud med sngo sangs ma mtshan dang dpe byad du ldan pa dbu skra
baiDUrYa'i chun 'phyang g.yon du 'phyang ba/ mig utpala'i 'dab ma 'dra ba mdzes shing

yid du 'ong ba zhig byung / de la lha rnams kyis u ma de wa zhes bya bar mtshan gsol/ don la srung ma spyi'i yum du gyur pa sngags srung drag mo e ka dza Ti nyid yin no/ /de
nyid lha kun gyis chung mar 'dod pa las/ phyag na rdo rje'i sprul pas nam mkha' las tshig bcad 'di skad grag go /lha yi rgyal srid mtho zhing brtan pa dang / /rigs drug
sems can bde la 'god pa dang / /lha min bdud kyi g.yul chen bzlog pa'i phyir/ /dbang phyug lha la u ma chung mar byin/ /zhes grag go /dus de tsa na ri rab kyi zom/ dzambu
gling gi nub byang mtshams yakSha ka ma la 'bar ba'i dur khrod na/ lha mahA de wa dge slong gi cha lugs su 'gog pa'i brtul zhugs drag po la bzhugs pa'i dus su u ma de wa
khrid nas btsun mor phul bas/ zhag bdun phrag bdun gyi bar du lus kyi drod la bcar zhing 'khrig pa spyad pa'i sbyor

mtshams nas/ gza' dang skar ma byung nas bar snang la song bar grag go /der lha mo u ma de wa la bu tsha ming sring gnyis skyes pa'i/ ming po la gshin rje mahA kA la zhes btags
te/ mdog nag cing bzhin mi sdug pa shin tu gtum zhing gzi brjid 'bar bas nag po drag po zhes kyang grags so/ /sring mo la mdog nag cing khros pas mahA ka li zhes sam/
tsa muntri te rgan byed mar grags/ dpal lha mo zhes kyang btags so/ /nag po chen po la phas gri gug lag char byin/ mas thod pa 'thung snod du byin te/ ming sring gnyis
chos bzang lha'i 'dun sar spyan drangs nas lha mang pos phyag byas/ lha'i dbang pos rnam par rgyal ba'i khang bzang du mchod pa byas/ lha'i dmag dpon nyi shu rtsa brgyad
kyis tshal chen po bzhir mchod pa byas/ dpag bsam shing gi rtsa ba dang /

rdo a mo li ka'i khar yang lha'i bu bye ba khrag khrig gis mchod pa byas/ chos bzang lha'i 'dun sar lha rnams kyi dmag dpon du mnga' gsol/ dpal phyag na rdo rjes bdud las rnam
par rgyal ba'i dbang bskur te/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa srung bar bka' bsgos shing dam la btags so/ /de nas skar ma rgyal gyi nyin bar nyi ma byang phyogs kyi gnod sbyin
chen po brgyad ni khyung chen dang lcags kyi bya khrar sprul/ btsan dang dri za'i tshogs ni skyes pa stag chas can gyi tshogs su sprul/ gza' rgod dang srog bdag rgyal
po'i tshogs ni sngags nag dang dgra bcom du sprul/ ya bdud dang ma bdud kyi tshogs ni bdud dmag khri chig stong du sprul/ de ltar lha ma srin sde brgyad kyi dmag tshogs
bye ba dung phyur dang bcas pa'i 'khor gyis bskor nas ming sring gnyis kyis lha rnams kyi dmag dpon byas te/ lha ma yin dang g.yul bkye nas 'thab pa'i tshe/

mahA kA la'i lag na gsal shing ri rab tsam zhig thogs te klad la bskor zhing brgyab pas lha ma yin gyi g.yul bcom/ da lta phyag mtshan beng dang gandhe 'ong ba'i rgyu mtshan
yang de yin/ lha ma yin gyi grong khyer gsum brtsegs kyang rdul du brlags/ gri gug gis lha ma yin gyi ske bcad/ thod par khrag bzed cing 'thungs pas/ lha'i rnam pa las
'gyur te gnod sbyin gyi gzugs nag cing shin tu 'jigs par gyur/ lha mos ral gri me'i phreng ba can gyis/ lha ma yin he ratna pakShu'i mgo bo bcad/ lha dmag mang po rnams kyis
mtshon gyi char phab nas lha ma yin gyi dmag rnams bsad/ mgon po dang lha mos lha min gyi khrag rnams thod pa'i nang du bcus shing rol bas khrag gis ra ro zhing mig rtsa
dmar por gyur/ lha min gyi khrag dmag mir sprul ba 'phel mi nus par byas/ tsa muntri'i

lto ba la lha dmag bye ba'i rdzong bcas nas 'thab pas lha ma yin pham par byas/ lha dmag dkar po rgyal te dpag bsam shing gi mnga' bdag tu gyur to/ /de nas srin yul lang ga
spu ri na srin po'i grong khyer bdun 'bum yod pa lha rnams kyis bcom nas/ srin po da sha gri ba dang / de'i sring mo na la rtse gnyis 'dus pas/ da sha gri bas lha mi 'dul
ba'i phyir/ sring mo lha dbang phyug chen po'i btsun mor phul/ de gnyis 'dus pa las bu mo ya mtshan can gcig skyes/ de lha mo tsa muntra'i g.yog tu phul/ des rim bzhin
bslus nas/ lha mo tsa muntri srin po'i chung mar song / de la lha mo u ma khros te dmod pa phyin ci log tu bor/ ming po mahA kA la yang khros nas/ srin po 'khor dang bcas
pa thams cad bcom/ yul lang ka pu ri gtan nas brlag par byas so/ /de'i rgyu mtshan brtags pas lha rnams kyis lan par

shes te/ mahA kA la lha rnams la yang khros nas/ lha'i mtshon cha 'khor lo'i nang du phyir bzlog pa'i sbyor ba byas nas bcug pas/ lha dang lha ma yin 'thab pa'i tshe/ lhas
'khor lo 'phangs pas 'khor lo phyir log nas slar lha rnams pham par byas/ der yab dbang phyug chen po khros te/ mgon po nag po ri rab kyi steng nas bskrad pas/ nag po rab
tu 'khrugs shing khros pa'i ha ha dang hU~M hU~M gi tsham rngams kyi gad mo bsgrags pas/ ri rab kyang 'gul 'degs 'gyel la khad pa tsam du gyur/ zhabs drag tu brdabs pas
sa gzhi thams cad g.yos shing dum bur 'khrugs nas mar babs te/ ri rab kyi kha khyer la gnas pa'i gnod sbyin 'od zer can zhes bya ba/ dbang phyug chen pos 'jig rten na dbang
che ba'i dngos grub byin pa gcig yod pa de bsad/ sha zos khrag 'thungs nas/ phas byin pa'i dngos grub

nyams par byas/ nag po yang gnod sbyin gyi gzugs 'jigs su rung ba mche ba zangs yag tu gtsigs pa gcig tu gyur to/ /de nas 'od zer can de dzambu gling du nya pa'i rigs zhig
tu skyes so/ /des kyang sngar gyi bag chags dang / las dbang gis rgyal po'i pho brang grong khyer gsum brtsegs dang nye bar/ lha ma yin gyi grong khyer gsum brtsegs dang
'dra ba'i khang pa gsum brtsegs byas nas/ der gnas te/ dbang phyug chen pos sngar bzhin thun mong gi dngos grub kyang sbyin no/ /der drag po nag po yang las kyi stobs kyis
dzambu'i gling gi grong khyer gsum brtsegs dang nye ba dur khrod so si'i gling du babs nas/ dur khrod kyi 'jigs byed pho mo thams cad dang / sha za dang / srin po dang
/ gnod sbyin dang / ma mo'i tshogs thams cad kyis phyag byas shing 'khor du bsdus nas/ grong khyer gsum brtsegs pa

rnams la gnod par brtsams pa na/ khong rnams kyis nag po 'ong ba'i lam srang du dug gi la du dang / myos byed kyi chang sna tshogs bzhag pas/ nag pos zos 'thungs pas/ mthun
rdzas su song nas slar nus pa ches cher rgyas par gyur/ de nyid bsrung bar 'dod pas/ grong khyer gyi shar sgor yungs kar/ lhor sgog pa/ nub tu rang byung gi rakta/ byang
du btsan dug byang shar du sha chen/ shar lhor dri chen/ lho nub tu tsha ba gsum/ nub byang du klad pa rnams bsregs pa'i dud pa btang pas/ des kyang slar mthu stobs dang
ldan par gyur pas/ da lta la du dang / chang dang / spos sbyor rnams dam rdzas su dgos pa'i rgyu mtshan yang de yin/ de nas nag pos phas byin pa'i gri gug phyag g.yas su
khyer/ mas byin pa'i thod pa phyag g.yon par thogs/ gsal shing gru mor bcug

ste 'khor gdug pa can rnams dang bcas pas/ spyir sems can gyi srog gi gshed ma byas/ khyad par grong khyer gsum brtsegs pa'i rgyal blon 'bangs 'khor dang bcas pa thams cad
bsad de/ sha zos khrag 'thungs/ grong khyer thams cad bshig bcom brlag par byas pas/ grong khyer gsum brtsegs 'jigs byed pa/ /zhes bstod pa'i rgyu mtshan de yin/ de nas sngar
gyi spyod pa rgyu mthun pa'i las kyi dbang gis/ 'od zer can nya par skyes pa de yang bsad nas sha zos khrag 'thungs so/ /der srid pa gsum na dbang che ba'i tshangs pa
dang brgya byin la sogs pas kyang ma thub par/ nang sems can brgya za/ nub sems can brgya za zhing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad brlag la khad du gyur pa dang / 'phags
pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis sems can rnams la thugs rjes gzigs nas/ nag po drag po 'dul ba'i don du khro bo'i dbang po

dpal rta mgrin du sprul nas/ dbu'i gtsug nas rta mgo ljang gu phyung ste/ rta skad lan gsum bsgrags pa/ nag po na re/ khyod la nga 'dul ba'i gnyer med kyi/ khyod rang nags
su song la rtswa zo zer nas ma thul lo/ /der dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas thams cad bka' bgros shing mgrin gcig tu thugs gtad nas/ nag po drag po de gzhan gyis mi 'dul zhing
/ phyag na rdo rjes 'dul ba'i dus la babs par dgongs nas/ phyag na rdo rje la zhal 'dzum pa mdzad cing / 'od zer gyis bskul bas/ phyag na rdo rje shin tu rngam pa'i skur
bzhengs/ 'jigs su rung ba'i rdo rje'i hU~M sgra drag po bsgrags/ nag po 'khor bcas/ phyag g.yas pas rdo rjes bsdigs/ g.yon pas sdigs mdzub kyis gzir bas/ nag po 'khor bcas
'jigs shing skrag pas rdo rje 'dzin pa'i spyan sngar 'khod de/

'di skad ces gsol to/ /kye/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ston pa lags/ /bdag gis khyed kyi gzi mi bzod/ /dam la btags 'tshal ci gsung bsgrub/ /khyed kyi bstan pa bsrung bar bgyi/

skyong ma'i spyan sngar phyin te/ dpon g.yog gnyis 'grogs nas srid pa gsum gyi sems can zad cing stong par byed pa'i dus g.yog mos bong bu'i phyir brgyugs pas thang chad

srin mo na la rtse'i rgod ma zangs kyi so can gnyis chags pa spyad pa las/ dre'u sngon mo rlung gi gshog pa can gcig byung ba la/ rgyu ma'i mthur brgyus zangs kyi sga bstad
nas jo mos khol mo'i bzhon par byin no/ /de nas jo mos bong bu gwa dmar la zhon/ khol mo dre'u sngon mo la zhon/

jo mos mi lpags gyon/ thod pa dang ral gri lag char thogs/ khol mos re lde nag po gyon/ lag na khram bam dang sho dhe'u thogs/ lha mo dpon g.yog gnyis mthu rtsal shin tu che
bar gyur te/ 'jig rten gyi ma mo dkar mo rdo rje pho nya mo'i tshogs dang / sngon mo ral pa 'dzing ma'i tshogs dang / dmar mo gtum mo'i tshogs dang / ser mo mkha' la bzhad
ma'i tshogs dang / dkar dmar mthing ser ljang ba'i lha mo dang / shin tu 'jigs pa'i bdud mo dang / sha khrag la rab tu dga' ba'i srin mo dang / dur khrod g.ya' gangs
nags khrod la gnas pa'i ba lam ma dang / rgya mtsho la sogs pa'i chu dang / rlon drod la gnas pa'i khri sman ma la sogs pa ma mo bsam gyis mi khyab pa mang po yang lha mo
dpon g.yog gi 'bangs bgyi'o zhes zer zhing bran du khas blangs/ lha mo des 'jig rten gyi ma mo thams cad kyi dpon mo byas te/

skye ba rnam bzhi'i sems can thams cad zos nas zad pa la thug go /lha mo dpon g.yog gnyis ni bud med kyi rang bzhin du gyur pas/ rtag par 'dod pa'i 'khrig pa spyod pa'i ched
du rje mo la khyo lnga/ khol mo la khyo bzhi ste/ rje mo'i khyo lnga ni/ gza' ra hu la/ srin po sgra ldan/ gshin rje ma ru tse/ bdud 'char kha nag po/ klu nA ga kunda li
dang lnga'o/ /khol mo'i khyo bzhi ni/ 'byung po dge ba/ bgegs bi na ya ka gnod sbyin yakSha kA la/ rlung wa ya we gdong dang bzhi'o/ /de lta khyo dgu ni dpon g.yog gnyis
kyis nyin bar mchan khung du skung zhing sbed/ mtshan mo dur khrod du rgyu zhing rol ba'i sbyor ba byed do/ /de nas lha mo de sngon mar me mdzad kyi bstan pa la sangs rgyas
shAkya thub pa'i bstan pa bsrung bar smon lam btab pa'i las 'phros sbrel zhing dge ba spyad

pa'i shugs kyis byang chub kyi shing drung na bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa bzhugs pa'i spyan sngar phyin te/ lha mo dpon g.yog gis byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed/ bcom ldan
'das kyi zhabs la phyag 'tshal te/ rang rang gi srog gi snying po phul nas bstan pa bsrung bar khas blangs so/ /de nas lha mo dpon g.yog de gnyis kyis/ a su ra'i brag
phug ces bya ba ri phug zab mo zhig tu phyin pas/ de na bram ze mchog sred sgrub pa byed pa dang 'phrad do/ /lha mos khyod 'di na ci byed byas pas/ bram ze na re/ sngon yul
khams 'di nyid na dge slong bstan pa'i sde dang / dge slong ma dar ma di zhes bya ba gnyis 'khrig pa spyad nas 'dul khrims nyams pa la/ rgyal pos chad pa bcad nas bsad
pa skye ba 'phos te/ bdud lam nga dge'u ri dang / ro sha kha da gnyis su gyur te/ yul 'di'i mi phal cher zos/ da ni nga la za res babs pas/ nga bdud de gnyis 'dul ba'i phyir
yum

e ka dza Ti ral gcig ma sgrub bo zer bas/ lha mo dung skyong ma na re/ nged dpon g.yog kyang sgrub pa byas na yon tan de lta bu yod dam byas pas/ bram ze na re/ khyed gnyis
ci 'dod pa yin zer ba las/ lha mos nged gnyis 'dod khams kyi dbang mo cher gyur nas/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa bsrung ba'i dngos grub 'dod byas pas/ 'o na bsgrub par bya'o
zer nas bram ze dang lha mo dpon g.yog gis lhan cig sgrub pa byas pas yum e ka dza Ti'i zhal mthong zhing grub pa thob/ e ka dza Tis lha mo dung skyong ma'i ming ni dpal
lha mo mahA kA lir btags/ khol mo'i ming ni yakSha re ma tir btags nas 'dod khams 'dul ba'i mthu mo cher dbang bskur/ shAkya thub pa'i bstan pa bsrung ba'i gnyer gtad/
lha mo dpon g.yog gis kyang rang rang gi srog gi snying po phul nas bstan pa bsrung bar khas blangs/ bdud lam lnga ge'u

ri dang / re sha kha da yang bsgral nas/ bram ze mchog sred kyis kyang rang gi dngos grub thob par byas so/ /bdud kyi khram bam nag po yang phrogs nas bong bu'i snga sha la
btags/ sa'i lha mo brtan mas rna gru mched brgyad 'bangs su phul/ der lha mo nag mo dpon g.yog gis sngon srin po dang 'khon pa'i dbang gis srin po'i yul du dmag drangs nas/
srin po rakSha kho re ral gri brgyab nas bsad/ srin po'i ya 'gal la bong sga'i snga ru byas/ ma 'gal la phyi ru byas/ rgyu mas mthur srab byas/ srin po'i ske rags sbrul
gyi zhags pas ske rags dang gong rmed byas/ srin po'i bzhon pa ba lang dmar po'i pags pa bshus nas 'dom phyed dkris/ srin po'i gos re lde nag po bshus nas 'dom phyed dkris
te gyon no/ /de nas 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug dpal rta mgrin du sprul ba'i sgrub pa byas pas rta mgrin gyi zhal mthong zhing gsang ba'i gzungs ma byas te
rje mo'i

ming dpal ldan lha mo nag mor btags/ khol mo'i ming rdo rje glog ma sprin du btags/ phyag rgya chen po'i dbang bskur las kyi lhar byin gyis brlabs/ lha mo dpon g.yog gis kyang
dpal rta mgrin la rang rang gi srog gi snying po phul nas bstan pa bsrung bar khas blangs te/ de nas sngon gyi ma lha mo u ma dang / srin mo na la rtse gnyis kyis kyang
bu mo gnyis dran nas srin lag gi rtses nu zhos 'thor zhing / dred mo'i ral pas g.yab nas bos pas bu mo gnyis rang dbang med par ma gnyis kyi drung du slebs/ dbang bskur
zhing dam tshig bsgrags/ bstan pa'i srung mar bskos so/ /lha mo dpon g.yog gnyis la 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal pos kyang / rang gi rtsa'i khrag dang khu ba'i mchod pa
byas te lha dang mi'i rgyal srid phul/ rma bya rin po che'i gshog pa can spyi bor nor bu rin po che yod pa gcig rje mo la nor skal du sbyin/

bya de mo nag mo spyi bo na rin po che yod pa zhig khol mo la nor du byin/ lha mo dpon g.yog gnyis 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal pos byin pa'i rma bya dang / de mo nag mo gnyis
la gtan gyi nor skal du byed cing chags so/ /de nas dur khrod ro thang nag po'i dbus ma ru rtse'i sgo 'gram du dpal lha mo dpon g.yog gis dpal khrag 'thung he ru ka'i
dngos grub bsgrubs pas dpal chen po'i zhal mthong dbang bskur rdo rje pho nya mo drug cu rtsa bzhi 'khor du bskos/ padma gar gyi dbang phyug gi sprul pa dang yang sprul du
lung bstan/ jo mo'i ming ni dpal ldan lha mo nag mo re ma ti dur khrod kyi bdag mo zhes bya bar btags/ khol mo'i ming ni gnod sbyin shan pa nag mo re ma tir btags/ lha
mo dpon g.yog gis kyang srog gi snying po phul zhing sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa bsrung bar khas blangs so/ /de nas ri bo ma la ya'i rtse mor lha mo dpon g.yog gis dpal phyag
na rdo rje bsgrubs pas

zhal mthong / srog gi snying po phul/ sangs rgyas stong gi bstan pa bsrung bar dbang bskur/ rje mo'i ming arYa re ma tir btags/ khol mo'i ming shan pa nag mor btags so/ /de
nas dpal ldan lha mo nag mo dpon g.yog de gnyis mthu dang rdzu 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pas srid pa gsum na 'gran pa'i zla thams cad dang bral bar gyur pas/ lha dang lha
ma yin thams cad kyis phyag dang bkur bsti byas/ 'dod pa'i khams thams cad la dbang bsgyur bas 'dod khams kyi dbang phyug ma'am gtso mo chen mor gyur te/ lha tshangs pas
rma bya'i rgyal mtshan phul/ khyab 'jug gis nyi zla'i rgyan phul/ rnam thos sras kyis sbrul gyi gdengs ka phul/ nam mkha'i lha phran rnams kyis dril bu rna ba'i rgyan du
phul/ lha mo srin mo sha za rnams kyis thod phreng dang thod khrag zhag gi thig le zo ris rnams phul/ lha ma srin sde brgyad la sogs pa dregs pa can thams

cad kyis 'khor dang bran g.yog tu khas blangs so/ /mdor na 'di pa'i lugs kyi lha mo u ma de wi ni yum chen e ka dza Ti/ dka' zlog ma/ 'jigs byed chen mo/ nag mo chen mo sogs
mtshan gyi rnam grangs dang ldan pa'i ye shes dbyings kyi rje mo zhes bya ba 'khor 'das thams cad dam/ dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad bskyed pa'i yum shes rab kyi pha rol
tu phyin ma'i ngo bor 'dod pa yin la/ lha mo dung skyong ma ni rje mo re ma ti zhes bya ba/ 'di'i rigs thams cad chibs su bong bu chibs shing / phyag mtshan ral gri dang
thod khrag ne'u le 'dzin pa/ glang chen dang mi lpags kyi stod g.yogs/ ba lang gi ko ba dang re lde'i smad g.yogs can du 'ong ba shas che/ srin mo dmar 'dab phur pa'i
lha ni khol mo re ma ti 'am bdud mo re ma tir grags pa yin/ 'di'i rigs rnams dre'u la zhon zhing phyag mtshan khram bam/ be con/ dbyug tho/ nad rkyal/ nal thod/

sho dhe sogs 'dzin pa/ re lde nag po'i stod g.yogs dang / stag gi sham thabs la sogs pa 'ongs pa shas che/ 'on kyang 'di rnams rgyud gcig pas rje mo dang g.yog mo'i rnam 'gyur
gang 'dul sna tshogs su ston pa yin pas/ mtha' gcig tu nges pa ni med do/ /zhar byung dam pas mdzad pa'i bskang gsor/ g.yog gnyis 'jigs ma zhes gsungs pa ni/ mai tri
pas mdzad pa'i bstod par mdun gyi sna 'dren chu srin gdong dang / slad kyi rjes 'brang seng ge'i gdong can gnyis la bshad pa ltar yin no/ /ba lang ma dang / khri sman ma
ni gong du bshad pa ltar dur khrod g.ya' gangs nags khrod la gnas pa dang / rgya mtsho la sogs pa'i rlan gsher la gnas pa'i ma mo'i ming gi rnam grangs yin pas/ ba glang
gi gdong can dang / kr-iShNa sa ra'i gdong can du 'dod pa sogs ni rang bzo'i tshod dpags yin par zad do zhes bla ma

'ga' zhig gi gsung las 'byung yang / bris thang rnying pa du mar ba glang gi gdong sogs bris pa 'byung bas cung zad brtag pa'i gnas yin par yang bla ma dag gsung ngo // ! //gsum
pa las mgon gyi lo rgyus ni/ sngon gyi dus rgya gar shar phyogs kyi bas mtha'i ri brag zab mo zhig na/ bram ze ming sring gsum tshangs spyod kyi dka' thub la gnas shing
dge ba spyod pa las/ yul de'i skyes pa dang bud med kyi tshogs rnams dad cing 'dun par gyur nas bsnyen bkur byas pas/ yul de'i rab byung dang sngags pa la sogs pa sngon
gzhan gyis bkur ba rnams la bsnyen bkur med par gyur to/ /de'i tshe de dag gi bsam pa la/ da lta bram ze ming sring 'di dag yod pas bdag cag rnams gzhan gyis spangs pas/
'di gsum gsad par bya'o zhes gros bshams nas/ rab byung dang sngags pa de dag gis rang gi bsgo ba nyan pa'i skyes pa dang bud med dag bskul

nas bram ze ming sring gi drung du phyin te gsod par brtsams pa dang / de gsum gyis gsod par shes nas smon lam log par btab ste/ ming po che bas bdag 'di rnams kyis bsad pa
dang / gshin rje ma rung pa zhig tu gyur nas/ 'di rnams gsod par gyur cig bsad nas kyang 'di dag nga'i bran du gyur cig ces pa dang / de bzhin du ming po chung bas kyang
tshe 'phos ma thag bdud ma rung pa zhig tu gyur nas 'di rnams bsad de nga'i bran du gyur cig sring mos nga bsad pa dang gnod sbyin ma chen mo zhig tu gyur nas 'di rnams
bsad de nga'i bran du gyur cig ces dmod bor/ de nas khong rnams kyis bram ze ming sring gsum bsad pa'i rjes/ sngar dge ba spyad pa dang / 'chi khar smon lam log pa btab pa'i
stobs kyi ming po che ba lho phyogs gshin rje thams cad kyi gtso bo gshin rje gsod byed ces bya bar gyur/ ming po chung ba

nub byang gi bdud thams cad kyi gtso bo bdud nag po ral pa spyi phyings zhes bya bar gyur/ sring mo ni byang shar gyi gnod sbyin mo thams cad kyi gtso mo srin mo nag mo gser
gyi spu gri ma zhes bya bar gyur/ de dag nang du skye 'gro rnams kyi srog bdud kyi tshul du lus kyi gnad la gnas pa ni/ ming po che ba gshin rje ni ltag pa'i bdud rtsa
nag po la gnas/ ming po chung ba bdud ni snying dkar nag mtshams kyi rtsa mdud la gnas/ sring mo ni srog rtsa la gnas nas sems can thams cad kyi srog bdud dbugs len gyi las
byed par gyur te/ thog mar rang gi gshed ma bsad 'phral du rang gi bran du skyes pa ni/ ru 'dren sde bzhir grags te/ skyes pa rnams btsan rgod du skyes pa/ g.yas kyi ru
'dren pa skyes pa stag chas brgyan pa brgya/ btsun pa rnams srog bdag rgyal por skyes pa/ g.yon gyi ru 'dren pa nyan thos dgra bcom pa brgya/ sngags pa rnams gza' rgod
dang bdud nag tu

skyes pa/ rgyab kyi rjes su 'brangs pa sngags nag ban phur thogs pa brgya/ bud med rnams nad bdag ma mo nag mor skyes pa mdun gyi shul byang 'dren pa bud med nag mo ral gri
thogs pa brgya/ gzhan yang de dag gi sprul pa yang sprul nying sprul dregs byed lha srin sde brgyad kyi tshogs dang bcas pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas stong gsum thams cad myul
zhing sems can thams cad la 'tshe zhing srog 'phrog par byas so/ /de'i tshe yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid kyis sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor
chen po sprul/ nyid kyi thugs ka nas 'od zer 'phros pas rang dbang med par bkug ste sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor chen por dbang bskur/ dam la btags/ khong rnams kyis srog gi
snying po mdongs gsol du phul nas/ bstan pa la sdang ba/ sems can la 'tshe ba/ sgrub pa po la bar chad byed pa rnams sgrol ba'i shan par khas blangs/ zas skal du de dag
gi

sha khrag dang srog dbugs byin/ gnya' gnon du mgon po lcam dral gyi thugs ka nas sprul pa'i gnod sbyin yab yum bskos te/ nag po chen po'i bka' nyan gyi gtso bor byas nas/ de
sgrub pa'i thabs su dregs pa pho mo'i rgyud ces bya ba gsungs par bshad do/ /pu tra ming sring 'di dag sa dang po la gnas pa'i tshul 'dzin pa yin no/ /zhes kyang sgrub
yig gi mchan bu rnying pa dag las 'byung ngo // ! //'dir zhar las 'ongs pa mon chung pu tra ming sring gi byung tshul ni/ sngon rgya gar 'phags pa'i yul du mu stegs kyi rnal
'byor pa zhig gis nags khrod gcig tu sgom zhing yod tsa na/ bdud lha sbyin bya bas dngos su 'ongs nas cha rkyen rnams phrogs/ lus brdung brdeg gis nyam thag par byas
pa na/ dus re zhig gi tshe/ mi nag po shin tu khros pa'i gzugs can zhig byung nas rkyal 'bud kyi man ngag zab mo byin te/ man ngag 'dis lha ma yin thams cad 'dul ba

yin no zer nas bka' rgyas btab nas song / de nas sngar gyi bdud lha sbyin de lngar sprul nas byung ba thams cad rkyal 'bul gyi man ngag rno zhing myur ba des bsad pas/ mon
mo sngo bsang ma lag pa g.yas na gser gyi spu gri thogs pa zhig byung nas/ ming po khyod rno la myur ba'i las shig byed kyi 'dug pa/ ngas kyang zhabs tog byed zer nas nub
re la lha sbyin re bsad pa dang / mon mo na re/ gdam ngag de nga la byin zer ba la/ bka' rgya dam pas mi ster byas pas/ mos gser srang bdun phul gdams ngag phrogs thabs
su khyer song nas/ mon mo de ming sring gsum yod pas/ gsum kas man ngag de'i sgo nas sdang dgra kun bsad/ de nas pha ma gnyis/ ming sring gsum dang bcas pa/ bcom ldan 'das
kyis dam la btags nas bstan pa bsrung zhing nag po chen po'i bran du bka' bsgos so/ /de nas paNDi ta dharma pha la bod

du byon dus lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po nas brgyud/ bla ma mal gyi bka' srung byas so/ /zhes rkyal 'bud man ngag gi lo rgyus kyi yi ge rnying ma las 'byung ngo / /de ltar lo
rgyus sam skye brgyud 'di rnams mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug dam pa kun dga' grags kyis mdzad pa'i lo rgyus kyi yi ge gsum las 'byung ba bzhin brgyud par ldan pa'i bla ma
dam pa'i gsung bgros kyis gsal bar byas pa yin no/ /'di dag gi khungs ni mgon po'i skye brgyud dur khrod nag po'i rgyud dang / dur khrod chen po'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa slob
dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ bla ma gong ma'i gsung bgros thor bu ba yi ger bkod pa dag las gsal bar 'byung ngo / /kha cig drag po dbang phyug tu skyes pa sogs mi 'thad
de/ gur las/ bcom ldan 'das kyi sku gsung thugs las byung ba'i mgon por bshad pas so/ /zhes pa ni rnam par ma brtags pa ste/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes gcig nyid gdul bya'i
rgyud

tshod dang mthun par tshul du ma ston pa ni 'di tsam mo zhes tshad gzung bar ga la nus/ de ltar na rgya bstod tshad ldan srin gzugs ma las/ grong khyer gsum brtsegs 'jigs byed
pa/ /zhes dang / de'i kha skong bod bstod tshad ldan las/ mahA de wi'i sras po drag shul che/ /zhes dang / legs ldan nag po grong khyer gsum brtsegs dgra/ /zhes sogs
gsungs pa ji ltar drangs legs par soms shig don 'di dag la dgongs nas rje tshar chen gyi mgon po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ sngon byung lo rgyus skabs
su bshad rgyud las/ /ston pa'i dngos kyi sprul par bshad pa dang / /byung tshul 'ga' ru dbang phyug chen po yi/ /sras su bshad pa kha cig 'gal zhes gleng / /'gal na rgyud
nyid gtso mod de ltar na'ang / /rgya bstod yongs grags tshad ldan 'di nyid las/ /ma hA de ba'i sras po drag shugs can/ /zhes sogs gsungs pa'i

dgongs pa ji ltar 'grel/ /mi 'gal na ni de yi 'thad pa dang / /phyi ma'i phyogs kyi lo rgyus gsal ba zhig /tshad ldan mkhas pa khyad par sa skya pa'i/ /bla ma gong mas mdzad
pa ji ltar yod/ /ces gsungs pa yin la/ de bzhin du lha mo'i skye brgyud rnams kyi khungs mkha' 'gro ma me lce 'bar ba'i rgyud dang / lha mo shan pa nag mo'i rgyud dang
/ ma mo srog gi 'khor lo'i rgyud sogs nas gsal bar bshad cing / 'di dag la rgyud tshad ldan yin min gyi dpyad gzhi cung zad snang mod/ 'on kyang slob dpon chen po padma 'byung
gnas sogs nas brgyud pa'i lo rgyus kyi yi ge tshad ldan du ni/ bla ma gong ma rnams bzhed pa yin pas/ log rtog che ba chos kyi snying por ma 'dzin zhig 'di dag nas
bshad pa ltar/ lha mo'i bstod pa dngos grub 'byung ba'i rgyud las bshad cing / bram ze chen pos kyang mdzad par grags pa las/ ting 'dzin dbang thob gzugs

khams gnas su byon/ /tshangs pa'i rgyal po la sogs phyag byas ma/ /gzhan la dbang bsgyur 'dod khams pha mthar phyin/ /dbang phyug chen po'i sku la dgyes 'khril ma/ /sum cu
rtsa gsum tshal du byon pa'i tshe/ /lha rnams dbugs dbyung brgya byin phyag byas ma/ /lha ma yin rnams pham par mdzad pa'i tshe/ /lha min dbang po kun gyis phyag byas ma/
/sku mchog ri rab rtse la 'gran pa'i tshe/ /lte ba'i thad ka'i phyogs nas nyi zla 'char/ /rgyal chen bzhi la sogs pas phyag byas ma/ /rgya mtsho'i klong nas me 'bar mtsho
skem ma/ /sa 'og dbang po kun gyis phyag byas ma/ /lha mo khyod kyis cho 'phrul 'di bstan pas/ /bdud dang gshin rje'i rgyal po 'dar zhing 'dud/ /ma mo srin mo'i tshogs
rnams dngangs shing rgod/ /ces sogs gsungs pa'i don rnams gong gi yi ge rnams nas gsal bar 'byung bas gzhung rnam

dag dang mthun pa'i tshad ldan gyi skye brgyud som nyi dang bral ba yin zhing / de las gzhan pa'i khungs kyi yi ge yid ches can bstan rgyu yod pa dka' bar snang bas/ des na
rtog bzo mkhan rnams smra ba bskyung ste gzu bor gnas pa'i blos bsam par rigs so/ /de dag gis ni sngon byung gi lo rgyus bstan zin nas// //gnyis pa rgyud las bstan tshul
ni/ mgon po 'di nyid la gur gyi mgon po zhes mtshan 'dogs pa'i rgyu mtshan yang / ston pa rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid kyis rdo rje gur gyi rgyud gsungs pa'i dus su de nyid
kyi srung mar nag po chen po 'di nyid sprul nas mgon po 'di nyid kyi sgrub thabs rgyud de'i le'u bco lnga pa dkyil 'khor chen po bsdus pa'i rtog pa las bka' bstsal pa
ni/ nag po chen po 'di nyid kyi rgyud rnams kyi gtso bo'am snying po lta bur gyur pa yin te/ de yang bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa chen pos/ nag po chen po 'di nyid kyi
sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las

byung ba'o/ /zhes pas ston pa'i dngos kyi sprul par bstan/ de nyid hU~M yig las skyes pa/ /zhes pas de'i sa bon dang / de las bskyed tshul bstan/ lag pa gnyis pa mgo gcig pa/
/kha dog nag po drag po che/ /'bar ba'i gri gug thod pa 'dzin/ /mgo bo rlon pas do shal byas/ /'jigs byed nag po mche ba gtsigs/ /gzugs thung pa la brjid po che/ /kha
nas khrag ni 'dzag pa po/ /zhes pas de'i sku mdog phyag mtshan rnam 'gyur sogs kyi mngon par rtogs pa bstan/ slob dpon la rtag gang sdang dang / /dkon mchog gsum la 'khrug
ldan dang / /sems can du ma gsod pa rnams/ /zhes pas de'i gdul bya'i gtso bo mngon spyod gang la bya ba'i yul bstan/ rang gi yan lag sha bcad nas/ /nag po chen pos za bar
'gyur/ /khrag gi rgyun yang 'thung bar byed/ /yang na mgo

bo'i steng 'dug nas/ /til tsam du ni gcod par byed/ /ces pas des de 'dul tshul bstan/ me tog spos dang byugs pa dang / /zhes pas mchod pa bstan/ chang dang shis byed sran dre'u/
/sha lnga bdud rtsi lnga nyid kyis/ /gtor mas nag po chen po mchod/ /ces pas gtor ma bstan/ oM mahA ka la ye/ shA sa na/ u pa ha ri ni/ e Sha a pashtsi ma kA lo a yaM
i da~M/ ratna tra yA ya/ a pa ka ri Ni/ ya ti pra ti dznyAM/ sma ra si ta da/ i daM/ duShTaM/ kha kha khA hi khA hi/ mA ra mA ra/ ghri hNa ghri hNa/ bandha bandha/ ha
na ha na/ pa tsa pa tsa/ di na mAe ke na ma ra ya hU~M hU~M phaTa? phaTa?/ ces pas bzla bya'i sngags bstan/ tsha ba gsum gyi gzugs brnyan byas pa'i lus la/ dug dang ske tshes
cho ga bzhin du bris la/ tsher mas bkang ba'i me la gang gi ming dang bcas pa bsro bar byas nas/ de de'i mod la mi mthong bar 'gyur

ro/ /zhes pas ling ga la bsten pa'i las sbyor dang / las sbyor de nyid 'grub pa'i dus dang bcas pa bstan pa yin no/ /rgyud 'di ni mgon po 'di nyid bstan pa'i khungs kyi gtso
bo yin zhing / rgyud tshig 'di dag gi phyi nang gsang gsum gyi sgrub thabs ston tshul sogs sbas don snyan brgyud kyi bshad pa thun mong ma yin pa ni bla ma'i zhal las shes
pa kho na'o/ /gzhan yang zhar las byung ba nag po chen po zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po mgon po sngon byung du grags pa le'u lnga bcu pa las/ mgon po 'di nyid zhal
bzhi phyag bcu drug la lha brgyad kyis bskor ba dang / zhal bzhi phyag bcu gnyis pa la lha mo bzhis bskor ba dang / zhal gsum phyag brgyad pa la lha mo bzhis bskor ba dang
/ zhal gsum phyag drug pa la lha mo bzhis bskor ba dang / zhal gcig phyag bzhi pa la lha mo gnyis

kyis bskor ba dang / zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa la lha mo gnyis kyis bskor ba/ de dag gi sgrub tshul las sbyor gyi rim pa sogs gsal bar 'byung ngo / /dpal rdo rje nag po chen
po khros pa'i mgon po gsang ba dngos grub 'byung ba'i rgyud le'u nyer lnga pa las/ gtso cher mgon po phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs mang du bstan cing / gzhan yang rnam thos
sras phyi nang gsang gsum dang / mgon po beng dang / lha mo la sogs pa'i sgrub tshul/ khyad par le'u bcu pa sbyin sreg gi le'ur mgon po 'di nyid phyag bzhi pa khros pa'i
sgrub tshul gsal bar bstan to/ /dur khrod nag po zhes bya ba'i rgyud le'u bcu gnyis pa las/ mgon po 'di nyid la gshin rje pho brgyad mo brgyad kyis bskor ba'i dkyil 'khor
mgon po gshin rje ltar sgrub pa'i sgrub thabs las sbyor gsal bar bstan to/ /gzhan yang ston pa byang chub kyi shing drung na bzhugs pa'i tshe/ nag po chen pos rigs sngags
phul ba nag po chen po'i gzungs dang / nag po chen po'i gzungs ring nad las thar bar byed pa zhes bya ba rnams kyis kyang shugs kyis bstan pa yin no/ /lha mo ni rdo rje
gdan bzhi'i rgyud rgyas pa'i lhag ma'i skabs nas bstan par bshad/ 'on kyang da lta bod na bzhugs pa'i gdan

bzhi'i rgyud rnams kyi dngos bstan la gsal bar ma byung mod/ bla ma rnams kyi gsung bgros la byang sgo srung ba'i ma mo 'bar byed ma 'di nyid yin par bshad pas des bstan pa'am/
yang na bod du ma 'gyur ba'i gdan bzhi'i rgyud rgyas pa zhig nas bstan par snang ngo / /bya rgyud rig pa mchog gi rgyud nas/ nam gru nag mos sems can rnams skrag cing
'tshe ba byed pa'i tshe/ drang srong rnams kyis bskul nas dpal phyag na rdo rjes/ nam gru khyod kyi cho 'brangs dang / /mtshan nyid dag ni bshad bya ba/ /nor bu'i rang
bzhin khyod kyi lus/ /rgyab ni 'dzam bu chu bo'i gser/ /khyod kyi gdong yang dngul yin te/ /lto ba'i ngos ni rdo rjes gtams/ /ming po mdzod dang mdzod bsrung ba/ /khyod kyi
ma ni kun 'gro ma/ /khyod kyi pha ni rlung zhes bya/ /skal ldan shing rta khyod kyi rus/ /lha gnas gsum du grags pa

yin/ /zhes sogs kyis nam gru'i rigs dang cho 'brangs la bstod pas dga' zhing dbang du byas te/ dpal kun 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor chen por bcug cing dbang bskur nas bstan pa'i
srung mar bskos par bshad do/ /ston pa byang chub kyi shing drung na bzhugs pa'i tshe/ lha mo nag mos rang gi rig pa phul zhing / ston pas gzungs dang phan yon gsungs pa
lha mo nag mo'i gzungs zhes bya ba dang / ston pa bya rgod spungs pa'i ri la bzhugs pa'i tshe/ lha mo nag mo drung du 'ongs pa dang / byang sems seng ge brtson 'grus kyis
ming gi rnam grangs zhus pas/ ston pas lha mo'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad phan yon dang bcas pa gsungs pa/ lha mo nag mo'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa rnams kyis kyang
bstan pa yin zhing / gzhan yang bla med kyi rgyud rdo rje mkha' 'gro/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud/ kye rdor brtag gnyis/ sambu Ta'i rgyud sogs las yul nyer bzhi dang / gnas so gnyis

kyi nang tshan de wi ko Ta zhes pa/ bod skad du lha mo'i mkhar zhes par gnas nas zhing skyong ma mo thams cad kyi gtso mo mdzad par bshad/ sngon gyi bstan bcos 'chi med mdzod
dang / de'i 'grel pa rab 'byor zla bas mdzad pa dang / yang sna tshogs gsal ba zhes bya ba ming gzhan mu tig 'phreng ba slob dpon dpal 'dzin sdes mdzad pa sogs las dbu
ma dang gcig par bshad nas ming gi rnam grangs dgu bcu tsam gsungs shing / gsang sngags rnying ma'i rgyud rnams las/ sngags srung lha mo'i bsgrub tshul rab tu mang po dang
/ lhag ma'i skabs su yang rgyas par bshad la/ zhar byung nA ro pa dang / mar los bsgyur ba'i lha mo dngos grub 'byung ba'i rgyud ces pa bstod pa til mar ma nang du 'byung
ba bla ma dag bzhed pa'i rgyud de dang / lha mo rje khol gyi rnam dbye dang / de dag gi skye rgyud sogs ston pa rnying ma'i rgyud gong du smos pa'i me lce 'bar ba sogs
kyis kyang gsal

bar byas pa yin no/ /gnod sbyin yab yum la skye rgyud logs su mi 'byung ba yang mgon po lcam dral gyi thugs ka nas sprul pa yin pas lcam dral dang thugs rgyud gcig pas na de
gnyis kyi skye rgyud kyi don thob shugs bstan gyi tshul du bstan pa yin la/ las mkhan zangs gri can phyi nang dang / sgo ma bzhi/ bran bdud sogs la skye rgyud dang rgyud
kyi dngos bstan gyis zin pa ma mthong / ber nag ni nang sgrub kyi tshe sras kyi tshul du bskyed pas sras zangs gri can du grags shing / gcer bu dang bran bdud gnyis la
ni sgrub thabs rgya gzhung bram zes mdzad pa yod par snang la/ gnod sbyin yab yum dang / pu tra ming sring gi bod rbad bsad gsum gyi sngags rnams ma mo srog gi 'khor lo'i
rgyud ces bya bar 'byung / pu tra ming sring la 'phags yul na dregs pa pho mo'i rgyud ces bya ba yod pa las/ 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis zur du bkol ba'i sgrub thabs rdo rje

gdan gyi ka ba'i 'og tu sbas par bshad do/ /don gyi dbang de dag la dgongs nas rje tshar chen gyis mgon po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ las mgon gnod sbyin
yab yum rnam gnyis dang / /sgo ma bzhi yi skye rgyud byung tshul gyi/ /yig cha dag dang zangs gri rnam gsum gyi/ /sgrub thabs rgya gzhung tshad ldan gzigs lags sam/ /rgyud
kyi skabs su mgon po lha mo gnyis/ /rdo rje gdan gzhi'i rgyud las bstan zhes pa/ /de lta'i tshig ris gsal ba ji ltar yod/ /mtho dman le'u'i rim pa gang nas bstan/ /de
bzhin mgon po mngon par 'byung ba dang / /mgon po khros pa'i rgyud kyis bstan zhes gleng / /de dag nas kyang tshig gsal gzigs gyur tam/ /dur khrod nag po zhes grags mgon
po'i rgyud/ /me lce 'bar dang gshan pa nag mo dang / /ma mo srog gi 'khor lo lha mo'i rgyud/ /'di dag dag gam min na sgrub byed gang / /lha mo'i

bstod pa til mar zhes grags pa/ /ji skad bya ba'i rgyud kyi nang na bzhugs/ /las mgon rnams la rgyud kyi dngos bstan gyis/ /zin pa'i gsal bya yod pa e ma gzigs/ /zhes gsungs
pa de dag gi don yang gsal bar byas pa yin no/ /sa skya pa'i chos skyong gur zhal rnam gnyis su grags pa'i gnyan mgon chen po zhal bzhi ba 'di ni/ gsang 'dus rtsa rgyud
le'u bcu bdun par/ drag po mi sdug khros pa ni/ /utpal sngon po'i mdog 'dra ba/ /phyag ni bzhi ldan cho ga yis/ /thod pa 'dzin pa rnam par bsgom/ /zhes dang / bde mchog
bshad rgyud rdo rje mkha' 'gro las/ ha ha rgod pa'i dur khrod dang / /zhing skyong lag pa bzhi pa ni/ /zhes sogs kyis bstan par bla ma 'ga' zhig bzhed cing / gnyan lo tsA
bas bla ma gnam kha'u pa dang / nye gnas dar ma seng ge la gsungs pa'i gsang ba'i zhal gdams kyi yi ge las/ chos

skyong chen po 'di gzhan las myur zhing rtsub pa'i rgyu mtshan zhus pa'i lan du/ spyir chos skyong du ma zhig la phyi nang gsang gsum gyi dbang gis/ 'jig rten pa'i tshul 'dzin
pa dang / ye shes pa gnyis gnyis yod la/ khyad par 'di la ni 'jig rten pa rang rgyud la lha dbang phyug chen po'i sprul par gyur pa'i zhal bzhi pa'i gtso 'khor dang /
de'i gnyen por gyur pa'i zhal bzhi pa ye shes pa gnyis yod de/ de yang gdul bya shin tu rtsub cing gnyan na/ de 'dul byed kyang shin tu lhag par gnyan cing rtsub pa zhig
'ong ba rten 'brel gyi chos nyid yin pas gnyis ka gnyan pa yin no/ /de yang da lta rtsub cing gnyan pa dang / shin tu myur ba ni phal cher 'jig rten pa'i zhal bzhi pa'i
rnam 'gyur yin pas de ltar 'ongs pa yin no/ /de yang sngon lha dbang phyug chen po 'khor dang bcas pas da lta gnang ba'i zhal bzhi pa 'khor bcas kyi bkod pa dang tshul bzung

nas skye 'gro thams cad kyi srog dbugs bsdud cing sha khrag la longs spyod pa'i tshe/ phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba thams cad kyis bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje la/ dbang phyug chen
po 'khor bcas 'dul bar gsol ba btab pa na/ bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rjes dbang phyug chen po 'khor bcas kyi bkod pa ji lta bar sprul nas/ dbang phyug chen po 'khor
bcas kyi lus kyi cha byad thams cad 'phrogs te rang gi sku dang rgyan du byas/ khong rnams kyi srog sngags kyi thog mar oM dang / mthar hU~M phaTa? sbyar bas byin gyis brlabs
te rang gi sngags su byas/ dbang phyug gi chung ma rnams 'phrogs te rang gi phyag rgya mar byas/ de'i nang nas g.yung mo ni lha mo u ma yin no/ /gnas thams cad 'phrogs
nas rang gi gnas su byas/ khong rnams de ltar tshar bcad nas rang gi bran du byas so/ /des na nges pa'i don du gdul bya dang 'dul byed ngo bo gcig kyang / gzhan gyi snang
ngo tsam du 'jig

rten pa'i zhal bzhi pa 'khor bcas ni dbang phyug chen po 'khor bcas dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i zhal bzhi pa ni phyag na rdo rje yin no/ /zhes gnyan mgon chen po 'di nyid
gdul bya dang 'dul byed kyi tshul gyi dbang phyug chen po dang / phyag na rdo rje'i rnam par 'phrul pa yin par gsungs la/ don de dag dang mthun par sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo
rje'i gsung las kyang / byang shar ha ha rgod pa'i dur khrod du/ /zhing skyong dbang phyug chen po'i rnam 'phrul mchog /ces 'byung ba yin zhing / yang gur gyi mgon po nyid
dang thugs rgyud gcig par yang bla ma dag bzhed de/ dam pa kun dga' grags kyis mdzad pa'i mnga' gsol gyi yi ge las/ nyid kyi thugs las sprul pa'i sras/ /mthu chen ldan
pa zhal bzhi ni/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /zhing skyong dur khrod kyi bdag po yab yum ni gsang ba snying gi 'khor

lo'i rgyud nas bstan pa yin te/ rgyud de nyid kyi gleng gzhi'i le'u las/ dpal he ru ka sku skye ba med pa'i ngang la yum rdo rje rnal 'byor ma dang gnyis su med pa sprul pa
yang sprul dang bcas te dur khrod chen po'i gnas na dngos grub 'byung ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ oM shrI badzra he he ru ru kaM hU~M hU~M phaTa?/ oM shrI
badzra yo gi ni hU~M phaTa?/ zhes gsungs pas 'jig rten gyi dregs pa can thams cad brgyal bar gyur to/ /brgyal ba sangs pa dang 'khor de rnams kyi nang nas dpal dur khrod
kyi bdag po stan las langs te/ dpal chen he ru ka la 'di skad ces gsol pa/ kye gdug pa 'dul mdzad he ru ka /bskal pa snyigs ma lnga yi dus/ /gdug pa can rnams 'khrugs pa
dang / /sa bdag klu yi nad yams dar/ /ma mo mkha' 'gro 'khrugs pa'i tshe/ /mi rnams bsod nams longs spyod chung / /rang bsags dngos po spyad dbang med/ /pha dang bu bral
longs spyod nyams/ /

de dus bcom ldan bstan pa 'di/ /dpa' bo bdag gis bsrung bar bya/ /zhes gsol ba dang / dpal chen he ru kas/ legs so dur khrod bdag po khyod/ /srog gi snying po bdag la phul/
/zhes gsungs pa dang / tadya thA/ oM gr-i ha rA dza gr-i ha rA dza/ ku ma ku ma khuM thi swAhA/ zhes mdongs gsol du phul zhes sogs gsungs nas/ 'khor lo bde mchog bstan pa
bsrung bar zhal gyis bzhes par bshad pa yin la/ 'khon ston sa skya pa'i bka' srung dkar bdud lcam dral phur srung dam can bcu gnyis zhes grags pa'i dkar bdud lcam dral
'di gnyis nges don du bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gzhon nu'i thugs gnyis su med pa'i ye shes gcig gis bsdus pa'i sprul pa yin te/ 'khon rog shes rab tshul khrims la bzhi thog
bla brang gi rgyab kyi nyi zla phug par chos skyong lcam dral gyi zhal gzigs nas dngos su gnang ba'i thugs dam bskang ba'i

cho ga las/ che ba'i che mchog he ru ka /de yis nyer sprul srung ma'i gtso/ /dpal mo lcam dral/ zhes gsungs pas nges don du de ltar yin kyang / kun rdzob tu dkar mo nyi zla
nyid 'jig rten 'das ma 'das kyi mtshams na bzhugs pa sogs rnam 'phrul du ma'i sgo nas mkha' 'gro bye ba'i gtso mo mdzad pa ste 'khor 'das kun la khyab pa'i tshul du bzhugs
pa yin te/ bskang ba'i cho ga de nyid las/ mthu stobs rdzu 'phrul mthu rtsal can/ /dpal ldan ma yis kun khyab cing / /zhes dang / ye shes dbyings kyi rje mo ste/ /gzhan
don 'jig rten pa ru sprul/ /'jig rten gnas dang 'jig rten 'das/ /'das dang ma 'das mtshams na bzhugs/ /zhes dang / ma mo chen mo rnal 'byor ma/ /kun gzhi yongs kyi dbang
phyug ma/ /snang srid kun la dbang bsgyur ma/ /zhes dang / mkha' 'gro bye ba'i gtso mo khyod/ /dus gsum gzigs

pa'i 'dod dgu'i gter/ /zhes dang / gzhan yang / srid gsum bdag tu mdzad la bstod/ /ces dang / 'khor ba ni yongs mi spong / /mya ngan ni yongs mi 'da'/ /sku yi ni tshad che'ang
/ /nam mkha' yi mtha' dang mnyam/ /rigs pas ni gzung du med/ /tshad kyis ni dpag tu med/ /srid pa ni kun la khyab/ /khams gsum ni dbang du 'dus/ /zhes sogs mang du gsungs
pas nges don du bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gzhon nu thugs gnyis su med pa'i ye shes spros bral chos kyi sku las ma g.yos bzhin du/ kun rdzob gdul bya'i snang ngor 'jig rten
'das ma 'das ma mo mkha' 'gro kun gyi gtso mo mdzad cing / 'khor ba ji srid pa de srid du sems can gyi don mdzad cing 'khor 'das brtan g.yo kun la khyab pa'i tshul du
bzhugs pa 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gnas lugs yin te/ kye rdo rje'i rtsa rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa las/ nga las 'gro ba thams cad byung / /nga las gnas

gsum po yang byung / /nga yis 'di kun khyab pa ste/ /'gro ba'i rang bzhin gzhan ma mthong / /zhes dang / yang de nyid las/ 'chad pa po nga chos kyang nga / /rang gi tshogs
ldan nyan pa nga / /'jig rten ston pa bsgrub bya nga / /'jig rten 'jig rten 'das pa nga / /lhan cig skyes dga'i rang bzhin nga / /zhes dang / rnal 'byor ma kun spyod las
kyang / gar mkhan dag dang ri mo bzang ltar snang / /gang zhig drug pa zhes bya'i sangs rgyas nyid/ /gcig pu nyid ni du ma'i gar mdzad do/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /bdud mgon
thod 'phreng can 'di ni nges don du bcom ldan 'das dpal he ru ka'i thugs kyi sprul pa yin pa'i tshul gong du bstan pa ltar yin la/ drang don kun rdzob tu bdud rgyal 'di
nyid sngon gyi dus su bdud nag po mthu bo che zhig tu gyur nas sems can mang po'i srog dbugs la mngon par longs spyod par gyur pa'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyis las 'bras kyi
chos

bstan nas dam la btags te/ phyi rabs kyi rnal 'byor pa la stong grogs mi brjed pa'i phyir thod pa'i 'phreng ba rtags su byin pa sogs 'di'i lo rgyus rgyas pa ni dpal he ru kas
gsungs pa'i bdud nag po chen po'i rgyud le'u bdun gyi bdag nyid can zhig 'byung ba de nyid las zhib tu rtogs par bya ste/ de'ang le'u dang po gleng gzhi'i le'u/ gnyis
pa gleng bslang ba'i le'u/ gsum pa sgrub pa'i le'u/ bzhi pa dam bca' ba'i le'u/ lnga pa bskul zhing rdzas bsag pa'i le'u/ drug pa bstan pa gtad pa'i le'u/ bdun pa gdams pa
bstan pa'i le'u rnams su yod pa'i rgyud de nyid kyis gsal bar bstan pa yin zhing / phur srung ma mo sde gsum po 'di rnams kyang nges don chos kyi sku las ma g.yos bzhin
du gdul bya'i snang ngor sngon bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gzhon nus gdul bya ru Ta ma rungs pa btul ba'i dus su rang rang gi srog snying phul zhing dam la btags nas bstan pa
bsrung bar zhal gyis

bzhes pa yin la/ de nas slob dpon rnam gsum gyis dam la btags tshul ni sngon gyi dus su slob dpon dha na sangkri ta la slob dpon chen po padma 'byung gnas kyis/ bdag rgya dang
bod kyi mtshams mtha' 'khob kyi gnas su phyin nas gdul bya'i zhing du gyur pa'i gdul bya rnams 'dul bar bsam lags na/ de rnams 'dul ba'i dus la ji ltar bab zhus pas/
babs par lung bstan nas/ de nas slob dpon padmas bal yul yang le shod kyi brag phug tu byon te/ bal mo shAkya de wa gzungs mar dbang bskur nas/ bcom ldan 'das yang dag mar
me dgu pa'i sgrub pa mdzad pas/ mi ma yin gyi gtso mo rgod ma kha bya ba dang / byi dur bya ba dang / bar snang gi glog ma sprin bya ba gsum gyis bar chad kyi cho 'phrul
sna tshogs brtsams pa la/ slob dpon padma'i dgongs pas nga phyag chen mchog gi dngos grub sgrub pa la 'byung po 'di rnams kyis bar chad byed par 'dug pas/ 'di rnams 'dul
ba'i dus la ma babs pa yin nam

snyam du dgongs pa'i tshe/ nam mkha' las sgra byung nas dur khrod bsil ba'i tshal nas slob dpon dha na sangkri ta gdan drongs la rdo rje phur pa'i sgrub pa zhag bdun gyis shig
des bar chad thams cad thul nas dngos grub thob par 'gyur ro zhes pa grags pa na/ slob dpon padmas rang gi nye 'khor gnyis gser gyi phyag rten dang bcas paN chen dha
na sangkri ta'i drung du spyan 'dren gyi pho nya mngags pas paN chen gyi zhal nas/ nga yong mi dgos/ sngar nam mkha' nas lung bstan pa bzhin gyis shig gsungs te/ bi to ta
ma la'i nang nas dregs pa can gnad la dbab pa'i rgyud mi khur gnyis bskur nas brdzangs/ de nas slob dpon chen pos paNDi ta'i bka' bzhin rdo rje phur pa'i sgrub pa zhag bdun
mdzad pas sngar gyi bar chad kyi mtshan ma thams cad rang zhir gyur te/ yang dag lha dgu'i zhal gzigs shing dngos grub thams cad stsal te/ de phyin chad la slob dpon

chen po nyid kyi lus lha dang / ngag sngags dang / thugs ye shes kyi rang bzhin las g.yo ba med pa'i ngang nas phyag rgya chen po'i rig 'dzin mngon du gyur to/ /de nas slob
dpon chen po padma 'byung gnas de nyid dang / slob dpon bi ma la mi tra dang / bal po shi la manydzu gsum gyis slar yang gnas der rdo rje phur pa'i sgrub pa zhag gsum mdzad
pa'i tshe dam can rnams kyis drod tshad brtags pa'i tshul ni/ zhag gsum po'i srod kyi cha la zangs kyi wa mo zha bkug pa 'dra ba gcig la zangs kyi bud med chen mo zhig
gis bzhon lag na zangs kyi zhags pa 'dom dgu brgya dgu bcu yod pa thogs pa zhig byung ba la/ slob dpon gsum gyi dgongs pas de nyid rdo rje phur pa'i srung ma yin par mkhyen
te/ slar yang dam la btags shing bstan pa bsrung ba'i gnyer kha gtad de/ shwa na mu kha'i dus la bab/ /ces sogs kyi bstod bskul yang de dus mdzad par grags so/ /yang

nam phyed tsam na bud med nag mo chen mo lcags kyi drel rta rkang gsum la zhon pa/ g.yu'i smin ma can mig skar chen shar ba tsam/ ral pa phur pas brgyan pa/ mi lpags phrag
la bkal ba/ lag pa g.yas na khram shing dang / g.yon du nad kyi rkyal pa thogs pa zhig byung bas/ de nyid 'jig rten gsum gyi bdag mo rdo rje phur pa'i srung ma yin par mkhyen
nas/ slar yang dam la btags shing bstan pa bsrung bar bka' bsgos te/ bdag nyid chen mo'i dus la bab/ /ces sogs kyi bstod bskul yang de dus mdzad pa yin par bshad do/
/yang slob dpon rnam gsum gyis tsha shod tsha ba rong zhes bya ba'i sgrub gnas su bzhugs pa na/ lan gcig srod kyi cha la babs pa'i tshe/ slob dpon padma'i drung du dbugs
tu tung byed pa zhig byung bas bar chad yin nam dgongs te gzigs pas/ bud med gcig 'dug pa bzung nas lcags kyi par pu'i nang

du sngags rgyas btab nas bzhag nangs par nam langs pa dang slob dpon chen pos chu mig byang chub ris su byon nas sngar gyi rgya bkrol nas gzigs pas bud med mdzes ma bzhi 'dug
pas/ slob dpon chen pos mkhyen bzhin du khyed rnams su yin gsungs pas/ de dag na re/ ngos cag rnams ni yul tsha ba rong gi sa'i cha/ me tog padma dgun yang skye ba'i yul
na gnas pa/ ming ni bse mo bzhi'am/ gru 'degs rgyal mo bzhi'am/ rgyal khams kyi mkha' 'gro ma bzhi'am/ dbugs 'phrog srog bdag ma bzhi zhes kyang bya zhing / sngar yang
'jig rten gyi tshe srog la longs spyad cing / da dung de la dbang pa'i dbang zhig bskur du gsol zhes zhu ba la/ slob dpon gyis de ltar du ma gnang bar sems can la gnod 'tshe
bkag nas dam la btags te/ rdo rje phur pa'i bstan pa bstan 'dzin dang bcas pa bsrung zhing skyong ba'i gnyer gtad nas/ de rnams lhan cig tu bzhag na

mthu che bas 'jig rten phung dogs gnas yul so sor bkar te/ spyi gtsug tu rdo rje bzhag nas dbu la dbang gi cod paN re dang / lus la dbang gi bse khrab re/ lha rta bzhon pa
re/ rten pa'i gnas su mtsho bzhi byin nas yul khams so sor bzhag go /de ltar phur srung bcu gnyis byung tshul 'di la sa bdag ma'i skabs su lha mo bzhi kar dam la btags tshul
dang / bdag nyid ma'i skabs su re ma ti rkyang pa dang / shwa na ma'i skabs su gdong mo bzhi'i nang nas wa gdong ma gcig pu dam la btags tshul 'dra ba zhig bshad kyang
/ don la sa bdag ma bzhi dang 'dra bar bdag nyid ma bzhi dang / shwa na ma bzhi yang so sor dus re re la dam la btags par mngon no/ /dam can bcu gnyis po byung tshul gyi
gtam rgyud 'di dag kyang / rgyud dngos ma yin yang / de dang 'dra ba'i tshad thub tu bla ma gong

ma rnams bzhed pa'i slob dpon padma'i gsung 'khrul med phur pa'i yi ge rnying ma rnams nas ji ltar 'byung ba bzhin bkod pa yin no/ /'dir smras pa/ de ltar rgyal ba'i ye shes
rgya mtsho che/ /rlabs chen thugs rje'i dri bzhon gyis bskyod pas/ /gang 'dul zhi drag rba rlabs zlos gar ni/ /grangs med g.yo 'di dpag par su yis nus/ /de ltar tshad med
snying rje'i chu yi gter/ /rab tu 'khrugs pa'i ngams nag dus mtha'i sprin/ /srid gsum za ba'i ljags kyi glog phreng g.yo/ /bdud dgra'i snying 'gems hU~M phaTa? 'brug stong
rgod/ /e ma 'di 'dra'i bstan srung lha chen po/ /yum mchog pho nyar bcas pa'i rnam rol gyis/ /dus gsum rgyal bas ma thul gdug can rnams/ /sgrol 'di rgyal ba'i rnam 'phrul
rab dang phul/ /cir yang 'char ba'i 'khor 'das snang srid 'di/ /phyi nang gsang ba'i dregs pa rgyud gsum du/ /'dus par shes shing de yang spros bral gyi/ /blo 'das
ngang du 'jog

pa zab mo'i bcud/ /de lta'i nges don nyams len gyis zin pa'i/ /gang shar bsnyen sgrub las kyi rnam rol du/ /shes pas ci byas chos su 'gyur ba yi/ /lam khyer mchog 'di kho bos
skal bas rnyed/ /brgyud ldan bla ma rnams kyis bu bzhin bskyangs/ /rang nyid gsung rab don la blo gsal bas/ /zab rgyas chos tshul rgya mtsho'i gnad tshang rig /bsnyen
bsgrub sbyor bas chos skyong mnyes par byas/ /'di dang phyi ma'i don chen snying nas sems/ /cir snang rmi lam sgyu ma'i rnam rol gyis/ /'phrin las rnam bzhis bstan pa 'dzin
pa la/ /rgyal ba dgyes pa'i sngags 'chang mi zer ram/ /deng sang bstan srung chos skor rgya mtsho rnams/ /don gnyer lta ci rjes gnang tsam re yang / /ma thob nyams len
byed la ring pa 'di/ /legs par brtags na khe nyen gang che soms/ /mtshan ldan bla mar gdams ngag rdzogs par zhus/ /rtags bzang ma thob

bar du bsnyen bsgrub 'bad/ /skabs su bab tshe lhag bsam rnam dag gis/ /las rnams sgrub na don gnyis 'grub bo kye// ! //gsum pa 'phags yul rgya gar du bshad srol 'byung tshul
ni/ bla ma mal lo tsA ba chen pos mgon po 'di'i chos skor rgya bod kyi bla ma gsum la gsan pa'i nang nas/ gtso bor gyur pa ni brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims la gsan
pa/ lo chen rin chen bzang po nas brgyud pa 'di nyid yin la/ 'di la bka' gter gyi brgyud pa gnyis byung ba las/ dang po bka' ma'i brgyud pa'i lo rgyus ni/ ston pa rdo rje
'chang chen po'am rdo rje nag po chen po sogs mtshan gyi rnam grangs du ma dang ldan pa'i thabs bde ba chen po'i ngo bo de nyid kyis mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur dang / 'jigs
byed chen mo dang / yum chen e ka dza Ti sogs mtshan gyi rnam grangs mang po dang ldan pa'i shes rab stong pa nyid kyi ngo bo de la gnang / 'di gnyis ngo bo

dbyer med zung 'jug tu bzhugs pa yin pas/ rgyud yig rnying pa rnams la lar rim bzhin smos pa dang / phal cher du rdo rje 'chang kho na smos pa ni dbye bsdu'i khyad par tsam
yin pas don la 'gal ba med par shes par bya'o/ /de lta'i mgon po 'di'i chos skor rnams 'phags yul rgya gar du byung ba'i brgyud pa'i rtsa ba lta bur gyur pa ni/ slob dpon
chen po bram ze mchog sred du grags pa 'di yin la/ 'di nyid bram ze chen po rin chen rdo rje zhes bya ba'i sras su 'dod pa dang / bram ze ka ru zhes bya ba'i sras su 'dod
pa sogs lo rgyus mi 'dra ba cung zad byung na'ang / 'dir rje btsun bsod nams rtse mo'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa/ rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug gis gsal
bar mdzad pa'i yi ge ltar bshad na/ de'ang rgya gar shar phyogs na kau ta rA ni zhes bya ba'i grong khyer 'bum tsho sum cu rtsa gsum yod pa/ rgyal srid des pas skyong
