ldan de sogs/ /dam chos don du dka' spyad cher mdzad nas/ /bstan srung dbang po'i zab rgyas gdams pa'i bcud/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir 'gro la spel mdzad pa'i/ /skyes mchog
de dag bka' drin bsam las 'das/ /ding sang bstan 'gro'i don phyir rgya bal sogs/ /dka' bas bsgrod nas dam chos ngom med du/ /'tsho ba lta ci rang nyid mi bslu ba'i/ /chos
tshul re re'ang rdzogs par mi slob pa'i/ /bdag 'dra'i snying med chos par

rlom rnams mtshar/ /'on kyang bslu med bla mar blo gtad nas/ /ci byas bstan 'gro'i don du gyur cig snyam/ /lhag bsam 'di la dam can rgya mtsho'i tshogs/ /rtag tu dgyes pa'i
'dzum zhal cis mi ston/ /de phyir mkhyen brtse nus ldan gzhan stobs kyis/ /rang dang rang la yid gtad gdul bya yi/ /'di phyi'i don gnyis 'bad med lhun grub tu/ /'byung ba
som nyi med 'di ngo mtshar gnas/ /lnga pa/ khyad par rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras la bka' bab tshul ni/ gangs can bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras la
nag po 'di'i chos skor gyi bka' bab chen po bzhi mnga' ste/ de yang bla ma ba ri lo tsA ba nas brgyud pa dang / bla ma zhang dgon pa nas brgyud pa dang / bla ma mal lo
tsA ba nas brgyud pa dang / kha che'i paNDi ta chen po shAkya shrI nas brgyud pa'o/ /dang po ni/ ba ri lo tsA ba chen po rin chen grags pa

zhes bya ba/ 'khrungs yul mdo khams dbyer mo thang pa/ gdung ba ri mdo tshang bzhi'i nang nas gling kha ba'i rigs su 'khrungs pa/ byis pa'i dus nas yi ge drug pa kho na bzla
zhing spyan ras gzigs kyi byin gyis brlabs pa zhig chung ngu nas mkha' 'gros lung bstan la brten nas/ dgung lo bcu dgu pa la dbus gtsang du 'byon par chas/ bar lam du sgrol
ma gtso 'khor gsum pa che chung tshon gang pa zhal 'dzum bag dang ldan zhing 'od mtha' yas pa gcig gzigs/ des lung bstan cing chom rkun gyi 'jigs pa las bskyabs/ de
nas dbu ru stod du phebs nas mkhan po ku su lu pa zhang yon tan rin chen dang / slob dpon stan gcig pa brtson 'grus grags las rab tu byung / mtshan rin chen grags su btags/
gzhan yang de dus kyi dge bshes mkhas pa dang bzang bar grags pa phal che ba la gtugs nas thos bsam rgya

chen po mdzad/ lha sa'i jo bo la skor ba 'bum gter btang bas mnal lam du jo bo'i sku'i g.yas na spyan ras gzigs bcu gcig zhal mi che ba tsam zhig bzhugs 'dug pa'i zhal nas/
khyod yo byad mang po khyer la rgya gar la song / don khyad par can mang po 'grub cing sems can la phan par 'gyur ro/ /zhes lung bstan pa la bsten nas rgya gar la 'byon
par chas te/ skyid rong nas bal yul brgyud de byon/ bal po'i paNDi ta ye rangs pa chen po la bde mchog rnal 'byor ma rdo rje gdan bzhi rnams kyi dbang sgrub thabs/ rgyud
rdzogs rim la sogs pa man ngag mang du zhus/ sgra bslabs pas mkhas par mkhyen/ de nas rgya gar du byon/ dang por bla ma mahA yo gi dang mjal/ rdo rje phag mo'i byin rlabs
dang gdam ngag rnams zhus shing / nub cig tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i dus su bla ma'i gsung gi nam mkha' na bcom ldan 'das

rdo rje phag mo bzhugs pa mthong ngam gsungs/ des bltas pas rdo rje phag mo gtso 'khor lnga bzhugs pa mngon sum du gzigs/ ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo du ma thugs la 'khrungs/ de
dus rgya gar na rtsod pa med cing yongs su grags pa'i bla ma rdo rje gdan pa chung ba dang mjal/ gsang sngags kyi dbang dang rgyud sgrub thabs mang du gsan cing / phal chen/
dkon brtsegs/ ting nge 'dzin rgyal po la sogs pa'i bshad pa'ang gsan/ gzhan yang bla ma rdo rje gdan pa chen po dang / paNDi ta don yod rdo rje la sogs pa la yi dam
lha'i sgrub thabs stong rtsa brgyad gsan/ de rnams kyi nang nas gang legs legs dang / zab zab nye bar mkho ba brgya rtsa brgyad phyogs gcig tu bsdus nas lo paN gnyis kyis
bsgyur/ /bla mas de rnams kyi spyi'i mngon rtogs gcig dang / so so'i sgrub thabs rab tu gsal ba re dang / de rnams re re la'ang bshad

lung / byin gyis brlabs pa'i lung / rjes su bzlas pa'i lung / dam bca' ba'i lung re dang bzhi bzhi'i bka' dang / lag len rnams spyan drangs nas dar bar mdzad/ gzhan yang bla
ma rdo rje gdan pas mu stegs kyi gnod pa bzlog pa'i man ngag kha 'bar ma'i gtor chen/ bha ya na'i man ngag drag po'i sbyin sreg rnams kyang gnang / de nas bod du 'byon
khar bas mtha' zhig tu skyo bsangs la byon pas yi dwags mang po ngu yi 'dug pas/ khyed rnams ci la ngu gsungs pas/ khyed bzhugs na nged rnams la gtor ma mang po sbyin pas
mi bkres par 'dug pa la/ khyed bod du byon na gtor ma gtong mkhan med pas nged rnams bkres skom gyis sdug bsngal bar 'gyur zer nas/ de dag gi ched du 'bras mi khur bzhi
bcu nyos nas yi dwags kyi gtor ma'i rgyun chen po btsugs shing / de'i chas la gser srang dgu'i rten bzhag go /de nas bal yul du phebs pa dang / bal po na

bod nas 'ongs pa'i mgron po rnams gang la bab pa'i gnas pos zong phyed 'khyer zhing / phyed la ji ltar ri ba bskur/ 'phral spyod lam cung zad ma legs pa byung na'ang rgyal
po'i chad pa 'ong / na tsha byung na khang par na sa dang 'chi sa med sgor 'don pa la sogs pa nyon mongs pa rnams kyi don du/ yam bu ya 'gal gyi phyogs gcig gi thang chen
po la rin bsam gyis mi khyab pa bcal nas nyos te bod thang zhes bya bar ming btags/ der khang pa chung ngu dang / sa phug la sogs pa mang po bcos nas/ bod rnams der bsdad
chog pa byas pas sngar gyi nyes pa rnams mi 'byung zhing / mgron po'i zong gi rang gang 'dod pa'i nor sgrub chog par mdzad do/ /gzhan yang tshad pa skyob pa'i ched du co
pa ri zhes bya ba rtsig pa med pa'i shing gi khang pa chen po yang dag pa zhig mdzad nas/ 'di zhig na gsos shig gsungs gnas po la nor mang po'ang bzhag skad/ de ltar

lho bal gyi phyogs su lo dgu bzhugs nas bzhi bcu zhe gsum la bod du byon nas/ thog mar lung steng pa dge bshes dkon mchog skyabs kyis sne len bzang po dang yun ring bar zhabs
tog mdzad/ gdul bya mang po la dbang rgyud sgrub thabs la sogs chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen po bskor/ de nas sa skyar bla ma dkon mchog rgyal pos spyan drangs nas chos
mang du gsan/ yun ring du zhabs tog mdzad nas mos gus can gyi slob ma rnams la chos kyang ci rigs pa gnang zhing / dgung lo drug cu re gsum pa bla ma dkon mchog rgyal po
gshegs pa'i shul du/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po sku gzhon pas sa skya'i gdan sar bzhugs par zhus nas gdan sa lo brgyad mdzad/ gdul bya rnams la chos kyi rnam grangs mang po
gsungs shing / rnal rgyal mchod rten thugs dam du bzhengs/ rnam rgyal gyi gzungs 'bum ther gsum dang khri tsho bdun bzhugs pa'i rnam rgyal gyi tsha

tsha/ rgya bod kyi rten byin rlabs can du ma nang du bcug gzhan yang bkra shis pa'i rten 'brel du ma mdzad cing / rab gnas kyi don du yang rnam rgyal cho ga stong phrag gnyis
mdzad nas/ tshes brgyad kyi nyin mo me tog 'thor bar mdzad pa na/ mchod rten gyi bum pa las 'phros pa'i 'od ser po gser btso ma'i mdog lta bus mig gis mthong tshad kyi
sa dang nam mkha' khengs shing / dril bu'i sgra lta bu 'khrol ba dang / legs so zhes pa'i sgra mi che ba lan bzhir kun gyis thos pas thams cad ya mtshan du gyur/ de nas
bzung ste phyogs dus kun tu bkra shis pa'i ltas bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ba ni skye bo kun gyis mthun snang du grub bo/ /dmyal ba'i zangs khar gnas pa'i sems can rnams
'don pa'i slad du g.yu mkhar mo'i gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa dang / gzhan yang mchod rten mang po bzhengs pa/ zam pa mang po 'dzugs pa/ mgron

khang mang po brtsigs pa sogs sems can gyi don rgya chen po mdzad nas dgung lo bdun cu don gcig pa la sa skya'i gdan sa gtad de/ bar phug rong gi dben gnas su thugs dam kho
na la bzhugs nas lo gnyis song ba bdun cu don gsum la dbyug pa zla ba'i tshes bcu bzhi la bla ma sa skya pa chen po sku drung na bzhugs pa la zhal lta gnang ba/ nga ni bde
ba nas bde bar 'gro/ yi dam gyi lha 'jam dpal/ rnam 'joms/ spyan ras gzigs/ sgrol ma/ rnam rgyal rnams nyin re bzhin du ji ltar 'dod pa na zhal mthong / khyad par thugs
rje chen po/ sa skya dang / la stod byang rgyab/ g.yas ru kha stod rnams su nyin zhag bdun re tsam 'bral med du zhal mthong bas lhag pa'i lhas rjes su bzung ba yin/ bde
ba yin mi 'gyod pa yin/ khyed jo sras kyi bu theg pa chen po'i rigs can yin pas/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dang sems

can gyi don kho na ma yin pa/ rang don gyi 'khri ba spangs nas ci byas chos su 'gro ba kho na mdzod/ ces pa la sogs pa'i zhal bkod mang po gsungs nas lus gnad kyi ngang nas
bde bar gshegs/ de'i rjes su gsol 'debs/ sku'i dod phyi rten nang rten bzhengs pa/ dus kyi mchod pa la sogs pa bla ma sa skya pa chen po nyid kyis rgyas par bsgrus so/ /rje
btsun sa skya pa chen po nyid kyis/ ba ri lo tsA ba chen po 'di'i drung du spyir mdo dang / rgyud dang / man ngag mang po dang / sgrub thabs brgya rtsa la sogs pa'i chos
thams cad rdzogs par zhus/ khyad par 'jam dpal dang / mi g.yo ba dang / sgrol ma dkar mo dang / dbang sdud 'dod pa'i rgyal po'i chos skor la sogs pa mang du zhus shing
/ dgung lo bcu gnyis pa'i dus sa skya'i 'jam dpal brag khung du 'jam dpal a ra pa tsa na bsgrubs pas/ res 'ga' dung gi

mi chen po gcig 'ong / re 'ga' seng ge chen po zhig byung ba bla ma la zhus pas/ 'byung po dpe dkar kho bar chad bya 'dod pa yin/ bar der jo bo mi g.yo ba'i bsgom bzlas gyis
gsungs nas de'i rjes gnang dang / chu'i bsrung ba sgrub thabs yan lag dang bcas pa rdzogs par gnang ste/ de ltar mdzad pas bar chad zhi nas 'phags pa 'jam dpal sku mdog
gser btso ma lta bu/ phyag chos kyi 'khor lo bsgyur ba'i phyag rgya can/ rin po che'i khri la bzang po'i 'dug stangs kyis bzhugs pa/ 'khor byang chub sems dpa' gser gyi
mdog can gnyis dang bcas pa mngon sum du zhal gzigs/ theg pa chen po'i chos kyi snying po zhen pa bzhi bral gyi gdams pa dngos su gsan/ blo gros chen po dang ldan pa'i mkhyen
pa'i spyan ras kyis skal ba dang ldan pa'i gdul bya dpag tu med pa'i don rgya chen po mdzad pa yin no/ /de lta bu'i lo tsA ba chen po de'i drung du

rje btsun sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po nyid kyis nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po 'di nyid pho rkyang dpa' bo gcig tu sgrub pa'i rjes gnang / sgrub thabs kun las btus
pa las 'byung ba/ bram ze chen po nyid kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs kyi rgya gzhung dang bcas pa zhus nas sgro skur gyi dri mas dben par bzhugs pa ni bka' bab dang po yin
zhing / bla ma 'dis sa skya pa'i rdo mgon du grags pa'i rgya gar 'phags pa'i yul gyi ri ma la ya gnam lcags yod pa'i rtse mo ru gsang bdag phyag na rdo rje'i thugs rje
las rang byon du byung ba la/ lha rnams kyis me tog gi char phab pa'i tshe/ sku la me tog chags pa'i steng du paNDi ta rnams kyis tshon gsol bas/ da lta yang tshon gog pa'i
shul la me tog gi 'dab ma'i rjes lta bu yod pa'i byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar ba 'di yang jo sras sa skya pa la gnang ba yin no/ /ba ri lo tsA ba

'di bla ma sa skya pa chen po la bka' drin shin tu che ba'i bla mar 'dug na'ang / ding sang 'di'i rnam thar shin tu dkon par 'dug pas/ rje rtse mos mdzad pa las ji ltar 'byung
ba ltar 'dir cung zad bsnyad pa'i rgyu mtshan de ltar yin no/ /bka' babs gnyis pa ni paNDi ta ga ya dha ra ste/ bod skad du sprin 'dzin nam klu 'dzin grags pa rgyal po
sprin gyi shugs can zhes kyang bya ba des bod yul du/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba chen po shAkya ye shes la chos sgo skyel gyi tshul du byon nas gnang ba'i nag po chen po 'di'i
chos skor la/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po birWa pa nyid nas brgyud pa'i lam 'bras pa'i lugs kyi gur rkyang dpa' bo gcig tu sgrub pa'i rjes gnang shin tu zab pa/ rje
btsun chen po'i gur rgyan du bshad pa'i bsnyen bsgrub las gsum cha tshang zhing mdor bsdus pa zhig dang / slob dpon chen po mtsho skyes nas brgyud pa'i gur mgon lha lnga'am
lha brgyad ma'i

rdul tshon dang / sindhu ra'i dkyil 'khor la brten nas dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa zhal nas snyan du brgyud pa ches zab par grags pa zhig byung / 'di rnams bla chen 'brog
mis bla ma se ston kun rig la gnang / des zhang ston chos 'bar la gnang ngo / /de'i drung du rje btsun sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying pos yongs su rdzogs par gsan pa
yin no/ /sa skya pa'i shing mgon yid bzhin nor bur grags pa bram ze mchog sred kyi spur sol las rang byon du 'khrungs pa'i mngon spyod kyi las la mthu rtsal shin tu myur
bar grags pa 'di ni pu hrangs lo tsA ba grags 'byor shes rab nas brgyud de/ bla chen sa skya pa'i phyag tu bab pa yin la/ bla ma 'ga' zhig shing mgon 'di bram ze chen po'i
thugs dam mar bzhed pa yang snang ngo / /bka' bab gsum pa ni/ bla ma lo tsA ba chen po blo gros grags la

rje btsun sa skya pa chen pos gsan pa'i chos skor rnams yin la 'di'i lo rgyus ni 'og tu rgyas par 'chad do/ /de ltar rje sa chen la bka' bab gsum byon zhing / rje btsun sku
mched kyi ring la de dag gi srol 'dzin pa ma gtogs de las gzhan pa'i bka' bab gsar pa ma byon/ dus phyis chos rje sa skya paNDi ta chen po'i dus su kha che'i paNDi ta bsod
snyoms pa chen po shAkya shrI bod yul du byon pa la nag po 'di nyid pho rkyang dpa' bo gcig tu sgrub pa dang / gtso bo mgon po la yum mche ba rnam par gtsigs ma dang /
ma ra li dang / sgal tshigs ma dang / nag mo chen mo ste mkha' 'gro ma bzhis bskor ba'i lha lnga ma zhig dang / de rnams bsgrub tshul gyi gdams pa gsang sgrub spu gri skor
gsum du grags pa ste/ phyi pho lha ltar bsgrubs pas mthu zhor la 'byung ba bsnyen pa'i man ngag bsgrub pa zhun chen gyi mar me la brten nas gnag pa zhag bdun la bsgral

ba'i man ngag las sbyor tsitta snying la brten nas dgra bo kha phub tu bsad pa'i man ngag ste gsum yod/ 'di rnams ston byed kyi yi ge bram ze chen po'i rgya gzhung chung ba
bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge de'i lag len zhal gdams las sbyor gyi gdams pa/ lo rgyus kyi yig chung rnams yod do/ /'di rnams kyi lung man ngag dang bcas pa kha che paNDi
ta nyid kyi drung du chos rje sa paN gyis gser zho brgyad dang / g.yu zho brgya ri ba gcig phul nas/ mahA paNDi ta'i srung ma rnams kyi nang nas thugs rtsis mdzad pa'i
chos skyong gi gsang sgrub cig yod 'dug pa bdag la cis kyang thugs rjes 'dzin par zhu zhus pas/ 'di lta bu ngas sngar rgya bod du slob ma su la'ang ster ma phod pa yin/
da khyed sa skya pa chos skyong 'di'i bdag por 'dug pas de ltar byed/ rjes gnang ni bram ze chen po nas brgyud pa sngar thob pa des chog man ngag ston

pa la slob ma gzhan 'dra 'ong ba 'dug pas rgya skad du bya'o/ /gsungs nas de ltar gnang / chos rje pas kyang shog ril la rgya yig tu bris nas/ phyi mchod rten khru gang pa
tsam yod pa zhig gi nang du bcug nas zhabs bsdom bsdams te rten gral na yod pa la/ chos rje pa rang gi slob ma bgres po dge slong zla ba rgyal mtshan bya ba lo bdun cu lon
pa zhig la chos skyong rang gi lung bstan byung nas spyad dngos thams cad spongs dag byas phul te 'di zhus pas gnang / khong gis bsnyen pa byas pa tsam gyis/ zhing la rkun
ma byung ba la rkun ma lnga zhag gcig la khrag bskyugs nas shi ba sogs nus mthu dpag med byung / des bla ma khams pa la gnang / des ri pa dge tshul dar ma dpal la gnang
/ de rnams kyis chos skyong 'di lan lnga lnga zhal gzigs par grags/ kha che paN chen gyi zhal nas rang la ci ri 'di la ri ba yin/ bod du 'di las zab pa'i chos skyong gi
man ngag yong myong ba med ces

gsungs par grags/ gong gi lo rgyus las 'byung ba ltar/ brgyud pa 'di ba'i lugs kyi srol 'di la rjes gnang zur pa mi byed cing / bram ze chen po nas brgyud pa'i mgon po pho
rkyang gi rjes gnang tshad ldan gcig thob na des go chod par 'dod pa yin no/ /ding sang kha cig 'di la rjes gnang zur ba byed cing / de nyid ches dkon pa'i zab gnad du byed
pa'ang thos pas dpyad par bya'o/ /'di la dgongs nas rje tshar chen gyi mgon po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ kha che paN chen shAka shis mgon po'i skor/
/su la gsan cing de nyid la brgyud pa'i/ /spu gri skor gsum ngos 'dzin ji ltar yin/ /lugs 'di'i rjes gnang chad dam da lta yod/ /ces gsungs pa'i dgongs pa'i don yang gsal
bar byas pa yin la/ sa skya pa'i bris mgon du grags pa 'di ni/ bram ze mchog sred kyi spur ras la/ zhal

bzhugs dus kyi shangs mtshal sogs byin rlabs rten 'dzom pos rgya gar gyi lha bzo bas bris pa byin rlabs kyi rtags mtshan du ma dang ldan pa 'di ni/ kha che paN chen gyi phyag
brgyud nas chos rje khu dbon gyi phyag tu bab pa bla ma dag bzhed do/ /drug pa de las snying por gyur pa'i lam srol ngos bzung ste bshad pa ni/ de ltar sa skya pa la gur
gyi mgon po'i chos skor gyi bka' bab/ sa skya pa chen po la gsum dang / chos rje pa la gcig ste rnam pa bzhi bzhugs pa rnams kyi nang nas gtso bor gyur pa ni/ skad gnyis
smra ba'i lo tsA ba chen po blo gros grags pa la/ rje btsun sa skya pa chen pos gsan pa'i skor rnams yin te/ thog mar brgyud pa'i khyad par yang / gzhan gsum la bka' ma'i
brgyud pa tsam las med la/ srol 'di la slob dpon padma nas brgyud pa'i gter ma dang / shraddha nas brgyud pa dang / spyan chen po nas brgyud pa bka' ma ste/ brgyud pa'i
bka' bab gsum

gyi steng du/ gyi ljang nas brgyud pa dang bzhi 'dus pa dang / bsgrub bya'i lha la'ang / gzhan gsum la pho rkyang las med pa las/ 'di pho rkyang mo rkyang sbags sgrub 'khor
rkyang sogs mang bar bshad cing / sgrub byed man ngag kyang gzhan gsum la phyi sgrub rkyang pa yin la/ 'di la phyi nang gsang gsum gyi man ngag bsam gyis mi khyab pa snyan
brgyud bzhi zam ma chad par bzhugs pa dang / 'di'i sgo nas mnga' ris stod du lo chen gyis bon po mang po la drag po'i las sbyor brtsams pa nas bzung / rje sa skya pa khu
dbon/ a nyan dam pa nas brgyud de sa skya pa rnams kyis mngon spyod kyi las phal cher 'di la brten nas bsgrubs pas las sbyor gyi lag len ma nyams shing 'phrin las kyi
nus mthu dang ldan pa/ rje sa chen yan chad du rjes gnang yang bse 'bag gi drung du min pa mi byed/ kyai rdo rje'i dbang gis ma smin pa la mi ster/ bka' shin tu dog cing
thams

cad kyi nying khu thugs rtsis shin tu che ba yin no/ /de yang bla chen 'dis 'khon sgyi chu ba'i bde mchog gi phyag dpe rnams bsnams nas gung thang na la rtse gnas sar na bla
ma mal lo tsA ba bzhugs pa'i drung du zab mo'i yang rtse 'khor lo sdom pa'i chos skor rnams gsan par bzhed nas phebs pa na/ de'i tshe bla mas chos rnams tshar re la mkhyen
pa dang / mal gyis thugs su ma tshud pa'i tshul mdzad de/ la las ni mi tshe phyid pa'i chos la/ la las tshar res shes su re ba gsungs nas bkyon skad/ lan gcig bla chen
'di med par/ mal lo dpon slob tshos rtog bdun gyi sngags shig thu yin 'dug pa dang / slob ma tshos ma shes pa la/ bla chen gyis der byon nas de la tshegs med/ 'di ltar
byas na mchis byas pas/ bla ma kag gis bzhengs nas/ shes na dga' ba tshos mi shes/ ma shes na dga' ba tshos shes 'dug gsungs nas gshegs song ba dang / der bla chen

'di thugs cung zad steng gin logs shig na bsam mno mdzad cing bzhugs tsa na/ yang khong tsho 'tshogs nas sngags thu yin yod pa dang / lhags pas shog bu khyer ba bla chen gyi
gam du byung nas/ de khyer te 'di la gda' zhus pas/ de rten 'brel bzang chos kyis phan thogs pa yong ba yin gsungs nas bla ma mal mnyes pa'i tshul mdzad/ de nas jo sras
sa skyar 'byon khar bla ma'i gsung gis nga'i chos 'di nges par 'tshang rgya ba'i chos yin pas/ mi nyid rigs kyis dbang bskur re byed zer nas re tshang zhig tu/ phub gog
gcig gi steng du padma 'dab brgyad gcig byas/ blu gu gcig gi skye la bal gcig dkris byed pa'i nyen yod do/ /de 'dra ma byed gsungs pas/ bla ma'i chos la de 'dra ci byed lags
zhus nas/ de nas mar byon te g.yas ru na mar dbang bskur sems bskyed 'dra mdzad pas gser srang bcu bdun 'bul

ba la byung ste/ de rnams sngags pa gcig la bskur nas bla ma la 'bul du btang pas/ bla ma ston mo chen po gcig gi tshogs dpon la phebs 'dug pa la zhu ba phul bas/ ltogs 'dod
za med cig yin pas za btung 'dra byin gsungs nas ma mjal/ de min par gda' jo sras sa skya pas gser 'bul du btang par gda' zhus pas/ 'phral thugs col chung ba 'dra ba gcig
yod pas khong rang byon nas 'bul ba ci yod gsungs/ gser zhig bdog zhus pas/ zho du yod gsungs/ srang bcu bdun tsam yod byas pas/ mnyes nas kho rang gi khug ma nas kyang
srang gang bton nas/ 'di yang de'i steng du snon la srang bco brgyad yod gyis la tshogs su phul gsungs/ de ltar byas pas bla ma'i zhal nas/ jo sras sa skya pa khong dam
tshig pa bsam gyis mi khyab par 'dug pa la/ ngas de ltar cung ma go da myur du yar byon/ sngar ma gsan pa'i

chos 'dra yod gsungs pa la/ bla chen gyis kyang myur bar byon pas/ sngar ma gnang ba'i bde mchog skor sogs zab chos mang po dang / lhag par chos skyong 'di'i skor shin tu bka'
dog pa yin pa la bla ma shin tu dgyes pa'i stobs kyis 'cham sku'i drung du rjes gnang sgrub skor man ngag dang bcas pa rdzogs par gnang zhing / rjes gnang gi dus sku
gsung thugs kyi rten khyad par rnams stsal cing bka' bsgo mdzad pa'i tshe/ 'cham sku bzhengs nas byon pa'i phyag dang / sa chen gyi phyag sbrel te/ bla ma'i zhal nas/ spyir
chos byed pa thams cad la chos skyong bzang po re bsten pa gal che/ khyad par du khyed brgyud pa dang bcas pa la gur gyi mgon po 'dis phan thogs pa'i rten 'brel mang po
yod/ bstan pa la yang shin tu phan pa yong bas/ rdo rje 'chang gi dngos su byin gyis brlabs pa'i bla ma bram ze mchog sred

kyi thugs dam bse 'bag nag po 'gro shes bya ba bla ma brgyud pa'i byin rlabs kyis nga yi bka' nyan du yod pa 'di khyed kyi rjes su gtong bas/ da nga rgas pas khyed mi dgos/
khyed jo sras kyi rjes la sa skyar song la/ kun dga' snying po mi brgyud dang bcas pa'i bka' bzhin sgrubs shig gsungs pa la/ 'cham sku lan gsum 'phar byung ba la/ bla ma
mal gyis phod ka'i phu rung gi g.yab tho lan gsum brgyab nas song zhes gsungs so/ /de phyin chad bse mgon gyis sa skya pa'i bka' bran bzhin du nyan yang / skabs su mthu
rtsal drag drags pa'i rnam 'gyur bag re byung nas bla ma la zhus pas/ mal gyi gsung gis bse mgon 'di rgya gar na yang mthu rtsal 'gran med du byed/ 'on kyang 'di'i dpung
g.yas pa'i thad du dpal phyag na rdo rje 'byung po 'dul byed re sgoms dang legs par 'ong gis gsungs te de bzhin du mdzad pas deng sang gi bar du bris 'bur gang la yang

chos skyong gi dpung zur du 'byung 'dul re byed pa'i rgyun yang de nas byung bar grags so/ /de nas sa chen dpon slob kyis 'cham sku sogs rten rnams spyan drangs nas byon pa'i
tshe/ drangs so'i thad kyi lam de la yang 'byon lam byung bas lam de shin tu 'grongs pas mgon po'i thig lam du grags shing / deng sang ni sgra zur nyams pas 'gong lam
zer bar 'dug de nas drangs so'i la la dpon slob rnams 'cham sku dang bcas phar phyogs nas byon pa dang / tshur phyogs nas rta pa zhig phyin pa la rtser 'dzoms pas/ 'cham
sku mthong 'phral rta pa de khrag bskyugs nas shi bas chos skyong 'di shin tu gnyan pa'i grags pas phyogs kun tu khyab cing / la de la yang khro bo'i rgyal po bse mgon 'di
byon pa'i la yin pas khro bo lar grags so/ /des na ding sang khra bo la zer ba ma dag par snang / de phyin chad zhal kheb sogs mdzad nas shin tu gsang ba'i tshul

gyis spyan drangs nas dpal sa skya'i sgo rum gzim spyil dkar por phebs pa na/ re zhig gi bzhugs sa da ltar bzhugs pa'i gzims khang chung ngu 'di nyid du mdzad de slar mgon
khang bzhengs pa'i dgongs pa bla chen gyi thugs la 'khrungs pa'i tshe/ bse mgon gyi gsung byon nas/ mgon khang gsar pa bya mi dgos/ da lta'i 'dug sa 'di kas rdo rje gdan
gyi byang sgo yang non zhing / bstan dgra gdug pa can rnams sgrol ba dang / bstan pa bstan 'dzin dang bcas pa skyong ba yang 'di kar gnas pas bgyid 'tshal lo/ /zhes bka'
stsal pa bzhin bla chen gyis kyang de ma thag bskang gso gtum chen mar grags pa mdzad de/ 'cham mgon yid bzhin gyi nor bu gnas de nyid du g.yo med du bzhugs su gsol nas bka'
bsgo dang 'phrin bcol rgyas par mdzad pa'i rten 'brel gyis dpal sa skya'i sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pa'i rgyun 'di ji srid thub pa'i bstan pa gnas kyi bar du

mi nyams shing yar ldan du 'byung ba'i rten 'brel thams cad rang 'grig tu gyur pa yin no/ /skabs der byin pa'i chos skyong gi gsung gi rten gyi dar nag ni phyi 'khyar byung
dogs bla ma gong ma'i nang rten zhig gi gzungs rdzongs la bzhugs skad/ thugs kyi rten lcags kyi rdo rje ni bla ma dam pa sogs kyis bar skabs su sku bsrung la phyogs su spyan
'dren par mdzad kyang / slar sgo rum sgam nag nyid du bzhugs su gsol nas da lta yod pa 'di kho na rtsod med yin par bla ma gong ma rnams gsung ba thos shing / yon tan
'phrin las kyi rten bse'i ga'u snying 'dra ba'i nang na bzhugs pa'i man ngag gang 'dod kyi yi ger 'ong ba de ni/ snga mo zhig nas shin tu gsang ba'i tshul gyis kun gyi
mi mngon par bzhugs pa yin te/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan gyi gsung las/ bse 'bag dang lhan cig rgya gar nas byung ba'i bse'i ga'u'i nang na yod pa'i

sgrub skor gyi yi ge deng sang ga na yod dkar chag gi yi ge sogs su mi gsal ba 'di/ sa chen zer ba'i bgres po des gter du sbas par 'dug go zhes gsungs shing / don la bdag chen
rang nyid rje sa chen gyi rnam 'phrul yin pas/ man ngag gi be'u bum de nyid bse mgon dang nye ba'i skor zhig na kun gyi mi mngon pa'i gter gyi tshul du bzhugs yod pa'i
gtan tshigs nges gsal can sngon gyi skye ba dran pa'i tshul gyis thugs la shar ba'i gsung yin par rje nyid kyi rnam thar las 'byung ngo / /bdag gi bla ma grub mchog dbang
po'i mtshan can gyi gsung las/ 'phrin las kyi rten de sku 'bag bzhugs pa'i sa stegs de nyid kyi nang na yod ces sngags 'chang chen po'i gsung rgyun las 'byung bas 'di
nyid kho na 'thad ldan yin no/ /zhes yang yang du gsung ba thos la/ de ltar bstan srung dbang po 'di nyid kyi bzhugs gnas sgo rum gzim spyil dkar por grags pa 'di la/ bla
ma

'ga' zhig gi gsung las/ sgo rum zhes pa zhang zhung gi skad yin zhing / de'i don bsgul du mi rung ba yin pas/ 'cham sku 'di gzhan du bsgul du mi btub pa'i don gyis de skad
du grags pa yin par bzhed cing / yang bla ma la la dag sgo rum zhes pa'i zhang zhung gi skad de/ dgra bgegs kun 'joms zhes par 'gyur bas des na dgra bgegs kun 'joms kyi gzim
spyil zhes bya ba yin no/ /zhes kyang bshad la/ yang dpal ldan sa skya pa la sngags pa snyan ngag dbang po'i nyer 'tsho las/ dpal ldan mgon po'i pho brang rim dgu rim
par phub pa'i rtse mo na/ /zhes gsungs pa dang ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi rnam thar paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa las kyang / dgu rim na chos rje sa paN
gyi dpe khang / zhes 'byung ba ltar na sngon gyi dus su gzim khang 'di la thog rim pa dgu brtsegs su yod pas dgu rim gzim

spyil dkar por grags pa la/ dus phyis sgra zur nyams pas sgo rum du song ba 'dra mo zhig kyang snang zhing / yang gzim spyil 'di la phyi nang gi sgo rim pa du ma zhig yod pas/
sngon gyi tshe na sgo rim gzim spyil zer ba la/ da lta sgo rum du song ba e yin snyam ste/ da dung 'di'i ming don la khungs thub kyi mtha' chod rang bzo dang bral ba
zhig blo gsal don gnyer can rnams kyis btsal te rang gzhan rna ba'i dga' ston du spel bar mdzad 'tshal/ 'di lta bu'i chos skyong yid bzhin gyi nor bu'i sku brnyan 'di ni
su zhig gis gsol ba btab kyang mchog thun mong gi dngos grub thams cad bde blag tu stsol bar nges te/ sngon rgya gar 'phags pa'i yul gyi rdo rje gdan gyi byang sgo'i mgon
khang du bzhugs pa'i tshe yang / than pa zhi ba/ rims nad bcad pa/ gzhan gyi dmag bzlog sogs bstan pa'i rim gro dgos pa byung ba'i tshe yang / bla ma nor bu gling pa sogs

de dus kyi gang zag bzang po rnams mgon khang du spyan drangs te gsol ba 'debs pa zhag re'am gsum tsam re mdzad pas gang 'dod pa'i don de thogs med du 'grub pa'i lo rgyus mang
du yod pa dang / lo chen gyis bon po ma rungs pa gdug pa can rnams 'dul ba'i tshe yang / 'cham mgon 'di la 'phrin 'chol drag tu mdzad pas bzhed don 'bad med du 'grub
pa dang / dpal sa skya 'dir yang bla chen kun dga' snying po nas bzung / sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po yab sras kyi bar du byon pa'i bla ma gong ma phal cher la yang mi
dang mi lab pa'i tshul gyis lung ston pa dang / bar chad sel ba/ gang bcol ba'i 'phrin las thams cad thogs med du sgrub pa/ da lta'i bar gyi sa skya pa'i 'phel rgyas thams
cad bse mgon chen po 'di'i thugs rje dang mthu rtsal gyi byin rlabs las byung bar nges shing / gzhan yang 'di shin tu gnyan pas zhal

'bag gi zhal gdangs ha cang ches pa la/ dpon chen byang rin gyis dngul gyi lkog stegs bcug pas/ 'khu ldog gi rnam pas dpon chen lkog ma skrangs nas shi la thug pa la/ zhal
'bag gi lkog stegs bton pas/ dpon chen nad las grol nas btang rag phul bar grags pa dang / gang zag mchog dman su zhig gis mjal yang / zhal 'bag gi kha dog la mthong snang
sna tshogs pa bstan pa'i sgo nas kyang de dang mthun pa'i dngos grub stsol bar nges te/ bdag gi bla ma grub mchog dbang po'i mtshan can la yang gzigs snang du ma zhig byung
ba'i tshul ni/ de yang rje nyid dgung lo bdun bzhes dus sngags 'chang chen po'i phyag phyir dkris nas sgo rum ye shes mgon po mjal bar phebs skabs/ 'cham mgon gyi rnam
pa de ma yin pa'i/ khyi gdong 'jigs su rung ba rnga ral chen po nam mkha'i dbyings su ye re ba/ phyag g.yas g.yon gnyis ral gri

dang bandha thugs khar steng 'og tu 'dzin pa/ gsol phod sngon po rdo rje gsang lam ma gsol zhing / sku gsham dkar po skya nyug ge ba dang bcas pa gsol ba/ mdor na nyid kyi
yab rje sngags 'chang chen po de nyid rdo rje phur pa'i smad las dang 'brel ba'i sku 'cham mdzad dus kyi sku chas bzhes pa'i skabs kyi ngo mtshar gyi sku'i bkod pa ji lta
ba bzhin du gzigs pa na/ de dus sku na phra bas yab rje nyid la zhu bar ma nus shing / slar gnas tshul rnams phul bas/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las/ de ni mi legs rgyu
med de/ bla ma mgon po dbyer med drag po'i chas su zhugs pa'i sku ru bstan 'dug pas/ mngon spyod kyi las rnams 'grub pa'i ltas yin no/ /zhes lung bstan dang bcas dbugs
dbyung gnang byung ba'i tshe/ rje nyid kyi thugs la/ nged rang las ma dag pas bsgribs pa ma gtogs ye shes kyi

mgon po logs na ga la yod/ sngags 'chang bla ma 'di ka mgon po dngos yin snyam pa'i thugs dad dang nges shes ci yang 'khrungs par gyur cing / yang dgung lo nyer gsum bzhes
skabs bse mgon mjal bar phebs dus 'cham sku'i zhal 'bag la gser gyi thig le 'od zer mang po 'phro ba can mngon sum du gzigs shing thugs la bde nyams chen po 'khrungs pa dang
/ 'di la gser 'bag zer ba dag rgyu yin pa 'dra snyam du dgongs shing / gzigs snang 'di ni rgyas pa'i las 'grub pa'i mtshan ma yang dag par mngon zhing / lan gcig bse
mgon gyi zhal dkyil dkar zhing snum pa bdud rtsi 'dzag la khad pa'i zil pa khrom khrom byed par mngon sum du gzigs pa ni zhi ba'i las rnams 'grub pa'i ltas yin gsungs shing
/ rgyun par bse mgon gyi sku mdog dmar smug la/ res 'ga' nag shas che shing / skabs 'gar dmar shas che bar rgyun chags

su gzigs snang la 'byung gi 'dug pa ni/ dbang drag gi las gnyis 'bad med du 'grub pa'i rtags su 'dug ces rje nyid kyi gsung las thos pa dang / yang drag po'i 'phrin las kyis
gdug pa can dngos su tshar bcad pa'i tshul yang chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa la/ hor rgyal pos rdo rje theg pa'i dbang zhu ba'i chos yon du chol kha gsum du grags pa'i dbus
gtsang dam pa chos kyi chol kha/ mdo stod ko le mi yi chol kha/ mdo smad gyi ling rta yi chol kha ste de gsum dang / de'i nang tshan khri skor bcu gsum zhes pa/ gtsang
la lha shang lho byang chu zhal drug /dbus na g.ya' phag thang mtshal rgya khri drug /gtsang dbus mtshams su ya 'brog khri skor ro/ /zhes pa ltar gyi/ de rnams phul ba
nas bzung sa skya pas 'jig rten gyi bdag po mdzad nas 'gro ba chos bzhin du bskyangs pa mi lo bdun cu rtsa

lnga tsam gyi bar du mdzad pa yin te/ de yang nang tshan du bzhi thog nas nyi shu rtsa lnga/ shar pas nyi shu rtsa lnga/ khang gsar chen mo bas nyi shu rtsa lnga ste yongs
bsdoms don lnga'i bar du zhal 'dzin gnang ba de'i mjug tsam nas/ si tu byang chub rgyal mtshan gyis sa'i bdag po byed par 'dod nas sde 'khrugs mang du byas pa la/ sa skya'i
rkang 'dzin dpon chen dbang brtson gyis yar klungs su khri skor bcu gsum gyi dmag lan mang du drangs kyang / si tu ba ma thub ste dbus kyi cha phal cher khong gis blangs/
phyis rta lo si tu byang rgyal gyi dmag dpung chen po sa skyar drangs te lha khang chen mo la bskor rgya byas nas sprul pa'i gtsug lag khang de nyid na bzhugs pa'i dngul
gar lugs las byas pa'i rten gsum thams cad bshigs te mdzo khal lnga bcu drangs pa dang / gzhan yang hor shel khyad par can las grub pa'i mchod cha sogs khyad nor rten
gsum ngo mtshar ba/ sa rgyan gnam rgyan la sogs pa

thams cad drangs/ lha khang chen mo'i rten gsum ma phug ron la sogs pa bya yi gnod pa mi 'byung ba'i ka khong tshang ma la shing gra khyad par can yod pa rnams kyang mer bus
te brlag par byed pa sogs mtshams med kyi las tshad med pa bsgrubs shing / de nas gtsang gi sa cha phal che ba yang 'og tu bcug de'i dus kyi sde dpon rnams kyi legs nyes
thams cad si tu byang chub rgyal mtshan shes su bcug dgos pa sogs sa skya pa la zhabs 'dren kham po che de bzhin sgrub pa'i tshe/ gdan sar dmag yong dus si tu pas bse mgon
chen po 'di nyid mjal bar chas te/ lha khang chen mo nas sa skya dan gyi bar gyi mchod zhing bya khra mar grags pa bkra shis rdzas brgyad nang tshan dung gi gzugs su
yod pas/ sa skya pa la snyan grags chen po 'byung ba'i rten 'brel de las byung bar bshad pa'i zhing de'i steng na tshur 'ong ba na/ si tu ba rang gos chen mtshal ga'i ber
zhig gyon pa'i

mtha' skor du khrab pa 'ga' zhig gis bskor nas byung ba/ skabs der sa skya rdzong chung na sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal ba bzhugs yod pas gzigs pa na/ pha gi rten 'brel bzang
/ lcags sder du snying bcug pa 'dra ba zhig 'dug ces gsungs shing / de nas sgo rum du 'cham mgon mjal bas/ bse 'bag gi zhal na snying rlon pa khrag dzar re ba zhig 'dug
pa ta'i si tu bas mngon sum du mthong bas shin tu skrag cing dngangs nas ha las te phyi 'gros su byas pas gan rkyal du 'gyel zhing / de nas yun ma lon par si tu tshe'i
dus byas pas/ sa skya pa'i chos skyong la sus kyang 'gran par mi nus pa'i snyan pa'i grags pas sa steng thams cad khyab par gyur to/ /de la sogs pa lo rgyus ngo mtshar can
du ma snang yang / 'dir yi ges 'jigs pas re zhig de tsam mo/ /de ltar na mal lo tsA ba'i bka' bzhin bla ma chen po dgung lo nyer dgur phebs pa'i byi ba'i lo/ bse 'bag
nag po 'phur

shes gdan sa chen por spyan drangs te/ dus de nyid nas bzung bstan srung kun gyi gtso bo gur gyi mgon po lcam dral/ phyi nang gsang ba'i las mkhan yang bran dang bcas pa thams
cad bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal sa skya 'dir ji srid bstan pa gnas kyi bar du mngon sum gyi tshul du bzhugs par zhal gyis bzhes shing / bla chen gyis bka' bsgos pa thams
cad bran bzhin du bsgrub par gyur pa de'i tshe/ sgo rum gzim spyil dkar po'i bla ma nyid kyi g.yos khang na chu ra'i zangs mo che ru long gi sgra chen po 'byin bzhin pa
zhig yod pa de la/ gsang ba'i las mkhan chen po pu tra lcam sring rnams rgyun du 'khor zhing dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur ci yang ston pa zhig byung ba las/ de rjes chos kyi rgyal
po 'phags pa'i sku ring la bzhi thog bla brang gi lho phyogs bod chol kha gsum gyi yongs sdud rnams bsdu ba'i gnas phyag mdzod nang so chen mor grags pa der/ sngar gyi
pu tra

gnas pa'i zangs mo che yang 'jog par mdzad pa na/ bla ma'i phyag rdzas rnams la las mkhan 'khor bcas shin tu mches pa'i rnam sprul ngo mtshar can du ma byung bas/ de'i gtang
rag tu gsang ba'i las mkhan gnas pa'i zangs la mgon khang zur chod du mdzad nas/ spyan gzigs sogs rgyas par bshams te de'i gtor gzhi'i rgyun yang phyag mdzod rang nas gnang
zhing / da lta yang nang so pu tra khang gi gtor gzhi rnams gdan sa mdzod chen gyis 'dzugs dgos pa'i rgyun 'di byung bar sems la/ mgon khang 'dir bzhugs pa'i pu tra
chen po gnas pa'i rten zhal 'bag smug chung du grags pa 'di ni/ sngon slob dpon padma 'byung gnas kyis rgya gar dur khrod bsil ba'i tshal du srin po'i sha khrag gis bam ro'i
sgrub pa mdzad pa'i tshe/ bar snang nas sprin nag rab tu g.yos te me drag tu 'bar ba dang bcas/ sprin gseb nas khrag gi thigs pa chen po gsum sa steng du babs pa na/
sa gzhi las kyang

rlung dmar drag tu langs shing g.yos par gyur te/ nam mkha' nas babs pa'i khrag thigs gsum po de/ srin po'i bam ro'i sha khrag rus gsum dang ro gcig tu 'dres pa la rgyu byas/
slob dpon rin po ches phyag bzo mdzad de/ deng sang bsam yas kyi spe dkar na yod pa'i zhal 'bag smug chung 'di dang / dpal sa skya'i nang so pu tra khang na bzhugs pa'i
zhal 'bag smug chung 'di gnyis dus gcig tu grub cing / slob dpon gyis phyag nas mdzad pa na/ pu tra dmar nag gnyis ka sku 'bag so so la dngos su thim zhing / chos skyong
so so dang byin rlabs nus pa mnyam par gyur pa las/ nam zhig dus la bab pa na/ rgya gar 'phags pa'i yul nas sku 'bag gnyis ka bar snang la 'phur te gshegs pa las/ bsam
yas chos skyong chen po'i sku 'bag de nyid bha ta hor yul gyi sgom grwar bab pa las/ rgyal po khri srong lde'u btsan gyi sku ring la sgom grwa bcom nas dngos spyad rnams
bsam

yas su khyer ba'i tshe/ zhal 'bag de yang bsam yas su byon pa yin la/ bod yul bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan srung bka'i las byed rnams kyi gtso bo'i mchog
tu gyur pa dpal 'phrin las kyi mgon po pu tra chen po'i zhal 'bag smug chung du grags pa da lta dpal sa skya'i nang so pu tra khang na bzhugs pa 'di ni/ rgya gar nas
'phur te re zhig bha ta hor yul gyi sgom grwar bzhugs pa las/ phyis rabs chos rje khu dbon tsam gyi sku ring la phyag tu byung ba de nyid/ gdan sa chen po 'dir spyan 'dren
par mdzad pa yin nam snyam du sems pa ni/ kho bos lo rgyus kyi yi ge mang po'i khong bsgrigs pas rtogs pa lags so/ /yang gdan sa chen po'i shar phyogs kyi mon pa grog po'i
phu na gnas pa'i mon chung pu tra ming sring gi byung tshul ni/ bla ma sa chen gyis la stod gung thang du byon nas chos skyong 'khor bcas kyi rjes gnang zhus dus/ mon
phrug gcig

'khyams pa bzhin byung ste/ bla ma mal la jo sras skya pa la nga'i gtad gnyer gyis shig zer zhing / res mi dngos su mthong zhing res mi mthong pa/ jo sras kyis gang bsgos kyi
g.yog byed pa gcig byung / ming mon chung pu trar btags/ gzugs snang dus g.yog gang dgos bsgrubs/ mi snang dus nga la gtor ma zhig slongs shig zer ba byung / de nas bla
chen gyis sa skya'i grog po shar gyi phu'i brag phug tu gnas nas/ gdan sa chen po 'di nyid kyi 'jig rten rjes gcod kyi srung ma byed par bka' bsgos te/ lo re bzhin rten
rdzas gos lham zung re gnang ba zhal gyis bzhes te/ de'i rgyun da lta yang bzhi thog gnyer khang nas cho 'phrul zla ba shar re bzhin/ ras kyi pho gos gnyis dang / mo gos
chung ngu lhwam dang bcas pa re mon chung gnas pa'i grog po'i mdo'i mgon khang du rgyun par 'bul ba 'di yin zhing / de nas bla chen gyis

mon chung gi rkyal 'bud kyi gdams pa'i skor rnams rje btsun sku mched sogs la gnang zhing / rje btsun chen po'i sku ring la gu ra ba'i gces phrug gcig gis nyes pa med par mon
chung yang yang brdungs pas/ rje btsun chen po'i drung du ngu zhing 'ongs skad/ khyod ci nyes gsungs pas/ khos zhib tu sngar gyi de tsho bshad dus re zhig tu song ba dang
gdams ngag sgrub kyin yod tsa na/ rje btsun chen po'i drung du gces phrug gi pha ma 'ongs nas/ byis pa sbos nas 'chi bar gda' ba/ mon chung gis ngan thabs byas pa 'dra
bar gda' ba bzod par gsol/ phan pa'i thabs byin rlabs la 'byon par zhu byas pas/ der rje btsun gyi zhal nas/ mon chung pu tra de ga na 'dug ltos dang / de la thug na 'chi
gsungs/ 'tshol du phyin pas/ mon 'go grog po'i nang na mi lag g.yas pa gcig la sba lcag gcig rdeg gin 'dug pa mthong nas/ de rje btsun la zhus pas/ lag pa de'i dbugs zad
dam

ma zad ltos shog gsungs pas/ lta mkhan gyis zad du cha yin 'dug zhus pas/ khyod da ci nas phrogs mi yong pa/ da la 'ur song la phrogs la shog gsungs pas/ de ma thag brgyugs
nas phyin pas/ khos ni bya ba tshar nas log yong gi 'dug go /de nas rje btsun gyis nad pa de'i rtsar byon pas/ nad pa de shi nas 'dug par gzigs nas/ mon chung pu tra'i mthu
yin pa gsang nas/ mon chung pu tra la bka' bkyon byon/ na bza'i thu bas phyag phab pas/ der kho ma dga' nas phyug po'i sgo rtsar phyin/ nga la bla mas phyag mang po phab/
bka' bkyon mang po byung pa de khyod kyis lan pas/ khyod kyi bu chung ba dang / khyod rang yang gsod dam byas pas/ phyug po des rje btsun gyi drung du phyin nas/ kho
'di skad du gleng gin byung zhus pas/ sngar ngas khyod la gsang ba yin/ da kho la ma rgol cig 'di mi dngos

ma yin/ chos skyong gi las mkhan mthu rtsal can gcig yin/ de'i don gyis res mthong res mi mthong / phal cher mi mngon par skad thos shing yod pa go mod/ mthong dus las byed
pas/ khong pa'ang brdungs pas lan pa yin gsungs/ phyug po pha bu gnyis kyis bla ma dang / mon chung pu tra la srog blus phul/ der bu rting ma ma shi'o/ /de ltar rje btsun
chen po bzhugs pa'i bar man chad du mon pa'i gzugs res ston/ res mi ston pa'i res 'jog kho na byed pa byung zhing / de nas chos rje sa paN hor yul la 'byon khar mon pa
de rnams 'das pa'i tshul gyis/ de phyin chad du gzugs mi mngon par gyur te/ gsang ba'i las mkhan chen po pu tra lcam sring gi las byed kyi pho nya'i kha lo pa byed pa'i tshul
gyis dpal sa skya'i bstan pa bstan 'dzin dang bcas pa skyong zhing / gdan sa chen po 'dir chos bzhin byed pa rnams

srung ba dang / chos min byed pa rnams tshar gcod pa'i las sgrub pa la nyin mtshan kun tu bya ra ba'i tshul gyis bzhugs pa yin no/ /gdan sa'i dus mdos chen mo'i skabs kyi 'cham
mgon las mkhan lnga dang bcas pa'i 'khor gyi mi nag dung longs can gsum po de yang / mon chung pu tra rnams kyi mtshon byed yin zhes sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i
gsung rgyun las 'byung ba bdag gi bla ma yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas de nyid yang yang du gsungs pa thos so/ /de lta bu'i rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug rje btsun brtse ba
chen po kun dga' snying po de nyid kyi phyag tu bstan srung kun gyi gtso bo dpal mahA kA la'i sku brnyan bse mgon/ shin mgon/ rdo mgon te rnam pa gsum dang / chos kyi bka'
babs gsum yongs su rdzogs pa babs pa nas/ dus ha cang mi ring ba zhig gi tshe/ chos skyong 'di'i sgo nas bstan dgra gdug pa can rnams drag po mngon spyod kyi las kyis

tshar bcad de rnam shes chos dbyings su sgrol bar mdzad pa'i tshul yang / dus der bdud sprul sngags nag bla chen stag tsha dang / bon nag re ba dzu gur zhes bya ba gnyis kyis
bstan 'dzin rnams la shin tu phrag dog pa'i sgo nas brtse ba chen po kun dga' snying po nyid la yang bar chad tho 'tshams byed snyam ste/ stag tsha'i slob ma khams kyi
ldan ma nas 'ongs pa'i ming rdor rgyal zer ba gcig gser gyis bslad nas bla chen 'grong du btang pas/ khams pa des kyang khas blangs nas sa skyar 'ongs pa'i tshe/ brtse ba
chen po kun dga' snying po de nyid sgo rum gzim spyil dkar por bzhugs yod pa la khams pa des mjal ga zhus pa na de 'phral sku zhogs su gnang ba'i tshe/ khams pa de na re/
bdag skye sa khams kyi ldan ma yin zhing / stod kyi phyogs su phyin nas lo du ma song / de nas bla chen khyed kyi snyan pa thos nas dad pa chen pos mjal du 'ongs pa lags/

da re zhig khyed kyi zhabs drung du bsdad chog par zhus pa la/ de bzhin du gnang zhing / gzhan yang 'phral du khams pa de gus gus ltar gyis thabs ci 'dra zhig byas nas bkrongs
pa drag gam snyam du sems pa'i tshe/ bla chen gyis mkhyen bzhin pa'i ngang nas/ nyin gcig gi tshe bla chen nyid kyi sku bem gyi nang du rje btsun sku mched rnams dang
bcas te yab sras lhan cig tu bzhugs pa na/ de nyid khams pas mthong ba'i tshe/ 'jig rten phal pa lta bu'i pha bu sdod lugs 'di 'dra ba dang bla ma lta ci/ chos pa tsam du
yang mi 'dug snyam log lta cher skyes pa'i tshe/ de nyid bla ma chen po'i ye shes kyi gzigs pas legs par dgongs te/ khams pa zhabs drung du 'bod par mdzad nas/ khyod la
rnam rtog ngan pa med mchis sam zhes gsungs pas/ khams pa nyid shin tu skrag ste tsab tsob tu gyur pa na/ bla chen gyi zhal nas gsang sngags

pa'i rdo rje slob dpon la log lta byed pa shin tu 'khrul pa yin gsungs nas zhabs gnyis shad kyis skyong bar mdzad pa'i zhabs mthil la kyai rdo rje dang / 'khor lo bde mchog
gi dkyil 'khor bris pa las kyang gsal ba gnyis khams pa la bstan pas/ rdor rgyal nyid shin tu 'gyod par gyur te/ sngar byas rnams bshags pa dang / phyin chad bla chen gyi
ched du lus srog gtong bar dam bca' phul/ de nas khams pa des bla chen stag tsha'i drung du phyin te/ sa chen bkrongs grub pa lta bu'i tshul smras pas/ bla chen stag tshas
de nyid bden par bsams nas mgo 'khor nas rdor rgyal la nye gnas bcol zhing / nged kyi mal sa dang phreng ba 'di la tho reg med cing shin tu gtsang ba rang dus rgyun du
bya dgos so zer ba sogs kyi bslabs cha mang du byas pa la khams pas bsam bzhin du mal sa yang yang du bshig bcos byed pa dang / phreng ba'i mdud pa bkrol te spyod

lam du dor mi mtshungs pa sna tshogs byas shing / de bzhin du bon nag la'ang byas pas/ khong gnyis kyi ngan sngags kyi tshogs shin tu 'khrugs par gyur to/ /de nas de'i skabs
der nus mthu'i mnga' bdag bla chen kun dga' snying po de nyid kyis chos skyong mthu rtsal can rnams bran du bkol te/ drag po mngon spyod kyi las la bskul ba'i sgo nas sngags
nag dang bon nag gnyis la dmigs pa'i las sbyor mdzad pa'i tshe/ sngags bon gnyis 'dug pa'i gnas der sngar med pa'i g.yag rgod rog po gnyis rwa brdar la sogs pa drag
po'i spyod pa zil dang ldan pa du ma byed pa re re byung zhing / gzhan yang bya nag khyi nag ce spyang sogs chos skyong gi sprul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'ang de'i dus byung
zhes grags la/ de dang dus mtshungs par dam tshig ldan pa'i khams pa rdor rgyal des/ sngags nag dang bon nag gnyis kyi slob 'khor rnams

phyogs gzhan dang gzhan du byer ba'i thabs byas nas/ de nas khong rang gcig pus zhag bcu phrag gsum gyi bar du sngags bon gnyis kyi zhabs tog la ches cher brtson pa ltar byas
nas/ zhag sum cu tsam lon pa na bla ma dang bstan pa'i ched du sngags nag dang bon nag gnyis rdzas dang mtshon la sogs pa'i sgo nas srog bral gyi cho ga yang dag pa la
sbyar nas/ khong gnyis kyi phung po chos skyong gi sprul pa'i g.yag rgod la bkal te gdan sar 'ongs pas/ sa skya pa'i chos skyong gi nus pas mtshan lam gcig la nyin lam drug
chod ces grags shing / de nas khams pas bla chen gyi drung du phung po gnyis phul bas shin tu dgyes shing / bla ma'i zhal nas/ khyod kyis spyir theg chen sems bskyed
dang ma bral zhing / bye brag bla ma dang bstan pa'i phyir du bya ba de bzhin bgyis 'dug par nyes pa mi 'byung zhing sngags bon gnyis kyang skye ba phyi ma ngan song du skye
nges pa'i las bsags pa'i rnam smin gyi 'bras bu rnams

tshe 'dir tshe thung ba tsam gyis sdug bsngal zad par byas nas/ bla ma dang chos skyong gi nus pas skye ba phyi ma phan chad du yang dag pa'i bde ba'i 'bras bu thob par 'gyur
ba yin pas na/ rang gzhan thams cad 'tshang ba yin no zhes gsungs shing / khams pa la bya dga' chen po gnang zhing / khyad par tshe gcig lus gcig la sangs rgya nges pa'i
gdams pa'i nying khu rnams gnang ste/ rdor rgyal gyis kyang khams su phyin te bsgoms pas grub rtags phyogs med du ston pa'i rnal 'byor pa bar dor phyag chen mchog gi dngos
grub 'thob nges pa zhig byung bar grags so/ /de nas bla chen gyis sngags nag gi snying phyung bar mdzad de hoM khung gi nang mdze thod kha sbyar gyi nang du bcug nas/
bse mgon chen po'i zhal gdong du 'jog par mdzad de/ mngon spyod kyi 'phrin las ci bsam 'grub pa'i bka' bsgo mdzad pa yin la/ dus

phyis bstan pa'i nyi ma sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyis kyang bse 'bag gi zhal gdong gi hoM khung kha phye ba mdzad nas mdze thod kyi nang
gi snying la nyams pa'i dgra bo lha gnas gnyis sogs la dmigs pa'i dgug gzhug lha dbye bden brdar sogs mdzad pas/ dam nyams rnams gtan brlag tu thong ba 'di bzhin byung ba
yin zhes bdag gi bla ma 'jam dbyangs sku mched kyi gsung las yang yang thos shing / da dung yang sa skya pa'i bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pa la gnod pa'i bstan dgra
mi srun pa rnams la shin tu myur ba'i las sbyor dgos pa byung tshe/ bsam pa rnam par dag pas kun nas bslangs te/ bla ma gong ma rnams kyi phyag len ltar bgyis na rtags mtshan
'byung ba la the tshom mi dgos snyam du kho bo sems so/ /sngags nag gi phung po byin sgo rum mgon khang gi them 'og tu bla chen nyid kyis mnan pa mdzad pa bzhin da
lta yang dbu rtse'i

skor lam nas phung po'i snod kyi rkyal pa kun gyis mthong bar yod do/ /bon nag re ba dzu gur gyi phung po chos khri thang mo che'i nub sgo'i 'khris kyi chu 'gram na mchod rten
gyi 'og tu mnan pa mdzad pa yin pas/ 'di la ched gtad kyi skor ba mi bya zhing / gal te byed kyang mgon po'i rtsa sngags dang bzlog bsad kyi sngags rnams bzla zhing skor
ba g.yon skor du bya ba yin par gsungs so/ /'dir skabs kyi sa chen gyi dngos slob khams pa rdor rgyal dang / bde gshegs khams pa rdor rgyal gnyis ming zur 'dra yang ngo
bo mi gcig ste/ phag gru'i mtshan la rdo rje rgyal mtshan zhes bya zhing / 'di'i ming rdo rje rgyal po zhes zer ro/ /de lta bu'i sngags nag dang bon nag gi lo rgyus 'di
rnams ni/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i gsung rgyun yin zhes sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyis bka' phebs ji ltar gnang ba bzhin

'jam dbyangs sku mched gnyis ka'i gsung las thos pa dang / lhag par 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang pos sa skya'i gnas bshad gsung rtsom gnang 'phro thor bur bzhugs pa rnams las
ji ltar 'byung ba bzhin bkod pa yin la/ de ltar na dpal brtse ba chen po nas chos rje sa paN yan chad du sa skya pa ste/ shes ldan kun yid smon gyi gnas su gyur pa 'di
yang rje btsun bla ma rnams kyi thugs rje las gzhan du ma 'das par shes par gyis shig 'dir smras pa/ 'jam dbyangs 'jig rten dbang phyug mthu stobs mgon/ /de rnams dbyer
med gzugs gzhan zlos pa'i gar/ /sa skya'i bla chen kun dga' snying po yi/ /ngo mtshar

rnam thar bsam brjod yul las 'das/ /rgyal ba'i pho brang rdo rje gdan nyid kyi/ /byang sgo'i srung mar sangs rgyas dngos kyi bkas/ /bskos pa'i rdo rje'i gur gyi mgon po de/
/dngos su bzhugs pa'i 'dra 'bag bse mgon ches/ /ye shes gzigs pas dam pa'i chos rnam dag /gang du dar ba'i gnas der bsrung brtson par/ /bzhed nas spro ba chen pos nam mkha'
la/ /chibs te nyid bstan skyong phyir sa skyar byon/ /dus gsum mkhyen pa'i blo gros dkyil 'khor can/ /sa gsum grags pa'i 'od kyis khyab mdzad de/ /kun mkhyen kun la rab
dga' ster mkhas pa'i/ /byang chub snying po mchog brnyes brtse chen la/ /gnam lcags las grub rdo rje thugs kyi rten/ /dbang sngon las grub drag sngags gsung gi rten/ /bse
mgon 'phur shes gang skur bcas pa ni/ /bka' bsgos zhal 'ches

dang bcas gnang nas kyang / /sa bdag klu dbang sa skya gnas pa 'dir/ /shAkya'i bstan pa bsrung phyir spyan drangs te/ /ri rab lhun po ji srid gnas kyi bar/ /zhing 'dir brtan
par bzhugs 'di e ma mtshar/ /bstan srung dbang po'i sku brnyan rnam bzhi dang / /zab rgyas chos kyi bka' bab rnam pa bzhi/ /yongs su rdzogs pa deng dus dpal sa skyar/ /sngags
'chang kho bo'i lag tu legs par bab/ /'di 'dra skal bzang nang nas skal bzang ste/ /ngo mtshar che ba las kyang che ba ru/ /shes pa'i shes ldan gzur gnas 'ga' yod
na/ /kho bo'i snyan grags snyan par cis mi sgrog /bstan pa'i bdag po dpal ldan sa skya pa/ /yin phyir dam pa'i chos kyi bsrung ba yang / /mthu rtsal che bar grags pa'i tshogs
kun kyang / /mchis shing 'phrin las sgrub pa dngos po'i gshis/ /dpal sa skya'i bka' srung zhing skyong stobs 'phrog dbang po zhal bzhi pa

'khor dang bcas pa dang / u rgyan mkha' 'gro'i gling gi dpal dur khrod kyi bdag po yab yum/ dkar bdud lcam dral/ phur srung dam can bcu gnyis bod du ji ltar byung ba'i tshul
ni/ de la spyir kha ba can gyi ljongs 'dir gsang sngags rnying ma ba dang / gsar ma ba dang / ches gsar ma ba dag las brgyud pa'i zhing skyong nag po chen po gdong bzhi
pa'i man ngag gi rigs mang po snang ba las/ gtso bor ni mgon po 'di nyid kyi chos skor 'phags yul nas spyan 'dren par byed po ni/ gnyan lo tsA ba chen po dar ma grags nyid
yin te/ de nyid nas brgyud de byang gi phyogs 'dir man ngag gi bshad srol ches cher rgyas par mdzad pa ni/ rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras brgyud par bcas pa dag yin pas/
de yang dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po dpal dbyangs kyi rigs rgyud du shab stod du sku 'khrungs pa'i gnyan

chung dar ma grags de nyid kyis rgya gar du byon nas sgra tshad bslabs pas mkhas par mkhyen/ de nas bla ma pandre pa chen po ratna kirti dang / rdo rje gdan pa sogs la chos
mang du gsan/ rig pa'i gnas lnga la thogs pa med pa'i blo gros rgyas/ bod la log 'byon khar bla ma pandre pa la gsang ba 'dus pa ye shes zhabs lugs kyi dbang zhus pas/ ngas
mi yong / kharsa pa Ni'i lho phyogs kyi ri sul gyi nags gseb cig na/ nga'i mched mo rnal 'byor ma rje btsun ku sa li bya ba gcig gsang ba 'dus pa'i sgrub pa mdzad kyin
yod pas der song la zhus shig khyod dang las kyi 'brel pa yod pas dbang dang gdams ngag gnang ba 'dug gi gsungs/ de nas bla ma pandre pa'i bka' bzhin mdzad nas gnyan los
byon pas/ ji ltar gsungs pa bzhin ri sul gyi nags gseb na shing sdong po chen po zhig gi khog pa na rnal 'byor ma dpon g.yog bzhi gda' skad/ de'i nang nas

g.yog mo gsum re mos kyis grong 'dabs na phar phyin te 'tsho ba btsal nas sgrub pa mdzad kyin 'dug pa la/ lo tsA bas lung bstan pa'i rnal 'byor ma yin min brtag pa'i phyir
g.yog mo rnams la khyed rnal 'byor ma yin na nus pa zhig ston gsungs pas/ gcig gis brang gshags nas khog gi nang nas gsang 'dus kyi lha grangs dang mnyam pa'i mar me bstan
nas nges shes skyes te/ gtso mo la phyag dang maNDal phul nas gsang ba 'dus pa'i dbang bskur zhus pas/ khyod la sus lung bstan gsungs/ nga la bla ma pantre pas bstan zhus
pas/ ngas 'jam pa'i rdo rje la gnang ba ma thob pas/ khyod rang sdod khom na lo gcig nas dbang bskur bya gsungs/ de bzhin bgyid zhus pas/ 'o na khyod la mtha' 'khob kyi
mi ngan dang / gcan gzan dang / dug sbrul la sogs pas 'tshe ba byung dogs yod pas/ grong 'dabs

pha gi na bram ze mdog sngo ba mi rkang gi gling bu bzung ba gcig yod pas de dang 'grogs la ci za ci 'thung gi kha nas byin/ ci 'byor pa'i mchod pa dang bsnyen bkur gyis shig
ngas bar chad mi 'byung bar byin gyis rlob bo gsungs/ de bzhin byas pas lo gcig song nas/ da ngas lha la gnang ba thob pas dbang bya yi tshogs kyi yo byad tshol cig gsungs/
gser zho gang la 'bras khal bcu gsum blangs nas chang byas/ zho gang la sha dang / zho gang la spos la sogs pa gzhan dgos pa'i yo byad rnams bsgrubs nas khyer te/ rnal
'byor ma'i drung du phyin nas tshogs rdzas rnams phul/ gdan mang po yang tshang 'dug pa dang / rnal 'byor ma'i zhal nas/ mgron spyan drongs gsungs pa la/ bdag gis mi
rnyed zhus pas/ 'o na kha sang gi grogs po bram ze de bos gsungs nas bos pas/ bram zes skra gseb nas mi rkang gi gling bu phyung ste bus ma thag phyogs bzhi mtshams brgyad
nas

dpa' bo mkha' 'gro dang / rnal 'byor pho mo lugs mi 'dra ba du ma/ zhing skyong bka' sdod bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'dus nas gral la 'khod cing tshogs kyis tshim par byas pas mnyes
te dbang bskur yongs su rdzogs par gnang / de nas tshogs gral de'i khrod nas grub thob brgyad cu rtsa lnga byon nas/ lo tsA ba khyod dngos grub gang 'dod gsungs/ de
dus dngos grub gang 'dod zhus pas 'ong ba la/ lo tsA ba thugs cung zad zhum nas gzhan zhu ma spobs/ bdag bod du gtsug lag khang mang po bzhengs pas/ de rnams su chos skyong
re zhu zhus/ grub thob kun bzhad gad mdzad cing / so so'i chos skyong re re gnang nas lo tsA ba'i g.yog byed par bka' bsgos/ de nas slar yang rnal 'byor ma'i drung du
gdams pa rgya mtsho ltar gsan cing thun mong ma yin pa'i gdams pa lnga gnang ste/ thugs dam du gsang ba 'dus pa'i gdams pa/ uShNi Sha

sbyor ba yan lag drug pa/ sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ chos skyong 'di'i gdams pa ma lus par gnang zhing / lhag par chos skyong gi dbang gi dus su bram ze khyod kyis kho'i g.yog
gyis shig khos ci bsgo ba bzhin 'phrin las rnam pa bzhi 'bad med du bsgrub par bya dgos so/ /zhes bka' bsgos nas dngos su gnang ba de ni chos skyong yid bzhin gyi nor bu
lta bu nyid yin pas/ byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa bar ma chad pas bsgrub thag nye ba'i man ngag dam pa shin tu rtsis che ba 'di yin no/ /de nas bla ma gnyan lo tsA ba de nyid
kyis rgya gar kha che khri gdan nas pu hrangs su byon pa'i tshe/ bal yul phan chad bram ze dang dngos su 'grogs shing / khres po 'khur ba sogs g.yog gang dgos bram zes
byas/ de nas chos skyong rang gi gsung las/ da phyin chad nged kyi gzugs rgyun par dngos su mi snang bar byed/ nam dgos dus dngos su 'ong / dus rtag tu ban chung gi gzugs
su sprul na/

nga bod kyi lha 'dre gdug pa can 'dul ba sogs la mngags par 'ong zer ba la/ bla mas kyang de bzhin du gnang ste/ de nas ban chung nye gnas kyi tshul du mdzad nas byon pas/
mnga' bdag btsan lde'i bsam pa la/ nga rgyal po yang yin/ mnga' ris stod na nga las grags che ba dang / dbang stobs che ba med pas/ lo tsA ba nga la mjal du 'ongs nas phyag
'tshal thang snyam/ bla ma gnyan gyi thugs dgongs la/ nga rgya gar gyi grub thob rnams kyi slob ma lo tsA ba yin/ khyad par rdo rje gdan pa bla ma pandre pa rin chen grags
pa/ mar me mdzad bzang po rnams kyi chos rgyud 'dzin pa yin pas/ btsad pos nga la phyag dang sna len sogs byed thang snyam nas/ bla mas tshong pa mang po dang 'grogs
nas byon dus mnga' bdag la rgya gar nas phra ma byung ste/ gnyan lo zer ba 'dis rgya gar gyi ngan sngags thams cad bslabs nas song pas/ der sha ma mi byed do zer ba dang
/ rgyal

po yang chags che bas 'khrul nas bden du rung snyam/ blon po dpa' rtsal dang ldan pa rta pa sum cu bla ma 'grong du btang pas/ bla ma'i mnal lam du rgyal pos brdzangs pa'i
blon po sdig can rnams yod par mkhyen te/ tshong pa rnams la phye phud sdus shig nged rang tsho la bar chad cig 'ong bar 'dug pas chos skyong la gtor ma chen po gtong dgos
pa 'dug gsungs gtor ma'i rgyu la spos 'bru sman sogs btab nas phul/ zhing skyong chen po tsa turmu kha 'di la gsol ba btab pas/ sngags bzlas pa tsam gyis tshong pa rnams
kyi mthong snang la mon pa sngon po lnga gar byed pa/ bro byed pa gnyis/ gri skor byed pa gnyis/ jo mo zhwa thebs can gcig 'khor bka' skyong mang po byung ba mthong skad/
de nas rlung nag 'tshub mas mtha' bskor/ bla ma dpon slob dbus su bcug nas byon pas/ blon po rnams kyi mthong snang la/ rlung nag 'tshub ma'i gseb

na a tsa ra gri skor byed pa gnyis min pa gzhan ci yang ma mthong ngo / /de'i mon pa gar byed pa rnams dang / a tsa ra gri skor byed pa 'tshub nag dang bcas pa ni/ chos skyong
'di'i rtags dang / mon pa bro byed pa ni yi dam sgrol ma'i las mtha'i nus pa dang / jo mo zhwa thebs can ni gnod sbyin gyis las sgrub pa'i rtags yin par bshad la/ de
nas blon po rnams kyis phyir log 'ongs pas/ bla ma dpon slob phebs grub 'dug pa dang / lo rgyus rnams rgyal po la zhus pas/ mnga' bdag rgyal po'i bsam pa la bla ma 'di chos
skyong bran du bkol nus pa zhig 'dug snyam nas 'gyod pa skyes te bab btang / bshags pa phul zhabs spyi bor blangs pas rgyal po rang ma grongs tsam byung rung / blon po
la la khrag bskyugs te shi la la brgyal/ la la smyo/ la la rengs/ la la 'bog ste thams cad shi ba dang 'dra bar byas nas chos skyong bran

du 'khol bar grags so/ /gzhan yang lam bar la lo tsA ba dpon g.yog la gnod pa che ba byung ba rnams su bla mas chos skyong la gnas der bar zhag gcig mdzod cig gsungs pa rnams
su rims nad thu ba re byung / gnod pa chung sa rnams su lo tsA bas chos skyong la gnas der nya mgo zhig non zhig gsungs pas/ der rims nad chung ba re byung nas lo tsA
ba dpon g.yog la gnod pa byed mi byung tshad shi skad/ de nas rim gyis phebs te lo tsA ba'i gnas gzhi dar lung dang snar thang byang chen dang / dpon gsum 'ong kha/ dpal
ldan sa skya'i phu gnam kha'ub skyed lhas rnams su bzhugs nas/ gnas de dag tu mgon khang gtsug lag khang bzhengs nas phyag nas mdzad/ chos skyong 'di la bka' gtad mdzad dus
gtsug lag khang la me 'bar te me 'bar gyi gtsug lag khang zhes grags/ de bzhi la bod kyi me 'bar gyi gnas bzhi dang / te si/ bsil

ba'i tshal/ po ta la/ ha ha rgod pa'i dur khrod bzhi la rgya gar gyi me 'bar gyi gnas bzhi zhes pa'i tha snyad kyang bla ma dag bzhed do/ /gnyan lo chen pos bla ma gnam kha'ub
pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan la chos skyong 'di'i rjes gnang sogs gdams pa rdzogs par gnang / de'i las tshogs la brten nas kha'u'i mdun ri la bon po'i grong mang du yod pa
dang 'gras pa las/ lo gcig gi nang du bon po pho mo brgya tsam shi nas grong khyer brlag par mdzad pa ni chos skyong 'di'i nus mthu'i sgo nas yin pas nus mthu myur zhing
che bar grags so/ /de nas lo tsA bas bod du gtsug lag khang ha cang mang ba bzhengs ma thub pas/ bla ma'i thugs dgongs la chos skyong 'di rnams rgya gar du brdzangs na
legs pa 'dug dgongs te/ lan gcig mchod gtor rgyas pa gcig phul nas/ da nged kyis lha khang mang po bzhengs mi thub pas/ khyed rang rnams rgya gar du byon cig ces

de ltar du gsol bas/ chos skyong gzhan rnams rgya gar du gshegs te/ de'i rtags su mi mang po'i mthong snang la/ bya rog bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung nas gtor ma zos te thams
cad rgya gar gyi phyogs su 'phur nas song ba mthong ba dang / mi kha cig gis thug bcom dang 'ur sgra chen po thos pa byung / de dus chos skyong 'di'i gsung gis/ nga ri sul
gyi rnal 'byor mas khyod kyi g.yog la brdzangs pa de bor nas phyin na bla ma'i dam tshig dang 'gal bas mi 'gro zer te log ma 'dod pas/ chos skyong gzhan las kyang bla
ma'i dam tshig la rtsi bas/ dam tshig gi mgon po zer ba'i rgyu mtshan yang de yin par snang / de nas dus ring zhig lon pa na/ bla ma gnyan lo sku mya ngan las 'da' khar/
chos skyong gi rnam 'phrul ban chung de la/ nga mya ngan las 'da' bar 'dug pas/ kha'u'i brag rdzong na nged kyi bu'i mchog bla ma gnam kha'u pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan zhes
bya ba

yod pas/ de'i drung du song la nga la ji ltar byed pa bzhin khong gi g.yog tshul bzhin du gyis la/ khong mya ngan las 'das pa dang rgya gar 'phags pa'i yul du gshegs shig ces
bka' gnang ba dang / bka' bzhin gnam kha'ub tu byon nas bla ma gnam gyi nye gnas mdzad do/ /de nas dus ring zhig lon pa dang / zhing skyong chen po 'di nyid bod kha ba
can 'dir bstan pa bsrung bar bzhugs pa'i rten 'brel gyis/ nyin gcig kha ba bu yug 'tshub pa zhig dang bstun gsol chu 'chu ba'i skyogs ri 'gram gyi chu khar lus pa/ kha'u'i
brag rdzong gi rtse'i sgrub khang gi dkar bsang nas phyag ring brkyangs nas bzhes pa/ bla ma gnam gyis gzigs pas/ khyod la gzhan las rtsal che zhing rdzu 'phrul du ma
ston pa zhig 'dug pa dang / khyad par da lan gyi rdzu 'phrul gyis skyogs len lugs de bzhin ngo mtshar che bas sprul pa yin nges su 'dug pas/ sku dngos su ston

pa zhig 'tshal zhes gsol ba btab pas/ bla ma de skad mi gsungs pa zhu/ nged rang gnyis ka la mi legs gsungs pa la slar gsol ba btab pas/ nga dam tshig bsrung du chug sngon
ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma'i bka' bzhin bla ma gnyan gyi phyag phyi byas/ da yang bla ma gnyan gyi bka' bzhin khyed nam gshegs bar phyag phyi byas mthar rgya gar la 'gror chug
gsungs/ slar nan gyis gsol ba btab pas/ des na bla ma rang skrag pa'i snang ba cung zad ma skyes pa mdzod gsungs nas zhal bzhi yongs rdzogs kyi zhal gzigs shing / sku
nam mkha'i khams khyab pa zhig sprul pa dang / zil che bas bla ma cung zad cig bde stong gi ngang du rtog med du gyur/ de las sangs te gzigs pas chos skyong gi sku sngar
bzhin 'dug pa dang / shangs mtshal cung zad byung ba'i rkyen gyis shangs mtshal gyi ras la sku de ji lta ba bzhin g.yas dkar g.yon dmar yod pa bris tshar mtshams gzigs

snang gi sku de nyid 'ja' 'od kyi rnam pas sgrub khang gi brag skyibs la thim pas/ dus ding sang gi bar du kha'u brag rdzong gi gtsug lag khang na tsa turmu kha dngos su bzhugs
par grags shing / bris sku de yang bla ma gnam gyi zhal gzigs mar grags pa da lta yang brag sgo rang na bzhugs so/ /rje btsun gnam kha'ub pa de nyid kyi drung du brtse
ba chen po dpal ldan sa skya pa kun dga' snying pos/ chos skyong 'di'i rjes gnang / man ngag sogs chos skor rdzogs par gsan cing rjes gnang tsam ni gnyan lo tsA ba'i drung
du'ang gsan par mdzad la/ spyir mgon po 'di la phyi bram ze ltar sgrub pa/ nang zhing skyong ltar sgrub pa/ gsang ba stobs 'phrog dbang po ltar sgrub pa dang gsum du
yod cing / phyi ma la yang bsnyen dus kyi mgon po/ sgrub dus kyi mgon po/ las sbyor gyi mgon po/ las bzhi so so'i mgon po la/ dkar po tshe 'phel/ ser po

rgyas byed/ dmar po dbang bsdud/ drag po bgegs 'joms rnams dang / gzhan yang spogs chog gi mgon po/ gnad dbab kyi mgon po/ shi sa bstan pa'i mgon po ste/ de rnams la rjes gnang
mi 'dra ba re re dang / bram ze sngags gtad du grags pa'i zab mo'i mthar thug de nyid sogs nus ldan du bya ba'i rjes gnang gi skor mang po dang / man ngag gi skor la
bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis dkar chag gi them yig ma mdzad kyang / chos skyong 'di'i skor rnams phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i phyag dpe'i bzhugs byang gi mjug na/
rang la ma dris par gzhan gyis man ngag brkus pa dang / po ti 'di phral ba sogs byung na dpal mgon gnyan pos ma thogs par chad pa chod cig 'khon sa skya pa blo gros kyi
zab chos te/ kun gyi thun mong ma yin no/ /zhes pa'i phyag yig 'debs par mdzad pa'i pod chung du longs pa tsam bzhugs

pa de nyid dang / sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin ngor phyogs nas brgyud pa'i mgon po'i chos skor gyi po ti ser pod du grags pa'i nang na yang / 'di'i man ngag gi yig skor mtha' yas
pa zhig bzhugs shing / yang rdzong phyogs kyi sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin rnams las brgyud pa'i zhal bzhi pa'i man ngag gi skor gyi po ti la/ mus srad pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan
gyis mdzad pa'i dkar chag dang bcas pa bzhugs pa dang / dus phyis rje btsun sa skya pa'i snyan brgyud kyi man ngag kun gyi bka' bsdu ba po lta bur gyur pa mkhas pa'i
dbang po tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtshos chos skyong 'di'i chos skor rnams mkhas grub kyi bla ma bdun las nos te/ 'di'i man ngag gi skor zab dgu de dag 'khrugs pa dang 'thor
ba'i skyon spangs pa'i phyir/ dkar chag gi yi ge khyad par can mdzad pa sogs lugs 'di'i chos skor gyi yi ge po ti longs pa dang / sil bur bzhugs pa sogs du ma zhig snang
zhing /

mgon po 'di'i man ngag gi bzhugs tshul gyi khog khrigs bla ma gong ma rnams kyi gsung las 'byung ba bzhin cung zad brjod na/ 'di la brgyud pa rnam par dag pa gsum las 'ongs
pa'i gdams ngag gi srol gsum yod de/ paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa nas brgyud pa dang / shrI paNDi ta ta thA ga ta rakShi ta las brgyud pa dang / kharsa pA Ni'i ri sul gyi
rnal 'byor ma ku sA li chen mo nas brgyud pa dang gsum gyi dang po ni/ mgon po gdong gnyan can nam las sbyor gyi mgon por grags pa de nyid de/ 'di'i man ngag gi skor rnams
yin la/ gnyis pa paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa nas brgyud pa ni/ bdag mdun mgon po zhal khra can nam sgrub dus kyi mgon por grags pa la byed cing / las bzhi bye brag sgrub
tshul shin tu zab pa zhig snang bas/ 'di'i skor gyi yi ge rnams yin zhing / gsum pa ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma las brgyud pa la/ zab cing rgya che ba phyi'i sgrub skor/
rdo

rje lus la gnad du bsnun pa gsang ba'am nang gi man ngag snying nang gi khrag lta bu khyad par gyi man ngag gsum las/ dang po ni/ yid ches shing khungs btsun pa'i phyir du
brgyud pa'i lo rgyus kyi skor/ nus ldan du bya ba rjes gnang gi skor/ rtsa bar gyur pa bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi skor/ gsal byed du gyur pa lhan thabs sam yan lag gi skor/
'phral du nye bar mkho ba gtor chog dang bskang ba bstod bskul gyi skor rnams su yod cing / gnyis pa ni rdo rje'i lus la gnad du bsnun pa gsang ba'am nang gi man ngag ste/
de yang rtsa gsum 'khor lo lnga'i sgrub gzhi la/ bsgrub bya las bzhi'i mgon po bkod pa'i bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi man ngag gi tshes 'dir zung 'jug rdo rje 'chang gi
go 'phang sgrub pa'i thabs dang / de'i cha rkyen las bzhi bye brag tu sgrub pa'i thabs ches zab pa zhig yin pa 'di nyid ston pa'i man ngag gi skor rnams yin zhing / gsum
pa snying nang gi khrag lta bu'i

man ngag la gnyis yod de/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor mas bla ma gnyan la gdams pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i shog ril nyer gcig dang / de las zab pa'i man ngag gi skor gnyis las/ phyi
ma la las bzhi'i mgon po'i sgrub tshul sogs man ngag mtha' yas pa zhig bzhugs shing / gzhan yang zhal gdams snying gi dum bur grags pa'i skor rnams dang / de rnams las
kyang ches zab pa yang gsang ha la nag po'i be'u bum ma yig bu yig dang bcas pa sogs mdor na mthu ldan gnyan gyi mgon po gdong bzhi pa'i chos skor zab cing rgya che ba
zhig rje btsun sa skya pa rnams las brgyud de/ da lta'i bar du rgyun ma chad par bzhugs pa'i chos skor de thams cad ma tshang ba med pa kho bo cag gis don gnyer cher bgyis
nas yongs 'dzin dam pa bka' drin can dag las legs par nos pa 'di yang bla ma dang bstan srung gi thugs rje las byung bar nges la/ zhing skyong dur khrod bdag po'i chos
skor rnams

ji ltar byung ba'i tshul ni/ sngon khams pa rga lor grags pa khams aM tshangs pa zhes pa'i brgyud pa khungs btsun pa'i rigs su 'khrungs nas/ der khong dal 'byor don yod bya
bsams te/ dbus gtsang na bstan pa yod zer 'ongs pas/ de'i dus na sha ra ba grags che bas gdams ngag zhus pas/ mi rtag pa bstan/ de la khong na re/ de go nas chos byed pa
yin mod/ de bas zab pa gcig med dam zhus pas/ med gsungs/ 'di la chos rje pa'i gsung gis/ sha ra ba khong bshad pa byed tsa na/ shes rab can sgrog tu mi gzhug dad pa can
g.yang la mi skyur ba'i 'ud yod de/ rga lo la bdag gzhan brje ba zhig ston thang pa la gsungs shing / sha ra ba'i drung der gtsang phyogs pa'i dge bshes drag pa tsho 'ang
'dug pas/ de ru phyin kyang med nges snyam ste rgya gar du byon pas/ nyang stod rtsa mi lo tsA ba dang mjal/ khong yang bod byung bas dgyes

te/ 'dir sdod ngas chos dang 'tsho ba gnyis ka bya zer bas bod snyam po la nyan pa mi yong / paNDi ta gcig la nyan bsams te byon nas rgya gar na su mkhas dris pas/ a bha ya
mkhas zer/ der 'gro bsam pas/ paNDi ta gcig mdo li la bteg byung bas/ su yin dris pas a bha ya yin zer/ gar bzhud byas pas/ tsa mi la chos nyan du bzhud zer/ 'o na mi phan
pa 'dug snyam khong can phyin/ dbang zhus dus 'khor tshar gcig gsan/ rdo rje gdan gyi mchod khang du sbyor drug bsgoms pas/ mtshan mo'i rnal 'byor rdzogs mthong lam skye
la khad par song ba dang / 'dzim los kyal ga byas te/ rga chung pa byas pas skad ma byung / khyod dang skad mi ster 'dug ste/ ma ga ta thams cad du ru kas khengs pas/
nged thams cad 'bros gyin yod do byas pas snying sngangs te/ nga 'bros sgo phye zer/ ku re yin byas kyang ma lo/ tsa mis khyed

rang kha 'gras pa'i ku re yin/ 'jigs na nged kyis kyang chos 'dir bshad kyi/ bar chad yin byas pas/ bar du bcad zin nga'i snying 'gas par 'dug go sgo phye zer sgo brdungs/
der phye bas smyo nas tsA mi dpon g.yog po mi sod la bkod/ dgong gcig bros bdas pas kyang ma zin/ nangs par btsal bas lha khang gcig gi nang du dbang phyug gi rten gcig gi
phrag gong na sgom du song 'dug ci yin byas pas/ mdang 'dir 'ongs 'dug 'jigs pa snyam byed/ der 'jigs rgyu med/ 'jig rten na che ba dbang phyug chen po yin te/ nga'i yi
dam dus 'khor gyi gdan na yod pa yin snyam ste 'dzegs pas 'dir thar/ der sgom du song 'dug zer/ der rgya gar na gdam ngag su che zer ba la dris kyang ma phan/ de nas rtsa
mi'i gsung gis/ da khyod kyi 'di la rgya gar na ni phan pa mi 'dug bod na bla ma sa skya pa bya ba rnal 'byor dbang phyug

gi gdam ngag la mkhas shing / de'i sprul par yang grags pa zhig yod 'dug pa de can song zer bas khams 'dus par song bas/ rgyags dang go lag ci yang med par de ka la zengs song
bas/ skyid grong du sleb sleb grang ba'ang ma tshor/ der mi rims nad kyis shi ba'i ra cog gcig gyon nas/ na la rtser bla chen bzhugs par sang nyin sleb pa'i do nub/ bla
chen gyis kyang thugs mkhyen gyis dgongs nas/ nye gnas la sang nyin su byung ba de thongs shig gsungs pas/ gzhan ni ma byung / mi smyo ba 'dra ba zhig byung nas/ nga bla
chen la mjal zer/ da lta sku mtshams la bzhugs yod mi mjal byas pas/ gzhan dang mi mjal yang / nga dang mjal ba zhig yin gyis dang zer/ sgo srung pa brdungs nas nang du
zhugs nye gnas kyis sgo mnan pas/ bla chen gyis thongs gsungs/ drung du slebs pa na/ khyed bla ma sa skya pa chen po yin nam zer/ yin gsungs pas/

der dang po chos la 'ong lugs/ rgya gar du phyin pa khams 'dus byung tshul sogs bshad nas gegs sel zhu zer ba la/ dbang ni tsa mis bskur bas go chod pa mdzad nas/ de ma thag
gdam ngag bstan te bsgoms pas/ sngar gyi sgom gyis brlan yod pa dang / snying rus che bas/ dmigs pa lan gcig gnyis rang gis bsangs drag der rga los brgyad stong pa gcig
spyi bor bzhag nas/ rgya bod gnyis na khyod las gdam ngag che ba yod re zer ma bsgags pa'i mna' zhig bskyal/ de nas bla chen gyis/ da khyed la yon tan zhig skyes pas tsa
mi can song la sgoms gsungs pas/ de tsa na sos ka yin pas tshad pa byung gis dogs nas dgun 'gro snyam tsa na grub thob yin zer grags pa chen po byung / chag stod 'brog pas
spyan drangs/ rgya gar la ni ma thon/ de nas brgyud de dbus kyi byang skyabs su byon/ sha ra ba dang

mjal bas bka' bkyon byung / rga lo khros nas dkar yol sa la brdabs pas/ gral gang gi phor pa sa la lhung / de la sogs pa'i rdzu 'phrul du ma bstan nas khams su byon pas longs
spyod chen po byung zhing / bstan pa dang sems can gyi don phyogs med du rgyas par grags/ de lta bu'i rga lo nyid kyis nor skyong dur khrod kyi bdag po yab yum gyi rjes
gnang / de'i rgyud gsang ba snying gi 'khor lo/ sgrub thabs bai ro tsa nas mdzad pa/ gzhan yang bsnyen sgrub las gsum zhal gdams kyi man ngag thor bu ba du ma dang bcas
pa'i chos skor rdzogs par mkhas pa bai ro tsa na las ji ltar gsan pa bzhin dpal brtse ba chen po nyid la phul zhing / de nas da lta'i bar du brgyud pa bar ma chad par dar
rgyas su bzhugs pa bzhin/ kho bo cag gis kyang rjes gnang nos nas rgyun ring lon pa'i rjes su don gnyer dang rtsol ba cher byas nas 'di'i rgyud dang / man ngag gi yi ge

gsar rnying yongs su rdzogs pa nos pa lags/ 'khon sa skya pa'i bka' srung dkar bdud lcam dral phur srung bcu gnyis dang bcas pa'i chos skor rnams byung ba'i tshul ni/ bod 'dir
bstan pa snga dar gyi dus su slob dpon rin po che padma 'byung gnas kyi dngos slob 'khon ston chen po klu'i dbang po dang / gcung rdo rje rin chen gnyis kyis chos skyong
dkar mo nyi zla lcam dral dang phur srung ma mo sde gsum gyi man ngag rnams slob dpon nyid la gsan te/ klu'i dbang pos yer ba'i brag la sgrub pa mdzad pas grub pa brnyes
te/ mkhas grub kyi grags pa cher byung / gcung rdo rje rin po ches kyang sgrub pa mdzad pas/ yi dam lha'i zhal gzigs shing grub pa thob ste mtshan grags thon/ de nas
'khon shes rab yon tan nas bzung / 'khon rog shes rab tshul khrims dang / 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po sku mched kyi bar du byon pa'i 'khon ston gong ma

de thams cad kyis/ yang dag dang phur pa la thugs dam gyi mthil mdzad pas grub pa brnyes/ chos skyong dkar bdud lcam dral dang / phur srung bcu gnyis la mdzad pas nus pa thon
pa sha stag byung / 'khon rog shes rab tshul khrims sku mched kyi skabs su sngags pa za 'dod can mang pos/ dbang phyug ma nyi shu rtsa brgyad kyi mgo brnyan gyon/ phyag
mtshan so sor khyer/ ma mo ral pa can gyi rnga stabs dang bcas nas khrom gyi dbus su 'cham gyin 'dug pa/ gcung dkon mchog rgyal pos gzigs nas gcen la zhus pas/ 'khon rog
gi gsung las/ da gsang sngags 'chol par spyod pa zhes bya ba'i dus byung bas/ da phyin chad rnying ma la grub thob mtshan nyid pa dkon pa yin/ rang la yod pa rnams rang
nyid dbang che ba yin pas/ rang gi dpe cha rten gsum rnams gter du sbed gsungs nas sbas pas/ dkar bdud kyi cho 'phrul cher byung nas/ yang phur gnyis kyi chos skor dang
/ chos skyong rang gi skor

rnams sbed ma thub pas/ phyis kyi gdung brgyud rnams kyis yang phur gnyis la thugs dam mdzad cing / chos skyong dkar mo nyi zla lcam sring la dus gtor ma chag pa mdzad pa 'di
byung ba yin pas/ des na 'khon sa skya pa'i yab chos yang phur gnyis kyi thun mong ma yin pa'i chos skyong dkar bdud lcam dral phur srung dang bcas pa'i man ngag yongs
su rdzogs pa rje btsun kun dga' snying pos rang gi yab 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po la gsan pa nas bzung / da lta'i bar du rgyun ma chad pa bzhugs pa las/ kho bos kyang 'di'i
rjes gnang sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas sgrub skor gyi man ngag la yang / bzhi thog bla brang gi rgyab kyi nyi zla phug par 'khon rog la chos skyong gis zhal dngos su bstan
nas gnang bar grags pa'i yi ge rnying ma'i skor rnams dang / bdud rgyal gyi rgyud zab mo man ngag dang bcas pa gzhan yang bla ma brgyud pa rnams kyis mdzad pa'i man ngag
gi yi ge gsar rnying

du ma zhig yod pa dag kyang zhib tu thob bo/ /de ltar bstan srung rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag tu gyur pa'i sa skya'i bla chen kun dga' snying po de nyid kyi rnam par thar pa cung
zad brjod na/ gcen 'khon rog shes rab tshul khrims kyis gcung 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po la nga ni rgas 'dug khyod gzhon pa yin pas gsang sngags gsar 'gyur slobs/ de yang
da lta 'brog mi shAkya ye shes mkhas pas der rgyugs gsungs pa la der ma thon/ 'khyin lo tsA ba la kyai rdo rje'i dbang zhus rgyud gsan/ rgyud cung ma rdzogs pa la 'khyin
lo grongs/ chos 'phro 'brog mi'i drung du zhus gsungs pa ltar zhur byon pas/ khyod kyis pha shi nas mes pho bsnyegs pa legs gsungs nas dgyes/ phyis yul zhing 'ga' btsongs
nas rta bcu bdun dang / rtswa rin nor bu'i 'phreng ba dang bcas pa phul/ gsung ngag rin po che zhus/ lam skor cha lag 'ga' re gnang / khyad par rgyud gsum gyi bshad pa
rgyas par gnang nas/ bshad bka' 'dzin pa'i bu

chen lnga'i nang nas mchog tu gyur/ gzhan yang 'gos lo tsA ba la gsang 'dus kyi skor gsan/ u rgyan gyi paNDi ta shes rab gsang ba la thig le lnga'i skor/ rma lo tsA ba la bde
mchog dang grub rnying gi skor la sogs pa gsan/ gzhan yang mal lo tsA ba/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ pu hrangs lo tsA ba/ gnang kha 'ub pa sku mched/ 'khon dge tshul/ skyu ra a
seng la sogs pa bla ma dam pa mang po la sems bskyed dbang bshad man ngag mtha' yas pa gsan nas sngags gsar rnying mtha' dag gi bdag por gyur/ g.ya' lung 'jag gshong du yab
dang gcen gyi phyi rten bzhengs/ de'i nang du seng lding gi phur pa byin rlabs can gcig bzhugs/ bra bo lung par dgon chung gcig btab nas lo 'ga' bzhugs pas ding sang sa
skya gog por grags so/ /de'i tshe dpon slob rnams kyis skyo bsang la byon/ ri kha nas gzigs pas/ dpon po ri glang po che nyal ba

'dra ba'i mkhal khung g.yas pa'i thad na sa dkar zhing snum pa chu g.yas su 'bab pa la sogs pa bkra shis ba'i dge mtshan du ma dang ldan pa gzigs nas 'dir dgon pa gcig btab
na bstan pa dang sems can la phan pa rgya cher 'byung bar dgongs te/ de skor gyi sa cha spyi'i bdag po jo bo gdong nag pa la zhus pas kyang gnang / sgos kyi bdag po zhang
zhung gu ra ba dang ban dhe grong bzhi lha yi grong bdun bya ba yod pa la/ nga 'dir dgon chung gcig byed 'dod pas/ khyed rnams la 'gal ba mi yong na/ khyed rnams la rin
gcig kyang 'jal gsungs pas/ rin ye mi 'tshal cis kyang mdzad par zhu zer/ 'on kyang phyi rabs tshun chad la 'thad gsungs nas/ rgod ma dkar mo gcig nor bu'i 'phreng ba/ mo
gos gcig la sogs pa gnang nas/ mon grog man 'bal grog yan bla ma bdag par byas/ bla ma 'di'i dgung lo bzhi bcu bzhes pa bag yod ces bya ba chu mo glang gi lo/ 'dzam gling
na

nyi zla ltar grags pa mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa'i gang zag bgrang ba las 'das pa 'dus pa'i skyed tshal/ chos dang zang zing gi dpal 'byor 'gran zla dang bral ba'i gnas
dpal sa skya'i gtsug lag khang chen po thog mar btab pa yin no/ /'di nas bzung ste dpal ldan sa skya'i gdung brgyud ces nyi zla ltar grags so/ /de lta bu'i bla ma des dgung
lo bzhi bcu pa nas re dgu'i bar lo sum cu tham pa gdan sa mdzad/ gdul bya dpag med smin grol la bkod nas/ re dgu pa lcags pho rta'i dbyug gu zla ba'i tshes bcu la ngo
mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te sa skya nyid du bde bar gshegs so/ /bla ma de'i jo mo rdo rje phyug mo la sras ye ma byung ba'i ngang nas dgung lo nga dgu bzhes pa'i
dus su/ bla ma gnam kha'u pas thabs legs kyis nyo chang dang zhag sa 'tshol du bcug nas/ mkha' 'gro ma'i rnam rol gu ra ma jo mo zhang mo'i sar zhag gcig bzhugs pas sras
gcig

'khrungs pa ni/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa'i rnam 'phrul sa chen kun dga' snying po yin no/ /'di cung zad mngon du gyur pa na bla ma la zhus pas/ de yongs su re nas thabs
byas pa yin/ da nga rang gis bskyangs nas mthar phyin par byed pas/ kha'u skyed lhas kyi sgrub khang dang nye ba'i dben sar khang chung bzos gsungs/ der gsang stabs su
bzhugs pas chu pho spre'u la 'khrungs/ 'khrungs nas kyang rdo rje phyug mo la gsang ba khong gis tshor nas/ khyed kyi gdung brgyud 'di chad du phangs pa yin/ zhang mo la
sras yod 'dug pa legs/ nga la gsang mi 'tshal/ da nga la nor gzhis mi dgos pa yin zer nas sa skya'i mchod zhing chen mo ma gtogs pa zhing dang nor rdzas thams cad zhang
mo la gtad do/ /de nas dgung lo bcu gcig gi bar la yab kyis legs par bskyangs te/ dbang bshad man ngag phal mo che gnang / bcu gcig pa la yab gshegs/ zhal chems la dgon
pa 'di klu rgyal

gtsug na rin chen gyi pho brang steng na yod pas dpal 'byor phun sum tshogs pa 'byung yang / phyis blo rtsings pa'i skyon 'ongs nyen yod pas/ nga'i phung po ma nyams pa 'di
grog po 'go ltum 'di'i ya snar mchod rten brtsigs la zhog gsungs pa dang mthun par/ rtsis mkhan gyis kyang gshegs rdzong gi chos 'khor dang / gdan sa bsko ba dang / phyi
rten brtsigs pa rnams dus mnyam na grub na dar rgyas phun sum tshogs pa 'byung zhes lung bstan pa bzhin du yum na re/ thog gcig la gdan sa gzhan gcig ma btsal na/ jo sras
kyi slob gnyer la gnod zer nas/ ba ri lo tsA ba g.yu mkhar mo na bzhugs pa gdan drangs nas gdan sar bsko ba dang / 'phrang brag dmar gnyis kyi dge 'dun bsags nas chos 'khor
byed pa/ zhal chems dang mthun pa'i phyi rten bzhengs pa rnams nyin gcig la bsgrubs pas phun tshogs kyi 'gram thams cad things so/ /bla ma 'di la sku che ba'i yon

tan bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ gdung brgyud thams cad kyi nang na 'di nyid mchog tu gyur pas rnam thar rgyas pa gzhan du shes par bya la/ 'dir mdor bsdu na/ rang don dang gzhan
don gyi yon tan no/ /dang po la lung dang rtogs pa'o/ /lung la thun mong ba ni/ gzhon nu nyid nas klog dang yig rtsis/ bzo dang gso dpyad/ lugs kyi bstan bcos sogs la shin
tu mkhas pas kun gyis ya mtshan du 'dzin no/ /thun mong ma yin pa ni/ ba ri lo tsA ba'i zhal nas/ khyed jo sras kyi bya ba slob gnyer byed dgos/ de la shes rab dgos/
de'i lha 'phags pa 'jam dpal yin pas 'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsa na 'di sgrubs gsungs nas rjes gnang mdzad/ 'jam dbyangs brag phug tu sgrub pa zla drug mdzad pas zhal mngon
sum du gzigs nas/ 'jam dbyangs kyi thugs ka nas ral gri bdun brgyud gcig byon thugs kar thim/ de bla ma la zhus pas/ khyed kyi brgyud pa 'di la 'jam dbyangs bdun brgyud

gcig 'byon par 'dug gsungs/ sngon jo bo chen pos kyang sa skya yongs pa'i yul phyogs la phyag mdzad nas/ 'dir 'jam dbyangs kyi sprul pa bdun 'byon par 'dug gsungs pa dang mthun/
