'jam dbyangs grub nas gsan sbyong la mdo'i phyogs ni/ rong ngur smrig gi brang ti dar ma snying po/ de'i zur chos pa bla chen mi dig byang chad pa khyung rnams la sa
sde lnga sdom gnyis la sogs pa chos mngon pa mtha' dag gsan/ nyang stod pa khyung rin chen grags/ grom pa g.yu rtse ba mes lhang tsher la tshad ma rnam nges/ rigs thigs/
chos mchog che chung / dbu ma rang rgyud shar gsum la sogs pa dbu tshad ma lus pa gsan/ gnam kha'u pa la byams chos bslab spyod/ dkon brtsegs/ phal chen la sogs pa spyod
phyogs ma lus pa gsan/ sngags kyi phyogs la/ yab dang 'khor dge chu ba la pha chos yang phur bde dges gsum la sogs pa ma lus pa dang / bla ma

gnam kha'u pa la gsang 'dus lugs gnyis 'grel pa cha lag dang bcas pa sogs dang / bya spyod yo ga'i skor ma lus pa gsan/ mal lo tsA ba la bde mchog gtso bor byas pa'i rgyud
dang man ngag mtha' yas pa gsan/ ba ri lo tsA ba la yang gsang 'dus dang gshin rje gshed skor/ mahA mA ya/ sangs rgyas thod pa/ rdo rje gdan bzhi la sogs pa mtha' yas pa
gsan cing / rgya gar shar nub sogs kyi mchod rten byin rlabs can thams cad kyi sa sna bsdus nas sa skya'i rnam rgyal 'bum par grags pa bzhengs/ sangs rgyas 'od srung gi sku
gdung la sogs pa sku gdung ring bsrel rten gsum byin rlabs can mtha' yas pa bzhugs pas byin rlabs shin tu che bar grags pa 'di/ bla ma ba ri lo tsA bas gtso bor bdag rkyen
mdzad nas bsgrubs te/ sa skya'i gdan sa lo brgyad mdzad nas/ sa chen dgung lo nyi shu'i steng du che 'don bsko bzhag mdzad de/ ba ri ba nyid bar phug tu gshegs so/ /zhang
ston chos 'bar la gsung ngag

rin po che lam skor cha lag dang bcas pa thams cad ma lus pa gsan te/ de ltar na sa chen 'di dang por mdo sngags phyi nang lung rigs kyi gsung rab mtha' dag tshar re gsan pa
tsam gyis mkhyen pas/ ma gsan pa'am mi mkhyen pa gang yang med/ snying rje dang bdag pas gzhan gces pa'i lhag bsam gyis 'brum bus na ba'i nad g.yog mdzad pas legs par gsos
nas rang nyid la 'gos te/ grongs la thug pa'i sdug bsngal dwang du blangs shing / gzhan yang slob gnyer gyi dus na yang bdag pas gzhan gces mang du mdzad/ phyis gzhan
don gyi tshe ni shin tu mang bar mdzad do/ /sbyor ba la bslab pa gsum las tshul khrims kyi bslab pa ni/ so sor thar pa'i dbang du byas na/ bla ma dge chu ba gshegs khar/
kun dga' snying po khyod rab tu byung nas 'khon tsho'i sde pa 'di skyongs shig gsungs pa'i zhal chems byung ba ltar/ rab byung bsnyen rdzogs la thugs shin tu spro yang /
bla ma gnam

kha'u pas bla ma mnyam po la nga gson po'i kha la nyon/ khyod rab tu byung ba bas ma byung na bstan pa la phan gsungs pa'i rkyen gyis rab byung mdzad dbang ma byung na'ang
/ dge bsnyen yongs rdzogs kyi sdom pa shin tu dag cing / tha na dge bsnyen gyi skyabs 'gro'i bslab bya lhan pa ser po la yang mi 'gom/ btsun chung rnams rdo sgor rgyag sar
byon nas/ tshe dang ldan pa bla gos gcig bzhes shig dge bsnyen rgad po phyag gcig 'tshal ba yin no gsungs shing legs par gus pa'i phyag mdzad/ gzhan de lta bu'i mdzad pa
bstan pa'i mnga' bdag bstan 'dzin kun gyi bla mar gyur pa sus kyang tshul de lta bu rmi lam du'ang sgrub par mi nus so/ /de bzhin du byang sems dang / gsang sngags kyi
sdom pa 'khor dang bcas pa la nyes ltung phra mos kyang ma gos pa'i blang dor shin tu bya dka' ba rnams kyang zhib tu mdzad pas tshul khrims kyi bslab pa mchog dang ldan/
lhag par ting nge 'dzin la/ spyir mnyam rjes kun tu zhi gnas

khyad par can gyi nyams dang mi 'bral/ khyad par rim gnyis kyi rnal 'byor mthar son/ yi dam dang bla ma zhi bar gshegs pa kun mnal lam dang mngon sum ci rigs par byon nas chos
gsungs/ the tshom gcod/ yang sgos rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pas rgyud sde bdun cu rtsa gnyis la sogs rgyud lung man ngag mtha' yas pa dngos su 'doms par mdzad do/
/lhag pa shes rab ni/ gsung rab mtha' dag gi tshig dang don la chags thogs cung zad kyang mi mnga' zhing / ma rtogs pa dang log par rtog pa dang the tshom mtha' dag myur
du gcod nus pa'i yang dag pa'i nges pa brtan po dang ldan zhing / chos gsungs pa thams cad kyang thugs nas gsungs/ ji lta ji snyed la gzigs pa rnam par dag nang na rtogs
pa khyad par can mnga' ba ltar/ phyi rol du grub pa'i rtags bstan pa yang / gzhan don mdzad dus nyin gcig la sku lus drug sprul te/ sa skya/ mnga' ris

'char kha/ zangs gdong ru khrod rnams su gdul bya mang po la lam 'bras gsungs pa gsum/ gung thang du bla ma mal gyi drung du dril bu chos skor gsan pa/ shab sgo lngar chos
'khor bskor ba/ 'bring mtshams mgron lha lcam gyi lha khang la rab gnas mdzad pa rnams dus tshod tshes grangs gcig la mdzad/ sku gshegs dus kyang sku'i bkod pa bzhi bstan
te/ gcig bde ba can/ gcig po ta la/ gcig u rgyan/ gcig gser mdog can du gshegs/ spur bzhu dus kun gyis yi dam zhal bzhi par mthong / la las brgyad par mthong ba yang bstan
pa sogs grub rtags bsam gyis mi khyab bo/ /gzhan don la sku dngos kyi gdul bya bla ma dge chu ba la dbang gsan pa'i sta gon gyi mnal lam dang mthun par/ zhang ston mnga'
brnyes chos 'bar gyis gsung ngag mtha' dag rdzogs pa'i mjug tu lung bstan mdzad pa bzhin/ lus ma spangs par phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub thob pa gsum/

bzod pa thob pa bdun/ rtogs pa dang ldan pa brgya phrag mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa mtha' yas pa byung ste/ gsum ni singgha la'i a tsa ra/ byang chub sems dpa' stag sgom
pa kyi 'bar ro/ /bdun ni rje btsun pa/ zhu yas/ dga' ston rdo rje grags/ nags sgom bsod rgyal/ mtshar kha'i rnal 'byor pa/ sgom pa 'od zer grags/ a ce mang chung ma rnams
so/ /phyi rabs kyi gdul bya'i don du brtsams chos kyang rgyud gsum/ bde mchog rtog bdun la sogs pa'i rgyud kyi TIkka nag po gzhung drug la sogs pa'i rgya gzhung gi bshad
pa/ spyir zab chos mang po/ sgos chos skyong gi sgrub skor/ yang sgos lam 'bras kyi gzhung bshad/ khrid yig kyang bcu gcig tsam mdzad de/ thams cad kyang tshig 'dus shing
gsal ba/ don rgyas shing zab pa mkhas pa kun gyi yid 'phrog par mdzad pas

snyan pa'i grags pa yang ding sang bod na dpal ldan birWa pa'i sprul pa zhig gis bstan pa rin po che la bya ba khyad par can byed do zhes rgya gar shar nub tshun chad du grags
so/ /brgyud pa phyi ma rnams la phyag rjes kyi bka' drin yang bla ma 'di rang che bar mkhas pa rnams bzhed de/ de'i rgyu mtshan mal lo tsA ba nas/ rdo rje gdan gyi sgo
srung bse 'bag nag po 'phur shes sogs dang / gnam kha'u pa la zhal bzhi pa legs par zhus te/ rjes 'jug rnams kyang chos skyong 'gran bral du kun gyis 'dzin pa 'di byung
ba'i phyir ro/ /zhes gsungs pa ni shin tu 'thad par mthong ngo / /de lta bu'i bla ma des dgung lo nyi shu pa nas re bdun gyi bar zhe bdun gdan sa mdzad nas/ sa pho stag
gi lo dbyug gu'i bcu bzhi la skya bo kha gdangs su ngo mtshar ba'i ltas dpag med dang bcas te zhi bar gshegs so/ /de lta bu'i bla chen de nyid kyis bstan srung dbang po rnams
kyi chos skor mtha' dag rang gi sras rje btsun

sku mched gnyis la rdzogs par gnang ba'i slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo'i rnam par thar pa mdo tsam bstan pa ni/ de yang rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa'i bstod pa gzhir
byas te cung zad bshad na/ bstod pa 'di la gsum/ mchod par brjod pa/ bstod pa dngos/ mjug gi bya ba'o/ /dang po ni/ khyod ni dam pa rnams kyi rigs 'khrungs nas/ /'gro kun
dga' ba'i dpal gyis nyer 'tsho ba/ /don gyi snying po rnam grol mchog brnyes pa'i/ /blo gros chen po bla ma'i zhabs la 'dud/ /ces pa ste/ bla ma chen po sa skya pa kun
dga' snying po la bstod pa'o/ /gnyis pa bstod pa dngos la gnyis/ rnam thar gyi sgo nas rgyas par bstod pa dang / don bsdu ba'i sgo nas bsdus te bstod pa'o/ /dang po la gnyis/
rnam par thar pa spyir bstan tshul dang khyad par rje btsun rang nyid la bstan tshul lo/ /dang po la gnyis/ skye ba brnyes pa'i

khyad par/ lung rtogs kyi yon tan ji ltar mnga' ba'o/ /dang po ni/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyang mi yi gzugs 'dzin pas/ /sna tshogs thabs kyis dus las mi yol bar/ /rnam mang 'gro
ba'i mgon skyabs du ma mdzad/ /bla ma mchog khyod 'jig rten kun la brtse/ /khyod ni rdo rje gsum las bskyed gyur pas/ /legs byas bsod nams dpag med kyis 'phangs te/ /myang
'das rtse mor phyin pa'i dam pa mchog /rtsod med mkhas pa'i dbang por kun la grags/ /bkra shis dge mtshan dpal gyis mngon mtho ba/ /sa yi mchog gyur sa sogs dkar mdangs
skya/ /cho 'brangs mchog gyur ma rig la 'khon te/ /spang bya'i g.yul las rgyal bar 'khrungs la 'dud/ /ces pa ste/ yab bla chen sa skya pa dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa gcig bzhes
pa chu pho khyi'i lo la dpal ldan sa skya'i chu mig rdzing gar sku bltams pa yin no/ /de'i dus su rdo rje gdan gyi sgo'i ma them la/

'jam dpal gyi sprul pa mkhan po bsod nams rtse mo rdo rje theg pa mtha' dag gi dbang phyug dam pa sa skyar skyes so zer ba mkha' 'gros yi ge bris pa/ kau shambhi'i paNDi ta
de wa ma tis mthong nas phyogs thams cad du bsgrags pa brgyud de bod nyid las rtsad chod do zhes bla ma rje btsun chen pos gsungs/ gnyis pa lung rtogs kyi yon tan ji ltar
mnga' ba la bzhi/ dgung lo bcu bdun man chad kyi rnam par thar pa dang / nyi shu rtsa bdun yan chad kyi rnam par thar pa dang / nyer brgyad man chad kyi rnam par thar pa
dang / khyad par du sa lam ji ltar brnyes pa'i tshul lo/ /dang po ni/ sngon gnas dran zhing byis pa'i spyod pa spangs/ /'dod lhas zhal bstan rgyud sde rgya mtsho yi/ /drang
nges don la blo rgyas bcu bdun tshe/ /ganggA tshun chad yongs su grags la 'dud/ /ces pa ste/ rgya gar du mi thub zla ba la sogs pa'i paNDi ta bcu gcig tu

brgyud nas skye ba bzhes te 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa dran zhing / yum las bltams ma thag saM skr-i ta'i skad gsungs pa dang / bdag ni byis pa'i spyod pa las 'das so zhes lan
gnyis su sbrel nas gsungs shing / dus kun tu skyil mo krung bcas te bzhugs pas thams cad ya mtshan du gyur to/ dgung lo gsum bzhes pa'i tshe/ rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs/
dpal kyai rdo rje/ rje btsun mi g.yo ba rnams kyis zhal dngos su gzigs shing / rgyud gsum/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kun las btus dang lnga thugs la gsungs so/ /gnyis pa nyer
bdun pa yan chad kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ bla chen 'dod lha kun la chos rnams nod/ /dbus gtsang mkhas rnams bsten nas sbyangs tshul bstan/ /bstan pa'i srog shing chen por
rtsa bdun la/ /'dzam gling yongs su grags pa khyod la 'dud/ /ces pa ste/ thog mar yab la rdo rje theg pas bsdus pa'i rgyud 'grel/ sgrub dkyil/ dbang byin rlabs/

gdam ngag phyag bzhes/ khrid bka' lung bka' dang bcas pa legs par gsan nas ma lus pa khong du chug par mdzad de/ dgung lo bcu bdun la nye ba'i tshe/ rgyud sde bcu bzhi thugs
la gsungs shing / ganggA tshun chad la rdo rje theg pa mtha' dag la mkhas par yongs su grags so/ /de nas dgung lo bcu bdun bzhes pa'i tshe/ bla chen kun dga' snying po
mya ngan las 'das pa'i rjes kyi bya ba rnams grub nas/ rje pa dgung lo bcu gsum pa la/ ngas dbus su phyin la phar phyin dang tshad ma la sogs pa mnyan la 'ong / khyod sa
skyar sdod la bshad pa gyis gsungs te gdan sa gtad nas/ gsang phu ne'u thog tu cha pa chen po chos kyi seng ge la chos gsan pa la snga phyir lo bcu gcig tsam gyi bar du bzhugs
nas mkhas pa chen por gyur te/ gser gyi gandzi ra dang / yum rgyas pa dang gzhan yang zang zing gi dngos po mang du phul

te mnyes par byas/ slob dpon cha pa'i slob ma che bar grags pa/ seng chen brgyad/ seng 'dra brgyad/ jo sras bzhi zhes bya ba la sogs pa yod pa la/ jo sras bzhi ni/ 'khon jo
sras rtse mo/ khu jo sras ne tso/ rngog jo sras ra mo/ gnyos jo sras 'od ma dang bzhi zhes grags pa'i nang nas mchog tu gyur pa 'khon jo sras rtse mo zhes yongs su grags
so/ /de nas dgung lo nyer drug bzhes pa'i tshe/ me mo phag gi lo la na la rtse gnas po che'i gtsug lag khang du chos la 'jug pa'i sgo zhes bya ba'i bstan bcos chen po mdzad
de/ de'i nang du bstan pa'i rtsis kyi rnam par gzhag pa skyon thams cad dang bral ba yang mdzad yod do/ /de ltar thos pa mthar phyin pas dgung lo nyi shu rtsa bdun bzhes
pa'i tshe/ 'dzam bu'i gling gi bstan pa'i srog shing chen po yin no zhes yongs su grags so/ /gsum pa nyer brgyad yan chad kyi rnam par thar pa la bzhi/ rnam

'phrul mchog bstan pa/ mkhyen pa rnam par dag pa/ spang bya'i dri ma dang bral ba/ don gnyis kyi mdzad pa phun tshogs so/ /dang po ni/ dus gcig gsung ngag ston tshe nam mkha'
la/ /mchod sogs dbus na 'jam dpal birWa pa/ /spyan ras gzigs dbang mthong snang gsum bstan nas/ /bcu dgu dag pa'i snang bar bsgyur la 'dud/ /ces pa ste/ dgung lo nyi shu
rtsa brgyad bzhes pa'i tshe gzim khang rnying mar lam 'bras gsungs pa'i lta ba'i skabs su/ tshes gcig gi nyin bar/ bla ma la slob ma rnams kyis mthong snang mi 'dra ba
gsum byung ste/ nam mkhar mchod sprin bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dbus na/ rje btsun rin po che la 'jam dpal/ jo sras lcags kyi rdo rje la birWa pa/ gnyan dang / rmog ston gtsug
tor dbon po sogs chos nyan pa phal che ba la spyan ras gzigs su snang bas ting nge 'dzin khyad par can skyes so/ /gnyis

pa mkhyen pa rnam par dag pa la gnyis/ thun mong gi thabs kyi mkhyen pa rnam par dag pa dang / thun mong ma yin pa'i thabs kyi mkhyen pa rnam par dag pa'o/ /dang po ni/ sgra
tshad pha rol phyin dang gsang sngags sogs/ /gzigs pa tsam gyis tshig dang don bcas pa/ /legs dgongs gzhan la phan pa lhur len pa'i/ /mkhyen pa'i spyan ras gsal ba khyod
la 'dud/ /ces so/ /gnyis pa thun mong ma yin pa'i thabs kyi mkhyen pa rnam par dag pa ni/ mnal tshe 'od gsal dag gi mnyam par 'jog /mthu stobs dbang phyug yi dam gang rung
la/ /nyin mtshan gang yang the tshom gcod mdzad pas/ /rig pa'i gnas lnga mtha' ru phyin la 'dud/ /ces so/ /gsum pa spang bya'i dri ma dang bral ba ni/ gang gi kun spyod
nyes pa'i dri ma bral/ /log smra mthar spangs bden don gsungs pa po/ /spros pa med thugs stong nyid snying po can/ /sa gsum snyan par grags pa

khyod la 'dud/ /ces pa ste/ sku'i kun spyod nyes pa'i dri ma dang bral/ gsung gi brjod pa log smra'i dri ma dang bral/ thugs kyi rang bzhin spros pa'i dri ma dang bral te/
sku legs par spyod pa dang ldan/ gsung bden don gsung ba dang ldan/ thugs stong nyid snying rje'i snying po can dang ldan pa yin no/ /zhes bya ba'i don to/ /bzhi pa don gnyis
kyi mdzad pa phun sum tshogs pa ni/ g.yengs pa med par 'chad rtsod rtsom pa dang / /rim gnyis rnal 'byor rgyun chad med pa yis/ /rjes thob sgyu mar gzigs nas sems can
la/ /sbyin pa rnam bzhis tshim mdzad khyod la 'dud/ /ces so/ /bzhi pa khyad par du sa lam ji ltar brnyes pa'i tshul ni/ po ta la dang dpal ri u rgyan sogs/ /nyin phyed
tsam gyis legs 'khor mkha' 'gro dang / /dpa' bo'i tshogs dang spyod pa'i brtul zhugs spyad/ /rnam 'phrul du mas nye gnas yid rang 'dud/ /ces

pa ste/ po ta la la sogs pa'i gnas chen rnams su bstan srung dbang po rnams dang / dpa' bo dang rnal 'byor ma'i tshogs dpag tu med pa dang lhan cig rgyud sde nas ji ltar bshad
pa'i kun 'dar dang kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa tshul bzhin du spyod pa'i rnam 'phrul du mas nye ba'i gnas thob pa khyod la shin tu yid rang ba'i sgo nas 'dud do zhes bya
ba'i don to/ /de la nye ba'i gnas zhes bya ba ni brda'i skad yin la/ thun mong du grags pa'i ming gis bstan na/ sa gnyis pa dri ma med pa mngon du mdzad do zhes bya ba
yin no/ /'o na sa chen gyi slob ma mchog thob pa'i nang du bgrang par rigs shing / de lta na mchog thob pa'i slob ma bzhir 'gyur ro zhe na/ de la mchog thob pa'i slob ma
gsum 'byung zhes pa ni/ gsum nges par 'byung ba'i don yin gyi/ gzhan bkag pa med la/ 'dir ni bstod pa de nyid las/ rdo rje 'chang dang 'jam mgon dbyer med pa/ /zhes sogs
shlau ka gcig po de'i don bla chen dang

slob dpon nyid tha dad pa med par bstan pas der bsdus te logs su ma bgrangs pa yin no/ /gnyis pa khyad par du rje btsun rang nyid la bstan tshul ni/ dbang dus dkyil 'khor gtso
dang dbyer med pas/ /zab mo'i don gsungs gnas dang mkha' kun la/ /'od dang 'od zer rol mo'i sgra bsgrags nas/ /bdag yid ting 'dzin sgo mang 'byed la 'dud/ /ces pa ste/
dbang gi dus su 'od zer gyi snang ba dpag tu med pa 'phro zhing / lha'i rol mo'i sgra dbyangs bsam gyis mi khyab pa sogs mchod pa'i sprin gzhal gyis mi lang ba dang bcas
pa'i dbus na bzhugs pa'i sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor mngon sum du bstan te/ dkyil 'khor de nyid du dbang bskur cing zab mo'i don bstan nas/ ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo bsam gyis
mi khyab pa 'byed par mdzad do/ /gzhan yang / rdo rje 'chang dang 'jam mgon dbyer med pa/ /bla ma mchog dang dam pa khyod nyid la/ /khyad par 'ga'

yang bdag gis yod ma shes/ /de slad byang chub bar du bdag skyabs mchi/ /khyod kyi yon tan dpag yas sangs rgyas dang / /byang sems chen po rnams dang dbyer med pas/ /bdag 'dras
bskal par brjod par ga la lang / /de ltar de 'dra'i skyes chen khyed la 'dud/ /chung ngu'i dus na khyed kyi thugs rjes bskyangs/ /rmad byung zab mo'i lam rnams rjes
su bstan/ /'di dang phyi mar phan bde'i sa la bkod/ /tshad med bka' drin yang yang dran par gyur/ /gnyen gyis 'brel bas khyed la dad min te/ /nges par sangs rgyas yin pa'i
nges shes kyis/ /khyed la cung zad bstod pa 'di bgyis pas/ /dge bas bla ma'i zhabs drung skye bar shog /kye ma bla ma bzhugs pa'i zhabs drung du/ /chos kyi bka' drin nod
pa'i skal bas dben/ /skyabs med bdag la thugs rje chen po yis/ /yang dag rtogs pa'i blo gros bskyed du gsol/ /zhes pa bstod pa'i rgyu mtshan dge ba bsngo ba dang bcas te
rgyas par bstod pa

bstan zin to/ /gnyis pa don bsdu ba'i sgo nas bsdus te ston pa ni/ yang smras pa/ tshangs par spyod pa'i dge bsnyen tshul 'dzin zhing / /bsod nams dpag med ldan pa'i dbang
phyug gis/ /shes bya ma lus gzigs pa'i rtse mor phyin/ /bla chen smra ba'i dpal la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes pa la/ sku gzhon nu'i dus nyid du byang chub sems dpa' chen po zla
ba rgyal mtshan la tshangs spyod kyi dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa blangs te/ rab tu byung ba las kyang btsun par mdzad pa yin no/ /g.yo med phyag rgya che la rol ba'i thugs/
/mdo rgyud man ngag char rgyun mi 'chad gsungs/ /'dzum mdzes mdangs gsal ldan pa'i sku mnga' ba/ /'gro ba'i skyabs gcig bla ma'i zhabs la 'dud/ /rgya chen chos kyi sgo rnams
mkhyen pa'i mthus/ /shes ldan slob ma'i sgo gsum tshim par mdzad/ /mkhas pas mkhas pa rtsod par mi bzod kyang / /dregs pa'i nyes

pa bral ba khyod la 'dud/ /dam pa'i gnas su chu pho khyi lo la/ /sku bltams zhing 'dir don mdzad zhe gcig pa/ /chu pho stag gi smal po bcu gcig nyin/ /bde ba can du gshegs
la mgos phyag 'tshal/ /zhes pa la/ de lta bu'i yon tan gyi tshogs tshad med pa dang ldan pa'i rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug 'dis dgung lo bzhi bcu zhe gcig bzhes kyi bar du
sbyin pa rnam pa bzhis sems can bgrangs pa las 'das pa tshim par mdzad nas/ rang rang gi skal ba dang 'tshams par smin grol gyi lam la bkod de chu pho stag gi lo smal po
zla ba'i tshes bcu gcig la chu mig 'ga' zhig la'ang sgo rum dpe khang du gshegs zhes kyang 'byung ngo / /rdzing kha'i bla brang du mya ngan las 'das te/ bde ba can gyi 'jig
rten gyi khams su mngon par gshegs par gyur to/ /de'i tshe bla ma rje btsun chen po dgung lo sum cu rtsa drug bzhes pa yin la/ chos kyi rje sa skya paNDi ta bltams nas
zla ba ngo bcu bzhes pa'i dus yin no/ /

gsum pa mjug gi bya ba ni/ 'jig rten kun gyi mig gcig bla ma la/ /cung zad bstod 'di dpal ldan sa skya ru/ /dge bsnyen grags pa rgyal mtshan bdag gis bgyis/ /dge bas 'gro kun
byang chub myur thob shog /ces pas bstan pa yin la/ de ltar mkha' 'gro chos skyong rnams bran du bkol nas po ta la dang / dpal ri/ u rgyan sogs nyul ba'i grub pa'i sa
la bzhugs pa'i slob dpon rin po che de nyid kyi gcung rje btsun rin po che ni/ yab sa skya pa chen po dgung lo nga dgu pa me mo yos kyi lo bltams shing / 'di'i rnam par thar
pa cung zad brjod na/ dad pa dang / tshul khrims dang / thos pa dang / gtong ba dang / shes rab phun sum tshogs pa rnams kyis shes par bya ste/ de yang dang por dkar
chos mtha' dag gi rtsa ba dad pa phun sum tshogs pa ni/ spyir bla ma dang dkon mchog la shin

tu mos pas sku tshe ril po bla ma rnams kyi ched du rten gsum khyad par can bzhengs pa dang / dus mchod 'dzugs pa dang / mchod pa 'bul ba dang / tha na rten gyi drung du mchod
pa gshom pa tshun chad la rtsal du 'don zhing / khyad par bla ma yab sras la rdo rje 'chang gi 'du shes khor yug tu mdzad nas/ zhal bzhugs pa'i ring la'ang bka' gang
gnang sgrub pa'i sgo nas legs par mnyes par byed/ sku'i rgyab mi ston/ ku re'i phyir yang bka' mi zlog mi mnyes pa cung zad kyang mi sgrub/ zhi bar gshegs nas kyang gsol
ba rgyun mi chad du 'debs pas sku'i snang ba dang mi 'bral/ gsung rab la the tshom gang byung thams cad maNDal phul nas bla ma yab sras kho na la gsol ba 'debs/ mdor na dge
legs thams cad kyi rtsa ba bshes gnyen bsten tshul la bod du 'di las lhag pa ma byung bar grags so/ /tshul khrims phun sum tshogs pa ni/ dgung lo brgyad pa la byang sems
zla rgyal

gyi drung du tshangs spyod dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa legs par nod de/ rten skya bor bzhugs pa tsam ma gtogs/ sha chang sgong gsum zhal la mi reg dge slong khyad par can gyi lugs
nyam dang mi 'bral/ sku 'khor gyi gtso bo yang rab byung la mdzad/ khyed rnams kyis gso sbyongs ma chag pa gyis/ ja ngas 'dren gsungs nas rab byung 'ba' zhig la dgyes/
mdor na sdom gsum legs par nod nas nyes ltung phra mos kyang ma gos pa mdzad do/ /thos pa phun sum tshogs pa ni/ gzhon nu nyid nas klog dang yig rtsis sogs tshegs chung
ngus mkhyen zhing / yab dang gcen la dbang bshad man ngag ma lus par gsan/ khyad par dgung lo bcu gnyis pa la sdom pa nyi shu pa dang / sgrub thabs mtsho skyes thugs las
gsungs/ bcu gsum pa la rgyud gsum gyi po ti zhal du gsol ba'i mnal lam byung ba bzhin du tshig don mtha' dag thugs la chud de/ yab gshegs pa'i chos

'khor la tshogs su gsungs pas thams cad ngo mtshar du gyur te/ blo gros chen por mtshan gsol/ mdor na bla chen yab sras/ gnyan gtsug tor rgyal po/ gnyan dbang rgyal/ zhang
btsun tshul grags/ bal po'i paNDi ta dza ya se na/ lo tsA ba dar ma yon tan/ sum pa lo tsA ba dang dpal mchog dang po'i rdo rje la sogs pa la/ rgya gar nas 'gyur ba'i mdo
bstan bcos/ rgyud man ngag mtha' yas pa zhig gsan cing legs par sbyangs/ ma gsan pa 'ga' re yang gzigs rtogs legs par mdzad de/ nga thos rgya can min yang mthong rgya can
yin/ ngas dge slong gcig 'grub tu re nas 'dul ba lung 'di yun ring por blta ba ma grub/ dge slong mi grub par shes nas legs par bltas zhes gsungs/ mdor na ma gzigs pa'am
mi mkhyen pa'i chos cung zad kyang med pas/ thos pas mi ngoms nyid dang ni/ /zhes pa'i sa gsum pa'i yongs sbyongs rdzogs par mdzad do/ /gtong ba phun sum tshogs

pa ni/ dge 'dun mang du bsags pa'i chos 'khor lan gsum mdzad/ rgyun ldan du dge 'dun brgya phrag tsam gyi 'tsho ba sbyor/ dbu rtse rnying mar grags pa'i gtsug lag khang / yab
kyi nang rten bkra shis sgo mangs/ mes kyi nang rten gser 'bum chen mo/ gcen dang gcung gi nang rten gser sku chen mo re re/ de dag gi drung du dkar me mtshan thub brgya
rtsa chag med kyi rgyun/ gzhan yang chen po la 'os pa'i bla re yol ba/ 'phan gdugs rgyal mtshan/ dril bu'i gdang ring / gser gyis mdo mangs dang rgyud 'bum la sogs pa'i
bka' 'gyur phal cher gsar du bzhengs/ gzhan gyis phul ba'i 'bum cha sum brgya tsam byung ba'i steng nas brgya phrag gcig gtsug lag khang der bzhugs su gsol nas/ nyis brgya
dge 'dun gyi sde so sor bstan pa'i rgyun la phul/ mdor na chos dang zang zing gi dpal 'byor gang la'ang 'dzin

chags cung zad kyang mi 'dzin par sbyin gtong kho na la dgyes pa 'dra ba sku gshegs kar na bza' phrugs gcig las ma lus par grags so/ /khyad par chos kyi sbyin pa la mchog tu
dgyes pas gang zhus de ma thag thugs nas gsung ba ma gtogs/ phyis bya gsung ba mi srid/ dus nam yang 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum kho nas dus 'da' bar mdzad do/ /shes rab phun
sum tshogs pa ni/ gang gzigs pa thams cad kyi tshig don la chags thogs cung zad kyang mi mnga' bar so sor rtogs pa'i shes rab kyis legs par dpyad nas ma gtogs/ log rtog
dang the tshom gyi dri ma cung zad kyang med par thugs su chud pas/ chos rje pas/ shes bya thams cad gzigs pa'i spyan yangs pa/ /zhes bstod pa mdzad cing 'jam dbyangs dngos
su gzigs so/ /de ltar rang gis mkhyen cing gzigs pa thams cad gcung dang / chos rje pa dang / dga' ston sogs grags pa'i mtha' can rnams la sogs pa dngos kyi gdul

bya rnams la nyin mtshan kun tu zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos 'khor bskor cing / dngos brgyud mtha' dag gi ched du legs bshad mtha' yas pa brtsams te/ mdor na bla ma'i mos
gus thugs dam thos bsam/ gzhan phan lhag bsam rnams nyin bar shugs shin tu che bas/ mtshan mo mnal lam du yang mtshan brjod la sogs pa'i zhal 'don thugs dam mang po dang
/ gzigs rtog dang rtog dpyod mtha' yas pa 'byung zhing / sa chen gyi thugs ka nas bla ma 'khor bcas/ kyai rdor gyi dkyil 'khor ston pa shAkya thub pa 'khor bcas sprul nas/
khyod dbang zhu na su la zhu/ rab byung len na su la len 'doms shig ces gsungs pa la/ de thams cad bla ma rje btsun khyed rang nyid la zhu ba lags/ zhes zhus pas dgyes
nas dbugs dbyung / khyad par chos thams cad gnad bsdus pa'i tshigs bcad gnang / lha rnams kyis bde ba can dang mkha'

spyod du 'byon par bskul ba na/ bdag la ltos pa'i 'gro ba mang du yod pas mi 'gro zhus pa dang / gzhan yang srid pa'i rgya mtsho las 'gro ba mang po sgrol ba'i mtshan ltas
la sogs pa mnal lam gyi rnam par thar pa yang bsam gyis mi khyab pa la sogs pa rnam par dkar ba'i mdzad 'phrin mtha' yas pa'i ngang nas dgung lo bdun cu pa me pho byi ba'i
dbo zla'i tshes bcu gnyis la kho bo 'di nas bde ba can dang / de nas gser mdog can du 'khor los bsgyur ba'i cha byad kyis zhing sbyongs/ lus gsum pa la lus de nyid kyis
phyag rgya chen po 'grub bo zhes gsungs nas gshegs so/ /bla ma 'di nyid 'khrungs pa'i sa yang sgo rum ye shes mgon po bzhugs pa'i mgon khang gi mdor 'khrungs shing / gshegs
pa yang de nyid du mdzad pas/ thog mar skye sa'i sa der mya ngan las 'da' mkhan kho bo tsam yin zhes kyang gsungs par grags/ de lta bu'i gangs khrod kyi rdo rje 'dzin
pa kun gyi gtsug rgyan/ dpa' bo

mkha' 'gro dam can srung ma/ lha klu gnod sbyin sogs gzugs med thams cad bran bzhin du 'khol ba'i mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug rje btsun chen po de nyid kyi drung du/ sa skya
pa'i chos skyong rnams kyi man ngag gi chos skor yongs su rdzogs pa chos rje sa paN nyid kyis gsan pa yin te/ 'di'i rnam thar bsdus te brjod na/ de yang mkhyen brtse 'phrin
las gsum gyi sgo nas rtogs par bya ste/ mkhyen pa la rang gis sbyangs pa dang / gzhan la bstan pa'o/ /dang po ni/ klu'i rgyal pos yum la gnas khang g.yar ba'i tshul gyis
bsam bzhin du mngal bzung nas/ dge byed ces bya ba chu pho stag gi khra zla'i nyi shu drug la yum gyi lus sems bde ba'i nyams dang ldan par sku bltams te/ gog thub pa'i
dus saM skr-i ta'i skad gsungs shing / rgya yig mang po bris nas bklags nas mi 'gom par bsubs pa dang / gzhon nu nyid nas klog yig bzo gso ba skad gnyis kyi rnam grangs
la sogs

pa tshegs chung ngus mkhyen/ rje btsun chen po la dbang bshad rgyud man ngag rgyun ma chad pa gsan te/ dgung lo brgyad pa la mtsho skyes/ bcu pa la brtag gnyis/ bcu gcig pa
la gur sam thugs las gsungs pas kun gyis ya mtshan du 'dzin/ mdor na bco lnga pa la rje btsun chen pos bum pa gang byo'i tshul du thugs su chud/ bco brgyad pa la a phyi
'bum pa'i drung du slob dpon dbyig gnyen la mdzod tshar gcig mnal lam du gsan pas thugs su chud cing / phyogs kyi glang po'i phug pa yin zer ba zhig tshad ma'i dpe chas bkang
ba'i lde mig gtad pa rmis/ bcu dgu pa la don mo ri ba zhu ston rdo rje skyabs la byams chos rtsa 'grel dang dbu ma mang du gsan/ nyi shu pa la nyang stod rkyang 'dur
du 'tshur ston gzhon nu seng ge la tshad ma rnam nges la sogs pa'i dbu tshad mang du gsan/ de'i bar skabs la sa skyar yab gshegs nas byon dgongs rdzogs bsgrubs/ sku skal
yang phul/ der rjes

bshad gsar dang bstun nas snga chos phyi chos mdzad de/ rnam nges zla gcig la shin tu rgyas par thugs nas bshad pas kun ya mtshan du 'dzin par gyur/ de nas khro phur kha che
paN chen phebs pa'i drung du byon/ chos mchog rgya skad du gsungs pa la bod dpe bkram nas gsan cing rgya skad du bskyar bas/ paN chen shin tu dgyes nas khong dpon slob
rnams kyis paNDi ta chen por mtshan gsol te rjes su bzung / tshad ma sde bdun mdo dang bcas pa dang / rgyan chos mchog lha shAka la sogs pa'i 'grel pa 'grel bshad/ de bzhin
du mngon pa/ 'dul ba/ sngags kyi bde mchog gsang 'dus/ khyad par dus 'khor cha lag sems 'grel gsum la sogs pa gsan/ paN chung dA na shi la la yang gtso bor tshad ma rnam
'grel/ gshin rje gshed skor la sogs pa gsan/ bal po sa~M gha shrI la sgra ka tsan/ snyan ngag sdeb sbyor/ mngon brjod zlos gar la

sogs gsan/ spyi lhas pa byang chub 'od dang / rtsis pa dbang phyug seng ge la yang byams chos/ dbu ma/ bslab spyod la sogs pa dang / khyad par spyi lhas pa la man ngag zhi
byed/ rdzogs chen/ rim lnga/ nA ro nai gu la sogs pa bod na yod tshad gsan te/ lan re zung re tsam gyis rdzogs par thugs su chud do/ /dgung lo nyer bdun pa la/ paN chen gyis
mkhan po/ spyi lhas pas las slob/ zhu ston rdo rje skyabs kyis gsang ston byas nas dge 'dun grangs dang mtshan nyid tshang ba'i dbus su/ nyang smad rgyan gong gi gtsug
lag khang du rab byung bsnyen rdzogs mdzad do/ /'khon sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud kyi nang na ngur smrig gi rgyal mtshan 'chang ba'i gtsug rgyan mdzad de/ gangs can pa thams
cad rab tu byung ba la/ ches gtso bor gus par bya ba'i rgyun gyi gtso bor 'di 'dzin to/ /de ltar tshangs par spyod pa mtha' dag gi gtso bo dge slong gi sdom pa bzhes
te/ so thar

yongs su rdzogs pa'i steng du byang sems dang gsang sngags te sdom gsum rdzogs pa'i tshul khrims kyi phung po 'chal tshul gyi dri ma mtha' dag dang bral bas 'dzam gling byang
gi phyogs na tshul khrims bsrung ba mtha' dag gi mchog tu gyur to/ /de ltar rang gi mkhyen pa yongs su rdzogs nas gzhan la ston pa ni/ mkhas pa'i bya ba 'chad rtsod rtsom
gsum gyi sgo nas yin pas/ 'chad pa ni rnam bshad rig pa sogs nas ji ltar 'byung ba'i tshul gyi yon tan mtha' dag rdzogs nas gsung rab gang 'chad kyang gang nas bshad
kyang 'brel/ ji tsam bshad kyang ran/ ji ltar bshad kyang 'thad pa'i tshul gyis rna bar snyan cing 'jebs pa dang / yid la 'thad cing 'phrod/ tshig gzung sla zhing don rtogs
par yang sla bas dngos kyi gdul bya thams cad mkhas pa'i go 'phang la myur du bkod de/ bshad pa'i bka' bab pa 'u

yug rigs pa'i seng ge dang / zhang btsun mdo sde dpal dang / shar pa shes 'byung sogs te/ mdor na khang gnyan zhang gsum/ shar nub gung gsum la sogs pa dang / man ngag gi bka'
bab pa dmar ston chos kyi rgyal po dang / lho pa kun mkhyen dpal la sogs pa dang / rtogs pa'i bka' bab pa tshogs sgom/ nyan chen/ grub thob yon tan dpal la sogs te/ mdor
na mkhas grub kyi bu chen bgrang ba las 'das pa bshad sgrub la bkod do/ /rtsom pa ni/ sgra dang snyan ngag dang ming gi mngon brjod la sogs pa'i bstan bcos du ma dang
/ rig pa'i phyogs la sde bdun mdo dang bcas pa'i don rdzogs par ston pa rigs gter rtsa 'grel/ lung gi phyogs la mdo sde rgyan gyi don 'grel du byas nas chos mtha' dag 'dus
pa thub pa dgongs gsal la sogs te/ mdor na mdo sngags lung rigs thams cad kyi tshig don nyung ngus 'dus pa mkhas pa'i yid 'phrog cing /

blun pos go sla ba'i brtsams chos mang pos dngos dang brgyud pa'i gdul bya thams cad mkhas pa'i go 'phang la myur du 'god par mdzad do/ /rtsod pa ni/ spyir sde bdun mdo dang
bcas pa'i dngos stobs kyi rigs pa mtha' dag legs par thugs su chud pas/ bod rgan po'i rtog ge pa mtha' dag rang blos sbyar ba'i skyon can du gzigs pas/ bod snga ma'i grub
mtha' la dgag pa legs par mdzad pa rnams kun gyis mi bzod/ khyad par de dus kyi 'chad nyan smar shos gnyal zhig 'jam pa'i rdo rje dpon slob yin pas/ shin tu ma bzod nas
bu dgu'i rigs pa bzang shos 'u yug pa rig pa'i seng ge yin pa/ chos rje la rtsod du btang nas/ chos grwar zhag shas bsdad nas 'gal du bsgugs pas ma rnyed cing / rtsod par
cung zad kyang ma nus kyi steng nas mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob ste zhabs pad yun ring du bsten pas bu chen du gyur pa lta bu dang / gtsang nags phug pas 'jam dbyangs dang
zhal mjal

'phro la/ chos rje la skur ba btab pas yun ring du ma mjal gsol ba drag tu btab pas/ khyod kyis nga la 'thab pa yin gsungs nas/ dang po mjal nas rtsod pa byed 'dod pa/ de nas
dad pa lhag par tshud de gdan drangs/ zla sbrel du chos zhus/ sku 'dra thugs ka na drod yod par grags pa da lta sgo rum na bzhugs pa 'di legs par bzhengs nas phyag nas
zhus te rtse gcig tu gsol ba 'debs pa lta bu dang / mkhas pa su zhig yin kyang sku mjal ma thag tu nga rgyal zhi bar 'gyur/ khyad par mu stegs kyi ston pa shin tu mkhas
shing nga rgyal gyis dregs pa 'phrog byed dga' bo la sogs pa drug gis/ rigs gter bod skad las rgya gar du bsgyur te rdo rje gdan du phebs pa'i mchod brjod kyi tshig la ma
bzod pas rkyen byas nas rtsod du yong pas/ paN chen shAkya shrIs dus tshes bsgrigs/ mnga' bdag rgyal pos dpang mdzad/ gang rgyal ba'i bstan pa la 'jug par byas te/ chos

rje nyid kyis skyid grong du byon nas dri ma med pa'i rigs pas pham par mdzad de/ bstan pa'i sgor bcug pas 'phags pa'i yul na'ang 'jam dbyangs dngos su grags so/ /de dag ni
mkhyen pa'i yon tan yin la/ brtse ba'i thugs rje ni hor gyi rgyal pos bod kyi ngo lta ma 'jags pa'i skabs su dmag dpung mang po brdzangs te/ mthong tshad sod cig thos tshad
'dar bar 'gyur ro zhes pa'i lung bud pa rim gyis lag len la bkal ba'i gtam thos pas/ bod 'bangs thams cad sems khong du chud pa'i skabs su/ thugs rje chen po 'khrungs
te/ dkon mchog la gsol ba btab pas/ dgung lo bgres po re gcig tu phebs pa na hor gyi rgyal pos gdan 'dren byung ba na/ bod 'bangs thugs kyi dkyil du bcug pa'i brtse ba chen
po dang / rje btsun chen pos lung bstan yod pa bka' bzhin sgrub pa'i mos gus chen pos kun nas blangs te/ sku

srog yal bar dor ba lta bu'i sku nyen dang dka' spyad khyad du bsad nas/ re gsum pa la bteg nas lo gsum gyi bar la lam gyi gdul bya'i don mdzad de/ hor gyi yul byang phyogs
rgyal po'i sar byon te/ bod 'bangs bde ba la bkod/ skad rigs mi gcig pa'i rgyal khams du ma sangs rgyas kyi bstan pas khyab cing 'phral phugs kyi phan bde la bkod de/ bka'
bzhin bsgrubs pa mi slu ba yang / dpon chen shAkya bzang pos/ chos rje pa'i gsung bzhin gdan sa chen po'i khur rnams dka' ba dang du blangs/ lha khang chen mo bzhengs
pa sogs don la bla ma'i zhabs tog kho na yin kyang / rnam pa dge sdig 'dres ma lta bu'i bya ba rlabs chen mang du mdzad pas dpon chen pa gshegs dus/ 'bri khung 'jig rten
mgon po'i gsung gis shAkya bzang po 'das yod par 'dug sdig can de ci 'dra zhig tu skye blta dgos gsungs 'od gsal gyi ngang nas gzigs pas/ chos rje sa paN nam mkha'i mthongs
su

byon nas/ na bza' ber zhig gsol ba'i phu dung nar te brkyangs nas/ shAkya bzang po 'di la 'jus la shog gsungs nas nam mkha' la drangs song ba gzigs pas/ 'bri khung pa'i gsung
las/ dpon chen khong bla dpon bzang po des drangs te song zhes gsungs par grags shing / 'phrin las ni/ gtso bor ji skad bshad pa de dag dang / rje btsun chen po'i nang
rten du 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba bzhengs pa sogs sku gsung thugs kyi rten dang / gtsug lag khang dang dge 'dun gyi sde gsar du 'dzugs pa dang / rnying pa gso ba dang
/ chos sde mang po'i zhal bdag mdzad de/ gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skya dang / byang phyogs ling chu rtser khab/ bar pa bsam yas/ nyang stod rkyang 'dur/ shangs sreg
shing / chu ba khams gtsang dbus gsum na shin tu mang ba'i bdag gnyer mdzad nas spyir rig gnas mtha' dag dang / khyad par rnam 'grel/ 'dul mngon/ phar phyin/

dbu ma sogs dang / bde kyai gsang gsum yo ga bya spyod sogs mdo sngags zung 'brel gyi bshad srol ding sang gi bar du yod pa ni bdag nyid chen po 'di kho na'i 'phrin las kyi
rgyun no/ /khyad par rgyas pa'i bstan bcos tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi grwa pa byang ngam ring / dbus rtse thang / na lendra/ skyid tshal gong 'og gser mdog can/ thub bstan
gong 'og gnyis/ mnyan yod bya gshong sogs dang / de dag las mched pa'i dpal ldan sa skya'i thub bstan lha chen sogs chos grwa mang po shin tu dar rgyas su gyur/ hor yul la
'byon pa'i tshe sa skyar mtshan nyid kyi tshogs dpon 'u yug pa rig seng / sngags kyi tshogs dpon zhang btsun mdo sde dpal/ spyi mchod nye gnas su dge bshes shAkya bzang
po bskos nas byon rjes/ rigs chen pa rang la cha brgyad cu byung bar grags pa lta bu bstan pa'i rgyun la phan pa'i 'phrin las ni bla ma 'di kho na che'o/ /rtsod dus kyi
gdul bya nyams dma' ba'i

skabs su 'phrin las rnam dag gi rgyun tshugs pa rnam thar gyi gtso bo yin gyi/ nyid kyis lha dang bla ma mang po gzigs pa sogs ni byis pa mtshar bskyed du zad do/ /de ltar
dgung lo so drug pa nas/ bdun cu'i bar so lnga gdan sa mdzad nas lcags mo phag gi smal po zla ba'i tshes bcu bzhi la brjod kyis mi lang pa'i ltas du ma dang bcas te/ byang
phyogs sprul pa sde'i gzim khang du bde bar gshegs so/ /bdag nyid chen po 'di chos skyong la mnga' brnyes pas/ rgyun du bse mgon dang gsung gleng mdzad cing / lan gcig
gur gyi mgon po sku nam mkha'i khyon gang ba/ na bza' ber dang phod ka brtsegs mar gsol zhing / gri thod gaNDe thugs kar bsnams pa/ zhal gdong g.yas phyogs su bsgyur nas
thur du mnan te ljags chen po bsgril ba/ zhabs gnyis zlum po'i stabs kyis bzhugs pa zhig mngon sum du gzigs/ lhag par hor yul la 'byon

khar sgo rum du chos skyong la bka' bsgos shing mchod gtor 'bul ba mdzad pa na/ 'cham mgon gyi zhal nas/ nga yang khyed kyi phyi la 'gro gsungs nas bzhengs byung pa la/ chos
rje pas bla gos bsnun te/ ci zer khyed 'dir bsdad nas sde 'di'i bya ra ba bgyis te/ bstan pa yun ring du rgyas dgos so zhes gsungs pas/ bse mgon nyid zhal mdun du cung
zad dud pa dang bcas pa sngar bzhin bzhugs par gyur to/ /zhes lo rgyus kyi yi ge rnying ma 'ga' zhig las 'byung ba bzhin bris pa lags/ de lta bu'i thub dbang gnyis pa sa
skya paN chen de nyid kyi drung du chos skyong gi chos skor rnams rdzogs par chos rgyal 'phags pas gsan pa yin te/ skyes chen dam pa 'di ni bstan pa snga dar gyi lo tsA ba
chen po ka ba dpal brtsegs kyi sku skyer slob dpon chen po padma 'byung gnas kyi lung bstan gsal bo yod cing / spyan ras gzigs dang gsung gleng rtag tu mdzad pa'i se ston
ri par grags pa gcig gi sku skyer de ma thag par zhal gyis

bzhes/ de'i grwa pa rnams ngo mkhyen pa sogs chung ngu nas byis pa'i spyod pa las 'das/ bslab pa'i gnas dang sgyu rtsal tshegs chung ngus mkhyen/ bla ma 'di dang 'gro mgon
phyag na ste sku mched gnyis kas sgo rum gyi nyi zer la na bza' dang 'khor gsum bkal/ kun gyis 'di ni 'phags pa'o zhes bsgrags pas 'phags par grags/ dgung lo gsum pa la sgrub
thabs mtsho skyes/ brgyad pa la skyes rabs/ dgu pa la brtag gnyis thugs las gsungs/ tshogs pa thams cad shin tu ngo mtshar/ de ltar na skyes stobs kyi thugs rab ni chos
rje las kyang lhag par mkhas pa rnams la grags so/ /bcu pa la chos rje'i phyag phyir gong du byon pa'i mar lam zul phur/ chos rje pas mkhan po/ zul phu ba na bza' 'phrad
gsol du grags pa chos dbang bas slob dpon mdzad nas rab tu byung / skyor mo lung pa shes rab seng ge la kA ri kA

gsan te lhag pa tshul khrims kyi bslab pas phyug par mdzad do/ /de ltar dgung lo bcu bdun pa'i bar chos rje la dbang khrid bshad pa phal cher rdzogs/ shin tu mnyes nas chos
dung / lhung bzed/ phyag dpe tshogs pa rnams gtad/ bstan pa'i khur bskur/ bcu bdun pa la chos rje dang / bco brgyad pa la byang phyogs rgyal po go dan yang gshegs/ de nas
se chen gyis gdan drangs/ brtag pa dang dri ba la sogs pa'i sgo nas yid ches shing / btsun mos mtshams sbyar nas mos gus khyad par can tshud/ dgung lo bcu dgu pa chu mo
glang gi lo gsar la se chen gan gyis dbang bskur zhus/ g.yang kri'u las byas pa yi ge sa dang rin po che'i ri mo yod pa'i dam kha phul/ ti shrI'i mtshan gsol/ gser dang
mu tig gi snam sbyar/ sku chos/ phyam tshe/ dbu zhwa/ chags lhwam/ bzhugs gdan/ gser gyi khri/ gdugs/ gsol zhal/ gsol sder la sogs tshang ma/ rnga mo dang chibs drel gser
gyi

sga skor tshang ma/ gtso bor dbus gtsang gi khri skor bcu gsum/ sgos su gtsang chu mig gi khri skor du gang gtogs phyag phyir phul/ phyi lo stag lo de la bandhe shed skyed
bod yig tu bris pa dang / dngul bre chen lnga bcu rtsa drug ja sig nyis brgya/ gos yug brgyad cu dang / dar yug stong dang brgya phul lo/ /stag lo 'di la rgya gar du ru kas
bzung yod mtshams hor dmag khyer/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems mche ba gdan 'grongs par byed/ de bar 'phags pa rin po ches byang ngos su byon/ chos rje'i sku 'bum bzhengs/Ordination
of 'Phags pa'u yug pa gdan 'dren btang nas mdo khams su bsnyen rdzogs mdzad rtsis la 'u yug pa grongs/ snye thang pa grags pa seng ges mkhan po mdzad/ las slob
jo gdan byang thang pa bsod rgyal/ gsang ste yar lung pa byang rgyal/ dad dge mkhan po sgro dang gnam 'phar ba sogs chos rje'i bu chen mang po

bsags nas dgung lo nyer gcig pa shing mo yos lo zla ba lnga pa'i tshes bcu bzhi'i nyin/ rgya bod kyi mtshams he ce'u dang nye ba'i sar rgyal ba'i bstan pa la zhugs la yongs
su rdzogs pa dge slong gi sdom pa rnam par dag pa bzhes so//dgung lo nyer gsum pa'i sbrul gyi lo zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes bcu gsum gyi nub mo/ chos rje mngon sum du byon nas
zab rgyas kyi chos gsungs lung bstan dbugs dbyung / bstod pa yang mdzad/ thos pa rgya mtsho ma yang de dus mdzad par byed do/ /de nas hor yi ge med pa la yig gsar brtsams/
de'i phud la bandhe shed skyed thags ma phul/ dbang yon bar ma la bod chol kha gsum/ tha ma la rgya'i mi yur chen mo phul/ bod thams cad sa skya pa'i chos lugs las gzhan
pa byed dbang med pa'i lung 'bud gsungs pa la/ rang rang gi chos lugs gang yod skyongs su 'jug pa cis kyang dgos gsungs nas/ yon mchod gnyis ka'i 'ja'

sa thams cad la rang rang gi chos lugs la 'bad pa thon gsungs pa sha stag yod pas dbang spus shin tu bzang ba yin no/ /rgya nag gi chos lugs log par spyod pa'i zin shing ston
pa bcu bdun bstan pa la shin tu sdang bar yod pa rnams ni rigs pa rnam dag gis btul nas bstan pa la btsud/ rgya/ hor/ 'jang / yu gur/ mi nyag la sogs pa'i skal ldan snod
du rung ba rnams la/ rab byung bsnyen rdzogs lo re'i nang du stong phrag re tsam rang gis gnang ba dang / mkhan po 'dul 'dzin chos mgon zhes bya ba sman rtse'i yul du
brdzangs nas/ des kyang rab byung dgu brgya tsam dang / rje nyid kyis gnang ba snga rting dril ba la bzhi stong bzhi brgya nyer lnga mdzad de/ rgya nag gi rgyal khams rab
byung gis gang bar mdzad do/ /de nas dgung lo nyer brgyad pa chu pho khyi la cha rkyen mang du bskur bar mdzad pa rnams la brten nas/ dpon chen shAkya bzang pos dbu rtse
sgo gsum gser thog chen mo dang

bcas pa/ gser 'bum chen mo g.yu thog dang bcas pa dang / thub pa chen po'i gser sku la sogs pa bzhengs/ de'i phyis lo chu mig chos 'khor sngan ma la dge 'dun brgyad khri tsam
la 'bul 'gyed gya nom pa gnang / hor yul nas yar byon pa'i lam gar mdo khams gtso mdo gnas gsar du nye gnas chen po rin chen ston tshul gyis do dam byas nas gser gyi glegs
bam phyed dang nyis stong la sogs pa/ rten gsum sde dgon mi nor gyi 'bul ba grangs med pa bzhes nas dgung lo so gcig shing mo glang la sa skyar phebs/ gser thog chen
mo'i zhugs tshags/ gser 'bum bkra shis sgo mang / rje gong ma'i phyi rten skya 'bum bdun pa gser gyi gdugs chos 'khor/ sgos su chos rje'i phyi rten la gser thog bka' 'gyur
la sogs pa gser gyi po ti nyis brgya lhag pa la sogs pa bzhengs/ de lta bu'i bstan pa'i mnga' bdag chos kyi rgyal po 'jig rten gyi gtso bor gyur nas

kyang / mdo sngags dbang bshad kyi rgyun zab mo nyams kyis dogs nas/ de dus kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen mkhas btsun bzang ba dang / lung rgya chen ba chung 'bring mtha' dag bla
mar bsten/ rang bzhed pa'i chos de 'dug na mo btsun phal pa gcig la 'dug kyang / nga rgyal dang khengs pa dang / gzhan gyis smod pa sogs gang la yang mi dgongs par gus
pas gtsug tu bzhes nas chos zhus te/ de dag gi rnam thar rgyas pa gsan yig sogs na gsal lo/ /chos kyi ched yin kyang 'di lta bu'i che 'gying bcag pa ni gzhan sus kyang sgrub
par dka' 'o/ /de nas dgung lo so gsum pa me mo yos la 'gro mgon phyag na sku gshegs pa'i chos 'khor chu mig tu mdzad pa la dge 'dun dgu khri la 'bul 'gyed bgrangs pa
las 'das so/ /de rjes de ma thag hor gyi gdan 'dren pa nan ches nas lo gzhug de la 'dam du phebs par byon/ phyis lo sa pho 'brug la dpon chen shAkya bzang pos

lha khang chen mo bzhengs/ khri skor bcu gsum bskul/ dpon chen kun dga' bzang po dang sbrel nas rdzogs par grub/ rin chen sgang / lha khang bla brang / dus mchod bla brang
rnams kyang bzhengs so/ /gong du phebs nas dgung lo so drug pa lcags pho rta la dbang zhus pa'i tshe/ me nyag rgya rgod kyi rgyal po'i shel dam la bcos byas nas/ shel dam
gling drug ma dang / mu tig gi 'ja' sa phul/ gnam gyi 'og sa'i steng na rgya gar lha'i sras po/ sprul pa'i sangs rgyas/ yi ge rtsom mi/ rgyal khams 'jags su 'jug pa po/
gnas lnga rig pa'i paNDi ta 'phags pa ti shrI zhes mtshan gsol/ dngul bre chen stong ra can dang / gos dar lnga khri dgu stong la sogs pa phul/ mjal res kyis mthong phyag
dang mjal dar dngul bre 'chag med sogs mdzad pas/ rgyal po'i 'phral gyi 'bul ba kun dril bas gser bre brgya lhag dngul bre stong ra can/ gos dar bzhi khri la sogs pa

byung bar bshad do/ /de nas zhe gnyis pa me pho khyi lo la sa skyar phebs bod kyi dge bshes skya btsun thams cad la/ bod kyi dbang bshad lung man ngag thams cad nga la yod
pas nyan du shog ces bka' gnang nas/ zhe drug pa'i bar la chos dang zang zing gi char phab/ khyad par glang lo la chu mig chos 'khor chen mo la zhag bco lnga'i bar du dge
'dun 'bum phrag gcig la chos dang zang zing gi sbyin pa mdzad tshul bsam gyis mi khyab/ de ltar bskyangs pa'i slob ma'i mchog kyang shar nub gung gsum/ khang gnyan zhang
gsum/ la ru ba/ nyan chen pa/ sru lung pa/ lo mchog dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ gsal la ba 'od zer 'bum/ dbus pa seng 'bum/ dam pa kun dga' grags
la sogs pa brgyud pa 'dzin nges kyang mang du byon/ snang ngor bstan pa'i rtogs pa'i yon tan yi dam gyi lha'i zhal

gzigs pa dang / 'od gsal rgyun mi 'chad pa dang / mngon par shes pa'i yon tan dpag tu med pa mnga' ste skyid grong du jo bo'i drung du byon pa'i tshe/ rje btsun spyan ras gzigs
dbang phyug zhal gzigs pa la mnal lam du bstod pa mdzad pa dang / ri bo rtse lngar byon pa'i tshe/ rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi zhal gzigs nas bstod pa mdzad pa dang
/ yang chos rje sa paN byang ngos la 'byon pa'i dus su/ yang dgon pas mjal te/ bla ma ni gong la gshegs par gda'/ bdag cag slob ma rnams la phyag dang bsnyen bkur byed
pa dang / mos gus kyi gnas su gyur pa'i sku tshab cig 'tshal bar gda' ba la/ dbon po 'di pa yang dag pa lags sam zhus pas/ dbon po rnal ma lags gsungs nas/ bla ma 'di pha
tshad na rdo gcig 'dug pa la bsnyes/ spyan ma btsum par mnal du song 'dug pa bstan nas/ 'di 'od gsal zin pa'i rtags lags/ spyir nged kyi mi brgyud rnal ma la 'od gsal
cung zad re rgyun

mi chad du yod pa yin gsungs/ rgya gar gyi paNDi ta go tam shrI bha tra la mtshan mo rmi lam ji ltar byung ba thams cad/ bdag nyid chen po 'dis mngon par shes pas mkhyen nas/
nangs par paNDi ta la gsung byon pa'i tshe/ mahA gu ru la mngon par shes pa a tse zer zhing dad par gyur to/ /bla ma 'di gong nas phebs/ 'u yug na bzhugs dus phyogs su
khral bsdud byung pa la/ shangs lha phu ba'i jo gdan gcig gis zhu ba la phyin dus/ sgar gyi mthar sems can la 'tshe ba byed pa/ hor sog mang pos mtha' bskor/ bla ma 'di
sa 'ja' li gcig la bzhugs/ g.yas na rtsom pa mdzad pa'i yig mkhan/ g.yon na bka' shog 'bri ba'i yig mkhan/ mdun na rgyun gtor shom pa'i gtor skad bton nas chab gtong ba rnams
mthong bas/ jo gdan gyi bsam pa la/ bla ma ci'i bla ma sems can la 'tshe ba/ mtha' hor sog gis bskor ba/ g.yon gyi bka' shog ni

nga zhu ba la 'ong pa dang 'dra/ gzhan mnar med pa yin/ g.yas kyi rtsom pas ci byed/ chos sems thog tu mi 'jog tshig gcig mi bsngo ba'i gtor skad kyis ci byed/ bla mar mi 'dug
snyam pa zhig byung ba dang / bdag nyid chen po 'dis jo gdan la spyan cer te gzigs nas/ gtor ma 'di la bshams pas thob pa khos bshams pa yin/ dmigs pas thog pa de ngas
byed/ /bsngos pas thob pa de khyod kyi gyis gsungs pa dang / jo gdan shin tu skrag nas/ mngon par shes pa thogs pa med pa mnga' bar 'dug pa la/ ngas log lta byas pa ma
legs snyam nas lus thams cad sa la phab pa'i phyag byas/ bshags pa phul/ mchog tu ngo mtshar bar gyur te bstod tshig gi sgra dbyangs kun tu sgrog par gyur/ bla ma'i mdzad
spyod thams cad gang la gang 'dul du rtogs/ sems can gsod spyod/ khral 'u lag sogs rang gi las su go nas nges pa'i shes pa khyad par can skyes par gyur

to/ /de ltar dgung lo bco brgyad pa nas zhe drug pa'i bar nyi shu rtsa dgu'i bar la gdan sa che 'bring chung gsum/ rgya bod kyi chos sde phal mo che'i bdag rkyen bkod bzhag
skyong dar la sogs pas nyin mtshan 'das par mdzad nas/ zhe drug pa lcags pho 'brug gi smal po zla ba'i nyi shu gnyis la dkon mchog gi drung du mchod pa rgyas par shoms gsungs
nas rdo rje skyil krung mdzad/ rdor dril thugs khar bsnol ba'i ngang nas rma bya chen mo dang / dpal mgon klu sgrub la sogs pa mngon sum du gzigs pa sogs ngo mtshar
gyi ltas du ma dang bcas te/ lha khang chen mo'i bla brang du bde bar gshegs so/ /bla chen 'dis hor yul du byon pa'i bar lam du sprin gseb tu gur gyi mgon po rta nag la
chibs te/ ber nag gsol ba/ phyag na gri thod 'dzin zhing / lha mo phyag gnyis ma rta rgyab tu bskyon pa/ rta nag gi rmig pa nas mi nag gsum gyis bteg pa zhig mngon sum du
gzigs

shing / de phyin chad grwa pa dag gis lcam dral gyi 'bag dang phod ka gyon/ rta nag zhon nas gzigs snang dang 'dra ba'i cha lugs su byas te chos kyi rgyal po'i zhabs 'bring
la 'gro ba'i zhal bkod mdzad de/ de dus kyi zhal 'bag dang phod ka sogs ma nyams pa dus phyis shing sgrom la g.yogs te/ sa skya'i tshoms bar sogs mgon khang rnams na bzhugs
pa la 'cham mgon rta thog ma zhes grags so/ /chos kyi rgyal po dpal ldan 'phags pa 'di nyid kyis bstan srung rnams bran du 'khol ba'i mthu rtsal gyis stod hor gdug pa
can btul ba'i tshul ni/ hor gyi rgyal po go dan la/ gcen po hu la hu bya ba dang / gcung po go pe la zhes pa se chen rgyal po dang mched gsum yod pa'i/ go dan gyis blon
thabs mdzad/ khrims ra thams cad la dbang bsgyur/ se chen rgyal sar bkod/ phu bo hu la hu la dbang rigs cher med pa nas/

go dan gshegs dang bstun ngo log brtsams se chen 'don rgyu yin pa la/ 'gro mgon chos rgyal 'phags pas thabs rten 'brel dang / byin rlabs srung 'khor sogs mdzad pas se chen
la rgol ma thub mthar 'u thug nas hu la hu na re/ da khyod rang rgyal po gyis/ nga rang sa cha gzhan du spyad pas chog dmag dum cig bslang / nga rang gzhan du 'gro zer ba
la/ se chen gyis dmag khri phrag bcu bdun byin pa rnams khrid nas stod du phyin/ sa cha hor yul ding chen zhes bya bar gzhi bcas/ mang du 'phel ba ding sang stod hor du
grags pa 'di yin zhing / bla ma 'phags pa'i byin rlabs kyis se chen la rgyal sa len ma thub pas/ 'phags pa rin po che la 'khon du bzung / 'bri khung pa dang phag gru ba'i
sbyin bdag byas/ deng sang 'phan nag tu grags pa'i stod hor gyi sgyer thags dang bkras thags gtso

che ba'i gos la gser bsgril thags kyi snang ba rab 'byams bkra ba'i gos 'phan mdun ngos gos chen kha bsgrigs dang / rgyab yug bsgrigs 'ba' zhig byas pa'i nyis thog ma khyad
'phags de nyid kyis gtsos pa'i 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa byas/ 'bri khung pa ci gsung dang len byed kyi yod pa'i skabs/ 'bri khung pas sdod ma shes/ sa skya pa la zhabs
'dren sgrub snyam/ dgon pa dpon pos stod hor 'bod par rang ngos kyis phyin/ hu la hus bu ga du rin chen du byas pa'i rgyal pos gtsos pa'i stod hor gyi dmag 'bum phrag
mang po khrid nas yong pas/ gdan sa nas kyang thos/ dpon chen kun dga' bzang po dang / dpon chen ag len gnyis kyis dbus gtsang gi dmag khri tsho bcu tsam khrid nas gdong
bsur phyin pas/ dpal mo dpal thang du thug bod dmag khri tsho bcu tsam gyis/ stod hor gyi dmag 'bum phrag mang po thal bar brlags/ hor stong phrag mang po bsad pa'i

rtags la rna ba g.yas pa rkyang bcad nas drel khal mang po bkal/ ga du rin chen dang dgon pa dpon po gnyis btson du bzung khrid yong pas/ lam du rna ba rnams rul byung pa thang
grang sar nyi ma la bstan nas bsang pa'i lhas la deng sang rna ba lhas su grags/ de dus 'phags pa rin po che pho brang na bzhugs pa'i skabs yin pas/ gong ma yon mchod
la gnas tshul 'bul ba'i gser yig pa mngags dus/ gong ma'i lung gis/ ga du rin chen la nyes pa med pas kho rang thongs/ dgon pa dpon por khrims chod ces phebs pa nas/ dgon
pa dpon po sa skya'i mdun la ma khrid/ dpon po ri rgyab bskor te/ mgo la su khug bkon/ mgo mdun rgyab bsgyur nas rta la bskyon te tsho 'dus khrims khang du khrid/ ske
bcad/ snying rgyab nas bton/ mgo snying gcig thug gzung la btsugs/ dkon khang gi mgon khang thog

na yod pa la/ phyis dpon chen ag len gyis khur nas mgo lha sa rdzong la yod pa/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyi mthu rtsal gyis/ lha sa rdzong pa gtan brlag
tu song pa nas da lta mgo ga na yod mi snang / snying thug gzung la btsugs pa de ka ma nyams pa da lta sna dkar rtse na yod zer ba bzhin/ kho bos dbus phyogs la gnas mjal
la phyin skabs dngos su mthong zhing / de nas 'bri khung pa gtan brlag la gtong ba'i bka' bkyon gnang rgyu yin pa la/ 'phags pa'i nye gnas chen po rin chen ston tshul la
sku ngo zhus/ 'phan nag tu grags pa'i 'phan khyad par can de nyid kyis gtsos pa'i 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa byas pa la brten/ 'bri khung pa nag las thar ba byas/ de
lta bu'i nag las thar ba'i 'bul ba'i gtso bo yin pas 'phan nag tu grags/ rin chen ston tshul gyis do dam byas phul bas rin chen ston tshul gyis phul

bar yang grags/ de skabs dbus kyi thag ring ba'i stag lung pa dang / rgya ma pa sogs dmag la ma slebs pa rnams la/ hor 'dul dus go chod pa'i mi rta rnams hor 'dra la brdzangs
mi la zug rgyab chas/ rta la chag chu rtsam pa nyin re la bre bcu re dgos tshul gyi dpon chen gyi phyag rtags sogs mngags/ sgo gnon gtong ba'i thog ma de nas byung bas/
nag chen rnams la dran 'dzin gyi khrims srol bzang po de lta bu btsugs/ 'phan 'di nyid las sum 'gyur gyis che ba'i gser 'phan du grags pa gser leb thags kyi sangs rgyas
kyi sku 'bum phrag mang po dang / chos srung nor lha sogs kyi sku stong phrag mang po bsgrigs pa'i khyad par can de/ 'phags pa rin po che la snye thang pa grags bzang gis
phul zer/ gser 'phan 'di dbu rtse rnying ma nas zhal lho gzigs la brkyangs/ 'di'i zhabs tog tu gdan sa dan nas nyi lde ba dang / shar nub gung gsum

sogs nas gser 'phan bkra shis khra ring sogs bya khra ma'i dar shing la thal mar sleb pa'i khyad par can mang po skyong / 'phan nag tu grags pa da lta yang lha khang chen mo'i
sgo dmar na bzhugs pa 'di nyid lha khang chen mo nas zhal byang gzigs la skyong / de skabs gdan sa chen po'i rang rang gi bla brang gzim khang gtsug lag khang brang khang
sogs so so nas rgya hor gyi dngos spyad mchod pa'i yo byad bsam gyis mi khyab pa bton te khang thog nas mchod pa'i sprin phung dpag tu med pa 'bul ba yin zhes 'phan
nag gi lo rgyus sogs yi ge rnying ma rnams las 'byung ba yin no/ /de dus stod hor gyi rgyal bu ga du rin chen sa skyar slebs dus/ der bzhugs kyi bandhe khri phrag mang po
g.ya' lung gi bya spe nas gdan sa'i bar khrom chen po 'tshogs pa bzhin star ma chad pa gzigs mo la byon pa/ rgyal pos mthong nas 'bri khung pa kho sa skya pa la dmag med
zer te/ bandhe

rang gi dmag kyang 'di tsam 'dug pa zhes zer ba la/ 'di rnams dmag min dge 'dun tshogs pa yin byas khong dga'/ yang rgyal pos lha khang chen mo mthong ba na/ dgon pa dbon po
kho sa skya pa la rdzong med zer te/ gzhan la med pa'i rdzong 'di 'dra 'dug zer ba la/ 'di rdzong min/ gtsug lag khang yin byas pas kyang kho dga' skad/ de nas sa skya
pa rnams kyis 'jigs 'jigs ltar byas nas/ g.yag gzeng dang / mi nag dung long can rnams kyi rol stabs dang bstun 'cham pa rgyal bus mthong bas/ nag rang pa pha gi tshos nged
kyi dmag sgar gyi gseb la 'ong nas me slang ba skad byas/ mi 'tshams pa sna tshogs byed mkhan de tsho yin pa 'dug zer/ g.yag gzeng mthong bas pha gi tshos nged rang hor
yul nas dmag la chas tsam nas bzung rwa rtse la blangs nas sa la brdeb pa sogs cho 'phrul du ma bstan mkhan de tshor 'dug zer/ tshul de dag ni don la chos

kyi rgyal po 'phags pa nyid la bka' srung rnams kyis 'phrin las sgrub pa'i rtags mtshan rgyun ma chad par bstan pa'i ngo mtshar ba'i rnam thar du snang ngo / /bla ma chen po
'di'i chos skyong gi man ngag yongs su rdzogs pa'i slob ma ni/ mgon po'i bka' bab dam pa kun dga' grags nyid de/ skyes chen 'di ni chos skyong la mnga' shin tu brnyes pas/
sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud dharma pha la gzhon nu la gshegs shing / bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal sman rtse'i yul nas 'byon ma bde bas/ sa skya'i gdan sa shar ba rin
rgyal ba la 'chol dgos pa byung dus/ bstan 'dzin thams cad kyi thugs la ma ran nas/ de dus dam pa kun dga' grags 'dis sa skya gdung brgyud rang gis 'dzin zhing / gdung brgyud
rgyun mi chad pa'i 'phrin 'chol chos skyong rnams la drag tu mdzad pas/ de'i nus pa la brten nas hor rgyal po'i pho brang gi steng du lcags kyi bya rog chen po ri bo
tsam bab ste/ de'i spu 'gul ba tsam gyis sa phyogs thams cad g.yo

ba dang / gnam kha 'ub kyis rdo rje'i char pa babs pa sogs cho 'phrul sna tshogs bstan pas/ hor rgyal po la thugs rtog cher byung nas/ sman rtse nas bdag nyid chen po myur
du spyan drangs te/ sa skya'i gdan sa gtad cing / gdung brgyud spel ba'i lung bud pa sogs byung ba yin pas/ dam pa 'di rang re sa skya pa la bka' drin mchog tu che ba yin
la/ rje 'di khams phyogs kyi khrom chen po'i gseb nas yod pa zhig la/ chos rje khu dbon gnyis kas gur mgon dngos su gzigs pas chos skyong gi sprul par yang grags/ bla ma
'dis mdo khams kyi tre maNDal thang zhes bya ba chos rgyal 'phags pa'i dbon po dharmA pha la gshegs pa'i gnas dang thag nye ba'i sar/ hor gyi rgyal po se chen go pe las
sbyin bdag mdzad nas/ rgya'i bzo bo shin tu mkhas pa dag gis bzhengs pa'i gur mgon lha brgyad kyi sku la/ bla chen 'phags pa spyan drangs te rje rang nyid dang bcas pas phyag
nas

mdzad de/ sku de rnams byin rlabs kyi zil shin tu che bar bzhugs pa'i tre'i mgon khang zhes bya ba yul de na snyan pa shin tu che zhing / dam can rgya mtsho'i tshogs nyin re
bzhin du sprin bzhin 'du bar grags pa de nyid gsar bzhengs su mdzad cing / gzhan yang chos skyong gi man ngag sngar yi ge med pa la/ shin tu zab pa'i shog ril drug dang
/ sngon 'gro shom gyi yi ge sogs shog ril bcu gcig gtor ma'i zhal gdams kyi yi ge gnyis dang / mdos bskang che chung dang / pho rkyang gi gshin rje dang gnod sbyin ltar
sgrub pa'i yi ge la sogs pa mdzad cing / bstan 'gro'i don rgya chen po mdzad nas/ mthar rgya nag ri bo rtse lnga nas sku lus ma spangs par mkha' spyod du gshegs kyang zer/
kha cig ni gnas der mya ngan las 'das pa'i tshul bstan nas/ de dang dus mtshungs pa khams kyi tre mgon khang na nyid kyi sku 'dra phyag nas ma zhig yod pa'i dbu thog tu
ring bsrel bya mo'i sgo nga tsam zhig

bab bo zhes kyang grags shing / la la ni da lta yang rgya nag ri bo rtse lnga na bzhugs pas skal ldan dag dang mjal du yod zer ro/ /bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan gyi dngos
slob yang dgon pa dpal ldan bkra shis kyi zin bris las/ 'phags pa la mgon po'i bka' bab kyi slob ma gsum byung ba ni/ a gnyan dam pa/ dam pa kun grags/ bu lung kun rdor
zhes bshad pa ni/ cung zad gsung bgros ma zin par snang ste/ a gnyan dam pa dang / dam pa kun grags gnyis mtshan gyi 'bod phyogs tsam ma gtogs gcig par snang ba'i phyir
ro/ /de lta bu'i dam pa kun dga' grags la sngon bla ma 'phags pas/ chos skyong gi man ngag rnams rdzogs par chig brgyud du gnang dus/ ma 'ongs pa na nged kyi tsha bo rnams
la cis kyang 'phrod pa gyis shig ces gsungs pa'i bla ma'i bka' bzhin bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal la bstan srung rnams kyi chos skor mtha'

dag ma tshang ba med par dgyes bzhin du stsal pa yin te/ de yang bla ma bdag nyid chen po 'di 'phags pa rin po che dang yum mi gcig pa'i mched zla/ slob dpon rin chen rgyal
mtshan dang ye shes 'byung gnas gnyis byung ba'i/ phyi ma'i sras su chu pho khyi la bo dong e ru 'khrungs/ gdan sa'i gser tog chen mo bzhengs lo dang gcig 'di'i dgung lo
bcu drug pa'i tshe 'phags pa rin po che sa skyar phebs dbang bshad mang du gnang / lan cig 'di la yun ring du gzigs nas/ mgo res pus mo la bab pa'ang srid/ yon tan 'bung
las slobs/ phyag na'i ri rgyud yin zer ba gnyis las mi 'dug ye 'byung gi ri rgyud yin zer ba mang du 'dug pa rmis gsung ba'i lung bstan stsal/ de ltar 'di bgres kyang pha
spun mnyam po la yum bzang ngan dang / grags che chung gis phyag na'i sras dharmA pha la gdan sar bskos 'di rang ka ba'i tshul du bzhugs/ dgung lo nyer gcig pa la mi chen

a 'bus gdan drangs nas gong du byon/ gong ma'i lung gis re zhig brtag dgos pas sman rtser rgyugs gsungs nas spyugs pas/ 'dis nyer bdun bzhes pa'i tshe/ sa skyar dharmA pA la
grongs/ gdan sa bu chen la bcol nas sa skya pa rnams ci bya la gtad pa'i dus/ yar 'brog gi dpon chen ag len gyis sems kyis ma bzod/ do dam cher mdzad/ de'i grogs khams
pa dpon nag ces bya bas kyang byas nas bka' bgros pa rnams la gros bskul/ ti shrI grags 'od pa gong na bzhugs pa la zhu yig byas pas/ ti shrI ba'i phyag phyi nyi lde ba shes
rab dpal dang / mi chen u dus byas nas gong ma la zhu ba nan gyis 'bul ba'i rgyu dang / lcam sring ma spyod nyes gcig kyang hor yul du phebs pa g.yang la lhung nas grongs
pa la 'ja' 'od dang ring bsrel byung bas/ nga'i bla ma'i rus pa yin tsam gyis chog par

'dug pas/ bzang po dpal ba tshol gsung ba'i lung bud/ de dus bla ma 'dis rje btsun ma la rtse gcig tu gsol ba btab pas/ nyi ma 'char gar tsandan sdong po'i steng nas zhal bstan/
bu 'dod pas ni bu thob 'gyur zhing / /nor 'dod pas ni nor rnams nyid thob/ /ces gsung byon/ dgung lo so lnga pa la sman rtse nas gdan drangs/ so drug pa la gong mas
gnang sbyin bzang po mdzad/ 'phags pa ti shrI'i dbon po yin nges su 'dug pas gdung brgyud spel ba'i lung phud sa skyar mgyogs par byon la gdan sa gyis gsungs pa bzhin phebs
te gdung brgyud spel ba dang / slob gnyer rnams legs par mdzad/ rgyal po'i lung yod kyang gsan sbyong gi stabs dang / cung zad mi mdzes pa la dgongs nas lo bcu'i bar
du lha khang bla brang du bzhugs nas/ gdan sar shar pa rin rgyal ba bzhugs su bcug de ltar na 'dis nyer brgyad pa nas zhe lnga'i bar lo bco brgyad kyi ring la dpal ldan

sa skya'i gdan sa shar pas byas/ da lta yang shar ba'i bla ma che 'don grub pa rnams chos khri steng du byon chog pa'i rgyu mtshan yang de yin/ bdag nyid chen po bgres kar
nga gnyis pa la rab tu byung / mtshan a mo gha dhwa dzar gsol/ thugs dam zab mo la rtse gcig bzhugs/ lha khang chen mo'i lcags ri chen po bzhengs pa sogs kyi phyag rjes kyang
bzhag thugs bskyed bzang ba dang bla ma yi dam gyi byin rlabs zhugs shing / chos skyong 'di rnams bran du 'khol bas/ sa skya'i chos dang zang zing gnyis ka 'di'i dus
kho na dpal 'byor che bar grags/ de ltar bla ma bdag nyid chen pos btsun mo bdun khab tu bzhes/ sras bco lnga/ sras mo gnyis te bcu bdun 'khrungs pa las/ sras thog ma gnyis
gzhon nu la gshegs/ de 'og bla chen kun dga' blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po skyes stobs kyi thugs rab che zhing lung rtogs kyi

yon tan phul du byung bas dgung lo bcu gnyis pa la gong ma rgyal po'i ti shrI mdzad/ dgung lo nyer drug pa la bla ma bdag nyid chen po sku gshegs rjes su gcung rnams la bla
brang khang bzhi so sor bgos te gnang / de la'ang mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pa'i blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ste sku mched gnyis la shel gyi dam ga dang bzhi thog
bla brang gnang / 'di dag gi gdung brgyud rnams la dang po bzhi thog bla brang pa zer te/ bdag chen blo gros dbang phyug pa yan gyi gdung brgyud rdzogs nas ding sang mi
bzhugs/ ti shrI kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas dpal bzang po dang / de'i gcung ti shrI kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po sku mched la gser gyi dam ga dang lha khang chen
mo gnang / 'di dag gi brgyud pa la dang po lha khang bla brang ba zer/ phyis la stod gcung dang / khams phyogs na bzhugs pa'i bdag

chen byang par grags pa rnams yin te/ bdag chen kun dga' legs pa yan gyi gdung brgyud rdzogs nas ding sang mi bzhugs/ ta dben gu shrI/ de'i gcung 'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal
mtshan pa/ de'i gcung thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ste sku mched gsum la shel gyi dam ga dang rin chen sgang bla brang gnang / 'di dag la dang
po rin chen sgang bla brang pa dang / phyis su dge sding bla brang par grags/ bdag chen blo gros pa yan gyi gdung brgyud rdzogs nas ding sang mi bzhugs/ sa'i len kun dga'
legs pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po la dus mchod bla brang dang gser gyi dam ga gnang / 'di pa'i sgos kyi gdung brgyud la dus mchod bla brang pa dang / ding sang gdan
sa chen po gzhung dang / rtse gdong pa zhes grags shing / lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas dar zhing rgyas par bzhugs pa 'di'o/ /de ltar bla ma bdag nyid chen pos chos skyong gi

skor rnams rang gi sras bzhi thog pa mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pa dang / rin chen sgang ba'i zhal ngo dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa sku mched sogs la gnang
/ yang 'phags pa'i drung du chos skyong gi skor rnams gsan pa'i zhang dkon mchog dpal ba la grub chen nam bza' brag phug pas gsan/ des chos rje bla ma dam pa/ des bla
ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ des grub chen buddha shrI ba dang / shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan pa gnyis la gnang / de gnyis car la chos kyi rje rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang
pos zhus pa'i phyi sgrub kyi man ngag yi ge gser pod du grags pa po ti chung ngu zhig bsgrig par mdzad/ chos skor 'di'i dkar chag rnam rgyal skor gsum la sogs pa'i cho
ga'i yan lag gi yi ge cung zad kyang mdzad/ 'di lta bu'i ngor chen rdo rje 'chang nas mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug kun mkhyen bsod nams
seng ge yongs 'dzin

dkon mchog 'phel/ grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ bdag cag gi
yongs 'dzin dam pa rje btsun mus pa chen po rdo rje 'chang sogs kyi bar du brgyud de/ ding sang ngor lugs su grags pa dar rgyas su bzhugs/ yang bla ma dam pa'i dngos slob
sngags 'chang gzung skyid dpal ba dang / theg chen chos kyi rgyal po sogs kyi srol 'dzin byang pa a nanda pa dang / zur ston shAkya shrI'i zhabs la gtugs pa chos kyi rje
mus srad pa byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis bsgrigs pa'i 'di'i chos skor po ti gcig 'di'i dkar chag lha brgyad kyi sgrub yig bskang ba rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyi them
yig sogs khong rang gis mdzad pa 'ga' zhig dang bcas pa/ yi ge'i dngos bstan gtsang ba zhig 'dug pa la ding sang rdzong

chung pa lugs su grags/ bshad srol 'dzin pa ha cang mang rgyu med/ yang rje btsun khu dbon gyi slob ma do pa ston tshul des rgyal tsha lung mang po/ des mkhas pa yon tan khri/
des mkhan chen seng ge bzang po/ des yar lung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan pa dbon brgyud rnams la rim par byung ba'i man ngag dang / seng ge rgyal mtshan pas chos rje bla
ma dam pa la gtugs te lugs gnyis kyi yi ge rnams gung bsgrigs/ yig rnying ma dag pa rnams la zhus dag zhib tu mdzad/ khong rang gis kyang lha brgyad kyi gtor chog nang sgrub
kyi khrid yig gtor chen gyi gsol ga sogs brtsams/ chos rje bla ma'i gsung las gsungs pa phal cher zin bris su btab pa'i yig cha shin tu rgyas pa mang ba zhig snang /
ding sang gi bar du khong rang gi dbon rgyud srol 'dzin yang yod par 'dug cing / gong dkar rdo rje gdan pa chen po sogs kyang phal cher srol 'di la brten par snang ngo /

/gzhan yang brgyud pa'i khyad par cung zad dang / man ngag thor bu ba 'dra mi 'dra dang / lag len mi 'dra ba'i khyad par mang ba zhig 'dug cing / de ltar ma gtogs pa'i dpyod
ldan 'gas bar skabs su sgro btags pa dang / blun po 'gas snying khams bskyed de byas pa'i yi ge dang lag len/ chos skor 'di la sbyangs pa'i mkhas pa gzu bor gnas pa dag
gis mthong nas snying rje'i gnas su 'gyur ba 'ga' yang mthong mod/ drang por smras na mtshang la phog cing / bsngags pa brjod na bstan pa la gnod pas btang snyoms su bzhag
go /de rnams kyi nang nas gong du bshad pa ltar 'phags pa rin po ches mgon po'i snyan brgyud kyi man ngag thun mong ma yin pa rnams gha a gnyan dam pa la chig brgyud du
gnang / des kyang bla ma'i bka' bzhin bdag nyid chen po ma gtogs gzhan la thun mong ma yin pa ma gsungs/ bdag chen pas mkhas btsun

nam mkha' legs pa la yongs su rdzogs par gnang zhing / phal cher chos rje bla ma dam pa la yang stsal/ bla ma dam pas khu dbon gnyis ka'i zhabs la gtugs te bum pa gang byor
gsan/ de la slob ma mkhas btsun bzang gsum dang ldan pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ba las/ mgon po'i snyan brgyud thun mong ma yin pa rnams rin chen sgang pa rang gi sgos
kyi dbon po bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa la gnang / des rang nyid kyi sras 'jam dbyangs chen po nam mkha' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po la gnang / 'di slob dpon padma'i
sprul par grags/ yab sras 'di gnyis kyis mgon po 'khor bcas mngon sum du zhal gzigs/ nus pa thon chos skyong gi bdag por byed/ 'jam dbyangs chen pos mgon po 'di'i chos
skor la rtsal thon mdzad de/ yar lung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyi dbon po mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog pa bsten nas srol 'di'i man ngag mtha'

dag gsan/ sbas pa'i rnal 'byor pa bar sding pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan zhes grags pa'i mgon po'i grub thob cig bsten nas gsang ba'i yig chung bco brgyad sogs zab mo'i yang tig
mang po gsan/ 'di sngags 'chang kun dga' zla ba'i chos skyong zhu sa de yang yin zhing / de ltar brgyud pa gsum gyi man ngag mtha' dag bzhugs pa yin no/ /'di la rigs kyi
sras gcen rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po dang / gcung rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po gnyis byung ba/ 'di gnyis kas yab kyi drung du mgon
po'i chos skor gsan/ chos skyong mang po'i zhal gzigs/ nus pa thon pa yin no/ /bdag chen rgya gar ba'i drung du sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje sku mched rnams kyis gsan/ sa lo
chen po de nyid dang / yang bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ mnga' ris pa dpal ldan rgyal po/ spyan tshab tshul khrims bzang po/ rje sangs rgyas

rin chen/ rje lha mchog seng ge sogs nas brgyud pa rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'phags chen dpal ldan bkra shis/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags sogs las snyigs dus kyi bstan
pa'i gsal byed dam pa sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyis gsan nas/ rang gi sras 'jam dbyangs sku mched sogs la gnang ba'i gcen grub mchog
bsod nams dbang po las/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams bdag gis zhal ngo nang brgyud ma chad pa'i gur gyi mgon po lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang thun mong ma yin
pa dang / gnyan mgon sgrub dus kyi rjes gnang / pu tra ming sring gsum gyi rjes gnang sogs dang / 'di skor gyi man ngag zab bsdus po ti gcig tsam gyi bka' drin nos shing
/ gcung yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa rgyal mtshan can gyi drung du/ sgo rum bse 'bag dang / rdo mgon gyi drung sogs su lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang lan
gsum/ dpal mgon

bsnyen dus kyi rjes gnang zhal ngo nang brgyud ma chad pa dang / las mkhan 'khor rkyang gi rjes gnang pu tra'i zur bkar grags pa/ zhing skyong dur khrod kyi bdag po yab yum
gyi rjes gnang / dkar bdud kyi rjes gnang sogs dang srung 'khor rdo rje brag rdzong ma sogs 'di skor gyi chos skor zab mo che rags shig sras kyi tha chung sa skya pa a nanda
bdag gis legs par nos pa'i skal ba mchog dang ldan par gyur to/ /yang yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje sogs las chos skyong
gi zab chos mang po zhig yongs 'dzin dam pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis gsan cing / rje de nyid dang bla ma gzhan dag las kyang 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtshos chos
skyong gi skor gsan pa rnams yongs su rdzogs pa/ bdag cag gi yongs 'dzin dam pa dus gsum sgrib med du gzigs pa'i rgyal ba mus

pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan la gnang zhing / rje btsun 'brel tshad don ldan de nyid kyi drung du bdag sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams grags pa
rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po bdag gis thog mar brgyud pa du ma 'dus pa'i lha brgyad dang / 'khor rkyang gi rjes gnang stsal ba sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas zab mo'i yang rtse
mgon po'i srung 'khor rdo rje brag rdzong ma'i phyi nang gi khrid dang / nang khrid du grags pa 'jam dbyangs sangs rin gyi yig cha'i steng nas nyams khrid dpe lung dang
bcas pa dang / zhal bzhi pa'i tshe sgrub srung 'khor ma rgyas bsdus gnyis kyi khrid dang lung / dpal dur khrod bdag po'i rgyud dang man ngag yongs rdzogs kyi lung phyag
khrid dang bcas pa smin rgyas kyi bka' drin thob pas/ yid rab tu tshim zhing zab khyad mang po chos kyi che ba tsam yin par kho thag chod pa lags so/Biographical Sketch
of bDag chen Blo gros rgyal mtshan/yang bdag chen 'jam dbyangs chen po'i rigs dang chos kyi sras mchog tu gyur

pa bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ni/ gsung ngag lam 'bras sogs dgyes pa rdo rje'i skor rje mus chen la gsan pa dang / yab la gsan pa'i chos skyong che chung
gi man ngag sogs la shin tu mkhas shing mkhas pa'i grags pa'ang thon/ rje sa skya pa chen po'i sku'i rnam 'phrul yin pa'i gtan tshigs mchog dang ldan/ dben pa kho na la
dgyes shing sgrub pa gtso bor mdzad pas nyams dang rtogs pa'i bdag nyid chen por gyur pa/ nang zab mo lus kyi dkyil 'khor dngos su gzigs pa sogs rgyud sde nas bshad pa'i
sa lam gyi yon tan tshad med mnga'/ bye brag tu mgon po 'di'i chos skor brgyud pa gsum 'dus snyan nas snyan du brgyud pa'i man ngag phra mo tshun yab kyi drung du rdzogs
par gsan/ bzhi thog pa bdag chen kun dga' dbang phyug pa la thun mong pa ngor chen nas brgyud pa yang gsan/ mgon po 'di'i chos skor

rags pa yongs su grags pa'i po ti che ba zhig bsgrigs te/ dkar chag yid bzhin gyi nor bu'i bang mdzod kyi sgo 'byed gsal ba'i yid 'phrog ces bya ba mdzad/ phyis po ti de nyid
jag pas khyer dus me 'bar bas ding sang mgon pod me 'bar mar grags/ gzhan yang gsang sgrub yid bzhin nor bu sogs shin tu gsang bar 'os pa'i yig chung mang po dang / lha
mos mnal lam du lung bstan pa'i bskang gso sogs zab cing mtha' chod pa'i yi ge 'ga' mdzad de/ nyid kyi gsung las/ bod yul bstan pa'i mnga' bdag mchog /sa skya'i rje btsun
las brgyud pa'i/ /nag po chen po'i man ngag la/ /nga mkhas zer ba mang na yang / /ji bzhin rtogs pa kho bo tsam/ /zhes sogs mkhas pa'i rtogs pa brjod pa yang mdzad/ /mgon
po 'khor bcas kyang 'phral nas 'phral du gzigs shing sku dang grib ma bzhin du 'grogs nas las thams cad kyang sgrub pa'i lo rgyus kyang bsam gyis mi

khyab pa snang ngo / /bdag chen rin po che yan chad du chos skyong 'di pa'i man ngag thun mong ma yin pa rnams gdung brgyud kho na la gcig brgyud du bzhugs pas/ de bzhin du
gdung brgyud cig la gnang dgongs nas/ 'phyi mo'i bar du bu slob rnams la rjes gnang / yig lung / phyi sgrub kyi lag khrid thor bu tsam las ma gnang zhing / me 'bar ma'i
dkar chag gi tshig bcad du yang / khams gtsang dbus pa'i grwa pa sogs/ /sngon chad slob ma mang byung yang / /snying nas dad ldan ma byung phyir/ /thun mong tsam la sbyin
pa med/ /snying por gyur pa'i man ngag rnams/ /yang mdzod dmar po'i thugs dkyil las/ /gzhan nas rnyed par mi 'gyur bas/ /dad ldan yod na blang bar gyis/me 'bar ma'i dkar
chag /zhes pa'ang rtsom pa gnang zhing / rtse gdong du sa lo yum sras bzhugs sar phyag rtags dang ja spob rtse sogs gnang sbyin gyi rten dang bcas pa gnang

nas zhal ngo gcig sa skya'i gdan sa mdzad pa dang / chos gzhan la ster ma phod pa 'dra yod pas nyan pa la byon gsungs pas/ yum thugs brel gyi g.yengs pa'i rkyen gyis/ zhal
ngo yang ma phebs shing / phyag rtags kyi lan tsam yang ma byung ba la brten/ phyis rdo ring rin po che'i sku'i bsod nams lta bur byung ba yin zhes bla ma rnams gsungs te/
de yang rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po dbus phyogs na bzhugs pa'i mnal lam du dpal ldan sa skya nas yin zer pa'i g.yag nag khyi nag mi nag a tsa ra mang po byung nas/ khyod
sa skya la 'gro dgos mi 'gro na gsod pa yin zer bsdigs pa'i rnam 'gyur du ma byed pa dang / khyed mi 'gro na 'di ltar byed pa yin zer nas phyag rdzas thams cad khur nas
bar snang la 'gro ba sogs nub mang po'i bar du byung ba/ phyis bsam pas/ bdag chenarin po che'i thugs rjes chos skyong rnams bskul du btang bar 'dug

gsungs/ de nas ring por ma lon par sa skyar bdag chen rin po che'i spyan sngar phebs/ 'khor gsum yongs dag gi 'bul ba mdzad/ bsnyen rdzogs kyi mkhan po zhus/ phyag phyi'i mthil
bzhugs mdzad/ mnyes pa gsum gyi sgo nas zhabs tog bsgrubs pas thugs yid gcig tu 'dres/ spyir zab chos mang po gnang / khyad par mgon po'i man ngag snyan brgyud 'di rnams
gdung brgyud gcig la spel dgos rgyu yin na'ang / go nad sna tshogs pa zhig 'dug pas/ de khyed rang gi bsod nams su gda'/ da khyed rang las 'os mi 'dug gsungs nas gcig
brgyud kyi tshul du tshang la yongs su rdzogs pa stsal nas/ ma 'ongs pa na nged rang sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud gcig la nges par 'phrod pa mdzod cig gsungs pa'i bka' rgya
dang bcas gnang / gsang sgrub kyi khrid kyi dus mgon po dang yum e ka dza Tis zhal gzigs byin rlabs kyi bka' bab/

'phrin las kyi nus pa mthar phyin/ gangs can gyi ljongs su mgon po 'di'i mnga' bdag tu gyur/rje 'dis spyir mgon po lcam dral gyi rjes gnang rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po
dang / bdag chen zha lu pa mthu stobs dbang phyug bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa la zhus pa nas bzung / rjes gnang man ngag ci rigs gsan pa ni/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug
mkhas grub gung ru sher bzang / drin can mkhyen rab chos rje/ chos rje don yod dpal ba/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ chos rje bsod nams dbang phyug kun mkhyen bsod nams
seng ge mus sred pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ gra thang pa/ mtshungs med shes rab zla ba/ 'dus pa dang po ngag dbang dpal ldan grags pa/ zha lu ba bsod nams blo gros/ ti'u ra
pa rin chen chos kyi rgyal po rnams la gsan pa yin la/ de lta bu'i rdo ring kun spangs pa chen po la slob ma'i tshogs bsam gyis

mi khyab pa byung yang / man ngag zab dgu rnams ni tshar pa chos rje blo gsal rgya mtsho nyid la gnang pa yin te/ de yang rje tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos rdo ring rin po
che'i zhabs pad dgung lo bcu bdun pa nas nyi shu rtsa gsum pa'i bar du 'bral ba med par bsten/ mgon dang skyabs gnas gzhan spangs nas gcig tu bsgril/ lus longs spyod thams
cad ltos pa med par phul/ ci gsung ba'i bka' thams cad dwang du blangs pa la brten nas thugs rje'i chu rgyun dad pa'i snod du lhug par babs te bka' chos thams cad ci 'dod
pa gsang ba dang sbed pa ma mdzad par rje nyid la pha phogs kyi tshul du gnang zhing thugs yid gcig tu 'dres/ chos zab gnad che ba rnams gnang ba'i tshe/ zhabs skor la
phebs pa ltar mdzad pa'i phyag phyir khrid nas rdo leb kyi steng du maNDal mdzad de gnang / mi gzhan byung ba na 'phro gcod cing

yang zhabs skor mdzad pa'i tshul ston pa yin zhes rje bla ma rnams yang yang gsung ngo / /phyis rdo ring rin po che gshegs pa'i spur gyi phyag phyi mdzad pa'i tshe/ bzhugs
gdan gyi kha na byang sems dkar po mtheb skor gyi rgya tsam zhig byung ba de zhal du lhag ma lus pa gsol bas rgyud pa zin pa'i rten 'brel 'grig ding sang kha'u pa zhes grags
pa'i snyan brgyud zab mo'i bstan pa'i rgyun 'di rje 'di nyid kho na'i bka' drin yin/ yig cha mdzad tshul ni me 'bar ma'i dkar chag chung ngu sogs dkar chag tsho lnga
khro bcu'i rjes gnang / lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang / gtor bsngo'i cho ga rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum/ gtor ma gsum gyi rnam bshad/ lhan thabs dngos grub rol mtsho/ gtor bzlog
dgra bgegs kyi stobs 'phrog rol pa sogs yig sna kun dril bzhi bcu zhe grangs tsam mdzad yod ces bla ma dag gsung / 'di dag thams cad snyan brgyud

po ti'i nang na tshang par bzhugs pa yin/ de ltar dpal ldan sa skya pa'i snyan brgyud zab mo'i bstan pa dpyis phyin pa spel bar mdzad nas/ mthar dgung lo drug cu re lnga pa
stag gi lo la chos 'khor yang rtse nas mkha' spyod dbang mos mkha' spyod du spyan drangs pa yin no/ /tshar chen rdo rje 'chang de nyid la slob ma'i tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab
pa byon kyang / chos skyong che chung / rdo rje 'jigs byed/ dmar po skor gsum sogs kyi man ngag 'chi med bdud rtsi'i thigs pa lta bu rnams ni rje mkhyen brtse'i dbang
phyug dang / rje blo gros chos 'phags/ rje gzhon nu blo gros/ rje bod mkhar ba don grub rgyal mtshan/ rje klu sgrub rgya mtsho sogs la bka' bab pa yin te/ de yang rje mkhyen
brtse'i dbang phyug nyid sku gzhon nu'i skabs/ rje tshar chen gyis gos chen nag po kha do dang / skud chun dmar po gcig gnang nas 'di rnams tshags mdzod/ gzhan gyi
lag

tu ma shor ba gyis gsungs/ de ni chos skyong che chung dang / dmar po skor gsum sogs kyi chos kyi bka' babs kyi snod du gzigs nas gnang ba yin par gda'/ yang rje mkhyen brtse
ba nyug na bzhugs skabs shig rje tshar chen 'phral du nyug tu phebs byung pa la/ bla ma dang mjal ba'i dgyes tshor chen po byung nas/ da lan ci la phebs pa yin zhus pas/
khyod gshin rje dang 'brel che bar 'dug pas 'jigs byed kyi chos rnams shod gsungs byung bas/ sa dang po thob pa lta bu'i dga' ba 'khrungs/ de nas 'jigs byed kyi dbang
/ rjes gnang / khrid/ las gshin gyi rjes gnang / ra spod kyi lung sogs yongs su rdzogs par gnang ba yin zhing / rje mkhyen brtse ba de la slob ma mang du byung yang snyan
brgyud zab mo rnams kyi bka' bab ni rje rta ra ba bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhan chen byams pa rab brtan/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan sogs byung pa las/

rje bsod nams chos 'phel gyis rje mkhyen brtse ba nyid kyi drung du spyir gsang sngags gsar rnying gi gdams pa rgya mtsho lta bu rnams dang / khyad par chos skyong gnyis kyi
skor sogs bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gsan/ rje de nyid las bdag cag gi yongs 'dzin dam pa mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos kyi grags pas ji ltar gsan pa bzhin
gyi sa skya pa'i bstan srung dbang po rnam gnyis kyi rjes gnang mtha' dag zab khrid so so/ lag len gyi phyag khrid/ rgyab rten gyi mgon pod gsar rnying kun gyi lung
yongs rdzogs sogs thun mong ma yin pa'i gdams pa mtha' dag zhib cing mtha' chod par sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams bdag la dgyes bzhin du gnang ba lags/ yang tshar
chen gyi dngos slob rje bod mkhar ba don grub rgyal mtshan gyi drung du/ 'di skor gyi chos skor rnams yongs su

rdzogs pa spyan snga chos kyi rgya mtsho bas gsan cing / des bdag gi bla ma chos kyi spyan ldan lo nas spyan snga rin po che kun dga' don grub la gnang ba las/ de nyid kyi
drung du kho bo cag gis gur gyi mgon po'i dkyil 'khor lnga'i dbang dang / chos skyong gnyis ka'i rjes gnang so so ba rnams yongs su rdzogs pa/ phyi nang gsang ba'i zab mo'i
