khrid kyi rim pa mtha' dag ma lus pa dang / me 'bar ma sogs mgon pod rnams kyi lung phal cher gyi bka' drin nos shing / yang rje tshar chen yab sras kyi dngos slob nyams
dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag grub mchog dbang phyug rab brtan gyi drung du yang gur gyi mgon po lha brgyad/ lha mgon bcu gnyis ma/ 'khor rkyang rnams kyi rjes gnang dang
/ zhal bzhi pa sgrub dus kyi rjes gnang rgyas pa/ bram ze mngags gtad/ chos skyong gnyis ka'i man ngag gi yig skor du ma'i lung dang phyag khrid/

dkar bdud lcam dral dang / zhing skyong dur khrod kyi bdag po yab yum gnyis kyi man ngag gi yig skor gsar rnying so so'i lung yongs su rdzogs pa/ khyad par gnyan mgon chen
po'i man ngag mthar thug ha la nag po'i be'u bum ma yig bu yig dang bcas pa rnams thugs spro ba chen pos stsal cing / bla ma de rnams kyi gsung las/ sngon chos rgyal 'phags
pas/ dam pa kun dga' grags la chos skyong gi man ngag thun mong ma yin pa rnams gnang ba'i tshe/ 'di rnams nged rang gi tsha bo rnams la 'phrod par gyis gsungs pa bzhin/
dam pas kyang bla ma bdag nyid chen po kho na la gnang 'dug pa dang / dus phyis bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis kyang / rje rdo ring pa la de dang 'dra ba'i bka' stsal phebs
'dug kyang / bar skabs kyi zhal ngo phal cher la 'di skor gyi man ngag yongs rdzogs bzhugs pa

zhig ma byung 'dug mod/ khyed rang skal ba dang brtson 'grus 'dzoms pas/ gur zhal gtso bor gyur pa'i sa skya pa'i bstan srung dbang po rnams kyi chos skor zab mo mtha' dag
lus pa med par bum pa gang byo'i tshul du thob pa 'di ni/ bla ma gong ma rnams kyi thugs rje dang / mkha' 'gro chos skyong rnams kyis 'phrin las sgrub pa'i dge mtshan las
byung ba yin yang dag pas shin tu ngo mtshar zhing rjes su yi rang ba'i gnas so zhes gzengs bstod pa'i gsung gi bdud rtsis kyang kho bo cag gi yid la dga' bde'i dpal ci
yang zhig thob par mdzad pa yin la/ yang lo phu ba 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor gyi drung du yang sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin rdzong lugs nas brgyud pa'i chos skyong che chung
gi rjes gnang / bram ze mngags gtad/ 'di skor gyi man ngag du ma'i yig lung dang bcas pa yang thos pa lags so/ /

/ /dpal rdo rje nag po chen po'i zab mo'i chos skor rnams byung ba'i tshul legs par bshad pa bstan srung chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba bzhugs so// smad cha/Volume
II, ff. 1a-213b (1979 ed.)

de lta bu'i bla ma brgyud pa de rnams chos skyong la mnga' brnyes pa'i tshul sogs kyi rnam par thar ba mdo tsam bdag nyid chen po man chad ni gong du brjod zin pa de yin la/
da ni mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pa sogs nas/ rang gi rtsa ba'i bla ma rnams kyi bar gyi skyes chen de dag gi bstan srung dbang po rnams bran du 'khol zhing nus pa thon
pa'i tshul sogs kyi rnam thar cung zad brjod na/ de yang rje mkhas btsun pa nyid la byang pa bdag po rta dben pas/

zhabs 'dren chen po byas dus/ de la dmigs te da lta sa skya'i bzhi thog na bzhugs pa'i gur gyi mgon po'i 'bur sku lcam dral las mkhan pu trar bcas pa dang / mgon po rkyang
ba'i 'cham sku rnams ched gtad bzhengs nas 'phrin 'chol rab gnas mdzad pas/ de dang dus mtshungs par byang pa ta dben pa mngon sum du tshar bcad pas/ sku de la yang ding
sang gi bar du byang 'dul mgon por grags pa 'di yin zhing / chos rje bla ma dam pa ni chos rje khu dbon gyi rjes su sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud gcig la

mkhyen rab dang / gsan rgya sbyangs pa sogs 'gran zla dang bral bas/ rig gnas phyi nang mtha' dag la ma gsan pa'am/ mi mkhyen pa cung zad kyang med cing / de yang re re la
'di kho na la mkhas par 'dug snyam pa lta bu'i mkhyen rab yongs su rdzogs/ spyir chos skyong mtha' dag la mnga' brnyes shing / lhag par pu tra nyid bran du 'khol ba yin te/
nyid kyi gsung las/ pu tra 'di la gtor ma ster rin chog pa byung / nged dpon slob rnams dbus gtsang la rgyu 'grul gcig po byed pa la dgra jag dang chus khyer ba sogs gcig
kyang mi byung

ba kho'i drin yin/ bar chad phran tshegs tsam sel ba la'ang khos ma slebs pa gcig kyang med pas shin tu snying nye/ byin rlabs dang nus pa che bas sus bsten kyang de bzhin
yong ba yin zhes gsungs shing / gong ma rnams kyi skabs su mgon po'i gtor ma'i mdun du las mkhan la gtor ma chung ngu mdzad pa la/ ding sang zhal bzhi pa'i bskang gtor gyi
g.yas su pu tra la gtor ma che ba re mdzad pa 'di chos rje bla ma man gyi phyag len la byung ba yin no zhes kyang thos so/ /bla chen kun rgyal ba ni mkhyen rab phul du
byung bas rang gi rtsa ba'i bla ma 'gro mgon chos rje'i bka' 'bum rnams bsgrigs par mdzad cing / gsung 'bum de nyid kyi steng nas dbang

khrid lung man ngag rgyud bshad sogs rtsal 'don du gnang ba'i zhal slob kyi gtso bo yang / theg chen rin po che/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ shar pa sogs dge ba'i bshes gnyen che rags
mang du 'dus shing / chos skyong rnams kyang shin tu 'go bas nus pa'i mnga' bdag tu bzhugs so/ /'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan ni mkhyen pa'i blo gros/ so skye'i
blo'i spyod yul las 'das pas/ nyi ma gnyis la rtsa rgyud brtag gnyis tshegs med du mkhyen/ gdugs gcig la 'khor lo bde mchog gi sgrub dkyil thugs su chugs pas kun gyis 'jam
dbyangs chen por mtshan gsol/ bstan srung rnams kyis 'phrin las thogs med du bsgrubs pas mthu stobs che ba'i snyan pas phyogs kun tu khyab par gyur to/ /grub pa'i dbang
phyug rgya gar

shes rab rgyal mtshan ni/ yi dam rdo rje phur pa dang / chos skyong che chung la shin tu mnga' brnyes pas/ rje nyid khams phyogs su bstan 'gro'i don rgya chen po bsgrub pa
la phebs skabs/ la bag ma la zer ba'i la chen po yod pa'i lam bar thams cad kha ba pus nub tsam gyis khyab cing / la de nyid rang la gangs dpang thog so gsum tsam babs te
lam stor ba na/ bla ma 'dis chos skyong la 'phrin las bcol bas/ sang nyin nam mkha' glo bur du dwangs nas nyi ma shar te/ grwa pa rnams kyis lam dmigs btsal bas/ 'brong
gcig gi rmig rjes sha re 'dug pa rnyed nas/ rjes de la brtsad de dpon slob rnams kyis phebs pa'i tshe/ kha ba'i dpang shin tu mtho bas lam mi 'dra 'phrang ga dog po 'dra
bas/ de mthong ba tsam gyis kun gyi sems skrag par byed cing / de nas rim gyis phebs pa na 'brong sum cu tsam zhig la kha

na phar 'gro bas gangs thams cad phar gshags tshur gshags byed cing / rwa rtse rnams gnam la gzengs te/ mjug ma rnams sa la 'tshub se ba dang bcas song ba der yod rnams kyis
mthong bas/ kun kyang ha las shing chos skyong gi sprul par thag chod do/ /yang bdag chen 'di dge sding du bzhugs skabs shig rgya mdud dpon bzang sogs dam nyams 'dra'i
ngan rgyab sde dpon che ba 'gas byas nas/ dge sding gi mtha' la dmag sgar brgyab nas rje nyid bzhugs pa'i bla brang la chu bskor bcug pa'i zhabs 'dren mi 'tshams pa byas
pa na/ bla ma 'dis chos skyong la ra zla dang bcas na bza'i g.yab mo sdebs pa mdzad pas/ g.yag rgod nag po dar tshon can gnyis byung nas rwa rtses chu bskor bcug pa'i rdzing
chen po phyogs med du dbral bar byed pa dang bstun/ rje 'di'i thugs dam rgyun pa'i rten 'dod khams lha mo'i sku brnyan zhig yod pa des/ dmag sgar gyi mtha' la nyul zhing
/ bzhon pa bong

bu des kyang kun gyis tshor ba'i skad bton pas/ thams cad kyang rtog bcas su gyur cing / sgar nad mi zad pas btab ste dmag 'phral du zhig par gyur nas/ de dus lha mo'i sku
de'i zhal 'gram la rngul gron mo shar gyis byung bas da lta yang sku de la lha mo rngul ris mar grags shing dge sding mgon khang na bzhugs so/ /bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo
gros rgyal mtshan ni/ sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud gzhan rnams las kyang / chos skyong gi skor rnams la mkhas shing grub pa'i phul du phyin par yongs su grags shing don la
gnas pa bzhin/ de'i tshul cung zad ni gong du brjod zin la/ 'dir yang cha shas tsam spel na rje sa chen gyi rnam sprul yin pa'i gtan tshigs ni/ sngon mus chen sems dpa'
chen po dang mjal nas 'dod chos kyi gsol ba btab pa'i tshe/ bla chen sa skya pa'i rnam thar gyi dpe zhig phyag tu gnang nas

khyed rang gi chos rnams 'di na yod pas/ 'di nang bzhin nged rang gis gang thob 'bul lo gsungs pa dang / bse 'bag nag po 'phur shes dang lhan cig rgya gar nas byung ba'i bse'i
ga'u sgrub skor gyi man ngag bzhugs pa'i be'u bum de/ ding sang gang na yod dkar chag sogs na mi gsal ba la rje 'di'i gsung las/ sa chen zer ba'i bgres po des gter du
sbas pa yin pa 'dug ces gsungs pa sngon gyi skye ba dran pa'i gsung las gzhan du ma 'das pa dang / gzhan yang sgo rum dpe khang sogs kyi rje sa chen gyi phyag bris gang
yin thogs med du ngo mkhyen pa la/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen pos/ 'di ltar mkhyen pa'i rgyu mtshan gang lags zhus pas/ de'i rgyu mtshan shin tu che ba zhig yod/ de tsam
gyis chog gzhan la de 'dra'i bgros ye ma btang gsungs pa sogs rgyu mtshan du ma la brten the tshom med par nges so/ /zhes rje rdo ring pa chen po yang yang du gsungs par
grags shing /

lus dkyil gyi lha gzigs tshul ni/ dus lan cig gi tshe kha 'u'i chu tshan nang du thugs dam la mnyam par bzhag pa'i dus su rdo rje lus kyi dkyil 'khor gyi lha brgya lnga bcu
rtsa bdun lag mthil gyi ri mo ltar mngon sum du gzigs shing / de yang gsang gnas kyi lha tshogs cung zad mi gsal zhing / snying kha'i thugs rdo rje lha tshogs ched du gsal
zhing 'od zer mtha' yas pa zhig 'phro ba gcig 'dug pas nged rang la 'phrin las kyi rgyud 'dzin ha cang mi mang zhing / gang yod nges don la blo kha phyogs pa zhig yong
bar 'dug ces rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po la dngos su gsungs par snang ngo / /'di lta bu ni rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi thun mong ma yin pa'i man ngag las/ nang ma mthong
bar phyi ma mi thong / /zhes gsungs pa'i don/ lus rtsa'i dkyil 'khor lhag pa'i lhar mthong ba/ zag med sa dang po'i bden pa mngon du mdzad pa'i ltas thun mong ma yin

par snang bas/ shin tu ngo mtshar ba'i rnam thar du 'dug go /yang skabs shig gi tshe bzhi thog gi bla brang dmar mo'i bla ma mkhas btsun chen po'i thugs dam 'cham sku'i drung
du mgon po lha brgyad kyi rtag gtor la brten pa'i bsnyen pa mdzad pa'i tshe/ mgon po mngon sum du zhal gzigs pa'i phyag dpung g.yon gyi steng du me 'bar ba dang / g.yas
pa'i gri gug gi phyogs bzhi'i rwa med par dbus ma la me 'bar ma gcig gzigs snang la byung bas/ rin chen sgang pa la brten pa'i gdung brgyud nged rang sku mched gnyis ka
yin pa 'dra gsungs pa'ang bu slob grwa pa kun la gsung rgyun thor bur byon/ de phyin chad dus dang rnam pa thams cad du 'bral med du zhal gzigs par 'dug de dus kyi mgon
po che ba'i zhal gzigs ngo bo bkod pa'i sku dngos dang khyad par med pa'i bris sku khyad par can de/ ding sang rgyal mkhar rtse na bzhugs par snang / de bzhin du dpal ldan
lha mo 'dod khams kyi dbang phyug ma

'di'ang snga mo nas skabs skabs su zhal ston pa gcig 'dug gsungs pa phyag phyi ma ngos ma 'ga' la phebs pa dang / khyad par a gro'i dgon don grub gling du bzhugs pa'i tshe
mngon sum du zhal bstan nas 'khor gyi tshul bzung ba'i dam nyams gcig 'dug pa 'di ngas sgrol ba yin/ nga la'ang bskang gso gcig rtsoms gsungs pa la brten nas lha mo'i bskang
gso khyad par can 'di thugs rtsom yang gnang ba yin/ mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa'i sku dngos kyang zhal gzigs nas/ mgon po 'di dar nag po'i phod
ka bzhes pa zhig yod ces yang yang gsungs pa dang / lan cig skyed lhas mgon khang du mgon po 'di nyid bram ze dkar po'i rnam pa dang dkar pos gos byas/ phyag g.yas na rtse
gsum dang snying 'dzin pa/ g.yon na thod khrag 'dzin pa/ yum bzhi dang bcas pa mngon sum du

zhal gzigs/ de phyin chad mgon khang der phebs res kyis de 'dra'i rnam pa can du byas nas bsu ba la 'byon pa yin 'dug gzhan yang rgyun par gtor bsngo mdzad dus chos skyong
'khor bcas nam mkhar khra chab pe bzhugs pa la 'bul ba'i gzigs snang yong ba yin zhes thos/ dam can pu tra 'khor bcas ni rgyun par drung du gnas nas bran ltar las kun sgrub
pa yin 'dug pas/ lan cig rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po la rje'i zhal nas/ mdang pu tra 'dis mi gcig gi mgo dar gyis bgril ba khur nas 'ur sgra dang bcas te sgo rum la
song gsung ba byung 'dug skyed lhas su sde dpon 'ga' zhig gi gtor gsos 'ong dus/ bsgrub khang sum cu rtsa gsum gyi steng du sngags pa nag po thod phreng 'dzin pa gcig gis
ma Ni bskul ba'i 'cham gdangs byas pa na/ kha'u'i lung pa thams cad 'dar ling ling 'ong gi 'dug gsungs pa dang / skyed lhas

rgyal po 'di mgon po'i 'khor gyi ru 'dren gcig yin pa 'dra/ lha 'dre gzhan 'di tsho skyed lhas mgon khang gi nang du ye 'ong mi nus par 'dug na'ang / 'di thal mar 'ong gin
'dug skyed lhas kyi shing phung re re'i rtsa ba na'ang mgon po'i 'khor du gtogs pa'i lha 'dre gdug pa can stobs chen po re re gnas pa yin gsungs pa sogs 'od gsal gyi ngang
nas thams cad thogs med du gzigs pa yin 'dug bstan srung rnams la ji ltar bsgo ba'i bka' rnams kyang thogs med du bsgrub par snang ste/ lan gcig skyed lhas mgon khang du
mgon po 'khor bcas las la bskul ba'i thugs dam zhag bdun gyi bar du gnang ba na/ yum chen sring mo bzhi po khrag gi ral pa shin tu ring ba dang bcas mgon khang du phebs
las grub yod pas gtang rag dgos zer yus pa'i tshul du ral pa dkrugs pa'i khrag gi 'thor ma rje rang gi sku lus la yang thor thor yong ba dang / de nas ma tshad phyin pa
na/ bsgral

ba'i byad ma mgo la gser gyi dbu rgyan gon pa byad mdangs med cing cung zad ser ba ngo gnong ba'i rnam pas 'dug pa gzigs shing las mthar phyin par grub pa dang / yang dus phyis
gal che ba gcig gi dus mgon po 'khor bcas las la bskul ba las de mthar phyin par grub pa'i tshe/ gzigs snang la lung pa shin tu yangs pa zhig gi dkyil na tshur mgon
po nyid mi dpon chen po'i tshul byas rta nag po zhig la chibs/ phyag g.yas pas mdung bskor mdzad cing / 'dun ma len na 'di bzhin len pa yin gsungs nas zhal pho 'don pa'i
rnam pa mdzad cing 'byon pa gzigs/ skyed lhas su sku mtshams dam por bzhugs pa'i skabs shig tu 'byung po chen po gcig dge bshes kyi chas su byas snam sbyar ber thul sogs
brtsegs ma mang rab gyon/ lag tu gtor ma khyer 'khor stobs che ba dang bcas kha 'u'i gzhung lam la zhugs/

phyag 'tshal sgang du slebs pa na 'phags pa brag khung gi gtor khang ldebs la dpal mgon chen po'i sku bram gzugs rje rang gi phyag bris ma gcig bkram yod pa las/ 'od zer sngo
nag phyogs mtshams kun tu 'phro ba dang dus mnyam du mi rkang gi gling bu'i sgra skad shin tu che ba grag pa gcig bus byung pas/ skad cig de nyid la bar snang la sprin
nag po 'khrigs/ 'byung po yod pa'i sa der thog ser shin tu drag pa gcig babs song bas/ 'byung po 'khor bcas gar song cha med du song ba byung / de dus kyi bris sku de'ang
phyis rgyal mkhar rtse pa la gnang nas yod do/ /lan gcig nor bu khyung rtser phebs pa'i tshe/ chos rje rkyang 'dur ba dpon slob dang gzim khang steng 'og tu mdzad nas bzhugs/
rje dpon slob rnams kyis tshoms 'og tu chos skyong rnams las la bskul ba'i rol mo drag brdungs mdzad pa na/ steng du chos rje rkyang 'dur ba'i dgongs pa la/

mtshan nyid pa rgan po'i skyon gyis bslad pas rnga brdung 'di la rang 'byung chen po med dam snyam pa byung / de nas cung zad song ba'i dus chos rje rkyang 'dur ba'i gzigs
snang la sprul pa'i mi nag khyi nag bya nag sogs pho nya mang pos 'byung po chen po snam sbyar ta hun gser ma thang thebs gyon pa dang bcas pa'i ske nas zhags pas bzung /
lag pa bsdams pa gcig dkar khung gi mthong ga nas tshoms chen 'og ma'i 'brub khung nang du thogs med du khrid song ba gzigs/ zhag gcig song rjes phyir shor song / dgongs
thun gyi thugs dam gyi tshe/ slar yang gong bzhin khrid nas mthu dang stobs med par dam la thogs pa gzigs/ skabs gcig gi tshe/ rje 'di nyid rgyal rtse nas gdan sa phyogs
la phebs pa'i dus/ khong pa'i mnal lam du sgo rum gdong gi thad na yar rta pa gcig gi sna a tsa ra dung long can gcig gis byas byung ba rmis pas/ sang phyag phyi /

ba rnams la mdang rmi lam 'di ltar byung / de ring mgron po su 'dra zhig 'ong ngam gsung ba'i de ma thag rje 'di nyid bde ba can du phebs byung zhes thos pa dang / bla ma 'dis
bsgrigs par mdzad pa'i mgon pod kyi phyag dpe la me 'bar tshul ni/ gzim dpon nam shes grogs mched kyis phyag dpe mgon pod chen po rgyal rtse nas blangs te/ sa skyar 'ong
pa'i lam zho nga'i mdar chom rkun pa 'ga' zhig gis bcom ste/ sde pas phul ba'i gsol ja dang bcas pa khong rnams kyis khyer nas yul du phyin pa na/ yul der mi 'dod pa'i
ltas sna tshogs byung zhing / khyad par phyag dpe gang du bzhag sar me 'bar bas/ khong rnams kyis gnyer cag ma nus par ra sa rdzong pa'i lag tu byung / der yang cho 'phrul
sna tshogs byung ste/ rnam rtog gi ngang du yod pa na/ re zhig nas sman grong drung rdor ba der byon pa'i dus/ de bzhin gyi gsung gleng byung bas rje'i phyag dpe yin
par nges /

te/ rdzong pa dngos kyis 'bul ma nus par drung rdor ba brgyud nas phul/ de phyin mgon pod de nyid ding sang gi bar gyi bu phyi yang phyi dang bcas pa rnams la mgon pod me 'bar
mar grags pa 'di byung / de lta bu'i bdag chen gyi phyag dpe dngos de dus phyis rgyal rtse ba'i zhal ngo mkhan chen 'phags pa tshul khrims pa'i phyag brgyud de kho bo'i
lag tu rtsol med du byung ba deng sang dpal sa skyar bzhugs pa 'di yin zhing / dpal 'khor bde chen du gsung ngag zab bshad gnang ba gcig gi dus/ tho rangs ka cig dpal
mgon chen po bram ze'i gzugs kyis/ mi 'di kha brdar drags 'dug pas na ru 'ong bar 'dug gsungs pa'i snang ba zhig byung bas/ de nub nas zhag 'ga' yar gyi bar khrag 'khrus
la brten pa'i sku khams mi bde ba byung pas/ mgon po chos la gces spras byed pa'i 'khu ldog tu dgongs nas/ de la dmigs pa'i mchod gtor phul /

bas/ sku khams legs par dwangs pa dang / yang skabs shig gi tshe gnas gsar ba'i gzhis rin chen sgang du phebs dus/ khong rnams kyis rtsis mgon gyi lha mo la bskang mdos phul
ba'i tshe/ rje nyid kyis khyod kyi lha mo la bskang mdos yang yang dgos pa 'di 'dra lkog pa la gsungs pas/ lha mo de cung zad ma mnyes par/ de nub tho rangs rje thugs dam
la bzhugs pa'i yun du shin tu 'jigs pa'i cha lugs su bstan nas byon pa na bar chad bya bar ni ma nus/ rnal 'byor pa lta ba la sbyangs 'dug gsungs/ zhal cung zad 'dzum
pa dang bcas nas de nyid du mi snang bar gyur/ gzhan yang 'od gsal gyi gzigs snang la thog bcas kyi dngos po sgrib mi nus par ji lta ba thams cad gzigs par snang ste/ lan
cig sa skyar bla brang shar na gsung chos gnang ba'i dus/ rgya 'dre dpon g.yog rnams sa skya'i nye skor na sgar brgyab/ skabs su dpon po de'i /

thog tu gdugs nyi 'og tu slebs pa tsam byas/ sa skya la skor ba phyin ci log thengs re byas dus rgyag 'dre mi bsad sogs yong ba zhig 'dug pa la/ rje 'di nyid kyis thugs dam
lta ba'i ngang nas mi dmigs mang du gnang bas/ zhag 'ga' nas gsung chos pa rnams phyir 'gro ba dang mnyam du mi sog po'i rnam pa can 'jigs su rung ba lus po kun la mes tshig
pa'i ri mo yod pa zhig rje'i drung du thogs med du byung nas zhabs dbang zhig gnang dgos zhu ba la/ khyod su yin gsungs pas/ bdag rgya 'dre'i dpon 'og ma drag shos yin/
kha sang nas khyed kyis dmigs pa mdzad pa des nged thams cad tshig da lan dpon po na drag sku mdun yong ma thub/ da nged rnams 'gro bas thugs dam glod dgos zer/ 'di la
zhabs dbang mi dga' 'am dgongs tsa na/ khos zhabs 'og tu mgo bcug nas khyed kyi slob ma brgyud 'dzin dang bcas pa la mi gnod pa'i dam bca' 'bul/ khyed nam sangs rgyas pa'i
dus nga 'khor /

gyi thog mar skye bar shog zer nas 'ja' yal ba ltar song ba dang / yang rje nyid mkhas grub gung ru shes rab bzang po la sogs pa dam pa mang pos zhabs kyis bcags shing byin
brlabs pa'i gnas/ rgyab ri dkar po zhes bya ba'i ngos dpal ldan rtser sku mtshams zla ba bdun tsam mdzad/ de'i tshe rgyal gyi phu na yod pa'i rnal 'byor pa bzang por byas
pa gcig gi nyams snang la/ dpal ldan rtse'i gzim khang gi mthar du ba sngo 'khyil le bas bskor ba'i gseb na a tsa ra dung long can zhig skor ba byed pa'i mthong snang byung
'dug cing / rje nyid kyi zhal nas kyang / gnas 'di phun sum tshogs pa gcig 'dug chos skyong srung ma rnams skyed lhas su 'byon pa bzhin 'dir yang phebs kyin 'dug gsungs
pa de/ rim bzhin brgyud de smon mkhar ba rnams kyis gsan te/ de mthun gsol ba btab pas gnas der mgon khang gi bkod pa /

dang / de'i dbus su mgon po'i sku rje nyid kyi phyag nas bzhugs pa gtor tshogs dang bcas pa zhal bkod gnang / de la mchod gtor 'bul zhing thugs dam bskul ba'i sngags 'chang
bzhi sde tsam gyi zhabs tog bdag rkyen yang smon mkhar nas mdzad/ dus der rje nyid kyi snyan grags kyis khams gtsang dbus gsum gyi grwa pa sbyin bdag bsam gyis mi khyab
pa phyogs mtha' dag nas dbyar gyi char sprin ltar 'dus shing / gang la gang 'os kyi chos kyi 'khor lo nam mkha'i mtha' klas pa bskor bas/ bstan pa spyi dang / khyad par dpal
ldan sa skya pa'i bstan pa rin po che sa phyogs der nam langs shing nyi ma shar ba ltar ches cher gsal bar mdzad pa na/ gzhan dag gi khrod nas shin tu mi mthun zhing
phrag dog gis myos pa'i rang dbang mi thub pa zhig chos rje smon lam pa yin/ gis/ ngan g.yo'i sbyor ba mngon mtshan can 'ga' byas shing / ding sang na lendra na yang /

sa skya'i btsun chung tshe zad gcig slebs yod pa 'dug zer ba sogs rlom sems kyi tshig ngan sna tshogs 'brug ltar sgrog pa'i tshe/ de dag la thugs brtse ba chen pos nye bar
dgongs nas/ rje nyid kyi gnas der ched du gtad pa'i thugs dam mdzad cing / de mthun rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po la'ang bka' lung phebs nas/ tro sa'i phug chen du mgon po'i
gtor chen mdzad pa'i tshe/ nub gcig gi mnal lam na/ phug pa'i rtsa bar nged 'di lta bu'i mi drag pa rang bcu gnyis shi zer ba'i ngud mo'i sgra chen po lhang lhang pa
byung / rje 'di nyid kyi thugs dam gyi nyams la mgon po'i las mkhan rnams kyis gser gyi mchod rten chen po 'od 'bar ba zhig byung nas dum bur gtub kyin 'dug pas/ nang thams
cad sol ba dang lhwam krad kyi dum bus brgyangs 'dug pa gcig byung / de'i tshe dgun shin tu grang pa'i dus yin kyang nam phyed zin la khad pa tsam gyi tshod la/ dpal ldan
/

sa skya'i bstan srung dbang po rnams kyi cho 'phrul sprin nag po 'jigs su rung ba dpag tu med pa glo bur du nam mkha' la 'dus/ skyid 'phan gnyis char du tshor ba'i 'brug gi
sgra shin tu drag pa/ glog gi 'od drag po 'khyug pa dang bcas pa'i dus/ rbod gtong byed pa'i byad ma de'i mgo la gnam lcags kyi thog chen po mi zad pa phab ste/ las ngan
gyi sbyor ba byed pa'i lus dang phral nas sems nyid dag pa'i zhing du skad cig nyid la spor bar mdzad do/ /de nas de'i 'khor du gtogs pa'i mi dang mi ma yin thams cad ni
bsam pa ma grub pa'i mya ngan gyis non zhing 'gyod pa dang bcas pa'i ngud mo'i sgra chen pos phyogs de thams cad khyab par byas so/ /yang mus chen sems dpa' chen po'i lung
bstan bzhin rje 'di'i khams phyogs la phebs pa'i tshe/ sngon gcen rin po che bdag chen rgya gar bas btab pa'i dgon pa don grub gling zhes bya bar spyan drangs te phebs
pa na/ dus phyis sa phyogs der sa skya /

pa'i gdung brgyud sogs 'byon bzhud nyung ba'i stabs kyis/ mi bdag bdag tu re ba'i rlom sems can/ yul de nas pha tshad phyin pa na karma pa'i sgar pa dpon slob tshan gcig 'dug
pa rnams kyis/ rje nyid der phebs pa la phrag dog gis kun nas bslangs pa'i skur zhus sogs mi dad pa'i rnam 'gyur mang po byas pas/ der gnas pa'i grwa pa rnams kyis ma
bzod de/ sa skya pa mthu'i bdag po yin zer bas/ da lan bstan pa la dgongs nas cis kyang 'di rnams la mthu'i rtags thon pa zhig mdzad dgos/ de phyin ma mdzad na phyin chad
phyogs 'dir sa skya pa'i sgra mi grag pa zhig yong zhes yang yang nan tan bskyed de zhus pa la brten nas/ khong rnams la zhag bdun gyi dus btab nas/ dpon slob bdun gyis
pu tra la brten pa'i las sbyor zhig mdzad pa na/ zhag gsum song ba'i nub mo sgrub khang du 'od 'khyug pa dang / thog tsheg pa dang / 'brub khung du /

ling ga skad ngan 'don pa sogs nang rtags kyi cho 'phrul sna tshogs byung zhing / de'i dus karma pa'i sgar de'i dpon 'og ma bka' gros pa rje nyid la skur zhus byed pa'i gtso
bo gcig yod pa de rgyu ma rul nas nyam thag pa'i skad 'don zhing tshe'i dus byas/ de ltar drag po'i las sbyor gyi rtags mngon sum mthong ba la brten nas sgar pa gzhan rnams
kyang gar 'bros cha med du gyur cing / rje dpon slob rnams la dgra rkun la sogs pa'i 'jigs pa mtha' dag dang bral zhing / snyan pa'i grags pas sa'i steng thams cad khyab
par gyur nas smar khams phyogs la thegs pa'i lam la rma chu gtsang po zhes bya ba'i chu klung shin tu che ba zhig yod pa'i 'gram du sgar pa sngon ma rnams kyis slebs
nas de nub de kar sdod rtsis byas pa na/ rje'i zhal snga nas rjes su phebs te/ da lta chu la 'gro grab gyis phebs pa na/ phyag phyi ba rnams kyis mgrin gcig tu/ do nub thams
cad thang yang chad/ nyi ma yang /

phyi mor song 'dug pas 'di kar bzhugs na legs pa 'dra zhes nan gyis zhus kyang ma gsan par/ da lta 'gro grab gyis gsungs shing / mchod g.yog pa nam shes la mgon po'i gtor ma
gcig da lta 'chos la chu 'di la rgyobs gsungs pa'i bka' lung mdzad pa na/ khong gis kyang de bzhin byas pas/ chu la che chung du mngon pa ci yang ma byung / de rjes rje
nyid kyis gtor ma gcig chu la brgyab pa gnang ba na/ lcags kyi tho lum me 'bar ba chur 'phangs pa lta bu'i sgra 'jigs su rung ba byung zhing / chu de yang de ma thag nas
gsum gnyis 'phri ba tsam du song / der rje rang gis chu de la sngon la phebs shing / de rjes sgar pa gzhan rnams kyang bar chad med par chu'i pha rol tu slebs pa tsam na/
chu sngar bas kyang bcu 'gyur gyi che ba tsam du song bas sgar pa thams cad 'jigs shing skrag la ngo mtshar zhing blo bde bar gyur/ rje'i gsung las/ da mgon po la gtang
rag gi mchod gtor phul/ thams /

cad ja skol blo bde bar thungs gsungs pa'i bka' lung phebs/ de'i rgyu mtshan yul phyogs de na gnas pa'i skye bo rnams kyis thos pa na/ sngar rma chu gtsang po la sus kyang
rab ma thon pa la/ da lan 'di 'dra ba'i rab 'don pa 'di su zhig yin nam zhes thams cad 'jigs shing ha las nas ngo mtshar ba'i gtam du gleng bar byed do/ /de nas yul phyogs
gzhan zhig tu phebs pa na chos la mi mos pa'i bon po gdug pa can 'ga' zhig gis sngar gyi lo rgyus rnams thos pas zhe 'jigs kyang / phrag dog gi dbang gis sems la rang dbang
ma thob par dpon slob rnams la tho 'tsham pa'i sems kyis sngar thog lam rgyun par yod pa'i sa cha shin tu gnyan pa sus kyang sdod mi nus pa zhig tu sgar pa khungs bstan/
der dpon slob rnams kyis bzhugs pa na/ srod thum pa nas sprin nag 'dus 'brug sgra shin tu drag pa dang / glog phreng rgyun mi 'chad pa tho rangs kyi cha zin gyi bar
mu ma chad /

par byung zhing / mi ma yin gyi cho 'phrul sbal pa nag po shin tu che ba 'jigs su rung ba cig cha ther gyi nang du byung ba la/ rje nyid kyis khro bcu'i srung 'khor dang /
bde mchog gi go cha drug la brten pa'i srung 'khor gdug rtsub kyi sbyor ba ma zhi bar du mdzad cing / phyag phyi ba rnams kyis sbal pa bsgral bas/ de nas zhag 'ga' yar gyi
bar gang phebs sar sprin nag po bya ra byed pa'i rnam pa byung ba de zhag re bzhin phar 'gyang phar 'gyang song zhing / thog la sogs pa'i bar chad kyi rnam pa gang yang
ma byung bas/ sa phyogs de skor na yod pa'i bla dpon mi dpon bon po sogs thams cad gnas 'dir bzhugs tshugs pa 'di pa dpon slob las ma byung zer/ kun ha las shing dad pa
thun mong ma yin pa skyes nas zhabs tog kyang phun sum tshogs par bsgrubs/ de la sogs pa mthu stobs nus pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i snyan grags kyis bon po gdug pa can /

rnams dang / gzhan yang grub mtha' mi gcig pa'i gang zag thams cad kyang tho 'tsham pa'i spros pa chod cing / ngo mtshar ba'i gnas su 'dzin pas dpal ldan sa skya pa'i bstan
pa phyogs der nam langs shing nyi ma shar ba lta bur gyur/ de lta bu'i ngo mtshar ba'i rnam par thar pa du ma'i mnga' bdag bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan
'dis ni mgon po'i man ngag gi glegs bam bsgrigs par mdzad pa sogs sa skya pa'i chos skyong skor la brgyud pa'i bla ma gzhan rnams las rgyu mtshan du ma'i sgo nas bka' drin
mchog tu che ba zhig yin zhing / bdag chen 'dis kha'u skyed lhas kyi dgon pa'i sum cu rtsa gsum gyi sgrub khang du yun ring bzhugs nas chos skyong che chung gi man ngag
sogs la 'chad nyan rtsal ston mdzad pas ding sang sa skya tshad kyi rna bar ma grag pa'i kha'u pa'i snyan brgyud kyi man ngag zab mo zhes kun la med pa'i g.yer chos su
/

mdzad pa 'di byung ba yin no/ /yang sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin kun gyi gtsug rgyan/ rgyal ba'i lung bstan brnyes pa'i skyes chen dam pa ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang
po ni/ yongs grags kyi yab sa skya ba'i gsol ja ba'i brgyud pa gci khung sgo pa nye gnas grub pa yon tan yin par bshad kyang / don gyi yab ni bzhi thog pa bdag chen kun
dga' rin chen yin par srad pa kun blo sogs kyis mdzad pa'i rnam thar las 'byung ba bzhin don la gnas pas/ sa skya pa'i chos skyong rnams kyang gdung brgyud rnams dang khyad
par med par 'go ba yin te/ sku gzhon nu'i tshe thos bsam mdzad dus bla brang shar na bzhugs pa'i mdo sde la chos rje sa paN gyis mchan btab pa sogs phyag dpe po ti drug
brgya brgyad cu lhag pa tsam/ dgu rim na chos rje sa paN gyi dpe khang gi phyag dpe rnams la res dpe khang dang / res 'ga' /

gzim khang du gdan drangs nas lo gsum gyi bar du po ti sum stong zin tsam la gzigs pas/ gsung rab spyi dang bye brag gi don la thugs skyed ches che bar byung zhing / gzhan
yang brang mo che/ zur khang / gung bla brang sogs gdan sa chen po'i dpe khang so so'i phyag dpe thams cad kyang ma gzigs pa med cing / mdor na thos pa dang gzigs rgya che
zhing mthar phyin par gyur te/ de lta bu'i bar skabs shig tu chos skyong gi grub thob sngags 'chang kun dga' zla bas brtag gnyis kyi TIkka lo spe rdor bsod ma'i stod sku
drung du phul nas/ pu tra na re 'di bla ma kun dga' bzang po la phul na/ smad khong gis rnyed zer gyin gda' bas khyed la phul ba lags zer nas phul/ de rjes lo gcig gi khongs
su de'i smad bla brang brang mo che'i dpe gseb nas rnyed nas 'grig par byung bas kun gyi ngo mtshar du gyur pa dang / yang sa skyar bzhugs dus gzhan gyis byad ka byas
pa'i cho 'phrul /

ngan pa sna tshogs byung par/ gur mgon gyi srung 'khor la nan tan mdzad pas bzlogs pa dang / ngor e waM chos ldan btab nas rdo rje 'phreng ba'i dkyil 'khor yongs su rdzogs
pa bzhengs par dgongs pa na/ bal po'i lha bzo ba wang ku li spun la sogs pa mkhas pa drug yong pa'i gtam yang med par glo bur du sku mdun du slebs nas/ ji ltar dgongs pa'i
dkyil 'khor rnams dang / gzhan yang thugs dam gyi rigs mtha' yas pa 'bad med du grub pa'i/ lha bzo ba a khe rA dza zhes bya ba zhig yod pa na re/ nged 'di rnams phan tshun
gcig gis gcig la gleng ba ma yin par thams cad bod du bla ma 'phags pa'i bu can 'gro zhes phyogs gcig tu gros 'cham ste bod du yong ba'i tshe/ la stod shel dkar dang
/ chu 'dus dang / sa skya rnams su khyed rang rnams 'di tso ru las ka byas na/ yon rdzong legs po ster zer yang / de tsho gang du yang sdod ma 'dod /

cing / gnas po mi nyeg gcig yod pa na re/ khyed rang e tsa khar phyin nas las ka byas na yon rdzong thams cad gser du yong pas/ 'gro na ngas bskyal zer yang 'gro ma 'dod par
bla ma'i drung du zangs slebs pa 'di/ bla mas sgom byas pa nged kyi snying la phog pa yin mod ces zer te/ chos skyong gis rang dbang med par bkug pa yin no/ /yang sa skyar
bzhugs dus gur mgon lcam dral dang zhal bzhi pa rnams la bstod pa re mdzad pas/ nub gcig pu tra na re/ nga la yang bstod pa byed dgos zer/ de'i bstod pa yang mdzad cing
/ dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur gzigs pa dang / gzhan yang pu tra na re/ sngags 'chang kun dga' zla ba ni mi sdod par 'dug nga la gtor ma zur du ster dgos zer ba dang / gser sku
chen mo bzhengs dus lha bzo ba'i rmi lam du a tsa ra rna ba la dung long btags pa gcig 'ongs nas/ nged kyi lha bzo la yong dgos zer khrid phyin pa rmis/ rmi lam /

ngan nas rim gro byed pa'i grab byas pas/ de'i zhag lha bzo ba 'bod mkhan mnga' ris pa dbon po a tsa ra grogs mched gsum gyis slebs pas/ sa skya'i chos skyong gi rnam 'phrul
du shes pa dang / las mgon rnams res 'ga' las bsgrubs kyang gtang rag ma byung zhes 'khang ba dang / res 'ga' khyed kyis ma bcol ba yang nga rang gis byas pa yin zhes kha
pho 'don pa dang / lam 'bras brgyud pa'i bla ma'i sku 'dra rnams bzhengs/ spra rtsi btab ste thang dkyil du bzhugs pa la mtshan mo mon dung long btags pa gcig byung nas/
dpon lha bzo ba la myur du longs/ lder sku rnams ka drug mar spyan 'dren gyis zer ba de ltar byas nas yun mi ring pa nas drag char chen po byung ngo / /khyad par e wa~M
chos ldan gyi dgon pa'i gnyer dang bstan srung ni chos skyong zhal bzhi pas byed pa yin zhing / 'di'i rjes gnang yang gdan sa pa nang rgyud du ma byung na chos skyong nyid
mi mnyes pa'i tshul ston pa /

yin te/ de yang mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen e wa~M gdan sar phebs nas/ rje yongs 'dzin nyid gzim khang thar ba rtser sku mtshams la bzhugs dus tshes brgyad gcig gi nyin yongs
'dzin gyi gsung las/ lha mchog seng ge chos rje sangs rgyas rin chen pas khri thog mdzad pa'i nyin man nas/ tshogs dung 'di la skad sngar dang gtan nas mi 'dra ba rang
zhig byung bas nyon gsungs nas gsan pas/ skad 'dzer 'dzer rang gi skad dung gnyis sbrags nas bus pa'i dbyibs shig byung / gzhan la rtsad bcad pas kyang / de bzhin rang
'dug zer/ 'di ltar 'dug lags zhus pas/ khyod da lta rang song la chos rje sangs rgyas rin chen pa la khyed kyis dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa'i rjes gnang su la thob dris shog
gsungs nas/ rje tshogs na bzhugs pa'i snyan du phul bas/ sngon sa skyar chos dbar la phyin dus gnam kha 'ub pa'i gdung brgyud la yang zhus/ phyis 'bras yul du chos rje drung
btsun pa la thob /

gsungs pa'i tshul phul bas/ de ka yin pa 'dug sngon kun mkhyen rin po ches kyang chos rje sangs rgyas rin chen pa la 'phrod par gyis gsungs pa'i bka' lung yang yod pas/ dge
'dun rnams 'du khang na yod ring la 'gro gsungs nas dbang khang du phebs/ de nub dpal mgon gyi rjes gnang rje sangs rgyas rin chen pa sku rkyang la gnang / khyed kyis lha
mchog seng ge la skabs su bab dus 'phrod nges mdzod cig ces gdams so/ /de'i phyi nyin man tshogs dung skad sngar kho na ltar byung bas kun kyang ngo mtshar du 'dzin pa
byung ngo zhes thos la/ yang ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi bla ma grub chen buddha shrI la yang chos skyong rnams shin tu mches pa yin te/ dus shig zhe dgon pa'i g.yag bdun
rkun mas khyer 'dug pa/ de nub gtor ma bsngo ba'i skabs su/ mon bu pu tra g.yag de rnams ma shi ba gyis/ rkun ma rnams srog la gnod pa ma skyel/ tsham rngam gyis la 'jigs
/

su chug ces gsung skad chen pos lan gsum gsung gin snang / phyis zhag gsum song dus/ 'jigs med zer ba'i spyi pa gcig 'dug pa de la/ chu 'og pa'i mi gcig na re/ khyed kyi g.yag
bor ba de nged kha cig gis rnyed yod pas 'bul zer/ gtam mang du byas pas/ bla ma'i byin rlabs dang / chos skyong gi gtor dbang dgos/ phyis chos skyong gis gnod pa mi
'ong ba'i srung 'khor dgos zer nas g.yag bdun ga bskyal yod 'dug pas/ cho 'phrul 'ga' zhig byung bar snang ngo / /dbon po shes rab seng ge la khong nad mthug po zhig yod
pa la gcod kyi dmigs pa 'dra byed du bcug pas cher ma phan pa/ 'byung po gcig gi bar chad zhig yin pa 'dra/ gur mgon gyi rjes gnang zhig zhus gsungs/ nyi shu dgu gcig la
zhus pas/ bka' bsgo byed pa'i dus su 'di'i bar chad zhi bar gyis gsungs pa'i tshe mus nyams byung ste/ rdo rje skyil krung du bzhugs bzhin pa la gtor /

ma phyag tu bzung nas 'phar te khong gi lus steng du 'phags pa byung / de kas nad gzhi de las grol lo/ /de la sogs pa ji ltar bka' bsgo ba bzhin sgrub pa'i lo rgyus mang du
snang ngo / /stag gi lo la da lo sa skyar 'gro/ da lan las mi sleb gsungs nas byon/ sa skya sa bzang gnyis su zla ba dgu bzhugs/ de'i tshe sgo rum du dpal rdo rje nag po
chen po'i sku la shel rgyan dang / na bza' dang / gtor ma cod paN mang po phul nas gsol ba btab pas/ sa skya pa cung drag tu 'gro ba'i rten 'brel zhig 'dug gsungs pa'i lung
bstan yang stsal/ 'di ni dus phyis sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i thugs sras sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen yab sras nas bzung / dpal sa skya'i
sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pa'i lugs gnyis kyi 'phrin las kyi rgyun yar ngo'i zla ba ltar 'phel rgyas su gyur pa 'di ma 'ongs mkhyen pa'i

gsung du snang bas shin tu ngo mtshar ba'i gnas so/ /yang ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi thugs sras rgyal tshab dam pa mus chen sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyis
sa skya pa'i nges don gyi bstan pa dar ba'i gnas gling dga' bde ba can gyi dgon gnas chen po ma bu rnams btab cing bshad sgrub spel mar mdzad pas/ chos skyong rnams kyis
zhal bstan cing 'phrin las bsgrubs pa'i tshul ni/ rje nyid kyi thugs dam rgyun pa'i rten mgon po'i bris thang zhig yod pa la phyag mdzub gtad nas/ nga'i dgon pa bde ba can
gyi chos skyong 'di la gnas pa yin no zhes gsungs 'dug pa ni/ gur mgon 'khor bcas kyis zhal dngos su bstan nas bris sku de la thim pa'i gzigs snang shar ba'i gsung du snang
ba dang / las thams cad chos skyong gis mdzad pas sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin gyi 'phrin las kyi rgyun zhig la mus chen sems dpa' chen po'i 'phrin las kyi rgyun las bzang
ba med de sa skya pa'i srol 'dzin

yod do cog la rje 'di'i 'phrin las kyi rgyun gyis ma khyab pa med ces bdag gi bla ma mus pa chen pos yang yang du gsungs pa ni don la gnas par mthong zhing / yang sems dpa'
chen po'i dngos slob grub chen dkon mchog blo gros nyid bsam gtan phug tu sku mtshams la bzhugs pa'i dus shig gzim mal du nyin gung gi thun la bzhugs yod pa'i mdun na/ gong
gi sems dpa' chen po'i thugs dam rten mgon po'i bris sku de bkram yod pas/ de'i zhabs 'og na yul pa'i grong pa gcig gi bu spun gnyis kyi mgo bo bcug 'dug pa mngon sum
du gzigs/ 'khrul pa yin nam ci yin dgongs na'ang de bzhin du 'dug de nas zhag 'ga' yar na/ mi tshang de pa la na tsha ngan pa zhugs te/ phru gu de gnyis dus gcig la shi
'dug pa rjes su dgongs pas/ bsrung ri'i khongs su ri dwags rngon pa 'dras la 'ju byas te/ chos skyong la mna' zos pa'i 'khu ldog tu

'dug gsungs pa yang / sa skya'i chos skyong rnams kyis rje sems dpa' chen po'i bka' las cung zad kyang mi 'da' ba'i shin tu rmad du byung ba'i rnam thar du snang / rgyal tshab
dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug la yang bstan srung 'di rnams mchog tu 'go bas/ zhal bzhugs dus e wa~M chos ldan gyi lugs gnyis dar rgyas kyang shin tu che bas 'phrin las
mtha' dag chos skyong gis bsgrubs par grags shing / mya ngan las 'das pa'i tshe yang sku gdung bzhugs pa'i mchod khang la pu tra sogs dkon gnyer gyi tshul du 'bral med du
gnas pa glo bo mkhan chen gyi gzigs snang la shar ba sogs mtha' yas shing / sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i gsal byed dam pa kun mkhyen chos kyi rgyal po bsod nams seng ge la bka'
srung rnams kyis 'phrin las bsgrubs pa'i tshul ni/ rje kun mkhyen nyid rta nag gser gling du bzhugs pa'i nub gcig chos khrims pas zhal ta zhig zhu ru phyin pas/ khyod
yong pa sngas

byung / mi nag po dung lo btags pa pu tra yin nam snyam pa gcig dngos su byung nas lab lab 'ga' byed grab yod pas/ da yal song gsungs pa dang / kha 'ur gtor sgrub bskang gso
gcig mdzad pa'i tshe/ gdong bzhi pa'i gtor ma'i ba dan de nyid rje'i phyogs su mgo dud nas 'dug pa dang / thub bstan du bzhugs pa'i dus nub cig mnal lam du mon pa phrug
gu gnyis skyed lhas kyi brag phug yin snyam pa gcig na 'dug pa/ sku 'khor ba yod pa 'dra la/ 'di tsho gdong bzhi pa'i sprul pa bram ze'i gzugs can yin tshod du 'dug gsungs
pas/ mon pa gnyis po de mgo gug gug kha 'dzum 'dzum byed/ 'o na khyed ye shes kyi mgon po yin pas mngon shes la thogs pa med tsa na/ tshe mjug la sgrub pa rtse gcig byas
na dga'am/ bshad pa byas na dga' gsungs pas/ de gnyis sgrub pa sgrub pa zhes

brjod nas mgo ril ril/ kha 'dzum 'dzum song ba rmis gsungs/ tshad ma'i spyi don rtsom pa'i tshe mnal lam du bla ma blo rin pa dang gnyis kyis bstod pa mi rtog ma la dbyangs
dang bcas 'then pas/ lung pa'i phu nas rol mo dang / 'od zer gyi tshogs du ma dang / dmag dpung du ma yong ba'i snang ba byung / ci yin dris pas/ dpal mgon gdong bzhi pa'i
dpung gi tshogs yin zer/ bltas pas zhabs kyi pus mo man chad kyi dpang la thog gsum tsam 'dug 'khor rnams go cha'i 'od lhag lhag lham gyi 'bur rnams ni khrom khrom 'dug
khyod kyi bstan bcos 'di'i bdag po nged tshos byed do gsungs pa byung ba dang / kun mkhyen nam bsod chen mo'i mnal lam du sa skya'i gur mgon phur mo chos rdzong du gom
pa gcig bzhag nas brag sba ba la sgar brgyab byung / ci yin dgongs pas/ phyi lo rje 'di nyid kyis rta nag gser gling du grwa tshang btsugs pa de la blta bar

'dug pas/ sa skya pa'i bstan pa dar bar yong ba 'dug gsungs pa dang / skabs skabs su bar chad kyi rnam pa cung zad byung pa la/ chos skyong gi gtor sgrub bskang gso zhag sbrel
tsam re mdzad pas bar chad las grol ba mngon sum gyis grub pa dang / yang rje kun mkhyen nyid gdan sa chen po'i dus mdos dang stabs gcig par gdan sar phebs skabs/ nyer
dgu'i nyin gdan sa pa dpon slob rnams kyis tshogs chen mor rol mo bcam ste/ sha sa na'i sngags dbyangs dang / las mkhan gyi bstod bskul gyi dbyangs rnams mdzad skabs/ kun
mkhyen chen po sgo rum ye shes mgon po'i drung na bzhugs yod pa'i thugs dgongs la/ dbyangs dang rol mo rang la dgos pa cher med dam/ de bas nged rang ye shes dngos dang
khyad par med pa'i bse mgon 'di nyid kyi drung du bzlas pa byas pa 'thad dgongs nas/ de bzhin mdzad cing bzhugs pas/ dar tsam zhig nas ye shes kyi mgon po

pa lcam dral las mkhan dang bcas pa rnams mngon sum du gzigs snang la shar te/ khong chos skyong rnams ni tshogs chen mo'i dbyangs rol dang bstun/ phan tshun gcig gis gcig
la/ da khyod 'gro ran byung / nga 'gro ran byung zer ba sogs mi la mi lab pa ltar byas nas/ thog ma las mkhan rnams dang / mthar gur gyi mgon po rang yang byon song bas/
kun mkhyen chen po'i thugs la/ sa skya pa'i phyag len rnam par dag pa'i dbyangs rol 'di rnams ting nge 'dzin lo brgya bsgoms pa dang / sngags lo brgya bzlas pa bas nus pa
che ba 'dug dgongs nas thugs lhag par dad de/ de dus zhabs drung na yod pa'i skal ldan 'ga' la a la la/ sa skya pa'i dbyangs rol gyi phyag len 'di rnams ngo mtshar chen
po red/ nged la mthong snang ya mtshan can 'di ltar byung gsungs gzhan yang nyams ldan gyi gsung gis/ ra lpags 'di tsho yang mnyed dgos rgyur 'dug bong skad 'di tsho

yang 'don dgos rgyur 'dug ces kyang gsungs par grags shing / yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba yang zhing gzhan du gshegs dus glo bor mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub nyid shin
tu dben pa'i thugs dam la bzhugs pa'i gzigs snang la/ bde ba can nas 'ongs zer ba'i lha'i bu mang po mchod rdzas du ma khyer nas/ nged rnams e wa~M chos ldan gyi gdan sa
pa spyan 'dren la 'gro ba yin zer ba dang / lhag par dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa 'khor dang bcas pa rnam 'phrul rmad du byung ba'i sgo nas/ nged kyis chos rje ngor pa bde ba
can du skyel du phyin pa yin/ gtor ma blangs zhes pa'i tshul gsal bar byung ba'i gtan tshigs dang bcas pa rgyun gyi zhabs 'bring pa dag la bka' stsol bar mdzad cing / don
de la dgongs nas rje mkhan chen nyid kyi gsung las/ mdzad pa rgya mtsho'i mthar yang dpa' bo dang / /mkha' 'gro bye ba'i zhabs 'bring dang bcas te/ /bde ba can gyi zhing

du mngon sum gshegs/ /dag pa'i snang ba mthar phyin khyod phyag 'tshal/ /zhes bsngags par yang mdzad cing / 'di'i mtshan ma kho bo la yang shar zhes gsungs la/ gzhan yang de
las 'phros pa'i rnam par thar pa 'ga' zhig 'dug kyang re zhig de tsam zhig brjod pa yin no/ /yang 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen nyid bstan srung rnams la mnga' brnyes
pa'i tshul ni/ dus gcig gi tshe gsung ngag rin po che snga ma rang gsung ba'i dgongs pa yod mtshams/ rje grub chen dkon blo'i gsung gis/ da res lam 'bras ma gsung / khyed
kyi chos gos de nga'i rtsar yang yang skyel du byung ba rmis pas/ thugs dam zhig mdzod gsungs pa la brten nas mgon po'i bsnyen pa mdzad pas/ khri chen po zhig la bzhugs
nas snam sbyar mang po sku la bzhes pa'i mnal lam byung ba grub chen la zhus pas de shin tu legs/ chos skyong gi byin gyis brlabs par 'dug pas da ni bar chad gang gis
kyang mi

tshugs shing 'phrin las nam mkha' dang mnyam pa 'byung ngo zhes lung bstan gnang ba bzhin/ ngor/ mus/ na lendra/ lo dgon pa sogs dbus gtsang gi sa skya pa'i dgon pa che rags
phal cher zhig gi zhal bdag mdzad nas chos 'khor bskor bas/ dus phyis byon pa'i sa skya pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen zhig la mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen 'di rang 'phrin
las che bar grags pa yang chos skyong gis byin gyis brlabs pa'i mtshan ma gzigs pa'i dge mtshan las byung bar mngon zhing / sa lo 'jam dbyangs chen po ni/ spyir rig pa'i
gnas lnga la mkhas pa'i paNDi ta mtshungs pa med pa bdag nyid chen po sa skya paN chen nyid slar 'das te byon pa lta bu'i rnam par thar pa mnga' zhing / khyad par sa skya
pa'i bka' srung rnams kyis zhal bstan cing 'phrin las bsgrubs pa'i tshul ni/ skabs shig shab dge sding mgon khang du rgyun ring bzhugs te thugs dam dang chos skyong gi gtor
'bul

bskang ba bstod pa rgya chen po mdzad pas/ de'i dus su kyai rdor dang rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po lcam dral/ khyad par pu tra chen po lus kyi stod nyeng byas pa
gcig mngon sum du gzigs shing / gzhan yang chos skyong mnyes pa'i rtags bud med rgyan bzang pos brgyan pa dang / 'dzu ge mang po dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur ci yang byed pa gzigs
te/ de nas chos skyong 'khor bcas la bstod pa dgra bgegs srog gcod kyi 'khor lo zhes bya ba dang / dpal lha mo'i bskang gso dngos grub rol mtsho gnyis brtsams par mdzad
pa yin la/ yang lho bdag pos spyan drangs nas la stod shel dkar du bzhugs dus/ der snga dro thugs dam grol mtshams shig rje'i gsung gis/ da rang tho rangs bram ze'i gzugs
ral pa'i khrod na seng ldeng gi rdo rje rtse lnga pa yod pa zhig byung ste/ khyod rang gi mi 'phrod yod do zer nas bande phyar zhags gyon pa gnyis gtad pa'i snang ba byung
/ phyi na mar ltos shig dang gsungs/ sde pas sgo phye 'phral

bltar btang pas 'bul bsdud pas btang pa yin zer ba'i ban dhe sle'u gyon pa gnyis sgo drung na slebs 'dug pas kun kyang ya mtshan du gyur cing / chos skyong zhal bzhi pas 'bul
bsdud pa rnams kyi lam gyi bar chad bsal ba'i mtshan mar yid ches pa dang / yang rje nyid dbus phyogs su phebs pa gcig la chu bo chen por gru bying ste/ sku la shin tu
nyen pa byung ba na/ chos skyong gi rnam sprul gyi bya rog cig gru'i rta mgo khar babs byung 'phral/ de'i nyes pa las grol ba sogs mdor na chos skyong rnams kyis sku dang
grib ma'i tshul du bzhugs nas 'phrin las thams cad 'bad med du bsgrubs pa zhig yin no zhes thos la/ e wa~M chos ldan gyi gdan sa pa rje btsun mkhas pa'i dbang po dkon mchog
lhun grub la yang bka' sdod dam can rnams shin tu mches pa yin te/ de yang ngor gyi gser sku lha khang du mgon po'i bsnyen pa mdzad dus dge

slong zhig gis gos bem ser po zhig bkab nas khri thog tu phyin pa rmis gsungs/ 'phrin las gang bcol thogs med du 'grub pa dang / gzhan gyis byad ka rbod gtong yang rang zhir
'gyur ba zhig ste/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen mnal lam du byon nas/ phyag bzhi pa 'di la yig cha yang gyis/ gtor ma yang byin/ gzhan gyi mthu mi yong gsungs pa'i lung
bstan la brten nas yig cha yang gnyis tsam mdzad/ gtor ma yang ma chag par mdzad do/ /ston gtor bsngo brgya tshar mdzad dus spyan zur la mgon khang nas mi nag dung long
can gcig lam zab lha khang la song / gcer te gzigs pas pu trar 'dug chos srung 'di rnams shin tu 'jigs gsungs pa sogs kyis mtshon te shes so/ /spyan snga dkon mchog rgya
mtsho la yang sa skya pa'i bstan srung rnams kyis gang bsgo ba'i las rnams mdzad pas 'phrin las mkha' khyab tu gyur te/ sngon 'jam dbyangs sangs rin gyis zhal

bdag mdzad pa'i dbus gtsang gi dgon pa phal cher gyi 'dzin skyong yang mdzad cing / lhag par dpal sa skyar bdag gi bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can sku mched
la gsung ngag rin po che cha lag dang bcas pa stsal nas/ sgo rum ye shes mgon po mjal ba la phebs pa na/ bse mgon chen po'i spyan dbus ma de shin tu gsal bar gzigs byung
pas/ de gong rje nyid kyi spyan gnyis ka grib kyi rnam pas dngos po phra rags gang yang gsal po mi gzigs shing / ljags lung mdzad dus kyang 'phar lung kho na gnang dgos pa
la/ de phyin chad spyan gnyis ka rang bye la song ste/ ljags lung sogs la thogs med gnang chog pa byung pas/ de'i tshul sngags 'chang chen po la zhu bar mdzad pa na/ sngags
'chang nyid kyi gsung las/ spyan dbus ma de ltar gzigs pa de/ ye shes kyi spyan gzigs par gdon mi za ba 'dug ces bsngags brjod ci yang zhig

mdzad kyin 'dug ces thos shing / gzhan yang gling dga' dgon pa'i bla brang mgon khang gi mgon po'i sku gsar du bzhengs te rab gnas mdzad pa na/ dkar khung la 'ja' sngon po
zug cing / thug gnyis la me dngos su 'bar ba kun gyis mthong ba sogs chos skyong 'khul ba'i rtags mtshan ngo mtshar can mang du ston par mdzad par grags so/ /yang sa skya
pa'i bstan 'dzin rdzong lugs pa kun gyi gtso bor gyur pa sngags 'chang gzung skyid dpal bas kyang / sa skya pa'i chos skyong che chung gnyis ka yang bran bzhin du 'khol
ba yin te/ gdan sa chen por phag mo grub pas dmag byung dus mdun skor rnams phal cher bcom nas/ gdan sa dan la yong grab byed pa la/ rje nyid kyis chos skyong la 'phrin las
bcol te mgyogs gtor 'phangs pas/ dmag rnams zam pa so so'i mtshams nas log pa dang / yang lan cig gdan sa'i sa dkar logs na rgyud sde spyi rnam zhig gsung gi yod dus/
chos rje bla

ma dam pa yang yang dran pa zhig byung ba dang / de dang dus mtshungs par srod gcig la pu tra dngos su byung nas/ khyed rang 'gro mgon chos rje mjal ba la myur du byon zer
byung bas/ chos 'phro myur du gsungs nas/ chos rje bo dong byang chub lung na bzhugs 'dug pa dang mjal bas/ chos rje'i gsung gis/ 'o nyid byung ba shin tu legs/ nged kha
sang nas nyid 'bod du gtong ba la thug yod gsungs/ de ci yin lags zhus pas/ 'o cag la kha sang gzhan phyogs 'ga' zhig gis mthu byas nas shin tu gtser gsungs pas/ de ji ltar
na sa sros nas gzim khang gi 'gram rtsa brdungs nas yom yom yong ba dang / 'bru ngag mi tshor ba'i lab ding ding mang po 'byung ba/ gzim khyis lung po'i mda' na mar phyin
nas mtho sa der ngus pas/ rab kha ba'i khyi byin 'tshogs nas de'i mtha' bskor nas ngu ba la sogs pa byung ba'i bzlog pa la/ chos

rje dpon slob rnams kyis chos skyong gi gtor ma dang / dbyu gu drug cu rtsa bzhi'i gtor bzlog la sogs pa mdzad kyin 'dug pa'i phyag phyi zhag 'ga' mdzad na'ang khyad tsam ma
byung bas/ nyid kyi thugs la 'di lta bu'i gang zag la 'di 'dra byed pa de la phar rtags thon na nga kun ji ltar gyur na'ang gyur snyam du dgongs nas/ chos rje'i drung du
'di skad zhus so/ /da drung pa'i blud du bdag 'gro bar 'os pas/ drung pa dpon slob rnams kyang sku rim la 'bungs mdzod/ bdag gis lung pa'i mdo'i gad pa gru gsum ma gir
phyin la dpal ldan zhal bzhi pa'i bsnyen sgrub las sbyor zhig byed lags kyi zhus nas/ der sbra nag gcig phub nas zhag bdun bsgrubs/ chos skyong gis las mdzad pa'i rtags su
zhag gnyis gsum song na mar thun gtor 'phangs pa rnams kyang me ru dmar na ra ra song zhing / gzim khang du kho'i cho 'phrul rnams kyang rgyun chad nas/ zhag bdun pa la
mthu byed mkhan bdun yod pa 'dug pa'i bdun ga'i thog brdibs skad do/ /de'i

dus su chos rje'ang der byon/ chos skyong la gtang rag btang / mgon g.yag rnams kyang der blangs dus su mgon g.yag rnams drung pa rnam gnyis kyi drung du sbra nang du yong
nas sna snoms/ lces ldag pa rnams byed pa byung gsungs/ des na bla ma dam pa rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po 'di nyid kyi brgyud pa dang bcas pa rnams kyi rje sa skya pa rnams kyis
thugs sras go chod kho na rim par mdzad pas/ chos kyi rje pas kyang kha'u skyed lhas su chos skyong gi bka' bsgo'ang gsan cing thugs sras mchog tu'ang mdzad do/ /des
na rje 'di gal che ba'i 'phrin las 'chol dgos pa byung ba phal cher thogs pa med par 'grub pa dang / chos skyong la thugs mches pa'i cha nas yi dam gyi lha dang dbyer med
pa lta bu'i dad gus mdzad/ khyad par chos skyong so so'i rjes gnang zhus pa'i tshe/ kho pa rang la dris la bya yi gsungs pa'i nangs par/ 'di skad byung gsungs nas rjes gnang
yong mi yong gi 'thang phyed pa sogs yong ba bu slob

kun mthun snang grub pas/ chos skyong rnams dang mi dang mi lab pa bzhin yod par the tshom mi dgos la/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po kun dga' bkra shis kyang rigs kyi che ba
tsam ma yin pa'i lung rtogs kyi yon tan kun gyi mnga' bdag tu gyur pas/ de dus kyi mkhas btsun kun gyi bla mar gyur cing / lhag par chos skyong rnams shin tu 'go ba'i tshul
ni dpal sa skya'i dbu rtser bzhugs dus mnal lam du gtsug lag khang gi khyams mthil du gur gyi mgon po'i rnam pa gsal zhing mtshan nyid thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa gcig
dang por gzigs/ de nas de res 'ga' phyag drug pa'i rnam pa/ res 'ga' phyag bzhi pa'i rnam pa sogs rnam 'gyur mi 'dra ba mang du ston pa zhig byung ba na/ de gsum ngo bo
gcig yin zer ba'i brdar 'dug snyam pa'i nges shes thugs la 'khrungs pa dang / yang lan gcig ngam ring du 'jam dkar la gsung bsnyen mdzad pas/ nyi ma shar tsam na dpal ldan
lha

mo 'dod khams ma dpon g.yog gnyis dre'u nag po la chibs nas bar snang la sha ra ra byung ba gzigs pa dang / lha khang bla brang na bzhugs skabs shig kyang dpon po ri'i rtse
la shar phyogs nas rgyangs kyis byung ba gzigs pa sogs lan mang du gzigs snang la byung bar rje rang nyid kyis gsungs so zhes bshad la/ yang dbu rtser bzhugs skabs dur khrod
bdag po yab yum gnyis mdun na gar stabs ling ling mdzad pa sogs rnam 'gyur khyad par du ma mdzad kyin phebs pa mngon sum du gzigs pa dang / gzhan yang bdag nyid chen
po rang gi zhal nas/ skabs shig pu tra 'di ding sang cha lugs 'gyur 'dug gsungs pa sogs mdor na mkha' 'gro chos skyong mi ma yin sogs thams cad bran du 'khol zhing las sgrub
pa zhig yin la/ chos kyi rgyal po 'di dgung lo re bzhi pa chu pho 'brug lo la rgya nag ta'i ming rgyal pos ta'i twa bzhin dang a nu dre bo

la sogs pa mngags te gdan drangs/ gus pa chen pos bla mar khur/ cing gyo/ twa'i ching / hwa wi/ swi then/ shwang shen/ kiM kwaM ta'i kShoM/ keng mi/ ba ho/ de bod skad du bsgyur
na/ 'phrin las sna tshogs rgyas pa/ dam chos mchog tu rgyal ba/ yang dag pa'i ye shes/ snying rje rgya chen kun nas rgyas par phan pa/ zhing bsrung zhing bstan pa bshad
pa/ yang dag par rig pa/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ nub kyi mchog tu dge ba/ rdo rje kun khyab/ 'od zer chen po'i sangs rgyas zhes pa'i mtshan gsol/ shel dam dang
lung bzang po/ gser gyi 'khor lo rtsibs stong pa la sogs pa'i 'bul ba'i rnam grangs brjod kyis mi lang ba phul te/ mdor na 'phags pa rin po che dang 'bul ba mnyam par grags/
khyad par lha khang chen mo phag gru ba'i lag nas nan gyis blangs te phul/ sa skya pa chus khyer gyi skra nas zin/ rgya nag tu lo gsum bzhugs nas

shing pho rta'i lo la bod du phebs/ dgung lo don bdun pa shing mo sbrul la lha khang chen mo'i yang steng nas bde ba can gyi zhing khams chen por gshegs pa'i tshul bstan te/
mdor na sa skya pa'i gdung rgyud cig la sku tshe dang mdzad pa 'phrin las rgya che zhing mthar phyin pa'i tshad zhig tu byung ba yin no/Hagiography of rDzong pa Kun dga'
rgyal mtshan/chos kyi rgyal po de'i thugs sras sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin kun dga' rnam gnyis kyi ya gyal rdzong pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan nam/ nyi lde ba kun dga' rgyal mtshan
du grags pa 'di'i/ mtshan dngos de ltar yin pa la/ rje nyid sku gzhon nu'i dus theg chen rin po che'i drung na bzhugs pa'i tshe/ tshad ma rigs gter gyi gzhung dang
/ bla ma dam pas mdzad pa'i bde mchog lU hi pa'i mngon rtogs gnyis nyi ma re re la thugs su chud cing ston pa shin tu bzang bar gyur pas/ slar yang theg chen rin po ches
mkhan 'jam dbyangs grags pa'i dpal zhes bya bar gsol zhing bu slob kyi

gtso bor mdzad pa yin no zhes thos la/ rje 'dis kyang bstan srung rnams bran bzhin tu 'khol ba'i tshul ni/ sgo rum na bzhugs pa'i bse mgon chen po la gzhan sus kyang reg pa
lta zhog nan tan du lta ba tsam yang mi nus pa la/ rje 'di nyid kyis zhal 'bag gi rdul sel ba dang / na bza' 'chos pa sogs mdzad pa la rtsub 'gyur cung zad kyang mi 'byung
zhing dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur du ma gzigs pa dang / gzhan rje nyid kyi gsung las ngas mgon po zhal bzhi pa'i rjes gnang zhus pa tsam nas/ lus dang grib ma bzhin du 'grogs
pa zhig byung na'ang / gtor ma snga phyi tsam la yang mchod g.yog pa khrag skyug tu 'ong ba sogs rtse rag rgod drags pa zhig byung pas/ 'jam par 'dod na lhag ma dang thug
phrad la bslabs zer ba'i man ngag de byas/ cung zad gnad la phab nas de phyin gtor ma ma chag tsam las ched gnyer ma byas kyang /

'bring tsham gyi mdo khrar phyin pa 'khor nas phyi res kha'u skyed lhas su yong pa na/ bsu ba byed pa la sogs pa dga' ba'i rnam 'gyur mang po ston gyin 'dug pas/ de phyin tshes
brgyad gtor ma yang ma chag par byin gsungs shing / yang rje nyid ngam ring na bzhugs pa'i dus nyid kyi thugs sras kyi thu bo chos rje rin po che a nanda pa'i drung
nas shel dkar du bzhugs pa snyung du byung pa'i sku rim gtor sgrub cig mdzad pa'i dus mchod g.yog pa rnams gtor ma skyong du song / rje nyid gzim khang na bzhugs pa cung
zad mnal du song pa na/ a tsa ra nag po ras kyi thod bcings pa gcig byung / khyod su yin gsungs pas/ tsa turmu kha yin zer/ gang nas yong gsungs pas/ da lta rang shel dkar
nas yong zer/ 'o na chos rje a nanda pa snyung ba ji 'dra yod gsungs pas/ kho ka na zer sems khral che che ltar 'dug da ji 'dra yong 'dri dgos snyam tsa na mchod g.yog
pa rnams

slebs nas gnyid sad byung gsungs/ yang yos lo rje nyid sa skya pa chen po'i sgrub gnas sku 'bum rnam rgyal na bzhugs dus sku khams bsnyel ba shin tu thu ba'i rnam pa bstan/
rlung ltas kyang bzang po mi 'dug gsungs thams cad 'jigs shing skrag par gyur pa na/ nub gcig gi tshe mnal lam du rje nyid rin po che'i khri gcig gi steng na bzhugs nas
'dug pa la/ zur bzhi nas mkha' 'gro ma bzhis bteg dpa' bo dang mkha' 'gro ma bsam gyis mi khyab pas bsu ba byas nas nam mkha' la gdan drangs pas 'og phyogs su gzigs pa na/
dbus gtsang gi cha sogs las brgal nas/ sngar gzigs ma myong ba'i zhing khams gcig gi steng na phebs 'dug pas/ da sa skya pa ji tsam na yod gsungs pas/ shin tu thag ring
zer/ 'o na der 'gro dgos pa yod ma rgan mo drin can zhig yod pas/ de dang ma 'phrad par 'gro ba'i thabs med gsungs pas/ de'i mod la bram ze'i gzugs can mdog

nag po mi rkang gi gling bu thogs pa zhig byung nas/ mkha' 'gro ma de rnams phyogs bcur bskrad nas drung du byung ste/ rnal 'byor pa'i a ma'i dad ka la/ da lan ngas bzlogs
yod do zer/ khyod su yin gsungs pas/ tsa turmu kha yin zer ba dang mnal sad 'dug sang nyin sku rim gtor sgrub pa rnams la mdang rmi lam 'di bzhin byung / mgon po chung ba
la bskang gso dang gtor ma rgyas par phul cig gsungs/ des na rlung ltas dang thugs dam gyi ltas de ltar byung nas kyang / zhing 'dir 'gro ba'i don du yun ring po'i bar bzhugs
pa ni gnyan mgon chen po zhal bzhi pas sku tshe'i bar chad bzlogs pa'i rmad du byung ba'i rnam thar du snang zhing / yang rje 'dis dgung lo bcu drug lon dus slob dpon
rtse mo'i sambu Ta'i TIka chen thugs 'dzin gnang ba'i tshe/ nub mang po'i bar du bud med dkar mo ras dkar gyi gos gyon zhing / ras dkar gyi thod bcings pa zhig gzim mal
gyi 'khris su

nyal nas/ tho rangs khar song ba na phug ron rer byas kyis 'phur 'gro ba zhag yang yang mnal lam du byung ba na/ theg chen rin po che'i drung du 'di bzhin byung ba ji ltar
yin zhus pas/ de ni TIkka 'di'i chos bdag tu dkar mo nyi zla bskos yod pas de'i rten 'brel yin/ TIka chen 'di la thos bsam byed pa rnams la dkar mo nyi zlas grogs byed pa'i
lo rgyus mang po yod gsungs shing / mdor na de nas bzung ste sku dang grib ma ltar du 'grogs par snang la/ gzhan yang rje nyid sku na phra mo'i dus su pu tra yang yang
gzigs pa dang / phyogs gzhan du 'byon pa'i tshe yang / zhag shas kyi sngon la pu tra byon nas gzim khang 'chag pa sogs byed pa rtsa gsal du mas mthong ba'i lo rgyus yod
cing / yang ngam ring du bzhugs dus shig srod la gtor bsngo mdzad pa'i tshe/ zhabs drung na gnas pa kun la/ rje'i gsung gis khyed tshos e mthong / da lta dur khrod bdag po
byon nas ka gdong 'di na gar mdzad kyin 'dug

gsungs pa dang /Hagiography of Mus srad pa rDo rje rgyal mtshanyang dpal mgon ni dril bu 'khrol ba'i lad mo byed kyi 'dug gsungs pa sogs mkha' 'gro chos skyong rnams dang 'bral
med du bzhugs pa zhig yin par mngon no/ /yang sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin rdzong lugs kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen mtshungs med mus srad pa chen po rdo rje rgyal mtshan yang
skyes sbyangs kyi mkhyen rab phul du phyin pas 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi sgo nas rje btsun gong ma'i rgyud man ngag gi bstan pa gsal bar mdzad cing / khyad par chos skyong
che chung gi man ngag so so'i dkar chag gi yi ge mdzad pa sogs lugs 'di la phyag rjes kyi bka' drin yang mchog tu che zhing bsnyen sgrub kyang mthar phyin pas chos skyong
rnams kyis zhal yang yang du gzigs shing gdan sa chen po'i bla brang brang mo che'i chos rje bzang po rgyal mtshan pa'i gzim khang du brgya dpon chos rje kun dga' bsam
grub pas/ rje nyid la chos rje gzung

pa la sogs pa'i chos rgyud dri ma med pa bzhugs par dgongs nas bla brang gi gdan sa mdzad par gsol ba btab pa bzhin/ gnas de nyid du gdan phab nas lo nyi shu rtsa drug gi bar
la sgrub pa la rtse gcig tu bzhugs/ de'i bar gyi thugs dam gyi rim pa ni/ tho rangs skya rengs dang po'i dus su bir srung thun mong ma yin pa dang / lam zab thun mong
ma yin pa la sogs pa mdzad/ de nas sngon 'gro mchod gtor gyi rnal 'byor rgyas pa/ rje btsun yab la brten pa'i lam dus rgyas pa brgya bzhi dang bcas pa mdzad do/ /de nas gdan
bzhes kyi gong du dkar cha bzhi/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg mdzad cing / de nas kha zas kyi rnal 'byor dang bcas pa'i gdan bzhes mdzad nas grol 'phral/ rje btsun
sa skya pa'i gsung rab mtha' dag dang / gzhan yang bka' bstan bcos dri ma med pa rnams la gzigs rtog ci rigs mdzad nas nyin gung la bab pa'i tshe/ sngon 'gro mchod gtor

'bring po dang 'brel pa'i lam dus 'bring po mdzad/ de rjes bdag med ma/ gur rigs bsdus man ngag lugs/ sambu Ti mtshon cha can man ngag lugs rnams la brten pa'i lam dus rgyas
'bring bsdus gsum gang yang rung ba re mdzad/ 'di la chag med kyi rgyun yod dam zhus pas/ chag med rgyun rang yod pa mi 'dug ste/ rgyud gsum po 'di la bla ma la zhu ba
dang / slob gnyer byed pa la dka' ba chen po zhig byung / da shes pa'i lugs yin pas nyams len dum re ma byas na bslabs pa la don mi yong bar 'dug pas byas pa yin gsungs/
gung tshigs thon nas slob ma thun mong ma yin pa 'ga' re la blo dang 'tshams pa'i gsung chos tshan pa re gnang / gang gnang ba de tshig don phyin ci ma log pa slob ma'i rgyud
la 'pho nges pa re mdzad/ de nas dril bu lus dkyil/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma la sogs pa chag med dang / gzhan yang dbang bka' gang gsan gyi

snying po lan bdun re dang / mdo rgyud kyi tshig gang yang rung ba'i shlau ka re thugs la 'dzin/ mdo rgyud man ngag gi dgongs 'grel gsal byed kyi rtsom pa mtshon re/ srod kyi
dus su gtor bsngo rgyas pa DA dril dang bcas pa/ lam dus bsdus pa/ sgrub pa lung sbyin/ nyal ba'i rnal 'byor dang ldan pas gzim pa'i tshul ston/ mnal sad pa dang ldang
ba'i rnal 'byor dang ldan pas sngar bzhin rgyun gyi rnal 'byor la 'jug par mdzad do/ /de lta bu'i sgrub pa la brtson pas ting nge 'dzin bsam gyis mi khyab pa thugs rgyud
la 'khrungs par mngon te/ bhu Tar mun khang brten pa'i dus su mi ma yin gyi bar chad kyi rnam pas gzim khang la thog brgyab pas sku pang du 'khyil ba'i tshe/ ting nge 'dzin
gyi cho 'phrul gcig yin dgongs nas cung zad de kar bzhag nas slar na bza' dkrugs pas mdun der thim song ba phyag g.yog kun gyis mthong ba sogs grub pa'i rtags mtshan
mang du ston par mdzad pa'i lo rgyus du

ma yod kyang 'dir ma spros/ de lta bu'i bla ma de dgung lo bdun cu don lnga'i bar du bstan 'gro'i don mthar phyin pa mdzad nas/ mthar bla brang brang mo che nyid du mya ngan
las 'da' ba'i tshul ston par mdzad pa yin la/Hagiographies of Yar lung pa and his nephewyang chos rje bla ma dam pa'i sngags kyi rgyal tshab chen po yar lung pa seng ge
rgyal mtshan khu dbon rnams chos skyong la mnga' brnyes pa'i tshul ni/ de yang spyir dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gdung rgyud rim pa dang / yar lung pa'i zhal ngo rim par byon
pa rnams dpon slob 'brel chags su byung ba yin te/ sa chen gyi dus yar sgom bse'o/ rje btsun gyi dus rgyal tsha lung mang po/ chos rje pa'i dus do pa ston tshul/ mkhas pa
yon tan khri/ chos rje bla ma dam pa'i dus yar lung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen blo gros pa'i dus mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog sogs rim par byon pa las/Hagiography
of Yar lung pa Seng ge rgyal mtsanchos rje bla ma'i dngos slob yar lung pa seng rgyal ni/

chu pho spre'u'i lo la sku bltams/ khu ston seng ge bzang po'i dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa phog cing / kyai rdor gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur nas dgung lo nyer dgu'i bar du phar
phyin/ spyod 'jug brtag gnyis sogs la sbyangs/ mkhan po bzang chen pa dang / slob dpon mon mkhar pa las rab tu byung / spyan snga grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis mtshan seng
ge rgyal mtshan du btags/ lo de la klu'i dgon par brtag gnyis la bshad gsar dang / dgung lo bcu pa la bsam yas su phar phyin la grwa bskor mdzad/ rang lo bco brgyad pa
la dwags po'i mkhar klu bzang du chos rje bla ma dang mjal nas mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob/ bsnyen rdzogs kyi mkhan po zhus shing / de nas bzung ste sku dang 'bral med du 'grogs
nas/ gsung ngag rin po che dang / chos skyong gi skor gyis gtsos pa'i sa skya'i yab chos rnams kyis thog drangs/ mdo sngags kyi chos tshul mtha' yas pa zhig gsan cing
thugs yid gcig

tu 'dres pa'i dpon slob tu gyur/ gzhan yang bu rin po che/ rgyal sras thogs med/ lo chen byang rtse/ bla chen bsod blo sogs bla ma sum cu so grangs tsam bsten nas gsan pa rgya
mtsho'i pha mthar son/ thugs dam la shin tu brtson pas ting nge 'dzin la brtan pa thob cing yi dam gyi lha mang po'i zhal gzigs/ skabs shig dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa a tsa
ra thod 'phreng thogs pa zhig tu sprul nas/ dbu sngas kyi mgor byung ste/ khyod mi rus kyi phreng ba 'di bzung na rang khe che ba yin te/ mi 'dzin par 'dug zer nas gnas
skabs kyi bar chad 'dra sel ba la gnyan mgon gyi rjes gnang gsan dgos pa'i bskul ma 'debs pa dang / yang phyag g.yog ngan pa zhig gis phyag rdzas mang po khyer ba ni/ 'khor
gzhan zhig la mon bu bab ste/ nga mnga' ris gung thang na la rtse nas 'ongs pa'i 'ba' ta yin/ su ra yin/ rkun ma

bsam yas 'ja' dkar na yod pa la/ khyed tsho 'dir mgo btum nas sdod dam zer ba'i khung ston pa yang byung ba sogs chos skyong rnams kyis go re len gyi tshul gyis 'phrin las
thams cad thogs med du bsgrubs pa dang / thugs dam gyi thun mtshams las sa skya pa'i snyan brgyud kyi man ngag gser chos su grags pa rnams gdul bya so so'i blo dang 'tshams
par stsal pas/ 'phags pa'i dbon rgyud slob dpon chen po blo gros rgyal mtshan pa dang / gsang phu'i gdan sa pa rin chen rnam rgyal/ dbon po rgyal ba mchog dbyangs sogs
bstan 'dzin gyi slob ma yang mang du bskrun/sku gzhon nu'i dus bla ma'i phyag dpe 'bri ba dang bstun gsung ba zin bris btab pa'i yig cha po ti du ma dang / dus phyis brtag
gnyis kyi 'bru 'grel/ kun rig gi dkyil chog sogs gsung rab kyang mang po gsar du mdzad/ chos rje bla ma'i drung du gsung ngag gsan dus/ nyams skyon med 'ba' zhig skyes
pas thugs nges shes gting nas drongs pa dang / dus phyis mar ngo'i tshes

bcu zhig la chos rje pa'i dus dran gyi sgrub mchod mdzad de/ tho rangs bla ma'i rnal 'byor tshar gnyis sgom pa'i ngang la mnal du song ba na/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa nyid
sku che zhing mdzes pa zhig byon nas/ 'o 'di yin te zhes pa la sogs pa'i gsung byon pas/ dngos su mjal ba las brgya 'gyur du lhag pa'i dag snang dang / mnal sad pa na'ang
dad gus kyi yus kyi snang byin rlabs kyi zi langs pa'i rkyen gyis bde gsal mi rtog pa'i ting nge 'dzin sngar las lhag pa zhig 'khrungs te/ phyis kyang thugs nyams su
yang nas yang du myong ba lags skad/ mthar yi dam gyi lha la dngos su gnang ba thob pa lho brag las kyi rdo rjes sku tshe 'di nyid kyi 'og rol tu 'jig rten gyi khams bde
ba can du skye ba bzhes par lung bstan pa bzhin du dben gnas bsam gtan gling du sku 'da' khar yang / snang ba mtha' yas kyi nyal 'pho dang / bde ba can gyi smon lam kho
na mdzad de/

dgung lo drug cu re dgu pa lcags pho 'brug gi lo hor zla gnyis pa'i gnam stong la zhi bar gshegs nas/ spur bzhus pas gdung rnams ring bsrel 'ba' zhig tu gyur pas kun mi phyed
pa'i dad pa la bkod do/Hagiography of bSod nams rgyal mchog/rje de nyid kyi sku'i dbon po thugs sras dam pa mkhan chen rgyal mchog pa ni/ yar lung lha ri dgon par lcags
mo byi ba'i lo la sku bltams/ dgung lo bdun pa la 'gro mgon chos rje'i drung du tshangs spyod dge bsnyen zhus/ dgu pa la mkhan po sngar gyi de dang / las slob 'jam dbyangs
shAkya rgyal mtshan las rab tu byung / mtshan bsod nams rgyal ba mchog dbyangs dpal bzang por btags/ mkhan po las rdo rje phur pa'i dbang rgyud gsum man ngag dang bcas
pa/ chos skyong che chung gi rjes gnang / dus 'khor sogs gsan/ nyer lnga pa la bsnyen par rdzogs/ de nas rang nyid kyi khu bo rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug seng ge rgyal mtshan
las snga phyir sa skya pa'i man ngag gser chos mtha' dag

bum pa gang byor nos/ gzhan yang spyan snga byams pa byang chub bam/ lo chen byang rtse/ sog dbon legs pa'i blo gros/ ta dben kun legs pa sogs bla ma nyi shu rtsa grangs shig
bsten nas gsan pa rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag tu gyur/rang gi khu bo zhal bzhugs dus zhabs 'bring ba 'bral med du mdzad cing / mos gus rtse gcig pa mnga' bas dam tshig gi
sel cung zad kyang med/ rang nyid dgung lo zhe gcig pa'i dus khu bo gshegs nas/ phyag rdzas thams cad dgongs rdzogs su btang / re zhig spros pa mtha' dag rgyang bsrings nas
dbyar mtshams dgun mtshams bcad de/ yi dam lha'i bsnyen pa/ kha skong gi sbyin sreg dang bcas pa mang du mdzad cing / chos skyong rnams kyi gtor sgrub la rtsal du bton
pas byin rlabs kyi rtags mtshan mang du brnyes/ de dus gdug pa can 'ga' zhig gis zhabs 'dren gyi sbyor ba sna tshogs byas pa la/ srung

mas tshar bcad pa'i rtags mtshan mngon gyur du bstan/ khyad par gnyan mgon gyi 'dzin gtor la bdud rtsi'i rgyun sbrang rtsi lta bu 'dzag pa zhig rgyun du yod pas sku tshe mthar
phyin pa sogs chos skyong rnams shin tu 'go ba'i lo rgyus ngo mtshar can mang du mnga'/ 'os su gyur pa'i gdul bya la dbang rjes gnang lung man ngag sogs rgyun du stsol
bas rgya nag dang dbus gtsang gi mi chen du mas btud cing / sde snod 'dzin pa'i slob ma'ang mang du thon/ mthar dben gnas bsam gtan gling du dgung lo bdun cu don bzhi pa
chu mo glang gi lo hor zla bdun pa'i yar tshes bcu la zhi bar gshegs par nye ba na/ nyin gcig rnal 'byor dbang phyug paNDi ta'i cha lugs su byas pa btsun mo dang bcas pa
zhig byon te/ de'i gsung las/ nga 'di nas dgon gsar la thengs shig 'gro/ de nas so wa na thar gshegs gsungs pa dang bcas zhal mngon sum du bstan/ yang nyin gcig slob dpon
rin po che byon byung gsungs

nas/ 'dir ni rje btsun rtse mor dad pa can/ /rgyud sde 'dzin pa'i bshes gnyen yar lung pa/ /seng ge rgyal mtshan zhes pa grags pa yis/ /bskul ba'i ngor byas bsod nams kyis
sbyar ro/ /zer ba'i bstod pa gcig yod pa de thon gsungs pa dang / de nas tshes bcu la bab pa'i tshe/ gsung las/ da lta birWa pa dbu la me tog 'phreng bas brgyan cing / phyag
na sba 'khar bsnams pa zhig dang / mal lo tsA ba gnyis byon nas zhal sprod du bzhugs 'dug dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor dang / mkha' 'gro mas bar snang gang
nas 'dug nga sdod sa 'di mkhar klu bzang yin nam chos rdzong yin nam chos yin pa 'dug rje btsun ma sgrol ma yang byon byung / mchod pa phul/ chos rje bas phyag nar gyis brkyangs
nas nga'i spyi bor bzhag byung / da de da lta 'gro bdud rtsi ril bu chang la sbyor la nga'i khar blugs shig gsungs/ sngags pa 'chi na 'di ltar byed dgos

pa yin gsungs nas/ sku la snam sbyar bzhes te/ rdo rje dril bu phyag tu bsnol/ yud cig thugs dam la zhugs nas/ de ma thag rang bzhin 'od gsal chen po'i klong du thim pa'i tshul
bstan to/ /de dus sgom chen pa dar ma dpal gyi gzigs snang la/ glang po che rgyan gyis spras pa zhig mkha' 'gro ma bzhis bzung nas rje nyid dag pa'i zhing khams su spyan
'dren rgyu yin pa'i mtshan ma shar ba sogs ngo mtshar ba'i rtags mang du byung bar grags so/Hagiography of Gong dkar rDo rje gdan pa/yang sa skya pa'i rje btsun gong
ma'i bstan pa spyan gyi 'bras bu ltar gces par 'dzin pa'i skyes bu dam pa nus mthu'i mnga' bdag rdo rje gdan pa chen po kun dga' rnam rgyal dpal bzang po ni/ bskal pa dpag
tu med pa'i sngon rol nas mchog gi go 'phang mngon du mdzad cing / slar yang sprul pa'i sku bgrang ba las 'das pa sku gsung thugs gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sgo
nas/ skal pa dang 'tshams pa'i gdul bya'i zhing

mtha' yas par 'bad med lhun grub tu 'gro don mdzad par nges te/ de yang sngon rgyal po bzang po mchog ces pa'i skyed mos tshal du padma'i sdong po lba ba lnga yod pa/ dbus
sngo/ shar dkar/ lho ser/ nub dmar/ byang ljang ba/ kha phye ba na khye'u kha dog padma dang mthun pa lnga 'khrungs/ de ni thod 'phreng rtsal rigs lnga yin zhing / de dag
gis sangs rgyas kyi sngags kyi bstan pa gar khyab tu sku'i sprul pas khyab cing / zhing rgyas dbang drag gi 'phrin las gsang sngags kyi bstan pa 'dzin par zhal gyis bzhes

de nyid

bod 'dir zhang sna nam rdo rje bdud 'joms su sku skye ba bzhes par rdo rje bdud 'joms kyi rnam thar las gsal zhing / de nyid zhing 'dir rje 'di nyid du gyur par u rgyan rin
po ches/ da lta'i dus kyi rdo rje bdud 'joms ni/ /ma 'ongs tshe lo lnga bcu kha ral dus/ /dbus gtsang mtshams su sde dpon tshul bzung nas/ /kun dga'i ming can rdo rje 'dzin
par 'gyur/ /zhes lung bstan cing / de nyid rdo rje phur pa'i grub thob tu nges pa las de dang mthun par 'dren pa 'dis phur pa'i grub rtags dngos su bzhag cing / de'i
phyag len dbus gtsang khams sogs su dar zhing rgyas par mdzad pas so/ /yang bar skabs su/ bla ma gnam kha'u pa'i sku'i sprul par yang grags te/ sdom brtson rdo rje 'dzin
pa chen po mus pa rnam rgyal bzang po zhes bya ba sngar nas yi dam chos skyong la bsnyen sgrub tshad du 'khyol ba'i sngags 'chang chen por gyur kyang / slad nas gnyan mgon
zhal bzhi pa'i sgrub skor la ched du thugs 'dun pas/

de dag zhu ba'i bla ma gang bzang dmod bor te chos skyong la gsol ba btab dus rmi lam du a tsa ra sngon po zhig byung nas khyod 'dod pa'i chos de bla ma gnam kha'u pa phang
na yod pas der zhus zer chos sde'i rgyab ri 'di bstan byung / de la bltas pas rgyab ri bya rog lding pa lta bur mthong zhing / sad pa na nges pa brtan po rnyed de/ rje 'di
nyid kyi zhabs drung du byon nas chos skyong skor gyi sgrub skor cha lag dang bcas pa ma tshang ba med pa gsan pa yin no/ /yang rjes su chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam
pa'i sku'i skye ba yin par gsal te/ de nyid kyi bka' tha mar/ bdag 'di nas 'phos te u rgyan gyi yul du skye ba gcig de nas bod 'dir skye ba blangs te bstan pa'i bya ba
lhag ma rnams bgyid ces stsal pa dang / de dang mthun par bsam yas su sku gdung zhugs la phul dus 'od kyi gong bu zhig sgra dang bcas te gong dkar phyogs su song zer ba
chos rje bla ma nyid kyi rnam thar na

yod pa ltar/ rje bla mas phyag len gyi rim pa rgyud 'grel sogs mgon po 'di nyid kyis ched du rgyas par mdzad pas kyang grub pa yin no/ /de lta bu'i skyes chen de nyid sku'i
skye ba 'dir rigs rus gang las byon pa ni 'di ltar thos te/ bstan pa snga dar gyi dus bod gangs can 'dul ba'i gnyan por 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi rnam 'phrul chos skyong
ba'i rgyal po srong btsan sgam po bya ba byon/ de'i bka'i 'phrul blon chen po 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi rnam 'phrul thu mi sambha dra bya ba shes rab can gyi mchog tu gyur
pa zhig byung / thu zhes pa rus yin/ mtshan dngos la sambho Ta zhes bod bzang por 'chad pa yod kyang / yi ge gsar rnying mang po na sambha dra zer ba yod/ de'i skad dod
kun tu bzang po yin zhing / mkhan po 'di nyid kyis mdzad pa'i bstan bcos rnams las kyang / kun tu bzang po'i rtsa ba brgyad pa zhes 'byung ba/ 'phags yul na'ang bstan bcos

kyi ming mdzad pa po las btags pa mang bas/ 'dir yang mdzad pa po las bstan bcos kyi ming byung bar gsal lo zhes mkhas pa dag bzhed do/ /'di ni rgyal po'i lung gis rgya gar
du chos slob tu btang / paNDi ta brgya rtsa brgyad bsten/ khyad par du lha rig pa'i seng ge dang / bram ze li byin las mkhas par bslabs/ bod du chos mang po bsgyur/ bod
yig brtsams/ 'jig rten gyi mig lta bur gyur pas lo tsA ba zhes pa'i thog mar byon pa yin no/ /de las rim par brgyud de byon pa dpon rdo rje bkra shis zhes pa'i bsod nams
can zhig byung ba rgya yul la byon/ du dben sha'i las ka lon pas rdor bkras du dben sha zer/ de'i sras dbon bzhi 'dzom zhes 'jig rten gyi mes po lta bu de la gong ma grags
pa rgyal mtshan gyis gzhis ka gong dkar gyi rdzong dpon bskos/ de'i sras rgyal ba shes rab ces pa mi'i lus la lha'i rnam

dpyod 'dra ba zhig byung / yab 'di dang / yum skye dgu'i bdag mo dpal ldan rdo rje bde ma gnyis kyi sras su 'khrungs pa yin te/ de yang dus 'khor ba'i lugs kyi ston pa mya
ngan las 'das nas lo nyis stong sum brgya dang brgyad 'das shing / dgu pa'i dus chu pho byi ba'i lo'i smin drug zla ba'i tshes bco brgyad kyi tho rangs rgyal chen gling gi
khang bzang du sku bltams so/ /de dus kyi sku'i rim gro gzungs grwa lnga la gtso bor byas pas mtshan yang grwa lnga rgyal po zhes gsol lo/ /chung ngu'i dus nas rigs sad
pa'i stobs kyis 'bri klog la sogs pa thogs pa med par mkhyen pa byung / yum gyi thugs dgongs la sde srid 'dzin pa zhig 'ong ngam snyam/ skye bo gso thigs dang / sa skya
legs bshad la sogs pa rgya bod kyi 'jig rten lugs kyi bstan bcos mang po dang / gzhan yang rta glang brtag pa dang / go mtshon brtag pa la sogs pa mang po slob tu bcug na'ang
/ lkog tu bde bar

gshegs pa'i gsung rab dang / rgya bod kyi mkhas pa'i bstan bcos mang po la gzigs shing / khyad par sa skya pa yab sras kyi gsung rab la shin tu mos par mdzad pas/ mngon sum
du mes po yin zer ba'i mi mdog nag pa sma ra dang thor cog dkar po yod pa'i rkang dung bzung ba zhig gis gtor zan skam po ster zhing khyod kyi grogs ngas byed pa yin zer
ba rgyun du byung gsungs pas/ de dus nas gnyan mgon zhal bzhi pas rjes su bzung bar grags so/ /de nas re zhig la gzhan dbang gi stabs su song nas dgung lo bco lnga pa me
pho stag gi lo la gzhis ka gong dkar du phebs/ yum gyi thugs bzhed dang bstun nas lo shas la sde srid 'dzin pa mdzad na'ang / de'i phun tshogs thams cad dug chu'i btung
ba bzhin du gzigs pas gtan nas bor te/ bstan pa la rab tu 'byung bar shin tu rings pas/ thog mar theg chen chos kyi rgyal po'i dngos slob

brag thog chos rje bsod nams bzang po'i drung du dbu skra bcad de dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa mnos/ dpal sa skya pa'i lugs kyi chos skor rgyud gsum man ngag dang bcas pa la sogs
pa'i dbang bka' bshad bka'/ man ngag gi bka' la sogs pa rnams kyi skor cha lag phran dang bcas pa yongs su rdzogs par gsan/ mkhas par bslabs/ thugs nyams su bzhes/ yi dam

gsan cing / khyad par gur phur la sogs pa'i gar 'cham dbyangs la sogs pa la mkhas par mdzad/ de nas dgung lo nyi shu rtsa bdun tsam la/ thams cad mkhyen pa byams pa gling
pa chen po'i drung du dge tshul gyi sdom pa bzhes te sku shin tu btsun pa'i mchog tu gyur/ mtshan kun dga' rnam rgyal dpal bzang po zhes gsol/ gzhan yang mkhas pa de'i drung
du mdo sngags

kyi chos mang du gsan cing / khyad par ka lA pa la sogs pa sgra'i bstan bcos cha lag dang bcas pa la shin tu mkhas par mdzad/ zhwa lu ba slob dpon rin po che ye shes rgya mtsho'i
drung du rnal 'byor rgyud kyi bshad pa phyag len cha lag dang bcas pa la mkhas par mdzad/ dus 'khor ba dpal don grub kun dga'i drung du/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang /
rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa/ rtsis kyi sa ris dang bcas pa la mkhas par mdzad/ grwa ston rig pa'i ral gri shes rab dpal ldan dang / byams chen rab 'byams pa kun mkhyen sangs
rgyas 'phel sogs kyi drung du bka' chen bzhis gtso byas pa'i phyi sde snod phyogs kyi po ti rnams la mkhas par mdzad/ bka' 'gyur bar grags pa sems dpa' chen po shAkya rgyal
mtshan pa'i drung du bka' 'gyur bstan 'gyur gyi lung ches shin tu rgya che bar bzhugs pa rnams yongs su rdzogs par gsan/ de nas dgung lo sum cu rtsa gsum pa shing pho

spre'u'i lo la dpal rdo rje gdan gyi gtsug lag khang btab/ dge 'dun gyi sde btsugs/ bar chad kyi mtshan ma tsam yang med par grub/ dgung lo sum cu rtsa lnga pa me pho khyi'i
lo la gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skyar phebs pas/ sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin yin pas zer nas/ gdung rgyud zhal ngo phebs pa lta bu'i bsu ba/ ser 'phreng / rol cha bkra
shis khra ring skyong ba sogs kyi bkur bsti mtha' yas pa byung / yab gzhis rnying mar phebs pa lta bu'i thugs dgyes tshor mdzad/ bdag po'i drung gis gzhi len yang dag dang
/ bla brang so so'i mkhan po/ brgya tsho dpon rnams kyis rnyed bkur phun sum tshogs pa mdzad/ dbu rtse gsar rnying gis gtso byas pa'i lha khang gzim khang thams cad du
phebs/ rten gsum rnams la na bza' snyan dar 'bul ba sogs dang / sgo rum du chos skyong la bskang gso mdzad pas bse mgon chen po sku yongs rdzogs su gzigs nas thugs

nyams 'ur/ nangs par kha'u la phebs pas/ dam tshig can la chos skyong gi bsu chang du grags pa'i kha'u gtsang po glo bur du 'ur sgra dang bcas te sngar gyi lam la mi shong
ba tsam byung / chos skyong la gtor ma mda' dar 'bul ba sogs dang bskang gso rgyas par mdzad/ de dus bskang gso'i skabs/ brag gseb nas mi rkang gi sgra byin gyis thos pa
byung bas/ thams cad kyi bung zhes byed de gcig gis gcig la lag pa 'jus shing ngo mtshar bar gyur/ rje btsun pa nyid kyis brag sgo'i thad na gnyan gyi mgon po bram ze'i gzugs
su sku phyed tsam gzigs shing / 'phrin las ji ltar bsgo ba bzhin mdzad pa'i tshul bstan pa byung bar 'dug nangs par phyir phebs dus skyed lhas su bzhugs gding lus pas/
dus phyis kyang 'dir 'khor ba'i rten 'brel yod gsungs shin tu dgyes par mdzad/ yar mar gyi lam bar rnams la chos sde che chung gi bla ma slob dpon rnams kyis chos

'brel dang bsnyen bkur zhu ba mang bar byung / yang rngog pa'i gdung rgyud byang sems bsod nams don grub pa'i drung du rngog lugs kyi dkyil 'khor bdun la sogs pa'i chos skor
mang du gsan/ lo chen shes rab rin chen pa'i drung du gsang sngags ci rigs dang / slar yang 'dul mdzod dang / sgra'i bstan bcos la sogs pa'i chos skor mang du gsan cing
/ khyad par bka' gdams pa'i thig le bcu drug gi bka' dang glegs bam gyi lung la sogs pa'i chos skor rnams yongs su rdzogs par gsan to/ /de nas dgung lo bzhi bcu zhe gsum
pa shing pho rta'i lo la dpal thams cad mkhyen pa byams pa gling pa'i zhal snga nas mkhan po/ mkhan chen rab 'byor seng ge bas las slob/ khrom yon par grags pa mkhan chen
nam mkha' lhun bzang pas gsang ste ston pa mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs pa mdzad do/ /grub pa'i dbang phyug ras chen chos rje'i drung du nai gu chos drug shin tu nye bar
brgyud pa la
