sogs pa'i zab chos mang du gsan cing / gzigs snang khyad par can mang du byung ba'i lo rgyus kyang yod/ yang grwa ston shes rab dpal ldan pa'i drung du u rgyan pa'i rdo rje
gsum gyi bsnyen sgrub dang / bka' rdzogs pa chen po la sogs pa'i chos skor cha lag dang bcas pa yongs su rdzogs par gsan/ kun spangs bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa'i drung du
rgyud sde gong 'og gi bka' lung rgya che bar gsan cing / khyad par du bde gshegs sgrub pa bka' brgyad dang / 'dus pa mdo'i dbang la sogs pa gsang sngags rnying ma'i chos
skor gyi dbang lung man ngag la sogs pa mtha' dag yongs su rdzogs par gsan to/ /de dag ni bsten yun ring la mkhas par sbyangs shing bka' drin che ba'i yongs su 'dzin pa
rnams yin la/ bka' drin mtshungs pa med pa ni brag thog pa chen po kho na yin no/ /yang dbang rjes gnang / lung man ngag thor bu ba tsam gsan pa ni/ sa skya 'khon gyi gdung

rgyud bdag chen rgya gar ba/ zhwa dmar ba sprul sku chos kyi grags pa/ paN chen nags kyi rin chen/ mkhan chen khrom yon pa/ mkhan chen bya brtson pa la sogs pa'i mkhas grub
mang du yod/ gzhan yang bka' lung rnam dag 'dug na gang zag rang ga ba yin kyang / mkhas pa'i khengs pa mi mdzad par bstan pa dang sems can gyi don la dgongs nas gus pa
dang bcas te gsan par mdzad do/ /de ltar na bdag nyid chen po 'di ni mdo sngags thams cad kyi bdag po yin yang / ding sang rdo rje theg pa'i bstan pa la dgongs nas spyir
gsang sngags gsar rnying thams cad dang / khyad par dpal sa skya pa'i bstan pa rdo rje theg pa'i skad du smra ba rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bu ltar gyur te sa skya 'khon gyi
gdung rgyud kyis gtso mdzad/ bod dbus gtsang gi bla ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen mkhas grub rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo nyin mtshan khor yug tu bskor bar mdzad pas/ bu slob bstan
'dzin gyi

tshogs kyang grangs dang tshad med pa zhig byung ba yin la/ rje 'dis chos skyong rnams gzigs tshul mtshon pa tsam zhig brjod na/ lan gcig dus gtor zhig gi dus su sngar bas
zil che zhing / zhabs 'bring ba rnams skyi g.ya' bar byung zhing / de'i srod kyi dus tsam na sgra chen po dang / 'phral du spos gtong mkhan med kyang chos skyong gi spos
sbyor gyi ngad chen po ldang ba dang gzi byin shin tu che ba'i ngang nas/ rje 'di nyid kyi sku mdun gyi nam mkha' la gur gyi mgon po pad nyi ro'i gdan la sku mdog sngon po
zhabs g.yas cung zad phyed krung gi tshul gyis rting pa la zhabs g.yon gyi brang gtad pa/ phyag gnyis gri thod steng 'og tu 'dzin pa/ dbu skra ser po gyen du langs pa la
thod skam lnga'i dbu rgyan can/ stag lpags kyi sham thabs dang rin po che'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ sku g.yon du cung zad 'gying zhing me'i rgyab yol dang bcas pa

'jigs su rung ba blta bar mi bzod pa'i gzi byin can zhig mngon sum du gzigs pa las/ thugs bde ba dang dpa' ba'i nyams dang ldan bzhin pa'i ngang nas ji zhig na mi snang bar
gyur pas/ de dag gi sku'i bkod pa 'phral du bri ba'i slad du zhabs 'bring pa rnams la ras gzhi zhig gi rtsol ba bgyis bka' stsal pas/ mtshan mo de ma thag ras gzhi chung
ngu tsam las ma rnyed pas/ rje nyid kyis de ka la sku dbyibs ji lta ba'i skya ris gnang / nangs par nas rig byed mkhyen brtse bas tshon ris rdzogs par mdzad cing / shin
tu gces spras kyi ngang nas mchod gtor gyi dbus su yun du bzhugs pa las/ nam zhig la nye gnas chen mo brgya byin pa sku khams ma bde ba'i dus/ bris sku 'di'i steng nas rjes
gnang tshar 'ga' gnang / re zhig sngas srung gi tshul du bzhugs pa las/ dus phyis kyang khong pa'i sger gzhis rnam rgyal rab brtan na rten gsum kun gyi

gtso bor bzhugs so/ /chos skyong gi bskang gso mdos gtor gyi dus/ pu tra lcam sring dang bcas pa rnams 'cham par bya ba'i phyir zhal 'bag rnams so sor grub ste/ 'cham gyi rim
pa ji ltar bya ba'i dgongs pa gtad mtshams mtshan gcig gzims mal du mi nag po zhig gis/ da lta bgyi ba'i 'cham gyi rim pa tshar gcig bgyis pa na/ mnal sad de chos skyong
nyid kyis bstan par thugs kyi nges pa rnyed nas/ dus mi ring bar rdo rje'i slob bu rnams la 'cham gyi rim pa ji lta ba bzhin bslab sbyangs gnang / de dang rjes su mthun
par 'cham yig kyang thugs rtsom phyag bris su btab bo/ /yang sku zhang 'jam dbyangs pa chos skyong la mnga' brnyes pa yin pas/ nam zhig na pu tra lcam sring rnams nam mkhar
byon dus mchod gtor 'bul bar brtsams pa na myur du phul/ nged gong dkar la 'gro dgos yod gsungs pa byung tshul gyi 'phros zab mo

yod/ de la sogs pa'i lo rgyus ngo mtshar can mang du yod kyang 'dir ma spros la/ mthar rje nyid dgung lo drug cu rtsa lnga pa me pho 'brug gi lo nag pa zla ba'i phyogs phyi
ma'i tshes gcig tsam nas snyung ba'i tshul bstan nas/ spyi sgos kyis sku rim rgya chen po bsgrubs shing / zla ba de'i nyer gsum gyi nyin 'du khang du 'dus pa'i tshogs la
gtor skyong rgya chen po bgyis zhes pa dang / sku mdun nyid du chos skyong gi sku byin rlabs can bkram pa dang / mchod gtor spyan gzigs sogs legs par bshams te/ thugs sras
kun dga' rgyal po dang / slob dpon bsod nams rgyal po gnyis la bskang gso mnga' gsol legs par bgyis zhes bka' stsal cing / rje btsun nyid kyis kyang thugs 'dun ched du
gtad de bstan pa bstan 'dzin dang bcas pa chos skyong la gnyer gtad gnang / de dag gi rten mchod gtor dang bcas pa ni sus kyang g.yo ma nus pas ding sang gi bar du

gnas de nyid du brtan par bzhugs so/ /de nas tha mal gyi gsung bcad de thugs dam la rtse gcig tu bzhugs te/ spyan gnyis nam mkhar lta stangs kyi ngang nas bla ma yi dam sangs
rgyas byang sems dpa' bo mkha' 'gro mngon sum du bzhugs pa la gzigs bzhin pa dang bcas nyer bzhi'i thun tha ma la phyogs pa tsam na dgongs pa chos dbyings su thim pa'i
tshul bstan cing / de dag gi skabs rnams su nam mkha' la me tog gi char dang / 'ja' 'od kyi gur/ sgra rol mo sogs kun gyis mthong zhing thos pas/ thams cad dad pa'i spu
long rab tu g.yos par gyur to/ /yang sa skya pa'i chos skyong skor gyi bstan pa la mchog tu bka' drin che ba'i bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan gyi snyan brgyud
gdams pa'i bka' bab rje rdo ring pa chen po kun spang chos kyi nyi ma nyid la dam can rgya mtsho'i tshogs kyis zhal bstan cing 'phrin las sgrub pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i
rnam thar

cung zad brjod na/ de yang rje 'di nyid sku na phra mo'i dus dpal mgon gyi sngags ring thugs la bzung nas de 'phral nya ra'i phyogs su byon nas lam du snod stong dang zhwa
longs sogs mi sdug pa'i mtshan ma dgu bstud nas byung / mthar thugs dran pas mi zin pa tsam byung pa na/ chibs gzhol te gur mgon gyi srung 'khor bsgoms pas ci bder song nas
ngo mtshar ba'i mtshan ma byung gsungs/ 'di lta bu'ang 'phral rtse reg gi rnam par snang yang nges par phugs rjes su 'dzin pa'i ltas su 'dug de bzhin du rten skya bo'i
dus nas dpal mgon gyi gtor ma bsngo ba'i skabs 'gar gtor ma'i zhal yud kyis bsgyur yong ba dang / glo bur du phebs bzhud dgos pa'i skabs 'ga' zhig tu dur khrod bdag po'i
rgyun gtor khru re tsam dang mtho re tsam ci rigs par 'phar ba kun gyis mthun grub tu mthong ba dang / chu mig bla brang du bzhugs pa'i nub cig nam phyed tsam na thug com
'ur sgra shin tu che ba zhig

byung ba'i rjes su rje nyid bzhugs pa'i sgo de shag ste phye nas/ pu tra 'di mi nag po gos nag can 'jigs su rung ba zhig tu byas/ phyag g.yas na ral gri'i 'od kyis nang thams
cad sgron me btegs pa bzhin lhag lhag 'ong ba zhig bsnams g.yon na mi mgo khrag thigs pa zhig khur nas/ 'di len pa dka' las chen po byung zer sdug yus dang bcas pas bskyur
nas song gsungs/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i drung du nag po chen po'i gsang khrid gsan nas sgom pa'i dus shig 'od gsal gyi gzigs snang la rang nyid gur gyi mgon
po dngos su gzigs shing / de'i g.yon phyogs na yum chen e ka dza Ti bzhugs pa'ang gsal bar gzigs/ 'khor gzhan rnams kyang yod snyam pa tsam byung gsungs/ lan cig mnal
lam gyi rnam par skyed lhas shar ngos kyi spyil po zhig na bzhugs 'dug pa'i tshe/ mi gcan

gzan gyi thul pa gyon pa mang po na la byung ba la thugs 'jigs pa'i rnam pas nam mkha' la 'phur te/ mgon khang gi mdun ngos kyi nam mkha' la phebs pa na/ mgon khang gi steng
gi seng phug gi thad nas mgul yan chad thon pa'i zhal bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa nam mkha'i mdog lta bu 'dzum zhing khro ba spyan re re la'ang nyi ma bye ba'i 'od tsam 'phro
bas mig gis blta bar mi bzod pa zhig 'dug gsungs/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan gyi drung du bdag chen zhwa lu ba nas brgyud pa'i dpal mgon chen po'i chos skor 'ga' gsan
pa'i tshe/ rje 'di'i sku zhabs su bram ze mdog sngo bsangs ras yug sngon po'i lding gon byas pa zhig glo bur du yud kyis byung ba gzigs 'phral thugs nyams 'ur ba dang / chos
rje pa gsung chos gnang 'phro bzhag nas dpal mgon gyi sngags 'don cing bzhugs 'dug gsungs/ lan cig skyed lhas su grib kyi rnam pas gsung 'gags te

ma thon pa sogs cung zad bsnyel ba'i rnam pa byung nas/ khrus chog sogs sku rim byed par rtsom pa na/ nye gnas la yar shog gsungs 'phags pa brag khung du sku mdun phyin pas
sku khams sangs dwangs nas/ khyed tsho'i rim gro mi dgos par 'dug nga rang la rim gro byed mkhan byung gsungs/ ji ltar byung zhus pas/ da lta a tsa ra lag pa g.yon na ku
ba chus gang ba dang / g.yas na ku sha khyer ba gcig byung nas/ khyed la sku grib byung 'dug pas ngas khrus chog byed pa yin zer nas khrus chu lus la 'thor zhing sngags
kyi rnam pa bton nas song bas/ de 'phral la phan byung gsungs pa dang / skyed lhas kyi mgon khang nang du byon res kyi phal cher bdag chen rin po che'i zhal gzigs kyi bram
ze dkar po dar gyi gos can rtse gsum dang thod khrag 'dzin pa 'di yum chen bzhi dang bcas pa brag sgo nas bsu ba'i tshul du 'cham stabs dang bcas nas 'byon/

res 'ga' a tsa ra gzhung ma'i rnam par yang ston gyi 'dug gsungs/ lan gcig na lendra'i gzim khang gi blos bslangs steng du slob ma nyung shas shig la gur mgon gyi rjes gnang
gnang dus/ mdun gyi nam mkhar sprin nag gi khrod na mgon po lha brgyad 'khor bcas me phung 'bar ba dang bcas pa mngon sum du gzigs/ shab stod du gtor sgrub cig mdzad pa'i
gral du spyan 'dren gyi dus rje nyid kyis rdo rje dril bu drag tu gsor dkrol mdzad cing / thugs yengs pa lta bu'i ngang nas sku mdun gyi lcog tse'i thad kyi bar snang
du rdo rje dril bu bzhag pas/ re zhig de kar chags byung pa la/ sku'i khris na yod pa des grub rtags gnang byung lags zhus pas/ slar phyag gis blangs te gang byung ba gsung
zer ba'ang thos/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen po 'phan yul dpal ldan rtse na bzhugs pa'i dus/ sa skyar ci rigs kyi zhabs 'dren gyi bca' bsgrigs sogs mang dag byung ba
la brten/

bdag chen rin po che'i zhal ta la de don la chos rje kun spangs pa skor cig 'byon dgos pa 'dug pas gnas tshul dang blang dor 'di bzhin gyis kyi zhal bkod zhib par phebs/ gang
ltar las chos skyong rnams kyis sgrub pa yod gsungs/ chos skyong rnams la'ang gsung gdengs mthon pos khong gi rjes la rgyugs shig gsungs pa dang / phar lam na lendrar
chos rje mkhyen rab pas chos shig gnang ba yod pas zhus gsungs/ rje 'di'i dgongs pa la chos rje rin po che mkhyen rab pa ni sku mtshams shin tu dam par yod 'dug ji ltar yong
ngam gang na'ang bka' ltar bsgrub dgos snyam nas byon pas na lendrar phebs/ brag pa'i spyi khang na bzhugs pa'i tshe/ gzim khang nas 'bod mkhan gnang byung / nga slebs
pa sus zhus/ rje rin po che sku mtshams grol ba e yin gsungs pas sku mtshams shin tu dam par yod/ zhal ta la chos rje

kun spangs pa phebs yod 'dug pas/ da lta gdan drongs shog gsung gin 'dug zer/ der byon pas mkhyen rab chos rje'i zhal ta la/ da rangs tho rangs bdag chen rin po che sngas mgor
byon nas/ chos rje kun spangs pa sa skyar brdzangs nas 'dir 'byon pa yod pas mjal ga thongs gsung ba byung / da rangs las mkhan rnams dang / bya nag g.yag nag khyi nag
sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa dpal ldan rtse nas sgo la mi shongs pa tsam song / bdag chen rin po che'i sku don gal chen rang zhig yod pa 'dra/ gang ltar nged kyis lam gyi
bar chad sel ba la gzungs grwa lnga'i dbang bskur zhig byed thugs dam da ci nas tshar gsungs nas gnang bas/ rje yab sras gnyis ka la mi phyed pa'i dad pa 'khrungs shing
spyan chab mang po lhug par shor/ de nas rim gyis brgyud nas phebs pa'i lam bar rnams su spyan zur la chibs kyi snga sha la byis pa'i mgo gcig phrul phrul yong / ched du
gzigs pa na med 'gro ba dang /

gzhan yang chos skyong gi rnam 'phrul 'jigs su rung ba mang po byung gsungs/ de nas sa skyar phebs gdong du gros ngan shom pa'i gtso bo de'i bu shin tu gces pa zhig shi gzhan
rnams la'ang mi 'dod pa'i ltas du ma byung bas/ thams cad 'jigs shing skrag nas zhal ta gang gnang lhur len pa byung / seng ge rtse ba'i bdag mo chen mos/ nged la gzhan
gyi byad ka'i rnam pas mi sdug pa'i ltas ngan du ma 'byung ba zhig 'dug pa/ mgon po'i sgo nas bzlog pa zhig cis kyang mdzad dgos zhes nan gyis gsungs pa la brten/ mgon
po'i mdos gtor sbrags pa gcig zhag 'ga' bsgrubs nas mthar 'phen pa la phyogs pa na/ phyogs de'i chos sde'i grwa ba sogs 'gas ji ltar byed dam zer co 'dri ba'i rnam pas ltad
mo la byung ba'i tshe/ mdos la rje nyid kyi phyag reg pa tsam gyis de'i khrod nas me phru ba 'bring tsam zhig nar

gyis chad nas/ mthar phyar ra chen po tsam du song nas stod phyogs la song ba dang / dpal mgon chen po'i gtor ma sa shin tu mkhregs pa la phyed nub tsam du thim song bas/ der
tshogs thams cad 'jigs skrag zhum zhing ha las/ kho sngags rgod bgrangs pa'i nus pa yod pa zhig yin pa 'dug zer zhing log bdag mo'ang dga' mgu yi rangs te rjes su sbyin
bdag gi mthil mdzad pa zhig byung / de nas zhag 'ga' nas byad ma de'ang dag pa'i zhing du song ba'i gtam byung nas rje nyid kyis rjes su 'dzin par mdzad pa yin no/ /yang
mngon spyod kho nas 'dul bar 'os pa mi bskyod rdo rje'i sar rings par chas pa'i skye bo mi bsrun pa zhig gis/ rje nyid la ngan smras shags 'debs sogs mi 'tshams pa du ma
byas pa'i dus/ rje 'di nyid nag po chen po'i gsang khrid nyams bzhes mdzad pa'i las sbyor gyi skabs dang 'grig pa byung bas/ ma rungs pa de la

thugs brtse ba chen pos kun nas bslangs te/ las sbyor gyi dmigs pa thun gcig gtong bar mdzad pa na gzigs snang du mdun thams cad gos lhab lhub nag po gon pa 'ba' zhig gis gang
nas/ gzhan ci yang mi gzigs pa zhig byung gsungs/ de nas bsgrub bya de khrag bskyugs te zhag gsum gyi khongs su shi rjes su bu brgyud rnams kyis rje nyid la gus pas btud
cing mgon skyabs zhus te gnas pa zhig byung / lan cig gsol ja cung dkon pa zhig gi tshe/ nye gnas kong po ngor la 'gro khar zhal kur gyi tshul du/ dur khrod bdag po la/
kho'i zla la rgyugs la ja khug shog gsungs pas/ khong tsho'i ngor mda'i ja pa zhig gi nang du gnas tshang g.yar ba'i tshe/ de pa'i g.yog cig la babs nas ja dgos tshul
smras pas/ rtog pa skyes nas gsol ja shin tu zhim pa bton nas tshong 'bul byas pa byung / de bzhin du phyogs nas 'bul ba

gnang che ba sogs 'ong ba'i nub mo 'di dang 'di yong ba yod zer ngo so'i rnam pa mang po byed pa dang / mdor na dpal mgon gdong bzhi pa/ pu tra mi sring / dur khrod bdag po
rnams rnam 'phrul du mas rgyun par gzigs snang du 'ong ba yin 'dug des na 'di rnams kyi rjes gnang yang gzhan dag ltar rang gi dga' sdug dang ngo 'dzin sogs kyi ched du
ye mi gnang / 'phral rmi lam gyi brtag pa byed dgos gsung / don la chos skyong rang gis lung ston par snang bas/ res 'ga' zhu mkhan ye med pa nas mchod bshom dang thugs dam
mdzad pa na/ skal ldan gyi slob ma thag ring nas rkang btsugs su slebs nas/ de 'phral gnang chog pa'ang mang po byung 'dug la las ji tsam gsol ba btab kyang mi gnang /
de yang lan cig lta grub mi mthun pa'i grwa pa zhig gis dpal mgon gyi rjes gnang zhur yong pa la/ rmi lam mi tshud pa 'dug pas mi 'ong gsungs kyang / mi gnang na lcebs zer
ba

sogs kyi nan tan zhus 'dug pas/ rje nyid mgon khang du phebs thugs dam mdzad pa'i mthar/ brag sgo phyogs la gzigs nas mi la lab pa ltar/ da rjes gnang mi byed byas kyang ye
mi nyan par 'dug pas/ byed mi btub na kun gyi mthun snang grub pa'i ltas ston gsungs pa sogs gnang bas/ de 'phral 'ur sgra dang thug chom chen po skyed lhas kyi ri de nyil
nas mgo thog tu lhung ba snyam byed pa kun gyis thos pa byung / grwa pa de'ang bla brang 'gag na chos bsgugs kyi tshul du yod 'dug pas re zhig dran med du brgyal/ slar
gsos nas thugs bden par 'dug da rjes gnang ye mi zhu/ 'khu ldog sogs mi yong ba'i byin rlabs shig dgos zhu ba byung ba de 'dra'i rigs can mang dag byung 'dug skal ldan rigs
la khams pa bla ma yakSha tro te zer ba zhig gis khams su mgon po zhal bzhi pa bsgrubs pas/ de'i sku'i

rnam pa mi langs pa'i lag pa brkyangs pa'i steng du zhabs gnyis bzhag pa gcig mtho ba'i zhal nas kha'u skyed lhas su rdo ring rtsar rgyugs gsungs pa'i lung bstan byung bas/
rkang btsugs 'ongs te rjes gnang zhus pas dus de nyid du ting nge 'dzin du ma rgyud la skyes nas mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob pa dang / ldan ma'i grwa ba zhig gis rjes gnang
zhus pa'i tshe/ bla ma nag po chen por gsal ba'i zhes pa'i gsung thos 'phral rje nyid nag po chen po dngos su mthong ba'i zhal gdangs pa'ang nang de dmar khrig ste gang
ba tsam du mthong nas lus nyams bzung bas mi thub pa byung zhing / phyis su'ang lam zab bsgoms pa tsam gyis lus nam mkha' la bya ltar lding zhing / thog so mang po la yar
mar gang la'ang thogs med du 'phur ba sogs ngo mtshar ba byung bar grags pa sogs mtha' yas so/ /rje de nyid kyi thugs sras rgyud 'dzin kun gyi gtsug rgyan dam par gyur
cing / dpal ldan sa

skya pa'i snyan brgyud kyi bdud rtsi spel ba la 'gran zla dang bral ba'i mkhas pa'i dbang po tshar pa chos rje blo gsal rgya mtsho grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes
mtshan yongs su grags pa de nyid bstan srung dbang po rnams kyi chos skor gyi rgyun la bka' drin che ba'i tshul sogs cung zad brjod na/ de yang rje de nyid kyis rdo ring
kun spangs pa chen po gtso bor gyur pa'i mkhas grub kyi yongs 'dzin mang du bsten nas/ sa skya pa'i yab chos gsung ngag lam 'bras/ chos skyong che chung / dmar po skor gsum
sogs kyi man ngag gtso bor gyur pa'i zab rgyas chos kyi bdud rtsi mtha' yas pa zhig gsol bas/ dus phyis byon pa'i bstan 'dzin zhig la gsan rgya che ba'i tshad du gyur
cing / lhag par sa skya pa'i bstan srung gur gyi mgon po dang zhal bzhi pa'i chos skor rnams brgyud ldan gyi bla ma du ma zhig la gtugs te/ lhag ma ma lus pa bum pa gang

byo'i tshul du gsan/ thos bsam sgom gsum gyis gtan la phab ste/ 'di skor la rang nyid las mkhas pa med snyam pa'i thugs kyi spobs pa khyad par can brnyes te/ chos rgyun rnams
mi nyams pa'i phyir bstan pa'i khur chen po bzhes nas/ de dag gi chos skor man ngag mtha' dag rnams kyi bka' bsdu ba po lta bu mdzad de/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis sgrig
par mdzad pa'i mgon pod me 'bar ma'i dkar chag tu chos sna'i rkang grangs dngos su thebs pa rnams dang / dngos su ma thebs kyang don thob la glegs bam der bzhugs dgos
rgyu'i nang sgrub dang / gsang sgrub kyi skor gyi dpe sna 'ga' dang / bdag chen nyid kyi dkar chag dang bcas pa'i yongs bsdoms yig sna brgya dang lnga bcu po mtha' dag
ma tshang ba dang 'thor ba'i skyon spang ba'i phyir/ tshigs bcad du bsdebs pa snying po gnad kyi sgron me zhes bya ba mdzad nas de'i mjug tu/ de lta'i man ngag glegs bam
'di/ /ming tsam yongs su grags pa'i phyir/ /yod ces

gleng ba mang na yang / /'di bzhin tshang ba nyin skar tsam/ /brgya la yi ge tshang na yang / /man ngag shes pa'i brgyud pa las/ /'ongs pa'i zhal shes lag len can/ /sngags
'chang u dum wa rar mtshungs/ /de yi rgyu mtshan 'di ltar yin/ /dam pa'i mgon dang mjal ba dka'/ /mjal yang lus dang longs spyod kun/ /phul nas chig bsgril bsten pa dkon/
/de phyir rdo ba'i ngos la ni/ /'bru yi sa bon btab pa'am/ /ko Ta pa las sa lu bzhin/ /rgyu 'bras bslu med gnad kyis so/ /des na 'khon ston rdo rje 'chang / /gang de'i thugs
sras kun spangs rje/ /kho bos gtsug gi rgyan du bsten/ /ci gsung bka' rnams 'bad pas bsgrubs/ /skyabs gzhan spangs nas gcig tu bsgril/ /de yi mthu las thugs rje'i rgyun/
/bka' drin bdud rtsis snying myos pa'i/ /tshul 'di shes pa kho bor gda'/ /zhes kyang gsungs

shing / me 'bar ma der ma 'dus pa'i chos skyong gi yig sna'i skor rnams rje nyid kyis sgrig par mdzad pa'i kha skong glegs bam du grags pa'i dkar chag gsal ba'i sgron me/ yang
shin tu zab pa'i man ngag rnams rje nyid kyis phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i snyan brgyud glegs lam gyi dkar chag gsang chen gnad kyi za ma tog nyid kyis bsgrigs pa'i gyi
ljang lugs kyi mgon po'i chos skor gyi dkar chag dang / khog phub kyi yi ge zab don gnad kyi lde mig dpal mgon gdong bzhi pa'i chos skor rnams rje nyid kyis sgrig par mdzad
pa'i dkar chag zab don nor bu'i do shal/ rang nyid kyis bsgrigs pa'i 'dod khams dbang phyug dud sol lha mo'i chos skor gyi dkar chag gsal ba'i me long rnams mdzad de/
de lta bu'i chos skyong so so'i chos skor rnams glegs bam du bsgrigs shing / dkar chag gi them yig gis spras pa 'di ni bka' srung dbang po rnams kyi bstan pa'i rgyun srid
mtha'i bar du mi

nyams pa'i phyag rjes ngo mtshar can yin pas/ lugs 'di skor la 'dren pa dam pa 'di bka' drin gzhal du med par shes ldan dag gis rtogs par bya dgos pa yin zhing / rje btsun
bla ma de nyid kyis gur gyi mgon po'i chos skor rnams bla ma so so la gsan tshul ni/ dam pa de nyid kyis mdzad pa'i nag po chen po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar
las/ ding sang dpyod ldan mkhas pa mi brin zhing / /blun po rdzun bag mkhan dang zog po ni/ /'ur rgyang can dag kun gyis mchod cing bsngags/ /'di 'dra bstan pa nyams pas
kun kyang blun/ /kho bos rje btsun kun dga' bzang po las/ /brgyud pa'i gser pod la sogs kun kyang thos/ /rgyud gsum smra ba pradznyA ratna las/ /rdzong chung pa las brgyud
pa zhib tu zhus/ /khyad par grub mchog dbang po kun spangs zhabs/ /ring du bsten cing gdung rgyud rim pa las/ /brgyud pa'i ma ti dho dza'i snyan brgyud kyi/ /gdams pa

ma lus bum pa gang byor thob/ /mdor na dam pa'i yongs 'dzin bdun la gtugs/ /tshul 'di'i phra rags chos la ring du sbyangs/ /dag dang ma dag yi ge mang du mthong / /mkhas dang
mi mkhas sngags 'chang du ma bgros/ /'dir ni thun mong tsam la cung zad dris/ /zhib par phyi nang gsang gsum man ngag la/ /'dod tshul mang mod chos 'di zab pa dang / /chos
skyong gnyan pas dri ba spobs ma gyur/ /ces gsungs nas/ de ltar rang gis chos skyong gi chos skor la mkhas par sbyangs kyang / dri ba rags rim rnams mdzad pa'i rgyu
mtshan bshad pa dang / dris lan 'debs pa'i yul min pa rnams btang snyoms su bzhugs par gdams pa dang / dris lan 'debs 'os pa rnams kyis dri ba po'i kun slong rnam dag la
dgongs nas myur du dri lan stsol bar bskul ba dang / dri ba'i yi ge de nyid kyi ming don ston pa rnams rim pa bzhin du de nyid las/ de ltar dris pa'i dam pa khyed rnams la/
/

bdag la med pa'i tshad ldan brgyud pa las/ /byung ba'i 'di skor yod na brda thongs shig /zhabs rdul spyi bos mchod nas len par spro/ /zhes dang / blun po rgyus med nor gyis
dregs pa dang / /chen pos smras tshad gtam du song ba dang / /zog po ya med rtog ge'i dug chus myos/ /de rnams la ni dri min btang snyoms bzhugs/ /zhes dang / rang nyid
mkhas par bsgrub pa'i dregs 'dod dang / /gzhan la skyon 'dzin 'dod pa'i zol zog min/ /tshul 'di dad dang 'dun pas bskul ba yin/ /gsung bar 'os pa rnams kyis lan myur zhu/
/zhes dang / de ltar lhag bsam rab dkar 'dab gshog can/ /dogs ldan snyan tshig mgrin pa'i rdza rnga sgrog /zab don dri ba'i ngang mo yid 'ongs khyod/ /sngags 'chang mkhas
pa'i thugs kyi rgya mtshor song / /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de lta bu'i dri ba'i yi ge de nyid las/

gang la dri ba'i yul ngos bzung ba ni/ rgya chen sngags gzhung rgya mtsho'i mthar son cing / /zab don snyan brgyud nor bu'i dpal 'dzin pa'i/ /dpyod ldan gzur gnas rdo rje 'dzin
dag la/ /dogs pa'i gnas 'ga' gsol gyi legs bshad stsol/ /ces pas dri yul ngos bzung nas/ dri ba dngos la don tshan gyi rnam grangs mang du yod pa'i/ de dag gi mtha'
chod rnams ni kho bos byas pa'i chos byung gi bstan bcos 'dis dbu zhabs bar gsum gyi seb tshags su gsal bar byas pa nyid kyis rtogs nus pa yin la/ yang rje nyid kyis mdzad
pa'i mgon po'i man ngag zab bsdus gsal byed kha skong glegs bam gyi dkar chag las/ kho bos rgyal khams yangs pa'i phyogs kun nyul/ /mkhas grub bla ma mang po'i zhabs pad
bsten/ /rang gzhan gdams pa zab mo'i gnad kun shes/ /dag dang ma dag 'byed pa'i spobs pa thob/ /khyad par nag

po chen po'i man ngag ni/ /brgyud ldan bla ma bcu phrag gcig la zhus/ /'gran zla kun bral drin can rdo rings pa'i/ /snyan brgyud zab mo bum pa gang byor thob/ /e wa~M pa ni
bsdus la spros pa chung / /mus srad pa ni dkar chag khrigs chags can/ /rdo rje gdan pa 'cham dang nus pa'i bdag /kho bos thob pa'i thun mong brgyud pa gsum/ /de dag las
'ongs so so'i ngos 'dzin ni/ /ngor lugs yi ge e yig rtags kyi rgya/ /rdo rje gdan pa las brgyud rdo rje'i rgya/ /mu srad pa ni yi ge mu yi rgya/ /bdag chen rdo rje 'chang
dbang las brgyud pa'i/ /rtsa ba'i yi ge mchod rten rgya yis mdzes/ /thor bu gzhan dag mchan bur btab pas shes/ /rdo rje gdan pa dang ni mus srad pa/ /gnyis las brgyud pa
brda yig gnyis kyis mtshan/ /dang po gsum ldan gsum gyi brda yig can/ /bzhi car tshang ba

brda yig bzhi yis spras/ /de ltar shes pas lung rgyun nges par 'gyur/ /de dag rang rang skal ba ji bzhin bshad/ /'on kyang mtshams dang 'gros kyi spros pa ni/ /'dod na rdo
rje gdan pa las gzhan pa'i/ /tshad ldan med phyir de yi lugs bzhin ston/ /phyi nang gsang ba'i man ngag snyan brgyud kun/ /lag tu blangs nas nges par bsgrub 'dod na/ /bdag
chen rdo rje 'chang dbang las brgyud pa/ /'di las gzhan na med pas snying la chongs/ /zhes rang nyid kyis nag po chen po'i chos skor rnams bla ma rnams las gsan tshul dang
/ kha skong glegs bam de nyid kyi yig sna so so brgyud pa gang las brgyud shes pa'i phyir/ e yig dang / rdo rje dang / mchod rten dang / mu yig dang / mchan bu btab pa
sogs kyi rtags kyi nges pa rnams so sor shes par byas nas rang gzhan gyi don sgrub tshul gyi zhal gdams dang bcas gsungs shing / yang dam pa de nyid kyis

gnyan mgon chen po'i man ngag rnams gsan tshul yang / rje rang nyid kyis mdzad pa'i dpal mgon gdong bzhi pa'i chos skor gyi dkar chag zab don nor bu'i do shal las/ rdo rje
'chang dang klu sgrub mgon/ /ba ling ta pa ye shes zhabs/ /mar me mdzad dang dpal de ba/ /sbas pa'i zhabs dang rin chen gnyis/ /rnal 'byor dbang mo lo chen gnyan/ /kha'u
pa dang sa skya pa/ /rje btsun sku mched paNDi ta/ /blo gros rgyal mtshan dkon mchog dpal/ /brag phug pa dang bla ma rje/ /bla chen 'jam dbyangs nam mkha'i mtshan/ /bdag
chen rdo rje 'chang dbang zhabs/ /mthu stobs dbang phyug kun spangs rje/ /gang des bka' 'bangs bdag la'o/ /phyi yi man ngag phal cher ni/ /bla ma dam pa yar lung pa/ /bsod
nams rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs che/ /de nas gong bzhin brgyud kyang chog /phyi yi sgrub skor 'ga'

zhig ni/ /chos rje bla ma dpal ldan pa/ /shar chen pa dang rdo rje 'chang / /bdag chen kun dga' dbang phyug la/ /'khon ston mkhas grub ma tis gsan/ /yig chung 'ga' yi lung
dag ni/ /bla chen bdag po zhwa lu pa/ /paN chen shAkya mchog ldan la/ /rje btsun chos rjes gsan pa'o/ /bdag ni snyigs dus kha ba'i ljongs/ /ma rungs rgyu ba'i khrod du lhungs/
/'on kyang sngon gyi las dbang gis/ /yongs 'dzin dam pa 'ga' dang mjal/ /khyad par zhing skyong nag po'i skor/ /mkhas grub dam pa bdun las thob/ /yang dgos drin can
rdo rje 'chang / /kun spangs chen po'i zhabs pad bsten/ /dad gus gser gyi lde mig gis/ /zab don thugs kyi sgo phye nas/ /snyan brgyud bdud rtsi'i bum bzang gnang / /rnam
dpyod snyim par rab bzung ste/ /nan tan ro 'dzin gyis myangs pas/ /nges shes snying gi dkyil du shar/ /phyogs gzhan smon pa'i re ba bral/ /e ma

kho bo skal ba bzang / /zhes gsungs pa ltar yin la/ de lta bu'i skyes chen de nyid la sa skya pa'i bka' srung rnams shin tu 'go zhing las bsgrubs pa'i tshul sogs cung zad brjod
na/ sngon kha'u skyed lhas su rje rdo ring pa'i drung du mgon po'i chos skor rnams gsan nas lan cig phyogs gzhan du byon nas/ slar zhabs drung du phebs skabs bar lam
kun tu a tsa ra'i rnam pa can gnyis kyis g.yas g.yon nas gar mdzad cing / sku gzhogs skyor ba'i gzigs snang kha 'ur nam phebs kyi bar du byung 'dug pa ni/ chos skyong mahA
ka la gnyis kyis 'bral med du skyong zhing 'phrin las bsgrub pa'i mtshan mar 'dug pa dang / rgyun pa'i thugs dam chag med la yang / ki la ya/ aShTa/ oM gsum ma/ ya ma
rA dza/ sha sa na rnams stong phrag re mdzad pa las/ gtso bor chos skyong gi rtsa sngags nyid la thugs dam gyi mthil mdzad par

snang ste/ de nyid kyi gsung las/ ngas gsang sngags gsar rnying gi sngags phal cher bsnyen tshad bzhin ma bzlas pa ye med/ de rnams kyi nang nas kyang sha sa na 'di nus pa
che shos la 'dug ste/ 'di bgrang pa'i 'phreng ba la dngos su me 'bar ba yong gin 'dug ces gsungs pas rtogs nus pa yin la/ yang snga mo'i dus shig zhabs cung zad bsnyel ba'i
tshe/ mnal lam du g.yag khyu chen po zhig byung bas/ thugs cung zad ya nga ba na/ g.yag chen po zhig gis mi'i skad du/ nged rnams chos rje la gnod skyel ba min zer nas/
rje nyid kyi sku smad la re ba nag po 'dra ba zhig bkab 'dug pa rwa rtses blangs nas rgyang ring du 'phangs song bas/ de ma thag snyung gzhi las grol cing / yang bud med
gcig gis sa la ri mo 'ga' zhig bris nas/ lo 'di'i bar la zhabs kyi bsnyel ro cung zad ldang / de nas sku khams shin tu bzang ba yong zer byung bas/ de kho na bzhin mngon
du

gyur 'dug pa dang / chos skyong gis las mdzad pa'i rtags su snang zhing / yang mdar gyi dgon par thug chen 'ga' la rab gnas mdzad pa'i tshe/ gur gyi mgon po'i sku nam mkha'i
khyon gang ba/ phyag na gri gug sgo che ba'i tshad tsam zhig mngon sum du gzigs pa dang / yang rje mkhyen brtse bas myug gi dben dgon dpal sbug rnam par grol ba'i ri khrod
du gdan drangs/ rje nyid dang rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po bsod nams chos 'phel sogs skal ldan gyi slob ma bco brgyad tsam la zla ba bdun gyi bar du gsung ngag rin po che
slob bshad yongs su rdzogs pa/ mgon po che chung gnyis/ dmar po skor gsum/ dmar chung ma skor gsum sogs chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen po bskor/ gsung ngag rin po che grol
nas gtang rag gi gtor 'bul la gzim khang gi steng du rje rang nyid phebs pa'i tshe/ mdun gyi nam mkhar sprin chol le ba

'khrigs pa'i khrod na/ mgon po'i sku thog so gang tsam gzi brjid dang ldan pa zhig zhal mngon sum du gzigs te/ mgon po'i zhal nas ha ha dang hU~M hU~M gi sgra dbyangs dang
bcas pa'i brag cha rgyab tu 'phos pa 'dra ba'i skad tsher tsher ba gcig gi ngang nas chos 'di'i bdag po sngar yang nged rang gis byas/ da rung nga rang gis byed zer ba'i
sgra lhang lhang pa gsan pa byung pa dang / yang snga mo'i dus skyed lhas su rdo ring pa'i drung du dpal mgon zhal bzhi ba'i rjes gnang zhus pa'i tshe/ rje nyid kyi sku'i
mdangs na bza'i kha dog sogs mthing gar gzigs shing / khyad par ye shes dbab pa'i bar la bar snang nas mi rkang gi sgra shin tu gsal ba dang / phun sum tshogs pa mnga' ba
gser gyi ri bo 'dra/ / kyi bkra shis kyi tshigs bcad dbyangs dang bcas nas sgrog pa gsal bar gsan 'dug yang lan cig dpal mgon gyi gsung bsnyen mdzad pas/ thog mar cung
zad 'tshub pa'i rnam pa

dang / rjes su gzigs snang la bar snang nas gos chen lcags nag gi phod ka chen po gyon pa zhig gis phu rung gi sbubs nas lag pa chen po gcig yang yang ston pa sogs byung ba
yang chos skyong gis dngos su rjes su bzung ba'i cho 'phrul du snang la/ yang 'khrul zhig bka' bzhi ba chen po mjal ba la rje nyid kyis phebs pa'i skabs shig de'i sngon
tsam du rje bka' bzhi pa'i gsung gi chos rje tshar ba khong 'phral du 'byon gyi yod pa 'dug zhal bzhi pa 'khor bcas snga 'gros kyi tshul du byon byung zhes gsungs pa byung
pa dang / yang skabs 'gar/ de ring rje tshar pa la bya ba khag che ba zhig yod pa 'dug zhal bzhi pa khong brel gyin 'dug gsungs pa sogs thol byung du bka' phebs pa zhig
yod 'dug cing / yang lan cig rje bka' bzhi pa dang mjal ba'i tshe/ gsung las rin po che pas bo dong du mgon po'i zab chos shig mi mang rab cig la

bshad yod pa 'dra/ pu tra 'di cung zad mi dgyes pa'i tshul ston pa zhig 'dug pas rtsub 'gyur 'dra byung dogs 'dug go gsungs pas/ lam bar du chibs pa g.yang la lhungs nas/ rje
nyid kyi sku la skyon med pa grog khar bzhugs shing / grog gting gi rdo zhig la chibs pa'i rmig rjes byung bas/ de dus kyi slob ma rnams grub rtags 'jog pa'i snyad kyis
de bzhin du bstan par 'dug zer bar byung zhing / slar bskang bshags rgyas par mdzad pas/ las mkhan chen po thugs rab tu dgyes pa'i rtags khyad par can brnyes pa dang /
yang lan gcig skyed lhas kyi sum cu rtsa gsum du dmigs yul zhig la ched du gtad nas rje rdo rje 'chang gi man ngag g.yul las rnam rgyal bzhin gyi las sbyor mdzad pas/ zhag
'ga' nas bsgral bya de pu tras dngos su khrid byung ste/ las 'di bzhin bsgrubs yod pas/ gtang rag tu bskang gso zhig 'phral du gyis zer byung bas/ pu tra'i sgos kyi bskang
gso khyad

par can 'di yang de dus gsung rtsom mdzad pa yin la/ yang lha mo 'dod khams dbang phyug ma la las bcol nas/ bla ma'i sku dgra myur du sgrol bar mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ rje nyid
kyis mdzad pa'i de'i chos skor gyi dkar chag las 'di ltar 'byung ste/ 'di'i chos skor zhu ba kho bos rje btsun rdo ring pa chen pos gtso mdzad bla ma dam pa bcu phrag gcig
la gur gyi mgon po lcam dral 'khor dang bcas pa'i chos skor mtha' dag yongs su rdzogs par thob/ khyad par dpal ldan 'dod khams dbang phyug ma 'di nyid kyi sgos sgrub/
tshogs bdag ltar bsgrub pa/ bka' sdod ltar bsgrub pa/ phyi pa ltar bsgrub pa/ nang pa ltar bsgrub pa la sogs pa ma lus pa thob kyang / sa skya pa'i lugs la lha mo 'di'i
rjes gnang sbags sgrub kyi khongs su mdzad pa 'di ka ma gtogs zur bka' mdzad pa'i srol mi 'dug pa dang / dam

pa'i bsgrub yig tu yum 'khor dang bcas pa bsgrub par bshad pa la'ang ngos 'dzin gsal ba zhig mi 'dug pas/ 'di rnams rtogs par 'dod nas bod na bzhugs pa'i gsang sngags gsar
rnying gi lha mo'i sgrub thabs ji snyed gcig zhus shing / yi ge mtha' dag la brtags pas/ dmag zor rgyal mo dang / lcags phur ma la sogs pa rnams ni khol mo re ma ti'i rigs
su 'dug cing / rje mo re ma ti la'ang brgyud pa so so las 'ongs pa'i rigs mi 'dra ba mang du 'dug pa'i nang nas/ rngog lugs kyi dud sol ma phyi sgrub kyi rgya gzhung bram
ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa 'di dang / sa skya pa'i lugs kyi lha mo phyi pa mu stegs ltar bsgrub pa'i rgya gzhung bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa 'di gnyis la khyad par
cung zad kyang mi 'dug cing / de bzhin du rngog lugs kyi 'grel pa zhal gdams mar grags pa dang / sa skya pa'i lha mo'i yig chung yid bzhin nor bur grags pa'ang bris bshus

lta bur 'dug sku mdog phyag mtshan yang gzhan khyad par ci yang med pa la/ g.yon gyi phyag dang po'i phyag mtshan shakti'i ngos 'dzin la/ sa skya pa mdung rnon 'dzin pa 'dod/
rngog lugs pa rnams mdung rting gi nang du rma bya'i sgro chun bcug pa lta bu'i 'phang mdung / sor mdung / thag mdung zhes bya ba la ngos 'dzin na'ang don la khyad par
cher mi snang / de bzhin du lha mo gsang sgrub 'di'ang dur khrod dga' ba'i tshal du rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa la lha mo nyid kyis dngos su gnang / de nas shar phyogs
nag po pa la brgyud par 'dug pas brgyud pa'ang 'brel chags shing / 'di pa'i lugs la phyi sgrub dang / gsang sgrub gnyis char la rjes gnang zur pa re mdzad/ sgrub tshul
yang phyi sgrub/ nang sgrub/ gsang sgrub/ yang gsang drag mo rkang thang du bsgrub pa/ dkar mo me long ma/ nag mo stag zhon/ 'khor

yang 'gugs 'dren gsod byed kyi ma mo gsum/ rigs bzhi'i lha mo bzhi/ phra men gdong can brgyad/ ka~M ka ma bzhi la sogs pa bsgrub bya lha dang / sgrub byed man ngag gi sgo nas
ches zab pa'i khyad par ji snyed cig 'dug pas/ 'di'i chos skor zhu bar 'dod pa'i tshe/ sa skya pa'i khrod na 'di'i rjes gnang dang / yig lung sna re tsam yod pa 'dug na'ang
/ gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang phyi sgrub la sbyar ba dang / chos skyong gzhan gyi rjes gnang gi rgyas 'gebs pa sogs sna tshogs gcig 'dug dwags po bka' brgyud pa'i bla
ma 'dra la brtags dus kyang de lta bu dang / khyad par chos skor yongs su rdzogs pa bzhugs pa mi 'dug pas/ blo kha ma khengs par dka' ba khyad du bsad nas rngog tshang
'og mar grags pa gzhung thar gling gi dgon par phyin/ bla ma dang lha la yid ches dad pa snying nas thob/ gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang ma gtogs 'di'i

chos skor yongs su rdzogs pa gnas de nyid du thob/ sa phyogs de na rje 'di nyid la shin tu mi gus shing / sku srog gi 'tsho ba 'phrog pa la nye ba'i bla ma'i sku dgra gdug
pa can gcig 'dug pas/ rje nyid la 'di lta bu'i chos skyong 'dug pa la/ dam nyams 'di sgrol ba skabs su bab zhus pas/ khong tsho'ang 'di mchod pa dang / mgon khang gi lha
mo'i lder sku 'di'ang khong tsho ngos la rgyab bstan pa zhig yod pa'i rten 'brel yin nam/ da lta bar ni ci yang gnod pa zhig ma byung / da dung yang ji ltar yong ngam tshe
sngon gyi lan chags 'ded pa zhig yin pa 'dra gsungs thugs yid chad de ba zhig mdzad kyi 'dug pas/ kho bos bdag la 'di lta bu'i bstan srung khyad par can 'di'i chos skor
yongs su rdzogs pa 'bad med du gnang ba'i sku drin bsab phyir/ bla ma'i sku dgra 'di lha mo 'di'i sgo nas bdag gis sgrol bar zhu zhus pas/ de 'dra byung na bka' drin

bskyangs/ gu yangs shing sa phyogs gtsang ba zhig yong ba yod gsungs byung bas/ kho bos de gong du lha mo rkyang sgrub dang / sbags sgrub kyi sgo nas lha mo 'di la bsnyen pa
'bum phrag lnga bcu tsam song zhing / de'i mgon khang gi rngog ston gong mas bzhengs pa'i lha mo'i sku de nyid kyi zhal dang / sku'i gnas rnams su gri khrag dang rang byung
gi khrag gis thig le bkod/ zhal gyi nang dang gtor ma'i gseb tu dam nyams de'i ming yig drag po'i spel tshig dang bcas pa bcug sa rngog gi bla ma brgyud pa'i mtshan
nas brjod de bka' bsgo drag po lan gsum byas pas rang nyid kyang skyi bun pa dang / lha mo'i sku 'dra de'ang sngar las khro zhing / zhal ras nag ngam byas pa 'dra ba zhig
byung / de nub nas lha mo 'di la gtor ma zur pa re bcos ched du 'phrin las drag tu bcol bas/ zhag bdun song ba'i nub drang srong srin po'i rir gnas tshang gcig gi khang
steng du cog bu phub nas bsdad/ srod

kyi gtor bsngos kyi mthar mchod g.yog gis khang pa'i bad steng du thun gtor phul ba'i gtor ma'i gseb nas me stag mtheb rdog tsam zhig chad song ba kho bo rang gis mthong /
de je cher song nas rdza ma tsam dang / mthar khang pa tsam du song ba mchod g.yog gis mthong ba la gzhung gi thad du babs song zer/ de nas ring por ma thogs par mi tshang
de pa la shi chad 'thon bud sogs mi 'dod pa du ma byung nas rjes stong pa gcig byung / brgyud pa 'di las 'ongs pa'i lha mo 'di la drag shul nus mthu 'di lta bu yod pas/
rjes 'brangs rnams yid ches par gyis la nan tan du bsgrub par gyis shig de nas rngog dkyil bdun la sogs pa'i rngog lugs kyi chos skor rnams zhus pa'i rjes su/ brgyud pa
'di pa rang gi srol la lha mo gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang 'di rngog pa'i bstan pa zin nges gcig la byed pa'i lugs yin gsungs nas gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang cho

ga shin tu rgyas pa'i sgo nas bka' drin chen pos gnang / de dus kyang lha mo dngos su gtad pa tsam gyi nges shes dang yid ches pa byung / gong gi mngon spyod kyi ltas byung
ba'i rjes nub mang po'i bar sdig pa dag pa'i rmi ltas ches che ba ji snyed cig byung bas/ lam thams cad kyi nang nas lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor 'di ka zab pa la nges
shes khyad par can me 'bar ba la shing bsnan pa lta bur gyur ces 'byung ba yin la/ yang mkha' 'gro ma rnams kyis mnal lam du bskul nas rje rdo ring pa'i rnam thar mdzad
pa'i tshe/ mthar phyin par nye ba na/ dpal ldan lha mos rnam thar de'i chos bdag mdzad par zhal gyis bzhes pa'i tshul ni/ de'i lo rgyus kyi yi ge rje nyid kyi phyag bris
ma las 'di skad 'byung ste/ kho bo thub bstan dge 'phel na yod pa'i skabs shig rmi lam du zla ba dang po la skyes pho mo mang po 'tshogs nas sgron me khur nas rdo ring kun
spangs pa'i grwa

pa rnams gar song 'tshol ba yin zer nas/ kho bo'i mdun phyogs su yad yud mang po byed pa la/ lan du rje'i grwa pa 'di dang 'di zhes bya ba mang po yod/ nga yang yin byas pas/
'o na rnam thar bshad rgyu yod dam zer ba la/ med pa snyam byed cing shin tu ngo gnong ba zhig la gnyid sad byung bas/ sems mi bde ba snyam byed pa zhag 'ga' byung / de'i
rjes kyi zla ba phyi ma'i nang du nub cig rmi lam na/ bud med snum bag can mang po brag steng gcig na 'tshogs/ khu di ri ri 'dug pa la bltar phyin pas/ de rnams thams
cad yi ge 'ba' zhig 'bri zhing kha mi 'cham pa'i zi re ba byed pa la/ don gang yin lab pas/ bud med rgan mo byad dmar chab pe ba so 'dzar ba gcig na re/ nged rnams kyis
khyed kyi bla ma'i rnam thar rtsom pa yin zer/ khyod rnams la lo rgyus yod dam byas pas/ po ti chen mo gcig 'dug pa la mdzub mo btsugs nas/ 'di phag mo

grub pa'i rnam thar po ti yin/ 'di'i nang nas 'bri ba yin zer/ khyod rnams gang nas yin byas pas/ nga ni slob dpon la wa pa'i dus kyi la ba'i dum bu za mkhan gyi mkha' 'gro
padma'i dra ba can yin/ gzhan gzhon nu gcig la mdzub mo gtad nas 'di sengge'i dra ba can yin/ gzhan 'di rnams phyogs bcu nas 'dus par 'dug zer/ der rjes gnyid sad/ bsams
pas rje bla ma phag mo grub pa'i rnam 'phrul yin pa ni nges can du 'dug snyam pa byung / de nas zhag 'ga' song ba na nub gsum bstud nas rmi lam du 'dre gnan gyi rnam pa
yang yang du 'ong ba zhig byung bas/ 'di 'dra'i rigs ni gu ba rnams la rlung dbu mar 'jug kha ma'i rtags su byed/ mgon po'i rgyud dur khrod nag po nas grib gnon lta bur 'ong
pa dang zhes chos skyong gi rtags su'ang bshad/ gang ltar dge sbyor du bsrangs pas 'dra snyam pa byas pas/ nub bzhi pa'i

rmi lam du sngar gyi bud med de byung nas/ lag tu snag tsha thod pa gang dang / lcags smyug gcig gtad byung nas/ nged rnams kyis gang lab kyang mi go bar 'dug mi gzhan gyi
bla ma'i grwa pas bla ma'i rnam thar 'chos kyin 'dug zer ba'i 'phro la gnyid sad byung bas/ kha sang nas kyi ltas thams cad 'dir 'dus pas/ da sang rang nas rje'i rnam thar
zhig rtsom dgos snyam pa byas nam langs dge sbyor grub nas gnyid zir tsam byung ba'i rmi lam du/ chos khri gcig gi steng nas bandhe gzhon nu zhig gis skyes rabs dpag bsam
'khri shing sgrog kyin 'dug pa/ nyan mkhan yin zer bud med gzhon nu mchor mo mang po glu len/ rkang bro byed kyin 'dug pa rmis/ sang de nas 'go btsugs nas brtsams pas
ma grub kyi bar la rje bla ma lan gsum rmis/ gzhan yang dge ba'i ltas mang po byung / tshar khar 'dod khams lha mo yin

zer ba'i bud med bong bu'i rna ba yod pa gcig gis gtso byas mang po byung nas/ 'di la bka' rgya zhig kyang gyis/ bstan pa nged rang gis bsrung zer ba byung / zhes rje nyid
kyi phyag bris dngos bshus las ji ltar byung ba bzhin bkod pa yin la/ yang rje nyid la dad gus dang ldan pa'i bu slob sbyin bdag tshun chad la/ 'di phyi bar do sogs byang
chub bar du bka' srung rnams kyis srung skyob mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ snga mo'i dus shig gnas gsar pa'i sde pa nam mkha' ba 'da' khar rje nyid spyan drangs te/ re ltos 'chol
ba'i zhu cha phul ba na thugs rje rab tu g.yos pa'i sdig bshags smon lam sogs kyi sgo nas thugs dam skyabs 'og rtse gcig pa dang / lhag par rje rdo ring pa la yus dang
bcas pa'i gsol 'debs drag tu mdzad pas/ nub gcig 'od gsal gyi ngang du rje rdo ring pa byon pa'i gsung las/ sde pa tshe 'das khong bdag chen rdo rje 'chang slob brgyud dang
bcas pa la shin tu mos

pas/ chos skyong rnams kyis 'bral med du 'grogs nas grogs byed kyin 'dug skye ba 'di 'phos nas tshe snga ma'i las kyi 'phen shugs kyis rgya nag gi mtha' 'khob tu ru Ta mo zhig
gi mngal du zla ba bdun 'jug dgos 'dug de nas ma de chos skyong gis bsgral nas/ sde pa khong lcang lo can du gnod sbyin gyi bu bde ldan 'od zer zhes bya bar skye ba blangs
nas phyag na rdo rje'i gsung thos chos thob nas/ khong gi bya ba des 'grub par 'dug khyed kyis 'bad rtsol chen po mdzad na ma de'i mngal du zla ba gcig tsam gyis chog
nyen 'dug gang ltar do nub mjal ba la yong ba yod do gsung ba byung pas/ de'i nub ched du thugs kyi 'dun pa gtad pas tshes bco lnga'i nub mnal lam du sde pa khong sku'i
cha lugs sngar ltar mdzad/ a tsa ra mang pos sku skyor ba'i rnam pa byas nas rje'i spyan sngar slebs byung ste/ bdag tshe 'phos

kyang bla ma rnams kyi thugs rje dang / a tsa ra 'di rnams kyis kyang grogs byas/ ci byas tshabs su song ba'i rgyal ga yod pa byung / bskyed rim gsal zhing gtor bsngo ye ma
chag pa byas/ bdag la phyag rdor gyi bskyed rim gsal 'debs gcig gnang dgos zhes zhu ba gsal bar byung bas/ de dus kyang gsal 'debs mdzad/ sang nangs par nas bzung phyag
na rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor du sde pa de nyid kyi mtshan byang lam ston lan gsum gyi bar du mdzad pas/ re zhig nas rje nyid kyi thugs dam gsal snang la/ bar snang la 'brug skad
snyan po zhig byung ba la gzigs pas/ gzim khang gi logs thams cad 'od kyi rnam pa can gyi nor bu mig gsum pas gang ba shin tu gsal bar gzigs pas/ rje nyid kyi thugs la
sde pa de nyid byang phyogs lcang lo can du gnod sbyin 'brug la zhon pa can/ ming bde ldan 'od zer zhes bya bar skyes nas drin lan

'jal du yong pa yin 'dug pas/ khong gnas skabs dang mthar thug gi phan bde la nges par 'god pa'i yid ches kyi rtags su 'dug snyam du dgongs nas/ rje nyid kyang thugs shin tu
bde bar byung zhes gsungs pa zhal slob rnams kyi gsung rgyun las brgyud de thos so/ /yang rje 'di nyid yar lung pa sengge rgyal mtshan gyi rnam 'phrul yin pa'i tshul ni/
skabs shig mdar brang mo cher bzhugs dus/ rje mkhyen brtse ba sogs phyogs kyi bu chen rnams 'dus nas/ gnyan mgon zhal bzhi pa'i gtor chen gyi phyag len zhu bar mdzad pa
na/ rjes kyang thugs kyis bzung nas/ gtor chen rgyas pa'i phyag len mdzad pa'i tshe/ de'i nub mo nyid kyi mnal dang 'od gsal 'dres pa'i 'char sgo la thog mar rje nyid rtse
gdong yin snyam pa'i lung pa zhig na yar byon pa'i mthar/ khang pa gcig 'dug pa de'i nang du byon pas/ khang pa de'i nang gdan khri

rkang pa can gyi steng na 'bol yug gi rnam pa btings pa'i g.yas ngos na rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po dang / g.yon ngos na chos rje rdo rje gdan pa chen po bzhugs 'dug pa la/
rje nyid kyis phyag phul byin rlabs zhu ba mdzad pas/ chos rje rdo rje gdan pas phyag len mdzad pa sogs che bkur bsam gyis mi khyab pa gnang gin 'dug pas/ rje'i thugs
la rje btsun rdo ring pa chen pos kyang 'di 'dra ba zhig gnang thang ba la snyam pa'i dgongs pa shar/ de nas rje rdo ring pa chen po'i gsung las/ chos rje kha sang nas gar
byon gsungs pa la/ rje nyid kyis bdag gis kha sang nas jo nang pa'i grwa pa 'jam dbyangs sgeg pa zer ba'i gzugs chung nge ba/ jo zhwa gyon pa gcig la chos shod kyin bsdad
lags zhus pas/ chos rje rdo rje gdan pa'i zhal nas/ khyed rdzun ma gsungs/ 'jam dbyangs sgeg pa dang / gnas gsar chos rje gnyis

gcig pa ma yin/ tha dad yin gsungs pa la/ rje rdo ring pa chen po'i zhal nas de gnyis la skyon med/ chos rje tshar pas gsungs pa de sngon gyi dus la dgongs pa yin/ chos rje
rdo rje gdan pas gsungs pa de/ da lta'i dus la dgongs pa yin don la khyad med/ chos rje tshar pa yar lung pa sengge rgyal mtshan du skye ba blangs pa'i dus/ gnas gsar chos
rje 'jam dbyangs sgeg pa yin/ der ma zad chos rjes bsnyel yod pa 'dra/ sngon u rgyan gyi yul du khyed rnal 'byor pa tha wi ra zhes bya ba yin/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma la
dbang zhus dus rnal 'byor pa sbrul gyi ga sha can de nga yin/ de'i dus khong rang gis gdug pa can mang po bsgral gsungs pa sogs/ chos rje rdo rje gdan pa dang rje nyid la
lo rgyus gsungs pa'i tshul mdzad byung pas/ nyid kyi thugs la gnyis snang mtshan rtog gi dri ma dang bral ba'i

bde chen gyi ye shes tshad med pa 'khrungs shing / sku skye ba snga ma'i tshul la nges shes khyad par can mngon du gyur te/ sang nyin mnal lam gyi tshul rnams zhal slob bu
chen rnams la sgrib med du gsungs 'dug pa 'di lta bu ni/ sngon yang sa skya pa'i snyan brgyud kyi bdag po yar lung pa sengge rgyal mtshan du bsam bzhin du byon cing / slar
snyigs ma'i dus 'dir yang rje btsun gong ma'i man ngag chad du phangs pa rnams kyi bka' bsdu lta bu mdzad pa la cher gtad byon pa yin yang dag pa'i gtan tshigs su kho bos
rtogs shing / mthar gzhan don la dgongs par nye ba na yang / lan gcig 'od gsal gyi ngang du rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po byon nas/ da lta rgya gar lho phyogs na mu stegs
pa'i rgyal po stobs che ba gcig yod pas/ de 'dul du khyed 'gro dgos pa 'dug gsung ba byung ba la zhag 'ga'i bar du rje rdo ring pa nyid la gsol ba rtse gcig tu 'debs
pa mdzad pas/ lan

gcig 'od gsal gyi ngang du nam mkha' la mthong khung lta bu zhig skya lam gyis dod byung ba de na mar 'od kyi spras pa gcig btsugs pa la/ bu mo dmar mo na tshod lo brgyad tsam
lon pa/ rus rgyan chab pe ba btags pa gcig rgyab 'bab kyi tshul du byung nas/ de na re/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen pos/ khyod 'bod du gnang pa yin/ 'gro 'am mi 'gro zer
ba la/ rje nyid phebs pa la thugs mi spro ba'i ngang nas/ ngas da lo lam 'bras shig 'chad 'dod pa de yang bshad ma tshar gsungs pas/ bu mo de'i gsung las 'o na khong mi
yong ba 'dug zhu'am zer nas spras pa de la rgyab bstan bzhin par 'dzegs song / de'i rjes la spras pa de'ang bsdus pa ltar yal nas/ mthong khung 'dra ba de yang mi snang
bar song bas/ de nas zhag 'ga' nas 'od gsal gyi ngang du rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po phebs byung nas/ mu stegs pa'i rgyal po rgan

pa de shi 'dug gzhon pa de dang khyod la las 'brel mi 'dug pas/ da lan gzhan zhig btang yod/ lam 'bras mgyogs po shod gsung ba gsal bar byung zhing / de nas ring po ma lon
pa stag lo rje 'di yongs grags ltar na dgung lo drug cu re lnga pa'i steng du son pa na ngo mtshar ba'i rtags kyi cho 'phrul du ma dang bcas dag pa'i zhing du gshegs pa'i
tshul bstan pa yin zhing / slob brgyud 'ga' zhig gi gsung las/ dam pa 'di snga mo'i dus thugs dam la bzhugs pa'i skabs shig chos skyong gis sprul pa'i mi ral ba can 'brog
pa 'dra ba zhig gi srung khra zhig phul nas/ sku tshe'i tshad yin zhu ba la/ bgrangs pas bdun cu don lnga byung pa bzhin dgung lo yang de tsam bzhugs pa yin zhes gsungs
shing / gang ltar sku tshe mthar phyin zhabs pad brtan pa 'di ni zhing skyong tsa turmu kha'i tshe sgrub zab mo thugs nyams su bzhes pa sogs kyi dge mtshan las byung bar
kho

bo sems so/ /yang sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i thugs sras snyigs ma'i dus kyi sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i gsal byed dam pa sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin
chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpa' bzang po de nyid ni/ nges pa kho nar ston pa thams cad mkhyen pa'am khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang chen po dang thugs rgyud gcig gis
bsdus pa yin mod kyang / gdul bya'i snang ngor phyag na rdo rje dang / kun tu bzang po dang / nyan thos chen po kun dga' bo dang / lo tsA ba bai ro tsa na dang / chos rje
sa skya paNDi ta rnams su sprul pa'i sku rim par bstan nas bstan pa dang sems can gyi don mtha' yas pa zhig mdzad de/ mthar shar phyogs mngon par dga' ba'i zhing khams su
de bzhin gshegs pa dri ma med pa'i dpal zhes bya bar sangs rgyas pa'i tshul bstan pa de nyid/ slar yang snyigs ma'i dus

kyi bstan pa nyams ches pa'i skabs 'dir gos dkar lcang los mdzes pa'i sngags 'chang rdo rje 'dzin pa'i skur bstan nas/ dpal sa skya'i sde bstan pa gdung rgyud dang bcas pa'i
thog drangs/ spyi bye brag gi bstan pa yar ngo'i zla ba ltar 'phel rgyas su mdzad pa yin pas/ dam pa 'di sprul pa'i sku yin pa'i gtan tshigs ni/ rje 'dis bla ma rnams la
chos gsan tshul/ dben par sgom sgrub dang gsung bzlas bye bsnyen mang po mdzad tshul/ snod ldan la chos gsungs tshul/ gtsug lag khang mang po'i nyams gso dang gsar bzhengs
mdzad tshul/ gsung rab glegs bam du ma brtsams tshul/ bsgom grwa/ sngags grwa/ bshad grwa sogs btab tshul/ mngon spyod kyi las kyis bstan dgra btul tshul/ 'jig rten gyi
lung khrims bzang po'i rgyun 'cha' ba mdzad tshul sogs bstan 'gro'i don du 'gyur nges pa'i

mdzad pa'i cha shas de dag re re'i phyag rjes la bsams kyang / de kho na sku tshe ril por mdzad pa lta bu'i so so skye bo'i blo'i yul las 'das pa'i ngo mtshar ba'i rnam par
thar pa mtha' yas pa zhig mnga' ba mngon sum du mthong zhing grub pa 'di yin pas/ de dag gi tshul rgyas par shes par 'dod na/ kho bos byas pa'i sngags 'chang nyid kyi rnam
thar ngo mtshar rgya mtsho sogs su blta bar bya zhing / 'dir ni bstan srung dbang po rnams bran du 'khol ba'i tshul sogs gtso bor smos pa mdo tsam zhig bsnyad na/ skyes
chen 'di nyid sku phra mo'i dus kyang mkhas pa rnams kyi yid 'phrog cing dad pa dbang med du skye ba'i mdzad pa rmad du byung ba du ma zhig mnga' ba yin te/ dper mtshon
na/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos/ sngags 'chang bla ma 'di nyid dang mjal bas mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob pa'i tshul ni/ chos rje tshar pa de nyid kyis lcog grwa mdzad nas
dbus phyogs la phebs pa'i

dus/ khong rang gi rnam thar lam yig tu bkod pa las 'di ltar 'byung ste/ de nas rdzi lung du zhag gcig bsdad/ sang nyin dge sding na dpal sa skya'i chos kyis mngon par mtho
ba'i khri la bzhugs pa bdag chen rin po che khri thog pa'i drung bzhugs pa dang mjal/ des snga nas dpon slob 'dris pa lta bu'i nang gtsang zhing thugs 'gol ba bka' lung
bag phebs par gnang / nged rnams la bdag chen thams cad mkhyen pa chen pos mdzad pa'i bla ma mchod chog rgyas bsdus kyi lung / de dang rjes su 'brel ba'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor
'dod zhus ltar bka' drin bskyangs/ sku na phra mo 'di lta bu la 'di 'dra'i lugs gnyis kyi gnang bkod ngo mtshar ba 'ong ba/ nges par 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi rnam 'phrul
yin pa la the tshom mi za ba 'dug snyam pa'i dad mos dang / sa skya pa'i rmongs zhen gyis blo bde ba tshad med pa byung / byin rlabs kyi rten gnang sbyin sogs yang dag thugs
rjes

bzung / zhes dang / yang lam yig de nyid las/ sprang rgyal khams phyogs med rgyu ba'i tshe/ /yul ya mtshan ltad mo 'di ltar mthong / /shab dge sding chos kyi pho brang na/
/rje sa skya lo tsA sku yi dbon/ /thugs gcig tu 'dres pa sras kyi mchog /khong 'jam dbyangs gzhon nu dngos dang mjal/ /gsung bag phebs kyi bdud rtsi snying la sim/ /chos
lam zab kyi rnal 'byor bka' drin zhus/ /khong skyon bral gyi mdzad 'phrin mthong ba'i tshe/ /nged sa skya pa'i 'dun ma grub 'dug snyam/ /sems dga' spro dad pas mchi ma 'khrug
/zhabs spyi gtsug tu blangs nas smon lam btab/ /ces gsungs shing / dus gnas kun tu skye bo mang po'i dbus su sngags 'chang 'di'i rnam thar gsungs shing / dgyes spro
dang dag snang dad gus dpag med mdzad pa zhig byung 'dug pas mtshon pa'i de dus kyi sa skya pa'i bstan

'dzin thams cad kyis skyes chen 'di'i ngo mtshar ba'i rnam thar rnams kun la ngom pa'i tshul gyis sgrogs pa zhig byung bar snang la/ sa skya pa'i bka' srung rnams kyis dngos
su zhal bstan tshul ni/ byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brag rdzong du sbas pa'i rnal 'byor chen po 'phags chen nyid las/ gur gyi mgon po'i nang khrid zab mo gsan par mdzad de thun
bzhir bcad de thugs dam la rtse gcig tu mdzad pa na/ gur gyi mgon po lha brgyad/ ser nag zangs gri can/ ru 'dren sde bzhi dregs pa'i 'khor dang bcas pa rnam 'gyur sna tshogs
pa dang bcas pa'i sgo nas yang nas yang du gsal bar gzigs shing / 'phrin las thams cad thogs med du bsgrub par zhal gyis bzhes pa yin no/ /zhes kyang thos la/ don gyi
dbang de dag la dgongs nas sngags 'chang nyid kyis mdzad pa'i gur gyi mgon po'i khrid yig chen mo gzhan phan rgyas byed kyi sbyar byang las/

mkhas grub dpal ldan bkra shis kyis spyan tshab pa'i drung du gsan pa bzhin shin tu rgyas shing zhib sed dang bcas thugs dgyes bzhin du gnang nas zla ba gnyis kyi bar la bsgrub
pa gang smin byas pas yid ches dang ldan pa byung ba gzhan gyi gsung rgyun cung zad zin pas kyang brgyan te bris pa lags/ gzhan rnams kyis kyang snying nang gi khrag
lta bu'i gdams pa khyad par can rnams cung nyams len dka' tsam 'dug na'ang snying rus bskyed nas dmigs thun re la zhag brgyad tsam nan tan byas bsgoms na byin rlabs kyi
rtags mtshan gzhan las che bas yid ches 'phral du 'byung ba myong bas grub pa lags/ zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /yang byas 'gyur du sku mtshams la bzhugs pa'i skabs shig nyin
re bzhin gzigs snang la byas 'gyur gyi gzhi bdag klu mo dkar mo dang / bdud kyi rta pa bco brgyad 'khor shin tu mang ba dang bcas pa snga dro lung pa'i mdo la

'gro ba dang / phyi dro phu la 'gro ba gzigs pa na/ snga mor dpal chen pho brang du rdo rje phur ba'i gsung bsnyen mdzad pa'i tshe/ dkar mo nyi zla dang bdud kyi rgyal po 'khor
dang bcas pa gzigs snang la shar ba dang / 'di rnams cha lugs 'dra ba 'dug cing / thugs rgyud kyang gcig pa srid snyam du dgongs nas/ gzhi bdag klu mo dkar mo bdud kyi
rta pa bco brgyad dang bcas pa la bka' bsgo mdzad de/ sgrub sde khyad par can 'di mi nyams shing yun du gnas pa dang / sgrub po rnams kyang bar chad med cing mthun rkyen
'dzom pa dang / bstan dgra gdug pa can rnams myur du tshar gcod pa'i 'phrin las sgrubs shig ces bka' bsgos pa na/ gzhi bdag rnams kyis kyang de ltar du khas blangs par
brten de'i gtang rag tu dmigs nas bsang yig rgyas par/ gzhi bdag klu mo dkar mo dang / /bdud kyi rta pa bco brgyad la/ /'khor dang yang bran 'bum bcas sogs/ /byas

'gyur lung pa'i gzhi bdag bsang / /zhes pa'i tshigs bcad 'di yang 'jug par mdzad pa yin no/ /zhes thos shing / dkar mo nyi zla lcam dral dang / byas 'gyur gyi gzhi bdag 'di
rnams thugs rgyud gcig par 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po'i byas 'gyur gyi gnas bshad dngos grub rgya mtsho las kyang gsal bar gsungs so/ /yang sngags 'chang bla ma 'di
nyid kyis zhing skyong chen po tsa turmu kha'i bsnyen sgrub mthar phyin pa mdzad pa na/ bstan srung gi dbang po zhal bzhi pa nyid bram ze'i gzugs sku mdog bai DUrYa ltar
sngo ba/ zhabs gnyis rol pa'i stabs kyis bzhugs pa/ sku shin tu che bas nam mkha'i khyon gang ba yum chen bzhi dang bcas pa zhig gsal bar gzigs pa de'i snang brnyan ji lta
ba bzhin bri bar mdzad pa ni/ da lta sngags thang chen po'i grwa la bzhugs pa 'di yin la/ yang lha khang chen mo'i yang steng gzim chung po

ta lar bzhugs pa'i skabs shig dge slong rin chen rnam grol zhes bya ba'i sngags 'chang nyid kyi zhabs 'bring pa chen po des gsol ba btab pa'i ngor/ gnam kha'u pa'i gzigs snang
ma ltar zhal bzhi pa zhig sngags 'chang nyid kyis phyag bris mdzad pa na/ de'i rab gnas kyi tshe sku 'khor ba rnams kyi mthong snang la/ a tsA ra mdog sngo ba zhig gzim
chung du song ba mthun grub tu mthong zhing / sngags 'chang nyid kyi gzigs snang la zhal bzhi pa yum chen bzhi dang bcas pa rngam brjid dang ldan pa zhig bris sku la mngon
sum du thim pa'i snang ba byung zhes sngags 'chang nyid kyis thugs sras rgyal tshab dam pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched la gsungs pa las brgyud de bdag gis thos so/ /yang
po ta la de nyid du bzhugs skabs shig nangs gcig thun gtor phul ba'i rjes su/ grags pa zer ba'i ban chung zhig yod pa des zhabs drung du 'ongs pa na gzims chung gi 'gag
gi skas 'gor/

bud med nag mo ral pas rting pa khebs pa/ lag gnyis spar mo gdengs shing / rkang pa gar stabs kyis 'dug pa zhig dang 'phrad pa dang / ban chung de shin tu 'jigs dngangs pas
cung zad brgyal zhing / de rjes sngags 'chang nyid la de'i tshul rnams zhus pa na/ de la skrag par byed mi dgos/ do nub kyi thun gtor len pa la sring mo byon byung pa dang
/ khyod rang rtsa gsal bas 'phrad pa yin/ nyes skyon gtan med ces gsungs par grags shing / yang byas 'gyur du sku mtshams yun ring mdzad pa zhig gi skabs/ gzim phug gi
sgo 'gram na pu tra nyid rgyun par bzhugs pa zhig 'dug pa la/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las/ 'dir pu tra rgyun par bzhugs kyin 'dug pas logs bris shig byas na legs par
'dug gsungs nas/ bdag nyid chen po rang gis las mkhan chen po'i sku phyag bris su mdzad pas/ pu tra

nyid de la dngos su thim pa yin zhes 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched kyi gsung las thos so/ /yang dben gnas de nyid du sngags 'chang yab sras dpon slob nyung shas shig gis mgon
po drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog cig mdzad pa'i tshe/ kyai bos so'i bskul tshugs pa na/ phyag g.yog las dag pa gnyis kyi mthong snang la/ byas 'gyur gyi bla brang nub kyi nam
mkhar mi nag dung lo can gnyis gros byed pa'i tshul gyis/ nged rang tsho thog mar rin spungs la phyin/ de nas lha sa rdzong la phyin pa drag pa 'dug zer ba mngon sum du mthong
zhing / de dus dbu zhwa zhwa nag gi tshab tu tsa ru nag pos nang byas pa'i dbu zhwa chung ngu zhig phyir slog tu bzhes pa la kha btags nag khra'i sked chings dang bcas
pa zhig mdzad pa yin zhes kyang thos la/ gzhan yang zhing skyong dur khrod kyi bdag po yab yum yang gar 'cham dang bcas dam nyams lha sa rdzong pa la mngon spyod kyi
las mdzad pa gzigs snang la shar ba bzhin/ da lta rdo rje phur pa'i sgrub mchod

kyi skabs dgra bgegs grub kyi 'cham dang bstun zhing skyong yab yum gyis lingga la 'gugs 'dren mdzad pa'i 'cham stabs 'di yin zhing / yang sngags 'chang 'di nyid kyis sgo rum
ye shes mgon po'i drung du shA sa na 'bum phrag bzhi dang / gnas gzhan dang gzhan dag tu yang gur gyi mgon po'i yi ge bdun ma bye bsnyen thengs gnyis kyi bar du mdzad
par brten/ dpal sa skya'i bzhi thog bla brang gi mkha' spyod phug tu bzhugs pa'i skabs shig gzigs snang la/ gur gyi mgon po'i sku shin tu che ba ro gdan dgu brtsegs steng
na za 'og gi ber dgu brtsegs gsol te 'gyings pa'i stabs kyis bzhugs pa/ nyi ma 'bum gyi gzi brjid 'bar ba zhig mngon sum du gzigs pa dang / bse 'bag nag po 'phur shes nyid
la dus rgyun par mi dang mi lab pa'i tshul gyis bka' bkyon dang / bka' bsgo 'phrin 'chol spel mar mdzad pa

dang bcas/ rje nyid kyi dbu zhwas bse mgon chen po'i zhal gdong gi rdul rnams phyi bar mdzad pa yin zhes sngags 'chang grags pa'i mtshan can gyi gsung las yang yang du thos
shing / yang sngags 'chang bla ma nyid sku 'khor nyung shas dang bcas byas 'gyur rdo rje brag rdzong du phebs nas/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan gyi thugs dam phyag bris
ma'i mgon po bzhugs pa'i bla brang nub kyi gzim chung du sku mtshams yun ring mdzad nas/ dam nyams lha sa rdzong pa la dmigs pa'i las sbyor mthar phyin par mdzad cing
/ de skabs rdzas gsang ba mal 'og gi gnad kyi man ngag zab mo phyag bzhes mdzad pa yang / da lta mig yod kun gyi spyod yul du gyur pa de yin la/ de dag dang dus mtshungs
par byas 'gyur gyi bla brang shar gyi mgon khang gi gur gyi mgon po'i sku ngo mtshar can 'di yang lha sa rdzong pa la dmigs nas gzungs gzhug 'phrin bcol sogs zab rgyas dang
bcas gsar bzhengs su mdzad cing / de'i skabs su mgon po'i

lder sku bzhengs tshul gyi yig cha khyad par can 'di yang mdzad pa yin te/ de nyid kyi mjug tu/ bla ma dam pa rnams kyi zhabs rdul spyi bos gus pas len pa sa skya pa ngag gi
dbang po kun dga' rin chen gyis/ rje btsun gong ma rnams kyi byin gyis brlabs pa'i gnas dben pa'i ri khrod byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brag rdzong du rdo rje nag po chen po'i
sku bzhengs pa'i dus yid ches pa'i rten 'brel du ma byung ba dang / phyag len gyi bsgrigs chags 'di rnams kyang gsal bar blo la shar nas sug bris bgyis pa 'di la nyes pa'i
tshogs mchis na bla ma dang mkha' 'gros bzod par mdzod las/ 'di la brten nas bstan pa'i dgra bo thams cad tshar bcad nas sa skya pa'i bstan pa rnal ma mi nyams shing gong
nas gong du 'phel ba'i rgyur gyur cig ces 'byung bas so/ /yang snga mo'i dus sprul pa'i lha khang chen mo'i steng gi mgon khang khyad par can 'di gsar bzhengs su mdzad
pa'i tshe/ gong dkar ba sprul

sku sbyin pa rnam rgyal gyis lha khang chen mo'i thigs khang du gur phub nas/ mgon po chen po'i ru shing dang spen 'dzugs la 'jim pa phal cher g.yogs grub mtshams glo bur du
rlung dmar chen po langs te/ gur bsgyel zhing las bya byed dang bral bar gyur pa'i tshe/ sprul sku nyid kyis sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po la de'i tshul rnams zhus pas/
bdag nyid chen po nyid thugs 'ur nyams dang bcas 'phral du phebs te/ gzim chung gi mdo'i g.yab steng nas dkar gong zhig bsnams te/ mgon po'i skya bzo phal cher grub pa
de la bsnun pa gnang song bas/ skya bzo'i sku'i nu ma g.yas pa'i 'og tsam du thim gyis song zhing / de mthun gsung las/ nga sa skya'i sde gog po 'di 'dzin pa dang / gtsug
lag khang khyad par can 'di dam nyams tsho'i lag tu mi 'khyar ba'i phyir/ mgon khang zhig bzhengs bsam pa la/ nag bgrad khyod gtor ma bza' yi sdod pa ma

gtogs/ rlung po 'di tsam bsrung ba'i nus pa yang med pa e yin zhes gsung shugs chen po dang bcas bka' stsal pa na/ de ma thag rlung dmar thams cad rang zhir gyur cing / dus
de nas bzung ste mgon khang nam grub kyi bar la rtsub 'gyur gyi rnam pa cung zad tsam yang ma byung ba yin no zhes thos la/ yang rje btsun gong ma'i phyi rten 'bum steng
chen mo'i zhig gsos gnang dus sngags 'chang nyid zug rgyab kyi tshul du phebs pa'i skabs nyin gcig gi tshe skyes pho mo las byed mi brgya lhag tsam tsha bzhes la 'bum steng
rang gi skor lam byang ngos na yod pa'i skabs/ de nyid kyi byang phyogs kyi spyi khang gi 'gram cag chen mo zhig yod pa glo bur du zhig nas/ der 'tshogs kyi skyes pho
mo thams cad ci bya gtol med du gyur pa'i tshe/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung chen pos/ bla ma la gsol ba thob ces gsungs byung pas

de'i mod la sa rdo thams cad bar snang la 'thor nas 'bum thang gi shar nub dang lho phyogs kyi skor lam sogs su slebs te/ las mi thams cad nyes skyon las grol bar brten kun
kyang ya mtshan du gyur pa'i skabs/ sngags 'chang bla ma nyid kyis gzigs rtog la phebs pa na/ sa rdo rnams kyi khrod nas shing leb ring thung khru gang tsam zhig gi ngos
la/ shing brkos legs po rang min pa'i yi ge dbu chen phral le ba gsal po min pa zhig 'dug pa la/ sngags 'chang nyid kyis 'di legs par khrus shig gsungs pa bzhin/ sku 'khor
ba rnams kyis legs par bkrus nas yi ge de nyid bklags pas/ da lta'i zug rgyab pa 'di ni mahA kA la'o/ /zer ba 'dug pa bdag nyid chen po la de'i tshul zhus pas/ he he de
nga la zer ba yin pa 'dra zhes gsungs pa de dus kyi skye bo kun la rlung ltar grags pa yin la/ yang sgo rum gzim spyil dkar po'i zhig gsos

kyi skabs/ lan cig tho rangs kyi cha zhig la sngags 'chang nyid kyi gzigs snang la/ bse 'bag nag po 'phur shes sngags 'chang nyid kyi drung du byon te/ da ni nga la bcos ka
byed ran par 'dug pas lus yon po 'di khar ma zhog pa shin tu 'drongs par 'chos shig ces gsungs pa zhig byung bas/ de'i nangs par sngags 'chang nyid kyis sgo rum gzim spyil
dkar por byon te/ bse mgon chen po'i sku la gzigs pa na/ snga mo nas yod pa'i sku 'bag g.yas phyogs su cung zad yo ba de/ slar cher song 'dug pa dang / snyan shal g.yon
pa la yang snga mo nas chag grub cung zad 'dug pa de rnams 'chos dgos par dgongs nas/ de ma thag gzim spyil dkar po nyid du mgon po'i ljags bsnyen kha gso zhag bdun mdzad
de/ gzhan gyi snang ngor phyag legs par bsil nas/ bla ma gong ma'i dam rdzas ril bu dang / rten 'dam

dpe grags ma sogs byin rlabs kyi phung po ma lus phyogs gcig tu bsdus pa la/ bla ma gong ma'i sgrub chu dang / ched gtad bsgrub par mdzad pa'i gzungs chu sogs kyis legs par
sbyar te/ sngags 'chang nyid kyis phyag bzo mdzad nas bse mgon chen po'i snyan shal g.yon pa'i nyams gso legs par mdzad rjes/ phyag gi 'phrul sogs la gzigs pa na/ shin tu
yun ring pas gsang thag sogs nur nur por gyur te/ sngon gyi bsgrigs mtshams sogs dang ha cang 'grig pa mi 'dug pas/ gos dar gyi bsgrim bu bzang po sogs gang 'tshams kyi
thabs mkhas kyis zhabs tog mdzad pa na/ 'on kyang snga mo'i skabs bzhin gyi bsgrigs mtshams rnams dang shin tu 'grigs par ma byung pa nas/ da ji ltar bya snyam du dgongs
pa'i tshe/ de ma thag khrog sgra shin tu che ba zhig byung ba na/ sku 'khor thams cad ha las te krab sgo'i phyir bros par gyur cing / bdag nyid chen

pos gzigs pa na bse mgon chen po rang nyid kyis phyag gnyis dkrug cing thugs kar steng 'og tu ma bsgrigs rang 'grig tu byung bas/ sngags 'chang nyid thugs lhag par dgyes par
gyur cing / sku 'khor ba rnams kyang mchog tu ngo mtshar du gyur pa yin no/ /'di'i tshul rnams sngags 'chang nyid kyis ye shes mgon po la che brjod kyi gsung mang po dang
bcas yang yang bka' stsal pa yin no/ /zhes 'jam mgon grub pa'i dpa' bo dbang po'i mtshan can gyi gsung las thos pa lags/ yang bzhi thog mgon khang gi zhig gsos kyi skabs/
de dang dus mtshungs par rta jag par grags pa'i ngan pa 'ga' zhig gis bla brang gi ba phyugs rnams bsam gling dgon par yod pa jag pas khyer ba la/ sngags 'chang nyid
thugs 'khrugs te bzhi thog mgon khang du byon nas/ byang 'dul mgon po'i sku la phyag mdzub bsnun zhing / khyod chos skyong

mi byed par zan skyong rang byed pa e yin/ dpon byang pa 'di la khrims med pa dang / dam nyams rta jag pa 'di rnams ngan lang shor bar brten/ rang re sa skya pa'i sgo 'gag
gi phyugs kyang mgo mi thon pa 'di 'dra dpe la srid pa e yin/ khyed rang da res kyi mi ngan de tsho la 'phral du rtags mtshan byung na/ gtang rag tu sma ra dang smin ma sogs
la gser shog cig ster ba yin/ de min gtsang po'i phar ga la skyur gtong ba yin no zhes mi la mis lab pa'i tshul gyis bka' bsgo mdzad pa na/ de'i nub mo gdan sa chen po'i
sde khrod nas btso chen po zhig nub phyogs su song ba kun gyis mthong zhing / de dang mthun par rta jag pa rnams la mi 'tshams pa'i ltas ngan sna tshogs byung bar brten/
phyugs ma rnams zegs 'thor med par bshags pa dang bcas slar phyag tu 'bul bar byung ba na/ sngar gyi zhal bzhes bzhin byang 'dul mgon po'i zhal rgyan dang spyan rmis
kyi gser shog 'di yang de dus

gnang ba yin no zhes kyang thos la/ yang kha'u skyed lhas kyi mgon khang zhig gsos kyi skabs/ brag sgo chen mo'i brag dang rtsig pa cung zad lug byung pa la/ sngags 'chang
nyid kyi gsung las/ sa rdo 'di rnams phyir gcig kyang ma gyar par gyis shig ces gsungs nas bla brang du phebs dgos shig byung ste/ yug gcig bzhugs nas slar mgon khang du
phebs 'phral rdo rnams la gzigs pa'i tshe/ gsung las/ rdo 'di dag gi khrod na ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i rten rdo zhig yong rgyu yin pa mi 'dug pas/ khyed las mi zhig
gis phyir bskyur bar 'dug gsungs nas/ mgon khang de nyid kyi skar khung nas gzigs pa na/ ji ltar bka' stsal pa bzhin/ las byed zhig gis rdo phal pa zhig dang nor nas phyir
chu rong rang du bskyur bar brten/ rten rdo de nyid zam pa'i 'khris kyi chu 'gram na 'od zer khrom me 'dug pa dpon slob der yod

kun gyis gzigs pa'i tshe/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las/ 'o rten rdo khyad par can de ma gi yin pas yar spyan drongs la sku khrus gyis shig ces gsungs pa bzhin/ de ltar
bgyis pa na rdo de nyid kyi tshad 'bo zan las che ba tsam pa'i ngos gcig la chos 'byung gru gsum dbus su che ba gcig dang / phyogs bzhir chung ba re re ste lnga tshom du
'dug pa'i dbus ma'i nang na bram ze'i gzugs can sku shin tu gsal ba dang / phyogs bzhi'i chos 'byung gi nang du yi ge bhyoHyig re shin tu gsal bar 'dug pa bdag nyid chen
po'i dbu thog tu bzhes shing / 'di ni brag sgo'i rten rdo dngos gzhir 'dug go zhes gsungs nas/ slar yang brag sgo'i nang du bzhugs su gsol ba yin no zhes thos shing / 'di
yang bdag nyid chen po nyid gnam kha'u pa chen po'i sku'i sprul pa yin par don gyi zhal gyis bzhes pa'i sngon gyi skye ba dran pa'i rnam par thar par snang ste/ brag sgo'i
rdo khyad par can de nyid 'di ltar bzhugs so zhes pa'i yig

tshang rnying pa dang snyan brgyud sogs gang yang med pa sngags 'chang nyid kyis rang ngo mkhyen pa'i tshul gyis ngos 'dzin dang zhabs tog mdzad pa 'di nyid kyis shes so/ /'o
na sngags 'chang nyid rje btsun dang / sa paN sogs kyi rnam 'phrul yin par grags pa dang / 'dir gnam kha'u pa'i sku'i skye bar bshad pa mi 'gal lam snyam na/ 'gal ba med
de/ bla ma de gsum ga sprul gzhi 'jam pa'i dbyangs nyid yin pas thugs gcig gis bsdus pa yin pas so/ /yang nang so pu tra khang gi zhig gsos dang / gsang ba'i las mkhan
chen po'i sku brnyan gsar bzhengs mdzad skabs/ de dus pu tra chen po dngos su gnas pa'i zangs chen khrag mtsho ma bkra shis 'od 'bar du grags pa 'di nyid mgon khang gi shar
nas nub phyogs su spyan 'dren mdzad pa'i tshe/ thog mar zangs kyi chu phal cher gtsang chab la spyan drangs nas/ de nas sngags 'chang nyid kyis sku 'khor ba rnams la
byin rlabs ril bu re re gnang nas/ da

zangs 'di nub tu drongs shig gsungs nas de ltar byas pa na/ mgon po bsam grub zer ba'i skye bo zhig gis byin rlabs ril bu ma zhus pa zangs 'degs pa'i las grogs byas pa na/
de ma thag sna khrag chu bo'i rgyun ltar brdol nas shi la khad pa byung ba'i tshe/ sngags 'chang nyid kyis pu tra la bka' bsgo mdzad pas nyes pa las grol zhing / de nas zangs
chen chab gtsang mas bkang ste/ mgon khang gi nub phyogs der bzhugs su gsol nas sngags 'chang nyid kyis rab gnas mdzad pa'i tshe/ dam can mon bu pu tra nyid dgyes pa'i
rnam 'gyur du ma mdzad cing zangs nyid la mngon sum du thim pa'i gzigs snang ngo mtshar can byung ba yin no zhes thos la/ dus phyis kyang grub mtha' mi gcig pa'i skye
bo sogs mgon khang der lhags pa na/ zangs chen 'di nyid kyis rtsub 'gyur sna tshogs bstan pa'i lo rgyus kyang yod mod kyi/ 'dir ma spros la/ zangs 'di la snga mo zhig sngags
'chang nyid kyis nyams gso mdzad

pa'i tshe yang / las mkhan gyi sprul pa'i bal po shrI dznyA na zer ba zhig glo bur du byung nas/ zangs kyi nyams gso grub ma thag bal po de gar song cha med du gyur pas/ las
mkhan gyi sprul pa zangs nyid la thim pa yin yang dag go zhes grags shing / mdor na dam can mon bu pu tra nyid sngags 'chang bla ma nyid dang 'bral med kyi tshul du bzhugs
nas rnam 'phrul sna tshogs pa ston pa dang bcas 'phrin las rnams bsgrubs par nges te/ skabs shig thugs sras rgyal tshab dam pa sngags 'chang grags pa'i mtshan can la/
nyid kyi sku 'bag khams gsum zil gnon gnang ba'i dus su/ 'di la pu tra nyid gtor ma len pa'i zhor la dngos su thim pa yin pas rtsis che bar gyis zhes gsungs pa sogs rgyu
mtshan mang du snang ngo / /de nas mgon khang gi zhig gsos phal cher grub cing / pu tra chen po'i sku'i skya bzo tshar ba na/ sngags 'chang

chos kyi rgyal po dpon slob rnams dge sding phyogs su khor tsam phebs pa'i dgongs gtad gnang ba'i tshe/ de'i nub mo bdag nyid chen po nyid kyi gzim chung lhun grub pho brang
gi gzim sgo dang shugs sgo sogs brdungs shing skad sna tshogs ston pa'i rjes su pu tra chen po nyid dung long skya khrol le ba dang bcas sngags 'chang nyid kyi drung du
thal byung nas/ nang so'i pu tra'i sku la rtsi tshon rab gnas sogs mi mdzad par rang 'di gar 'jog pa yin nam zhes pa la/ da lta mtshal sogs stabs bde ba med pas/ dge sding
'khor nas byed rtsis gsungs pa la/ yang pu tra na re/ mtshal gyi tshab rdo btsag la mdzad pa zhu zhes zhu ba na/ 'o na de bzhin bya yi gsungs nas/ de'i nangs par snga
bar gdung sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched dang / sprul sku mgon po tshe dbang sogs zhabs drung du 'bod par mdzad de/ mdang nub mo nged la snang tshul 'di bzhin byung bas/
dge sding phyogs su 'gro ba'i sngon la nang so

pu tra khang gi tshon rtsi rab gnas sogs thams cad mthar phyin grub pa legs pa 'dug ces gsungs pa bzhin myur du grub par mdzad pa yin no zhes thos la/ yang sngags 'chang nyid
kyi thugs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can dgung lo drug bzhes shing / yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas 'khrungs ma thag pa'i phag lo 'das nas byi lo gsar du
shar ba'i skabs der g.yas ru byang ba'i dpon rigs mdar gdong gnyis 'khrugs par gyur te/ de dus gdong dga' bas sa skya pa la rgyab bzhengs dgos pa'i snyan 'bul zhus kyang
/ spyi mchod yin pas skabs su mi bab gsungs nas/ mngon gyur chen po ma gnang zhing / 'on kyang sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po dpon slob rags bsdus shig mdor mar phyag phebs
te/ ka drug ma'i spe 'ur gdan chags nas/ mgon po'i gtor bzlog cig sgrub par mdzad pas/ de dang dus mtshungs par dpal sa skya'i sgo rum ye shes mgon po'i mgon khang du

sa srab rib cig la sku gnyer gyis bskang gso gtor bar phyin pa na/ mgon khang mdo'i 'brong gsob kyi 'og der/ mi 'ga' re gleng mo byed pa lta bu'i/ dam nyams stag sna 'dzom
chen kho zer ba'i tshig ris gsal ba la/ gzhan go min mi go min gyi lab rdzi dar dir mang po dang bcas thag sgra shin tu che ba zhig byung bas/ lan cig sku gnyer gyis phyir
bros shing / slar grogs dang bcas blta bar phyin pas/ 'brong gsob kyi 'og der spyan gzigs kyi ral gri shin tu bzang ba zhig bskyur ba'i 'khris na/ shog bu la khrag gi yi
ge 'dza' 'dzog mang po bris pa zhig 'dug pas/ de dag khyer te rgyal yum sku mched la gnas tshul byung ba rnams phul bas rang res mi shes/ zhabs drung rang du 'bul mi btang
ba 'thad gsungs nas/ ral gri khrag yig dang bcas pa sngags 'chang nyid kyi drung du phul ba/ 'byor ma thag shog bu khrag yig can de la gzigs nas/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi
gsung las/ nged la bse mgon chen pos lung bstan gnang bar 'dug da lam gyi gdong dga' ba'i dpung 'di/ stag sna dang gzhis chen brgyud nas 'jug rtsis yin 'dug kyang / de
bzhin byas na mi legs/ mang mkhar brgyud pa rang legs zer ba 'dug pas/ de bzhin gyis shig pa'i phebs sgo stsal pas/ gdong dga' bas kyang bka' bzhin bsgrubs pa na/ sngags
'chang nyid kyi

mthu rtsal gyis mdar gdong gnyis kyi dpung gi mtshams nam mkha' sngo bsang nge la glo bar du sprin nag 'dus te thog 'brug gi sgra rgyun mi chad sgrog pa dang bcas ser ba chen
po babs pa'i rkyen byas/ mdar pa'i dmag rnams 'ur langs te skad cig la byer bar gyur nas/ gdong dga' ba'i phyogs kyis g.yul rgyal dpe med lon te/ mdar gzhung gi skye bo
rnams kyi phyi nang gi dngos po thams cad gdong dga' ba'i dmag mi rnams kyis hab thob tu khyer zhing / longs spyod kyi dpal

gyis gya nom par gyur cing / mdar pa'i dmag mi rnams kyis phyir 'khrug pa lta zhog rdzong nang du yang sdod mi chags pa lta bu'i dngangs skrag chen po byung ba sogs de dus
rgyus yod kyi mi rnams kyis ngag nas brgyud de thos shing / skabs der stag sna 'dzom chen gyis sa skya par don med kyi lta log chen po byas par brten/ chos skyong rnams kyis
bka' chad kyis kho rang 'thab bral du song / mgo bo gdong dga' bas sa skya'i sgo rum mgon khang du phul ba dus phyis stag sna pa rang gi spyan gzigs khrab sogs phul nas
mgo bo phyir slog mdzad pa yin no zhes grags la/ dus de nyid kyi tshe dmag gi don ma go 'dras/ mang mkhar gyi rje tshar pa'i dgon pa dmu'i mgon khang la bcom khyer che
ba byung pa na/ tshar pa'i ma chen rdo rje bkra shis kyis/ rang re'i dgon pa ni dmag mi rnams kyis bcom song / mthu yod na da res sa skya pa mchod yon rnams la rtags thon
pa zhig cis kyang

mdzad dgos/ zhes zhus pas/ rje'i gsung las/ khyod ci zer ba yin/ nged ni mgo bo lus srog gi bdag po 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi dpe bzhin/ nged rang gi mgo bo gcod kyang sa skya
bdag chen khong rang sku dbang btsan pa yin pas/ 'o skol sa skya pa'i chos kyi sgor zhugs phyin/ rje btsun gong ma brgyud pa dang bcas pa la dam nyams byas nas ci mno ba
yin/ ngas ni mi shes/ khyod kyis yong na gyis dang gsungs pas ma chen rdo rje bkra shis ngo nag du re bsdad 'dug go zhes de dus rgyus can gyi gang zag rdzun mi zer ba dag
gi ngag bgros rnying pa las brgyud de thos pas yid ches pa'i gnas yin zhing / gzhan yang rje tshar chen de nyid/ sa skya pa'i bstan pa bstan 'dzin dang bcas pa la dad
zhen gzhan las che ba zhig yod 'dug pas/ sngags 'chang nyid kyis dpal sa skya'i sde bstan pa gdung rgyud dang bcas pa dar rgyas su mdzad

pa la thugs kyi dag snang chen po'i gsung las/ bdag chen kun dga' rin chen 'di ma byon na/ sa skya pa'i bstan pa 'di grum ze gung med 'dra ba'i mtha' yod kyang dbus med pa
zhig yong nges su 'dug kyang / bdag chen 'dis bstan pa'i khur bzhes pas sa skya pa'i 'phrin las mtha' dbus med pa rgyas pa 'di rang re rnams blo bag dro ba'i tshad yin zhes
yang yang gsungs pa sogs mdor na tshar chen nyid dang / sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po gnyis phan tshun so so nas thugs mthong dang / dad pa dag snang 'gran pa lta bu'i
thugs nang shin du dkar ba'i sel med kyi rang bzhin du bzhugs pa yin nges kyang phyis rje tshar pa'i rnam thar byed pa 'dras/ sngags 'chang nyid dang tshar chen thog mar
dge sding du mjal nas dpon slob tu gyur kyang / phyis bdag chen 'dis dmu'i mgon khang bcom pa sogs rje tshar pa la mi legs pa mdzad pa ni/ gzhan gyis mthu bzlog

byas pa dpon slob 'byed pa'i las sbyor du song ba yin zhes bris snang yang / de ni phyogs 'dzin dang ma brtags pa'i gtam kho nar zad pas yid brtan par mi bya'o/ /yang sngags
'chang chos kyi rgyal po dang / grub mchog bsod nams dbang po gnyis yab sras lhan cig dbus phyogs su phebs pa'i skabs shig bde chen chos 'khor du gtor bzlog drug cu pa
zhig gnang ba'i tshe/ bskul mdzad cing bka' bsgo'i gdangs tshugs pa na/ rje btsun nyid sku bong sngar bas nyis 'gyur gyis che zhing / yang zor yang shin tu che ba dang /
mthu stobs kyi zil chen pos sus kyang sku la lta mi nus pa lta bur gyur cing / de dang dus mtshungs par gtso gtor dang pu tra'i gtor ma la me lhab kyis 'bar ba dang / bran
bdud kyi gtor rtse thag sgra dang bcas chad nas rgya mthong la 'phar ba de nyid me phung chen por gyur cing / de las kyang me phung sgo tsam pa du mar byung ste smyug la
phyogs su song ba phyag

g.yog sogs der yod kun gyis mthong bas kun kyang skrag cing ngo mtshar bar gyur to/ /zhes kyang thos so/ /de nas sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po yab sras kyis chos 'khor lha
sar phebs pa na/ nangs gcig gi tshe sngags 'chang nyid kyi drung du bsam yas dbu rtse bar khang gi srung ma rgyal po shing cha can de za 'og ber gser gyi thig le yod pa
zhig gyon nas byung ste/ dbu rtse chen mo'i steng 'di la zhig gsos shig mi byed ka med yod pas khyed kyis mdzad dgos/ drung nas ma mdzad na/ da 'di la zhig gsos mdzad mkhan
yong ba med pas/ de'i tshe bsam yas dbu rtse 'di zhig na bod spyi mthun gyi bde skyid la gnod pas/ da lta zhig gsos kyi skabs rang la 'dug zer ba la/ sngags 'chang nyid
kyis kyang / 'o na de ltar bya'o zhes zhal gyis bzhes nas/ de'i sang nyin snga bar bdag nyid chen po yab sras gnyis kas chibs thog khel te bsam yas phyogs su myur bar
phebs pa na/

sbrang lung pa'i mdo der sa ma srib tsam la phebs pa'i tshe/ char mun yang shin tu che ba 'thib pa'i skabs/ 'jam dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can nyid la/ sngags 'chang chos kyi
rgyal po'i gsung gis/ khri thog pa dpon slob rnams da lta bsam yas su sngon bar la song la/ nged slebs gdong du gtor ma grub par gyis/ rang re rnams slebs 'phral la bskang
gso gtong ba yin pas rtsol ba bskyed pa'i 'byon lugs mdzod/ bar lam la rtog pa zhib po gyis/ 'on kyang lam rgyus la rkang rjes gsum yong ba yod pas/ rkang rjes che ba
gnyis la nges pa cher med/ sor brgyad tsam yod pa de la gtad nas phyin pas 'khrul pa gcig kyang yong ba med do gsungs byung ba la/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can
dpon slob rnams kyi thugs dgongs la ci gsungs pa yin nam/ da sa ni srib nas song / char mun 'di 'dra ba rkang rjes ji ltar mthong ngam snyam du dgongs nas

thugs yid the tshom log ge ba dang bcas mgyogs par phebs pa'i tshe/ sbrang mda' nas mda' rgyang gsum tsam gyi sa nas srod chen tsam du gyur pa na/ dpon slob rnams kyis lam
