bor te/ res 'ga' ni ri 'gram du phebs yong ba dang / skabs 'gar chu 'gram gyi bye mar bying ba sogs nges med sna tshogs kyis ci bya gtol med kyi rnam pa byung ba'i tshe/
dpon slob rnams kyis sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung dran nas gsol 'debs drag tu mdzad pa na/ thog mar 'jam pa'i dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can nyid kyis rkang rjes gsum srab
srib tu yod pa gzigs nas/ slar yang gsol ba drag tu btab pas rkang rjes chung ba de shin tu gsal bar gyur pa'i rjes brtsad nas dpon slob rnams kyis byon pas/ lam la nor
'khrul cung zad kyang med par bsam yas su nam ma phyed tsam la phebs par gyur cing / de nas cung zad song ba na mchod g.yog phyag phyi ba slebs byung nas/ khong gi mthong
snang la rdo mchod thang kha'i 'og tsam

nas mi shin tu che ba gsum song zer nas rab tu 'jigs par byung ba'i snang tshul rnams sngon bgros su phebs pa'i dpon slob rnams la phul zin nas dar tsam song ba na/ sngags
'chang chos kyi rgyal po dpon slob rnams phebs byung ba'i tshe/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can nyid kyis sde yangs su phebs bsur phyag phebs te/ dpon slob rnams
phebs lam bde bar byung lags zhes zhus pa na/ bdag nyid chen po'i zhabs 'bring la yod pa'i chos rje rin rgyal dang / chos rje kun dga' bkra shis sogs na re/ nged dpon slob
rnams la dal la gong nas/ 'dir ma phebs bar la me phon chen po gsum kha sprod du bzung nas/ me de dag gi rtsa bar phebs par nye ba na/ 'od je gsal du 'gro ba dang nyin
mo phebs pa bas kyang gsal bar byung zhes gleng gi 'dug pa la/

sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las/ he he nged rgan po tsho la ni de 'dra byung / khyed tsho la ji ltar byung gsungs pa dang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can dpon slob
rnams kyis thog mar lam stor tshul dang / de nas gsol 'debs mdzad pas/ slar rkang rjes kyis lam bstan tshul rnams rgyas par zhu bar mdzad nas/ bdag rnams rnam rtog rags
pas/ thog mar rkang rjes gsum yong ba yod gsung ba'i dus su ji ltar yong ngam snyam pa'i the tshom tsam byung bas/ de la thugs kyis mi khrel mkhyen zhes zhu bar mdzad pa
la/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las/ khyed tshan pa 'di tsho la/ kha bla ma la/ yid mi ches pa'i skyon cig ka yod/ nga kha na so 'di ru song nas rdzun lab dogs med/ he
he/ do nub kyi rkang rjes de gsum sngar khri thog pa spun rang la byas 'gyur du ngo sprod byas pa'i ming sring gsum po de ka yin/ 'on kyang rkang rjes de gsum tsam mthong
ba la ngo mtshar rgyu med/ nged lo nyi shu rtsa grangs kyi dus ding

ri phyogs su phyin pa na/ rtsibs ri'i byang ngos de la ltung bshags kyi sangs rgyas so lnga po khra lam me bzhugs pa gsal bar mthong zhing / de'i byang shar gyi phyogs na 'phags
pa klu sgrub dang / sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa yin snyam pa'i paNDi ta na bza' ngur smrig bsnams pa gnyis kyang 'dug cing / yang nged lo bcu gcig tsam 'gro ba'i dus
su phung po ri bo che'i byang ngos la gnas brtan bcu drug po sku re re nas rnam 'gyur ya mtshan can sna tshogs mdzad pa dang bcas pa shin tu gsal bar mthong ba yin zhes sogs
ngo mtshar can gyi gzigs snang byung tshul mang po zhig gsungs nas/ gang ltar pu tra 'dis dus dang gnas skabs kun tu phan btags pa 'dra ba gzhan sus kyang phan pa med
pas/ 'di la rngan pa zhig ster dgos pa yin gsungs nas de ma thag bskang gso rgyas par mdzad pa yin no zhes thos la/ 'di'i gong gi do nub kyi rkang rjes de gsum sngar khri
thog pa spun rang la byas 'gyur du ngo sprod byas pa'i ming sring gsum

po de ka yin/ zhes gsungs pa 'di ni/ sngon 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched la byas 'gyur du bdag nyid chen pos pu tra ming sring gsum gyi rjes gnang stsal pa de nyid la dgongs
par gsal lo/ /yang dus lan gcig gi tshe bstan dgra lha sa rdzong pa'i ngan rgyab byang pa bkra shis stobs rgyas pas byas nas 'brog pa brgya dpon smad pa rnams la ngan slob
byas te/ rta jag par grags pa'i 'brog pa rnams kyis rta ru ba dang / ko 'dre ru ba sogs gdan sa chen po la gtogs pa'i sgos rus dang / sa skya'i mi sde'i ba phyugs sogs
dang / chos gzhis so so'i phyugs lug sogs 'khyer bcom nyin re bzhin byas shing / de dang dus mtshungs par mnga' ris rig 'dzin chen por grags pa dang / gshin rje mkhan po
nub dgon par grags pa dang / gzhan yang sngags pa mthu che ba'i rigs mang po lha sa rdzong du bsdus te ngan gtad gyi rigs mang po byed du bcug cing / bdag po bkra shis stobs
rgyas pa rang gis gshin rje tshe bdag gi mchod rten bcas chog thod pa zhal dbye sogs

mthu gtad bung che ba rgyun bsrings nas byas te/ mdor na sgo du ma nas bdag nyid chen po la zhabs 'dren gyi tshogs nus gang thon byas pa na/ sa skya pa la gus zhen yod pa'i
sde dpon rigs la sogs pas 'di bzhin byed par 'dug tshul sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i drung du zhus pa na/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las/ kho rang tsho de bzhin ci
byas kyang nga'i ba spu yang g.yo bar mi nus mod/ 'on kyang sde bstan pa gdung rgyud dang bcas pa dang / khyad par chos skyong la yang brnyas par 'gyur ba 'dug pas/ lan
du rtags thon pa rang zhig byed pa yin no zhes zhal bzhes gnang ste/ de nas bzung ste sngags 'chang nyid kyis dgong phyogs bskang gso rgyun pa'i tshe/ zor gtor khrag byugs
pa bzhi re bskang gtor gyi mdun du bshams par mdzad de/ thugs dam drag bskul rnga shon dang bcas pa gnang ba dang bstun nas mchod g.yog pa res mi rkang g.yab dar dang
bcas pa dang / gzhan ma phyag g.yog res gong gi

zor gtor chang phud dang bcas khyer te/ ban gtsang ba bsnyen song rnams la bdag nyid chen po'i gsung gis/ khyed rnams re mos kyis shA sa na 'dren cing sman zhing steng du song
la chang phud 'thor zhing / rkang gling gsum re bus nas/ g.yab dar lan gsum brdabs te zor gtor dgra phyogs su 'phen par gyis zhes gsungs nas zla ba gcig tsam de bzhin
mdzad cing / de nas bdag nyid chen pos sgo rum ye shes mgon po'i drung du las sbyor gyi sku mtshams bdun phrag gsum tsam gnang nas/ de nas mgon khang de nyid du las sbyor
drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog sku rkyang gis bsgrub pa gnang rjes ban gtsang pa sogs dang bcas phyag len gnang nas/ sngar gyi sman zhing steng gi zor gtor bskyal sa de nas 'phen
par mdzad cing / de nas gdan sa'i dus mdos chen mo nyid nub phyogs la zhal bsgyur bar gnang ste/ de yang brgya dpon brang mo che ba sangs rgyas dpa' bor grags pa dpal
mgon zhal la mnga' brnyes pa la brten nas zhal gyi gtor ma 'phen par

gnang zhing / mkhan chen dpal ldan bzang po la pu tra'i gtor ma 'phen par bka' stsal/ gzhan yang bsnyen song nus pa che ba rnams la bdud rgyal dang spyi gtor 'phen par bka'
phebs shing / zor las pa rnams kyis so so'i bsnyen pa kha gso dang / gtor bsngo skabs dmod bcol sogs rang rang gi bsam pa rnam par dag pas kun nas bslangs te gang grub gyis
shig ces bka' gnang bzhin legs par grub pa dang / de nas dus mdos dngos gzhi'i dus su chos skyong gi 'cham mgon spyan 'dren par mdzad pa yang 'phags pas phyag nas gnang
ba hor bzlog mgon por grags pa lcam dral dang / bzhi thog pa mkhas btsun chen pos byang pa ta dben bsgral dus chos skyong gi lung bstan bzhin bzhengs pa'i byang 'dul mgon
por grags pa sogs ye shes pa bzhugs nges pa'i shin tu gnyan pa'i 'cham mgon lcam dral bdun spyan 'dren par mdzad de/ de'i 'khor du ru 'dren gyi tshul gyi skyes pa go
mtshon can rnams dang /

sde'i bud med khyim pa mo rnams lag tu stag dang 'u lu thogs/ ngag tu bhyoHdang dmod mo gang shes 'don bzhin pa dang / gzhan yang dge 'dun tshogs pas sher snying bdud bzlog
sngags pa mang pos drag sngags zlos pa la sogs pa'i zhal bkod dang bcas sngar gtor zor 'phen pa'i gnas sman zhing du phebs te/ dam nyams gnas pa'i sar zhal phyogs pas dpon
slob byin pos pho nya bskul ba'i ring la/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos slob dpon padmas mdzad pa'i 'jig rten 'das dang ma 'das kyi chos srung thams cad la bden pa
brdar zhing dmod bcol rgyas pa'i tshig rnams dang / rje btsun gong ma rnams kyi man ngag la brten nas mkhas pa yon tan khris mdzad pa'i drang srong dmod pa'i bskul sogs dmod
bcol drag tu gnang nas/ thog mar zangs gzhong gcig gi nang na mtho gang tsam gyi gtor ma smug rtsi sogs kyis kha ma bsgyur ba'i zor gtor 'dra ba'i rtser nor bu mig gsum
dang / zur la me

ris khyi gzhug ma byas pa bdun tshar zhig yod pa rnams la sgyogs 'phen par mdzad rjes/ gur gyi mgon po'i gtor chen gnang nas/ na bza'i g.yab rdo dang 'phrin bcol mang du gnang
zhing / de bstun zor las so sos kyang dmod bcol dang gtor ma brgyab grub mtshams nam mkha' 'jam par yod pa la/ glo bur du sa skya sde nas 'tshub ma chen po zhig langs
nas zor lam phyogs su song nas lung grog phan thal rlung chen pos khrig 'gags shing / de'i gseb tu nam mkhar bya rog kha gdangs nas dgra phyogs su brgyugs pa dang / sa la
khyi mang po kha gdangs nas brgyugs pa ni der 'tshogs kun gyis mthong ngo zhes thos la/ skabs der sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i gzigs snang la/ rlung nag 'tshub pa'i
khrod na chos skyong gi pho nya las mkhan rnams drag po'i rngam stabs dang bcas dgra phyogs su brgyugs pa mngon sum du gsal bar gzigs nas/

gtor bzlog grub pa'i bzhugs gral gyi skabs su sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las/ bka' srung rnams dgra bgegs la shin tu rngam par 'dug pas/ chos srung rnams la gtang rag zab
dgos par 'dug go zhes bka' stsal gnang bar mdzad la/ de skabs nas bzung srod tho rangs btso brgyug la sogs rtags mtshan mang du byung / de dang dus mtshungs par gong du
bshad pa ltar gyi lha sa rdzong du mthu mkhan 'dus pa rnams la tshogs 'khor zab par bshams pa'i gral gtam la/ mnga' ris rig 'dzin pas/ bdag po bkra shis stobs rgyas drung
dang / lha sa nas khyed zhang dbon sku stobs dang ldan pa'i skabs 'dir/ chu 'go ya gir chos log mkhan 'di tsho med par mdzad dgos rgyur 'dug ces gleng ba na/ dpal rtse ba
dang / mtsho sgo ba sogs dpon rigs thams cad yid ma rangs par mgrin gcig tu/ sa skya pa'i zhal ngo gdung rgyud kyi sar 'thad mi 'thad sna tshogs la brten zhabs 'dren phran

bu yang zhu dgos yong gi 'dug mod/ grub mtha'i cha rgya bod hor sogs thams cad du chos lugs dpal ldan sa skya pa las lhag pa gzhan med ces mkhas grub thams cad mthun snang
grub cing 'gran zla dang bral ba yin/ de 'dra'i gtam ci zer chos spong gi las gsog par 'dug rna ba dgab dgos pa'i gtam yin zer ba sogs thams cad rgyud 'khrugs te gral la
'ur lang dang rdog pa rdeb pa sogs rnam 'gyur sna tshogs byung zhes phyis der 'dus pa thams cad gleng bar grags shing / de nas lha sa rdzong gi mchod yon rnams so sor gyes
te/ mnga' ris rig 'dzin pa byang gi theg mchog gling du brdzangs pa yin no zhes thos so/ /de nas myur bar mnga' ris rig 'dzin pa tshe'i dus byas pa na/ byang pa bkras stobs
pas slob dpon padma'i sku thog tshad ma gcig bzhengs de'i khog tu rig 'dzin pa'i phung po bcug nas kha rin spungs la bstan/ ro'i kha gdangs pa'i nang du khong rang tsho

la gnag pa'i byang pa'i dpon rigs/ rin spungs pa'i zhal ngo dpon blon rnams kyi ming rus sogs dang / rgyal mkhar rtse pa'i zhal ngo rnams kyi ming rus dang / lhag par sngags
'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i mtshan byang 'jug par byas te/ rig 'dzin chen po khong gi kha chems yin zer nas mthu byas pa'i lugs su byas shing bkras stobs pa rang nyid kyi
tshe bdag mchod rten bcas chog sogs sna tshogs byas so zhes thos shing / de de'i skabs nas sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po nyid/ chos rgyal bsod nams lhun grub pa sku mched
rnams kyis rgyal mkhar rtser spyan drangs te phyag nas legs par phebs nas/ de skabs su bstan pa dang sbyin bdag rnams la dgongs nas/ rtse rgyal mgon khang du gur zhal
'khor bcas kyi rtag gtor 'dzin gtor yang 'dzugs par gnang ba yin no zhes kyang thos la/ gzhan yang sde srid zhal ngo rnams kyi sku rim du rdo rje phur pa'i gtor bzlog cig
kyang gnang bar mdzad cing / de dus rgyal

rtse li ma lha khang gi g.yab khrar sde srid zhal ngo rnams la pha rol gyi byad ka rbod gtong gi rtags che bar byung bas/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po la de bzhin gyi gnas
tshul phul ba na/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las kyang / byad ka'i rtags 'dra shin tu yang 'dug pas/ de la dmigs nas gur zhal la brten pa'i gsang gtor zhig byed pa yin
no zhes bka' stsal nas/ de bzhin bsgrub par mdzad de/ de nas zhag gsum tsam song ba na/ sde srid bsod nams lhun grub nyid sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i zhabs drung
na bzhugs yod pa'i skabs su/ mgron gnyer bas 'brug pa'i sgar pa yin zer ba gcig sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal por phyag dbang zhig thugs rje che dgos zhu bar 'dug pa na/
sde srid bsod nams lhun grub pas/ sngags 'chang nyid la 'di ltar zhus te/ sgar pa de skye sa rong lhun rab pa lags shing / gshin rje'i las mtha' ngan sngags 'ba' zhig byed
pa'i

chos rgyal dpal bzang zer ba'i ngan pa zhig yod pa de yin 'dug pa nas phyag 'bul la sku drung du mi gnang ba dgos zhes zhus pa na/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las/ kho rang
tshan 'di pa dad nas phyag 'bul du yong pa min/ gshin rje sogs la brten pa'i mgo 'jog 'khor lo zer ba'i gzhan gyi tshe dang bsod nams mthu stobs sogs nyams par byed pa
ngan sngags kyi 'khor lo zhig yong bas/ kho'i mgo gtsug na 'khor lo de btags yod pa de'i khar nga'i rab rkang pa/ de min lag pa 'jog dgos rgyu yin pas/ nged la de 'dra'i
rigs kyis glags rnyed pa zhig yin na/ da tsam nged kyi ming gi lhag ma yang sa steng na lus pa med/ khyed rang zhal ngo tsho gtor ma'i mdun du bzhugs la gtor ma la nas 'bru
sogs 'thor du ma 'jug la/ gzhan khyad par med pas btang bas chog gsungs nas/ khong dpon g.yog gsum 'dug pa la/ mjal dar bkra shis kha btags shig phul song ba na/ sngags

'chang chos kyi rgyal pos phyag gnyis kar gyis phyag dbang gnang nas/ dpral ba mthil zhal la thug gi bar gnon par mdzad song pa'i tshe/ sgar pa de shin tu 'jigs shing dpa'
khongs gdong rngul 'dzag cing 'dar zhing dngangs pas phyir thon par gyur cing / de nyid kyi mgo la sngags 'chang nyid kyis bka' stsal pa bzhin gyi tim pa'i thum byas pa'i
bsrung ba zhig btags 'dug go zhes kyang thos la/ de nyid kyi nub mo sde srid bsod nams lhun grub nyid sngags 'chang nyid kyi drung na bzhugs yod pa'i tshe/ thugs dam gtor
ma'i rtse mo chad byung ba na/ de nas cung zad song ba'i tshe tsheg sgra dang me stag khrom khrom byung ba'i mtshams/ gtor ma nas me 'od chad de g.yab khra'i phyir song
ba na/ phyag g.yog sogs phyi na yod pa rnams kyi bsam pa la gzim khang gi nang la me shor bar 'dug snyam nas g.yab khra'i nang du tab tob tu sleb par gyur cing / de nas
me de nam mkhar 'thor

nas phyogs thams cad la song ba der yod kun gyis mthong ba yin no zhes grags la/ de nas thugs dam gsang gtor de nyid nag rtsi shar steng nas gnang ste skabs der sngags 'chang
nyid kyi gsung las/ nged rang mchod yon gyi dgra bgegs rnams la rtags mtshan myur du yong ba 'dug pas/ gtang rag tu sa skya'i mgon khang rnams su thug kha gso ba/ spyan
gzigs/ gtor gsos bskang gso sogs zab par mdzod gsungs shing / de nas sde srid zhal ngo rnams kyis tshogs 'khor rgyas par zhus nas/ so so nas 'bul sgrub bsam gyis mi khyab
pa gnang skabs su sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i gsung las/ da lam rten 'brel shin tu legs shing / dam tshig mchog tu gtsang bar 'dug pas/ rnal 'byor pa'i lam sgom
pa'i rtags shig 'don pa yin no gsungs nas/ sing sbal chen mo re shong ba'i dngul skyem mda' tshad ma zhig chang gis bkang nas/ dal bus blugs shig ces

bka' gnang nas/ zhal gyen du cung zad gdangs tshul gnang bar/ gzim g.yog pas dngul skyem btegs nas zhal du zhus pa na/ chu sbugs su chu 'gro ba ltar bde bar khyu ru ru 'gro
ba'i ngos dngul skyem gang po zhal du rdzogs par gsol te/ sku la ma bde ba'i nyams sogs gnod pa cung zad kyang med pa/ chab bsang pa tsam yang mi dgos pa sogs rgya gar grub
chen rnal 'byor dbang phyug gis yul khams bco brgyad kyi chang dus gcig la zad par gsol yang myos pa med pa la sogs pa'i rnam thar dang mthun pa'i grub pa'i rtags mtshan
de lta bu mngon sum du ston par mdzad cing / de nas sngags 'chang bla ma de nyid kyis thong lcags su phebs nas/ de nyid kyi mgon khang na sngon bdag chen blo gros rgyal
mtshan pas las sbyor gnang ba'i drag po'i 'brub khrung lingga sngags can mdze thod kha sbyor/ drag po'i thun sogs bcas tshang ba yod pa dang / drag po'i

sbyin sreg gi thab khung sogs dang / bdag chen rin chen de nyid kyi gsol phod re phod/ dbu zhwa zhwa nag bzhugs gdan sogs thams cad da lta'i bar du cha tshang yod pa'i drag
po'i mgon khang khyad par can der/ spyi sgos kyi bstan dgra rnams la dmigs nas bdun phrag gsum du sku mtshams bcad rgya gnang nas/ las sbyor las mtha' btul ba sogs mthar
phyin par gnang rjes su bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan pa'i gsol phod re phod/ dbu thebs sogs sku la bzhes pa'i chas gzhug mdzad de/ de'i phyag phyir sde srid bsod nams
lhun grub kyi drung dang / ban gtsang pa'i phyag g.yog dang bcas drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog cig gnang zhing / mgon khang de nyid du rdza sder gnyis su mgon po khro bcu'i gtor
ma mar gyi nor bu mig gsum me ris kyi rgyan cha tsam yod pa cha gnyis byin rlabs mdzad de 'jog pa gnang nas/ 'di gnyis rgyal rtse ba la dgos

khag che ba gnyis yong bas de dus re re 'phangs pas don 'grub par yong gsungs pa'i lung bstan dang bcas 'jog pa gnang zhing / de dag dang dus mtshungs gdan sa chen por drag
po'i las sbyor 'grub pa'i ngo mtshar ba'i rtags mtshan 'di ltar byung ste/ de yang gdan sa nyid na gzhir bzhugs kyi skya ser phyogs mtha'i mi dmangs thams cad kyis mthong
bar/ hor zla gsum pa'i nyer dgu'i nub sa rub pa na/ 'ga' zhig gis mthong snang la gdan sa chen po'i bzhi thog nas byung zer ba dang / la las pu tra khang nas byung zer
ba'i gang ltar yang kun gyis mthong bar gdan sa dan khrod nas btso rdza ma tsam zhig byung nas dal bus lung grog thad du cung zhig 'dug pa na/ de rjes kha'u'i rong nas langs
pa lta bu'i btso snga ma las nyis 'gyur gyis che ba gcig byung nas snga ma de'i rjes tsam du slebs pa na/ de nas sde'i dkyil nas byung pa 'dra ba'i btso shin tu che ba
zhig byung nas dbus ri'i thad tsam du me stag mang po

chad nas phyogs bcur 'thor/ de nas btso gsum po de reg la ma 'dres tsam du dbus ri brgal nas song ba thams cad kyis mthong zhing / dbus ri brgal nas cha gnyis su byas nas/
gcig 'brog la brgya dpon gyi sa cha shrI brag gi rtsa bar babs pas/ brag gas pa'i srub nas khrag brgyugs pas bong chu'i gzhogs gcig khrag mdog tu gyur pa sogs byung zer ba/
sa yul de phyogs nas byung ba'i skya ser thams cad mgrin gcig tu gleng ba byung zhing / slar gdan sa rang nas bsher 'don la phyin pa'i mi sna rnams kyis kyang dngos su
mthong ngo zhes thos la/ cha gcig ngam ring theg mchog gling gi spen bad la phog pa na/ de'i tshe byang pa bkras stobs pas theg mchog gling du sngags pa mang du bsdus pa
rnams dang khyad par bo dong gi sngags pa rnams ngag mthun par/ rngod la'i rtser btso gsum byung nas tshur slebs pa na gcig tu 'gril te theg mchog gling rang gi spen pad
la phog pas/ spen mas

me blangs te tshig pa na/ der 'dus pa'i sngags pa rnams kyis gtor ma dang thun 'dra brgyab/ mdo phran gyi po ti 'dra brdebs pa sogs ci bya gtol med du gyur nas 'dug ces kho
rang sngags rnams kyis dngos su sgrog par gyur cing / phyis sor byang pa'i dpon rigs rnams kyang mgrin gcig tu gleng bar byed ces thos la/ de nas yun ring ma lon par rgyal
rtse nas sde srid rnam par rgyal ba mnga' zhabs chos sde dang bcas pas dmag gi dpung chen bshams te/ sa skya pa'i zhabs 'degs su dmigs nas lha sa rdzong hod 'tshangs kyis
blangs nas gdan sa chen por 'bul sbyor gnang rtsis mdzad de/ dmag rnams mtshan mo kha'u'i zug gu la bton nas dgon pa skyed lhas kyi mdun du slebs pa na/ sgrub sde na
yod pa'i dam nyams dbon po sa nag par grags pa dang / kom 'dre ba dge slong bsod blo gnyis kyis skyed lhas dgon pa'i thod la phyin nas lha sa rdzong du bya btang zhing /
dus

de nyid kyi tshe sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po gdan sa chen por ma bzhugs pa'i skabs shig yin pa la brten nas/ lha khang chen mo nyid na rgyal yum sku mched kyi phyag phyir
gdong dga' ba dpon sa dpon du grags pa yod pas/ byang zhen byas nas lha sa rdzong pa'i rgyab tu byang dpung co rir yod pa la mi btang ba sogs kyi dbang las rgyal rtse
nas dpung chen gyis lha sa rdzong la hod 'tshangs gnang ma bde ba'i tshe/ sde srid rnam par rgyal ba'i gsung gis/ dam nyams bsgrub pa de gnyis dang / gdong dga' ba rgad po
de'i byed pa la brten nas bsam pa rdzogs pa zhig ma byung / zhes kyang gsungs par grags shing / skabs der sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po nyid slar gdan sa chen por phebs
pa na yang gzhir bzhugs thams cad la dgongs par ma bde ba tsam dang / khyad par gdong dga' ba rnams la sa skyar yong mi dgos pa'i bka' stsal sogs kyang phebs pa yin no
zhes thos la/ 'on kyang der skabs shar ga nas dpung chen gyis bstan dgra lha sa rdzong pa'i 'og tu

gtogs pa thams cad la shing bshu me rgyag 'phrog 'joms sogs tshad med pa mdzad nas dam nyams 'khor bcas 'jigs shing skyi g.ya' ba dang bcas sems mya ngan gyis non par gyur
to/ /de nas lo zla ma 'gyangs par sngags 'chang mthu rtsal can nyid kyis gong du brjod pa bzhin/ bstan srung rnams drag po mngon spyod kyi las la bskul zhing rbad par mdzad
pa de'i mthu stobs kyis g.yas ru byang ba nang 'khrugs pa'i tshe/ bsam 'grub rtse nas sde srid byang pa gzhung gi zhabs tog zhus nas/ bkra shis stobs rgyas pa 'khor bcas
rnams 'phyong rgyas sogs dbus phyogs su gnas dbyung byas shing / byang khang gsar ba sogs phyogs gtogs thams cad kyang phyir phud/ dam nyams lha sa rdzong pa yang sel
'don byas te/ der skabs bsam rtse nas bstan pa'i sbyin bdag zhing shag rdo rjes sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i drung du zhu 'phrin byung pa la/ byang pa bkras stobs pa
dang / lha

sa rdzong pas zhabs drung de nyid du snga phyir zhabs 'dren stobs ches pa nas/ da lam gdan sa nas kyang lha sa rdzong du dmag 'dren skya 'thor sogs gnang ba skabs thob yin
pas/ de bzhin du gnang dgos zhu ba ltar/ bdag nyid chen pos kyang de dang mthun par bsam pa rdzogs par mdzad cing / de nas lha sa rdzong de nyid lha sa ba rang gi cha zhabs
rang khul nas sa rdal du bsgyel ba'i rdzong ri de nyid du sngags 'chang mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug 'di nyid 'khor rdo rje 'dzin pa'i tshogs dang bcas pas/ bla ma gong
ma'i thugs dam ma'i ye shes pa bzhugs nges pa'i 'cham mgon lcam dral byin rlabs can thams cad spyan 'dren par mdzad nas/ bdag nyid chen po dpon slob rnams kyis mkha' 'gro
chos skyong srung ma mthu rtsal can rnams la/ dam nyams gtan brlag tu thong pa'i gtang rag rgyas par 'bul ba mdzad pa dang bcas/ slad nas kyang ri 'di la skye bo su zhig
gis btsan gnas su dmigs pa'i mkhar 'debs pa byed pa byung na/ sa skya pa'i bka' srung dam can rgya mtsho

'jig rten dregs pa'i tshogs dang bcas pa rnams kyis/ rdzong ri la mkhar 'debs byed po de nyid lo zla ma 'gyang par tshar bcad de zhal du bzhes shig pa'i bka' bsgo 'phrin 'chol
drag tu mdzad de/ de dus kyi bzhes khra'i shog ril de nyid da lta yang sgo rum ye shes mgon po'i zhal gdong na yod pa 'di yin la/ de nas bzung ste lha sa rdzong gi ri
'di la sde dpon che phra su zhig gis mkhar las byas kyang de nyid mthar mi phyin cing / byed pa po rnams la yang myur ba nyid du rtags mtshan drag po mngon sum du 'byung
ba ni ding sang gi skye bo thams cad la rlung ltar grags shing kun gyi kha na rgyu ba 'di yin no/ /de dag dang dus mtshungs par sngon btso babs nas brag gshags pa'i sa phyogs
de nyid du 'brog pa brgya dpon smad pa'i ru pa'i dpon mtshan 'bum du grags pa dang / kun bzang dpal chen gyi bu gnyis dmar bshal gyis myur du 'das shing / de nas bzung
ste gdan sa chen por zhabs 'dren byed pa'i rta jag par grags pa'i

'brog ris thams cad rims nad kyis gtan brlag tu song ba yin no zhes thos la/ mdor na bdag nyid chen po 'di nyid la bsam sbyor ngan par byas pa'i dpon rigs che phra sogs bdud
kyi rigs de thams cad la la rtsa ba nas stong pa dang / kha cig stobs shed nyams pa sogs rtags dang mtshan mas kun la khyab ste/ rang rang gis byas pa'i las kyi rnam par
smin pa rang thog tu smin te snang tshul 'di bzhin du gyur pa rgyal khams kyi skye bo yongs kyi mngon sum gyi spyod yul du grub pa 'di nyid do/ /de ltar sangs rgyas bstan
pa la gnod par byed pa'i gdug pa can rnams drag po mngon spyod kyi las kyis tshar gcod par mdzad pa 'di dag ni gzhan las ches rmad du byung ba'i rnam par thar ba ste/
ji skad du rtsa rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa las/ bstan la gnod par byed pa dang / /bla ma sangs rgyas 'jig pa nyid/ /bla ma thub pa la zhus nas/ /snying rjes gsad par bya ba
nyid/ /ces gsungs shing rdo rje gur

las kyang / gdug la byams pa nyid mi bya/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ bla ma dang sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la gnod pa'i gdug can rnams mngon spyod kyi las kyis bsgral bar ma byas
na/ rig pa 'dzin pa'i dam tshig kyang nyams par 'gyur bar gsungs pa yin te/ gsang sngags snga 'gyur ba rnams kyi rgyud dag las kyang / nyams pa dus su mi sgrol ba/ /de yang
dam tshig nyams pa yin/ /zhes dang / gzhan yang gsang sngags gsar 'gyur ba la grags pa'i rtsa ltung bcu bzhi pa'i gzhung las kyang / gdug la rtag tu byams ldan pa/ /byed
pa de ni bcu par 'dod/ /ces gsungs so/ /des na sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dang / bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu dam pa rnams la bdud dang mu stegs la sogs pa nag phyogs la dga'
ba rnams kyis bar chad byed par sangs rgyas rang nyid kyis gsungs shing / de dag bzlog cing gzhom par byed pa'i thabs kyang rdo rje 'chang nyid kyis rgyud sde rin po che
dri ma med pa rnams las

chos skyong ba'i srung ma'i tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig gsungs shing / de dag dang 'brel ba'i drag po mngon spyod kyi las tshogs kyang grangs dang tshad med pa zhig gsungs
pa yin pas/ de na blo dang ldan zhing bsnyen sgrub las gsum mthar phyin pa'i skyes bu dam pa rnams kyis bstan pa bstan 'dzin dang bcas pa la gnod par byed pa'i las
ngan can rnams la dngos su mtshon bsnun pa la sogs pa dang / gzhan yang sngags kyi las sbyor dang / mnan pa dang / bskrad pa dang / bsad pa la sogs pa'i 'khrul 'khor dang
/ ngan sngags dang / sman gyi sbyor ba la sogs pa dag gis kyang gdug pa can rnams tshar gcod par bya dgos pa yin te/ gshin rje gdong drug gi rgyud las/ blo ldan bsgrub pos
sems can la/ /phan pa'i bsam pas srog mi bcad/ /ces gsungs pa'i rjes su/ gdug pa can la ldog ste bya/ /dngos su 'am yang na sngags dang gzhan/ /'khrul 'khor dang ni ting
nge 'dzin/ /sman gyis kyang ni bya

ba ste/ /de ltar mi byed de yi ni/ /dam tshig nges par nyams par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / mdo las kyang / ded dpon snying rje chen pos tshong ba lnga brgya'i srog bskyabs
pa'i phyir du/ mi nag mdung thung can la kho rang gi lag gi mdung bsnun te bsad pa lta bu dang / bod kyi bstan pa snga dar dang phyi dar gyi mtshams der lha lung dpal
gyi rdo rjes/ rgyal po sdig can mtshon bsnun nas bsad pa sogs mdor na sprul pa'i skyes mchog rnams kyis bstan pa dang sems can gyi don rgya chen po bsgrub pa'i phyir bdud
rigs gdug can rnams thabs sna tshogs kyi sgo nas bsgral te mi dge ba spyod pa'i rgyun dang / ma 'ongs pa ngan song gi srid par skye ba len pa'i las rgyun gnyis dus gcig
tu bcad de mtho ris dang thar pa'i gnas su 'dren par mdzad pa 'di ni gzhan las ngo mtshar mchog tu gyur pa'i rnam par thar pa yin gyi/ de lta bu bsgrub pa'i nus pa dang
mi ldan pa rnams ni de dag mos pa tsam du zad pa'i phyir ro/ /de lta bu'i

'gran bral gyi skyes bu sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po de nyid kyi chos dang rigs las 'khrungs pa'i thugs sras kun gyi gtsug rgyan/ bdag cag gi 'dren pa dam pa rigs ldan chos
kyi rgyal po sku mched zhal rnam pa gnyis kyi ngo mtshar ba'i rnam thar rgyas pa ni kho bos logs su byas pa las rtogs par bya zhing / 'dir skabs su babs pa sa skya pa'i
bka' srung dbang po rnams la mnga' brnyes pa'i tshul cung zad tsam spel na/ de yang gcen 'jam pa'i dbyangs bsod nams dbang po ni/ yum gyi mngal du byon pa tsam nas bzung
/ bstan srung rnams 'bral med du 'khor ba zhig ste/ de dus yum la nyin mtshan kun tu chos skyong gur zhal gnyis 'bral med du gnas pa yin snyam pa'i 'jigs ngam ngam pa
dang / dga' yal le ba rgyun du byung bar grags pa thos shing / bltams nas kyang sku na shin tu phra ba'i dus su zhabs skyil krung dang / phyag gnyis thugs kar chos 'chad
kyi phyag rgya mdzad de bzhugs pa sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos

gzigs nas/ byis pa 'di'i sdod lugs kyi 'dug stangs 'di bzhin/ 'jam dbyangs yin zer bar 'dug khyed rnams kyis gtsang sbra dang bca' gas thon par gyis zhes phyag phyi ba dag
la gsungs pa dang / sku tsog la bzhugs thub pa tsam gyi skabs su sku drung na su yang med pa'i skabs shig gi tshe/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po phebs nas zhabs 'bring
pa rnams la/ khyed rnams bu tsha la bca' ga cher mi byed 'dug na'ang / 'di rang la grogs grul btub gcig slebs 'dug ces gsungs pa la/ zhabs 'bring ba rnams kyis grogs de nyid
su lags zhus pa na/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung gis/ de pu tra yin pa 'dug ces gsungs par grags pa la sogs pa mdor na gzhon nu'i dus 'di nas dam can pu tra chen po 'bral
ba med pa'i tshul gyis 'phrin las rgya chen po bsgrubs pa yin no zhes thos la/ yang rdo rje nag po chen po zhal gzigs pa'i tshul ni/ rje

'dis byas 'gyur du sku mtshams lo gsum thengs gnyis gnang ba'i snga ma'i dus su/ shing mgon yid bzhin nor bu'i thugs ka nas 'od sngon po zhig byung ba/ rje nyid kyi thugs kar
thim pa'i gsal snang dang bcas/ brag phug chen po me 'bar ba zhig gi khrod na bzhugs pa'i dpal gur gyi mgon po'i sku gzi brjid dang ldan pa zhig mngon sum du gzigs pa
dang / sgo rum gyi bse mgon yid bzhin nor bu la yang las bzhi thogs med du 'grub pa'i gzigs snang ngo mtshar can byung tshul gong du brjod pa ltar yin pas/ de lta bu yang
ye shes pa dngos kyi zhal bstan pa dang khyad par mi 'dug cing / yang zhing skyong tsa turmu kha nyid kyi sku'i snang brnyan bstan cing 'phrin las sgrub pa'i sgo nas rten
rdo khyad par can gyi bka' babs byung ba'i tshul ni/ rje nyid dgung lo nga dgu tsam bzhes pa'i ston gyi cha la stod byang gsang sngags rnying ma'i dgon gnas srid gsum drag
po dpal 'bar gyi slob dpon rin po che'i gzim phug tu bzhugs pa'i skabs

shig mnal lam gyi tshul du bram ze'i gzugs can zhig byung nas/ 'di skad du/ chos kyi ming ldan dgon pa ru/ /dgon gyi ming can gang zag gis/ /snye thang zhes pa'i gnas mchog
na/ /gnyan lo chen po'i thugs dam gyi/ /tsa turmu kha'i sku brnyan mchog /dbang gi ming can skye bo la/ /bsgos te pho nyar mngags pa na/ /'dod don rta lug mtshams su 'grub/
/ces pa'i lung bstan zhig smras byung bas mnal sad pa na/ bram ze'i gzugs can yang de kar dar tsam zhig 'dug ste/ phyag g.yog cig zhabs drung du byung ba'i rkyen byas
las song ba'i tshe/ rje nyid kyi thugs la lung bstan de ya mtshan che dgongs nas/ de'i tshul rnams nyid kyi zhabs 'bring ba chen po chos rje kun dga' bkra shis la sgrib
med du gsungs shing / de nas yun ring ma lon par dbus phyogs su chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur ba'i skabs/ sngar gyi lung bstan ngo

mtshar can de mngon du gyur pa'i tshul ni/ bstan pa'i sbyin bdag rnam rgyal rab brtan pas rje nyid dpon slob rnams spyan drangs pa na/ khong tsho'i cha zhabs bla ma rngog pa'i
dgon rnying chos 'khor gling zhes bya ba der/ dgon smad slob dpon par grags pa'i gang zag des/ snye thang na bla ma gnyan lo tsA ba'i thugs dam rten rdo zhal bzhi yongs
rdzogs kyi sku sogs rang byon khyad par can mang du yod pa'i rten rdo ngo mtshar can de bzhin yod pa'i gnas tshul snyan du phul byung ba na/ rje nyid kyi thugs la sngar
srid gsum drag po dpal 'bar du bzhugs dus kyi lung bstan de dus la bab par dgongs nas/ de 'phral rten rdo spyan 'dren pa'i pho nya gnang ba'i tshe/ snye thang gser khang
pas rten rdo 'bul du ma 'dod pa la/ slar gzhis ka chen po bsam 'grub rtse nas/ rje 'di nyid kyi bka' bzhin stobs kyi 'khor los bsgyur ba karma phun tshogs rnam rgyal gyis
gzim chung pa lha dbang zer ba zhig do dam

par gnang bar brten/ sngar gyi lung bstan la/ 'dod don rta lug mtshams su 'grub/ /ces pa de mngon du gyur te/ lo de gnyis kyi mtshams su bdag nyid chen po dge sding chos kyi
pho brang na bzhugs pa'i skabs rten rdo ya mtshan can de phyag tu 'byor ba na/ thugs dgyes spro dpag tu med pa dang bcas mchod gtor rgya chen po bsham par mdzad nas gtor
'bul bskang gso rgyas par gnang zhing / rten rdo la sku khrus gsol ba na/ rdo mdog byin rnams kha dog smug po la/ logs shig la zhal bzhi yongs rdzogs kyi sku dang / logs
gzhan rnams la yum chen bzhi'i sngags rnams rdo mdog byin pas dmar ba zhig gi rang byon du gsal ba/ de yang dri bzang gi chu dang 'phrad na rang byon rnams ches cher gsal
bar 'gyur zhing / rgyun par cung mi gsal ba'i tshul gyis mig yod kyi mngon sum gyi spyod yul du gyur pa'i rten rdo khyad 'phags de nyid re zhig dge

sding gi bya 'dabs 'dra 'dri chos rdzong khams gsum zil gnon du bzhugs par gnang ba la/ dus phyis kho bo cag gis dpal sa skyar spyan drangs nas bzhi thog bla brang du bzhugs
su gsol ba 'di yin la/ 'di lta bu'i ngo mtshar rten gang du bzhugs pa'i gnas de ni/ zhing skyong dbang po'i pho brang me 'bar gyi gtsug lag khang zhig dang byin rlabs mnyam
pa'i nges shes dang ldan pa lags shing / de ltar bshad pa'i rnam thar de dag ni/ sngon gnyan lo chen po'i bran du zhing skyong dbang po nyid kyis bram ze'i gzugs dang
ban chung gi rnam par sprul nas go re len gyi zhabs tog mdzad par grags pa dang tshul mtshungs par gdon mi za bas shin tu ngo mtshar ba'i gnas su shes par bya'o/ /'phrin
las kyi mgon po pu tra chen po yang rgyun par zhabs 'bring pa'i tshul du bzhugs pa yin te/ nyid kyi gsung mgur bde chen phun tshogs su/ 'dug grogs su pu tra ngo mtshar
che/ /zhes gsungs pa dang /

kho bo cag gis rje nyid kyi drung du byas 'gyur bla brang nub kyi mgon khang khyad par can der/ gur mgon lha brgyad/ dpal mgon zhal khra can/ pu tra ming sring gsum gyi rjes
gnang rnams zhu ba'i dus rje nyid kyi gsung las/ kha sang byas 'gyur gyi maNDal na mon pa ming sring gsum gar byed kyi 'dug pa 'tshub ma zhig tu song nas brag 'di la thim
song ba da res rjes gnang 'di byed pa'i rten 'brel du 'dug gsungs pa sogs kyis shes so/ /gzhan yang snga mo'i dus yar lung bkra shis rtse'i chos sde gsar pa na/ rje tshar
chen gyi dngos slob rje gzhon nu blo gros bzhugs pa'i drung du/ bdag nyid chen pos sa skya pa'i chos skyong gur zhal gnyis kyi zab chos snyan brgyud khyad par can rnams
bum pa gang byor gsan par bzhed nas/ chos skor gzhan rnams gsan grub rjes/ mgon po'i gsang khrid slar 'bul bar bzhed nas/ rje gzhon nu blo gros pa'i gsung gis/ gsang khrid
'di

bdag gis ma thob ces zhus pas/ de'i nangs par rje mkhan chen nyid kyi gsan yig bya rog gnyis kyis khyer nas/ bdag nyid chen po'i sku pang du bskyur byung ba la gzigs pas/ gsang
khrid kyang gsan 'dug pa dgongs mtshams/ mkhan chen rin po che gzhon nu blo gros pa dpon slob rnams gsan yig stor bas thams cad tsab tsob tu gyur pa na/ nyid kyi gsung
las/ mgon po'i gsang khrid de bdag la gnang na/ gsan yig de chos skyong tshos bdag la gnang byung bas 'bul rgyu yod ces bzhad mo dang bcas sngar gyi lo rgyus rnams zhus
shing / mkhan chen rin po che'i phyag tu gsan yig 'bul ba gnang bas/ rje gzhon nu blo gros pa'i gsung gis/ khyed rang chos skyong bran du 'khol nges su 'dug pa/ 'tshub
bya sogs mi yong ba yid ches pas/ da ni do nub rang nas gsang khrid 'bul ba yin no gsungs te/ de dgong nas chos thun tshugs par mdzad de/ gsang khrid sogs zab chos rnams
lhag lus med par stsal cing /

mgon po'i sku byin rlabs can zhig 'bul bar mdzad de/ phyag thugs kar thal mo sbyar nas/ khyed rang chos skyong gi bdag po/ chos skyong gis bka' bzhin bsgrub pa la kho bo yid
gnyis dang bral ba'i dad pa skyes so/ /zhes gsungs shing / mkhan chen rin po che yang thun mong ma yin pa'i thugs dad lhag par skyes par gyur la/ skabs der bkra shis rtse'i
mchod yon rnams kyi sku rim du rje nyid kyis mgon po drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog cig gnang ba'i tshe/ sgrub khang du yang las sbyor gyi rtags mang du byung zhing / lhag
par gtor ma 'phang par mdzad pa'i nub mo/ bskul rnams mdzad cing phyir phebs pa na/ nam mkha' gzhan rnams shin tu dwangs pa la/ rje nyid gang du bzhugs pa'i dbu thog tu sprin
nag gru gsum 'jigs ngam can zhig 'bral med du yong ba der yod skye bo kun gyis mthong zhing / gang zag las dag pa 'ga' re'i mthong snang la/ sprin nag

gi gseb tu mgon po'i las mkhan du ma dang / me lhab lhab 'bar ba mngon sum du mthong zhing / zor gtor rnams 'phang bar mdzad pa na btso gsum sbrel du brgyugs pa sogs mthu stobs
bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga' ba'i rtags mtshan ngo mtshar can mang du ston par mdzad pa dang / de nas rtses thang bsam gtan gling du phebs te/ de'i gtsug lag khang dang
rten rnams mjal bar mdzad pa na/ gnas der sngon dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i thugs dam phyag nas bzhugs pa'i zhal bzhi dngos dang byin rlabs mnyam par grags pa'i bram gzugs
gyi zhal 'bag cig yod pa la/ rje nyid kyis byin rlabs zhu bar mdzad pas zhal 'bag las 'od sngon po zhig byung ste/ nyid kyi sku la thim pa der yod kun gyis mthong ba dang
/ de nas gdan sa mthil du phebs pa na/ sa yul der mgon po zhal bzhi pa gnas nges pa'i sa mthong mgon khang du grags pa zhig 'dug par tshes brgyad kyi thugs dam dus gtor

gnang bar dgongs pa na/ phyogs de'i zangs ri khang dmar pa dpon g.yog rnams sbugs zhugs kyis grub mtha'i phyogs 'dzin gyi kun slong kho nas brag kha ba brgyud pa'i mgon khang
du thugs dam mi gnang ba dgos tshul zhus byung ba na/ nyid kyi gsung las/ mgon khang du bskang gso ma byas pas chog 'tshub cha bzhin byung na khag med do gsungs nas/ bzhugs
gnas de kar dus gtor 'dzugs pa gnang ba na/ spyan 'dren grub nas byon skyems phul mtshams glo bur du sprin nag 'dus te glog mang du 'khyug pa dang / thog 'brug gi sgra
rgyun mi 'chad pa dang bcas ser ba mthe bong tsam gdan sa mthil dang / zangs ri gnyis kar babs cing / zangs ri'i rdzong du thog babs pas lcags ri nyis rim 'gyel ba sogs
chos skyong gi rtsub 'gyur shin tu che ba byung bas kun kyang 'jigs shing ha las te/ der yod kyi dpon sa dpon g.yog rnams dang /

spyan snga ba'i gcung po sogs sku drung du 'byor bas rje nyid la zang zing gi 'bul rgya chen po dang bcas bshags pa snying thag pa nas 'bul ba dang / slar 'tshub cha mi yong
ba dgos pa'i snyan 'bul zhu bar byung zhing / yang dus phyis gdan sa chen po'i lo dus kyi sku rim mgon po drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog dang / lo de'i phyi ma'i zla ba gnyis
pa'i rdo rje phur pa'i gtor bzlog gnyis ka'i zor las rje nyid kyis phyag bzhes mdzad pa na/ drug cu pa'i skabs su lingga dgug gzhug mdzad pa'i dus/ lingga gcig gis phyag
dril la 'jus shing gcig bros stabs su 'gro ba mchod g.yog pas mthong ba dang / phur bzlog gi gdab las gnang skabs/ lingga'i snying gar 'od yungs 'bru tsam zhig 'dug pa gcen
lung sde pa bya btang ba phyag 'degs la yod pas mthong nas/ rje nyid la dogs gcod zhu ba nged rang gis thos shing / yang rje nyid kyis tsha mo rong glang gi brag la phu
ri rdo rje'i brag rdzong khams gsum zil

gnon gyi sgrub gnas gsar du 'debs par mdzad nas/ de'i bdud 'dul phug tu bzhugs dus dkar bdud lcam dral gnyis dang / bud med dmar mo ral pa rting par khebs pa/ lag na zangs
kyi zhags pa ring po thogs pa zhig gzigs pa/ phur pa'i srung ma zhig yin pa 'dug gsungs pa sogs mdor na nyi ma re re'i nang du yang chos skyong gi rnam 'phrul mtha' yas pa
zhig gzigs par gdon mi za zhing mthu stobs dang nus pa'i mnga' bdag tu bzhugs so/ /bdag nyid chen po de nyid kyi gcung / bdag la bka' drin mchog tu che ba'i yab rje sbas
pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang rgyal ba'i rgyal tshab sems dpa' chen po grags pa'i mtshan can de nyid la bka' srung khyad par can rnams kyis zhal bstan cing pho nya dang
mngag gzhug mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ rje nyid sku gzhon nu'i dus dpal sa skya'i chu mig rdzing ga'i bla brang bde mchog pho brang du dpal kyai

rdo rje'i gzhi bsnyen mdzad pa'i rjes de ma thag par gur gyi mgon po'i sgom bzlas zhag bdun pa zhig mdzad pa'i tho rangs kyi cha mnal lam du/ sa skya'i rgyab ri dpon po ri
nas gdong nag gi bar gyi nam mkha' la sprin nag gru gsum 'khrigs pa'i dbus su gur gyi mgon po nyid phyag gnyis kyi gri thod nyu ge ba dang / de'i steng gi phyogs su khyung
chen gsum/ g.yas su bya nag gsum/ g.yon phyogs su khyi nag gsum/ rgyab phyogs su lce spyang gsum/ mdun phyogs su mi nag gsum rnams shin tu gsal ba dang / sprin nag gi gseb
na me ris shin tu legs pa bzo ris pa mkhas pa sus kyang bskrun par mi nus pa lta bu 'ur sgra dang bcas 'bar ba yun ring du gzigs shing / de'i ngang nas gur gyi mgon po'i
sku yongs rdzogs je gsal je gsal 'gro ba zhig 'dug pa la/ zhabs 'bring pa zhig gis mnal sad byung pas shin tu phangs pa zhig byung gsungs shing /

yang rje nyid dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa'i gsung bsnyen la bzhugs pa'i dus shig gi tshe/ da lta zhing skyong mar grags pa'i hor sil khyad par can 'di nangs par phyag tu 'byor rgyu'i
do nub mnal lam du/ mi smug tshon pa zhig gis ras kyis gril ba'i sil snyan zhig rgyab la khyer nas shar phyogs nas byung ba'i rjes su/ mi skya bshar ba zhwa thebs gyon
pa mang po dang / ban chung mang po lung pa khengs pa tsam slebs byung pas/ de ma thag a tsa ra nag po 'jigs su rung ba gnyis glo bur du byung nas/ sngar gyi mi skya
bshar ba dang ban chung thams cad khong gnyis kyis lung pa ma brgal gyi bar du phyir bskrad de/ de'i mod la mi smug tshon pa de drung du slebs pa dang mnyam du mnal sad byung
ba na/ ci yin snyam du dgongs pa'i tshe/ de'i nyin mo hor sil 'di mnal lam du byung ba bzhin ras 'gril dang bcas nas zhabs drung du 'byor byung ba'i tshe/ nyid kyi gsung

las/ sil snyan khyad par can 'di chos skyong zhal bzhi pa rang gis bkug par 'dug cing / 'di la rjes 'brangs shig yod 'dug kyang chos skyong rang gis ring du bskrad nas/ da
cha skyon yong ba med pas/ hor sil 'di'i ming la yang zhing skyong mar thogs shig gsungs pa bzhin da lta'i bar du yongs su grags pa 'di yin la/ de lta bu ni zhing skyong
dbang pos mthun rkyen dngos su bsgrubs pas ngo mtshar ba'i rnam thar du shes par bya zhing / yang zhal bzhi yongs rdzogs kyi bris sku 'ga' zhig phyag bris mdzad pa'i tshe
yang / skyed lhas kyi sgrub sde'i khrod na rje nyid bzhugs 'dug pa la/ sgrub khang zhig gi nang na a tsa ra gdong pa dmar nyag can 'jigs su rung ba du ma 'dug pa dang /
g.yag rgod nag pos lung pa gang ba sogs mnal lam ya mtshan can mang du byung gsungs pa yang / chos skyong nyid shin tu 'go zhing mnyes pa'i rtags su mngon zhing / yang nyid
kyi rigs sras sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' dbang rgyal gyis gsol

ba btab pa'i ngor/ pu tra chen po'i sku rkyang pa bzhugs pa'i bris thang khyad par can 'di phyag bris mdzad pa'i mnal lam du a tsa ra pho mo gsum byung ba'i gral 'go ma de
shin tu dga' ba'i rnam 'gyur ston pa la/ gzhan gnyis po de cung zad khros pa'i tshul gyis 'dug pa la/ de'i nangs par/ rje nyid kyi gsung las/ nged la mdang nub rmi lam 'di
bzhin byung ba/ bris thang 'di la pu tra ming sring gsum ga ma bris pa'i lan par 'dug ces gsungs shing / 'di yang 'phral la 'khu ldog ltar snang yang / don la chos skyong
'go zhing 'ches pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i rtags su shes par byas shing / gzhan yang ngos cag rnams kyis gsol ba btab nas gur gyi mgon po lha brgyad kyi bris thang khyad
par can rnams phyag bris mdzad pa'i dus su/ bris sku rnams kyi sku skyed man tsam grub nas zhag 'ga' thugs brel

gyi dbang gis 'gyangs pa'i tshe/ rje nyid kyi mtshan lam du bya nag khyi nag sogs ro stod yan chad med pa mang po sku mdun du phung phung byung ba na/ de'i nangs par gsung
las/ nged kyi rmi lam de bris sku myur du 'bri dgos pa'i rtags su 'dug gsungs nas thugs rtsol chen pos phyag bris legs par mdzad nas rab gnas dang bskang gso rgyas par mdzad
pa'i dus su yang ngo mtshar ba'i rtags du ma byung ba yin la/ yang skabs shig karma zhwa dmar ba'i sprul sku dang / gtsang nas sde ba kun spangs drung mchod yon gdan
sa chen po'i gnas mjal la byon dus/ nang so pu tra khang mjal ba'i tshe/ mgon khang gi nang du yon mchod gnyis 'byor 'phral/ pu tra chen po gnas pa'i zangs chen khrag mtsho
ma bkra shis 'od 'bar gyi nang gi chab rnams/ de dus dgun yin pas chu 'khyags chen por song ba de tsheg sgra dang bcas gas te/ phan tshun du

'khor ba'i mod la zangs mo che'i phyi rol gyi ru long rnams kyang khrog sgra 'byin pa byung bas/ mchod yon kun thugs ha las te phyir 'gros kyis mgon khang gi phyir byon par
gyur cing / de nyid kho na la karma pa'i sgar ba dmangs dang / sa skya'i skya ser tshan gcig 'khrugs rtsod che ba byung bas/ sa kar grub mtha'i rten 'brel dbang las/ chos
skyong gi 'tshub 'gyur yin par sde pa kun spangs pas rig nas/ de dus yab rje mthu stobs kyi mnga' bdag nyid lha chen rig 'dzin pho brang na sku mtshams bcad rgya dam po
la bzhugs yod par sde pa rang la zhal mjal byin rlabs bka' bsgo gnang dgos pa'i gsol ba nan chen btab pa bzhin/ sngags 'chang nyid kyis kyang thugs brtse ba chen pos rjes
su bzung ste/ sde pa nyid bka' srung gi 'khu ldog gis 'jigs pa las skyobs par mdzad pa'i gtang rag tu ko cag gi chos gzhis rgya dpang

che ba 'di rnams kun spangs drung rang gis 'di phyi'i don kho na la bsams nas dpal sa skya'i sde bstan pa gdung rgyud dang bcas pa'i zhabs 'degs su dmigs nas dge rgyun gyi
thebs su gnas 'jags zhus pa yin gsungs nas/ gong nas gnang rten gang yang ma zhus par dad 'bul kho na mdzad 'dug pa/ 'di'ang dam can mon bu pu tras 'phrin las mngon sum du
bsgrubs pa'i dge mtshan las gzhan du ma 'das pa'i shin tu ngo mtshar ba'i gnas so/ /gzhan yang zhing skyong dur khrod bdag po dang / dpal ldan dmag zor rgyal mos kyang
zhal dngos su bstan pa'i lo rgyus yod mod kyang yi ges 'jigs nas ma spros la/ yang gdan sa 'dir bar skabs shig tu skye bo mi bsrun pa dag gis bsam sbyor ngan pa'i 'khrul
'khor la brten nas lo dgra sad ser ba sogs dus rgyun du byung ba'i tshe/ slob 'bangs rnams kyis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor bdag nyid chen pos bla ma gong ma rnams kyis lo dgra'i
gnyen

por bzhengs par mdzad pa'i rigs gsum mgon po'i mchod rten la nyams gso mdzad par bzhed de/ rje nyid dpon slob rnams kyi rim pas phyag phebs te/ rigs gsum gyi mchod rten rnying
pa'i zhig ro'i rmang gang na yod 'tshol bar mdzad pa'i tshe/ sku 'khor ba rnams kyis yun ring du ma rnyed pa la/ dar tsam zhig nas bya rog cig skad snyan po sgrog bzhin
pa dang bcas/ da lta mchod rten yod pa'i gdong nag gi ri chung 'di'i khar babs nas/ brag la mchu yang yang 'dzug shing skad du ma sgrog gin 'dug pa la/ bdag nyid chen
po'i gsung gis bla ma gong ma rnams kyis lo dgra'i kha gnon du 'debs par mdzad pa'i rigs gsum mchod rten gyi thes ro bya rog babs sa ya gi na yod par 'dug pas/ rang re rnams
myur du 'gro ba yin gsungs phyag phebs pa'i tshe/ ji ltar bka' stsal pa bzhin sngar gyi bya rog babs pa'i shul na mchod rten gsum gyi bum

ldir yan zhig pa'i bang rim dang / seng khri man gyi rtsig pa shin tu gsal ba 'dug pa mthong ba'i tshe/ zhabs 'bring pa kun ha las par gyur cing / de nas sa yul der da lta'i
rigs gsum mgon po'i mchod rten 'di legs par bzhengs nas phyag nas bkra shis mnga' gsol mdzad pa nas bzung / da lta'i bar du phyogs de nyid nas ser ba sogs kyi rgyun 'byung
ba gtan med du gyur pa ni gdan sar gnas pa'i skye bo kun gyi blo yul du gsal ba 'di yin no/ /de lta bu'i 'gran zla dang bral ba'i yongs 'dzin dam pa 'di nyid la/ bdud
kyis gnas mal snying la bcas pa'i gang zag 'ga' zhig gis log sgrub brtsams pa de'i tshe sa skya pa'i bstan srung dbang po rnams kyis mngon sum du tshar bcad pa'i tshul ni/
de yang skabs shig gi tshe bstan pa dang rnal 'byor ba la do bsdo ba'i gsang ba'i dgra bo stobs ldan zhig gis log sgrub chen po sgrub par nye ba na/ bdag nyid chen pos
chos skyong rnams la

'phrin bcol drag tu mdzad pa'i tshe/ rje nyid kyi gzim chung gi gtor khang gi mdun gyi spyan gzigs kyi rgya ral 'khyog po zhig la khrag rlon pa mngon sum du 'dzag pa byung
ba dang bstun/ nyid kyi mtshan lam du bande zhig gis rgyu ma glo snying sogs nang g.yos tshan gcig khur byung ba bzhes pas/ nangs par yang sku khams log pa'i rnam pa byung
ba chos skyong gis sha skal byin par 'dug gsungs shing / de dag dang dus mtshungs par mig mthong mkhan zhig gi mig lam du/ bstan dgra dmigs yul gyi mi de nyid kyi phung
po khyogs la bteg nas mgon po'i las mkhan rnams kyis khyer byung ba rmis pa na/ de nas zhag 'ga' ma lon par stobs ldan gyi bstan dgra de nyid tshe'i dus byas nas log sgrub
mtha' dag rang zhir gyur pa yin no/ /gzhan yang 'di 'dra ba'i rigs can 'ga' zhig yod mod kyang brjod pa'i skabs ma yin pa'i phyir re zhig bzhag go /yang bdag

cag gi bla ma dus gsum sgrib med du gzigs pa'i rgyal ba mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan zhes mtshan yongs su grags pa'i rdo rje 'chang mi'i sku gzugs can de nyid la
rdo rje'i chos skyong ye shes kyi spyan ldan rnams kyis zhal mngon sum du bstan nas bka' las cung zad kyang mi 'da' zhing 'phrin las mtha' yas pa bsgrubs pa'i tshul ni/
de yang rje 'di dgung lo bdun cu rtsa gnyis su phebs pa glang gi lo kho bo cag zhabs drung du sleb rgyu'i snga char dge slong byams pa dpal dang / rje dbon sangs dar sogs
drung na gnas pa rnams la rje'i gsung las/ de ring gza' skar bzang ngan ci yod kyang de la ltos pa med/ mdang nub bla brang 'dir nged rang sa skya zhabs drung dang mjal
zhing / bzhin ras dang dbyibs tshul 'di ltar 'dug ces dngos su gzigs pa ltar sgra ji bzhin du gsungs pa ni/ kho bo cag rje nyid kyis 'od gsal gyi ngang nas gzigs par gdon
mi za bar 'dug cing / lhag par bla brang

gzim chung gi bla ma rabs rim gyi gzim mal 'di na gur gyi mgon po 'khor bcas kyang sngar las gzi brjid bkrag mdangs che zhing na bza' sogs kyang zab pa byas byon 'dug ces gsungs
shing dgyes dgyes du ma mdzad kyin 'dug ces thos la/ de ltar bkod ma thag pa'i gsung gi tshig rigs la dpags na de gong nas kyang bstan srung rgya mtsho'i tshogs 'khor
dang bcas pa mngon sum du yang yang gzigs pa la the tshom mi dgos par snang zhing / yang bsam gtan phur bzhugs pa'i skabs shig na dpal dur khrod kyi bdag po yab yum sku
tshad shin tu che bas zil dang bcas gzim phug gi mdo der 'cham stabs du ma mdzad pa zhig kyang dngos su gzigs par grags shing / yang lan cig sku mdun na a tsa ra mang po
bro byed kyin 'dug gsungs/ de gang lags zhus pas/ nai gu'i chos skyong rnams yin par 'dug gsungs shing / gzhan yang rje nyid dpal

sa skyar phebs pa'i skabs der sgo rum nang so sogs bstan srung mngon sum du bzhugs pa'i gnas rnams mjal bar phebs pa'i tshe na'ang rtags ngo mtshar can du ma byung ba yin zhing
/ lhag par kha'u brag rdzong du phebs nas nyi ma gsum gyi bar la mchod gtor rgya chen po mdzad pas/ de'i nyi ma dang po'i nyin gtor tshogs kyi steng gi nam mkha' la
ral gri me 'bar ba zhig 'dug pa mngon sum du gzigs shing / nyi ma bar ma'i nyin 'phags pa brag phug na thugs dam la bzhugs dus bar snang la bram ze dkar po zhig phar 'gro
tshur 'gro byed pa mngon sum du gzigs gsungs shing / chos skyong bram ze'i gzugs can nyid mngon sum du gzigs pa'i skabs der/ gzhan yang gzigs snang khyad par can du ma byung
bar mngon la/ de ltar zhing skyong dregs pa'i gtso bo gdong bzhi mthu rtsal can 'di ni/ rje nyid la sa skya pa'i chos skyong gzhan rnams las kyang lhag par 'go ba yin
te/ phyi

nang gsang ba'i bstan dgra bdud sprul 'ga' zhig gis rje'i thugs rgyud dkrugs tshe/ gsung shugs chen po dang bcas dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa dam nyams bstan dgra 'di zhes bya ba
zhal du bzhes shig ces gsungs shing phyag phreng brdabs pa sogs mdzad pa na/ dmigs yul de la lo zla ma 'gyang par rtags byung ba myong bas grub cing yongs la grags pa yin
la/ yang skabs 'gar rje nyid dang thugs yid gcig tu 'dres pa'i slob bu 'ga' zhig 'das pa na yang / dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa nga'i mi chung re re gnyis bdag gnyer yang mi
yong ba zhes gsung shugs chen pos chos skyong nyid la bka' bkyon pa'i tshul du ma mdzad pa drung na gnas pa rnams las thos so/ /mdor na rdo rje nag po chen po zhal bzhi pa
'di nyid bdag gi bla ma 'di dang mi dang mi lab pa'i tshul gyis bran bzhin du 'khor ba'i rnam par thar ba mang du yod kyang 'dir chos skyong gnyan pas 'bri bar ma nus so/
/

gzhan yang chos skyong rnams kyi rnam sprul du mas zhal bstan cing lung bstan brnyes pa'i tshul ni/ rje nyid mus rdzong dga' ldan rtser zab rgyas dam pa'i chos kyi dga' ston
du ma stsol zhing bstan pa dang sems can gyi don 'phel rgyas su mdzad pa'i ngang du bzhugs pa'i skabs shig na/ tho rangs shig rje nyid kyi mnal lam du spras pa ring mo
nam mkha'i mthong la ye re ba zhig la mi nag po 'jigs su rung ba gcig 'dzegs song nas/ rje nyid la nga'i rjes la shog zer byung pa la/ spras pa 'di la ma thar pa yong ngam
snyam thugs bag tsha ba tsam 'dug pa la de ma thag ban chung dril chung g.yer kha mang po btags pa zhig byung nas spras pa de la yar rgyug mar rgyug mang du byas/ 'di tsam
la mi thar pa yar song zer phul byung bas/ rje nyid kyis spras pa de la 'dzegs byon pas/ spras 'gor sngar gyi mi nag po des phyag 'dren btang byung ba sogs rmis mtshams
mnal sad byung ba na/ zhabs drung na gnas

pa kun la nged la rmi lam 'di bzhin byung zhes snga bar gsungs pa'i phyi dro'i cha la bab pa tsam na/ bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal sa skya'i chos grwa chen po nas sprul sku mgon
po tshe dbang dpon g.yog rnams/ dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos thugs dam dang bcas gsang sngags bde chen gling gi
mkhan por rje nyid spyan 'dren la rdzong bar mdzad pa rnams 'byor byung bas/ rje'i gsung gis/ spyir dgon pa'i 'dzin skyong dang / chen po'i mchod gnas sogs blo la gtan nas
med kyang da lam ni phyin na legs pa 'dug ste/ mdangs nub rmi lam du byung ba'i mi nag po de gur gyi mgon po yin tshod du 'dug la ban chung de zhal bzhi pa'i sprul par
'dug gsungs shing / 'di lta bu sa skya pa'i chos skyong gi gtso bo chen po gnyis kyang bdag cag gi bla ma 'di la gus 'dud kyi sgo nas spyan 'dren gyi pho nyar byon pa'i mtshan
ma yang dag

'dug pas shin tu ngo mtshar ba'i gnas su snang zhing / gzhan yang bstan srung dbang po rnams bka' las mi 'da' bar bran bzhin du khol ba'i tshul ni/ rje nyid gling dga' bde
ba can gyi gdan sar phebs nas ha cang yun mi ring ba zhig na zab don nai gu chos drug gi khrid gnang ba'i tshe/ de'i tshogs 'khor gyi yo byad la dgos pa'i sha sogs spus dkon
pa tsam byung ba la/ skabs der 'brog gzhon zhig gis sha stobs che ba rje nyid la phul bas/ shin tu dgyes shing khrid zhu ba rnams la'ang tshogs 'khor rgya chen po mdzad
ces thos la/ de nas 'brog pa de log phyin pa'i gdong du ru tsho mi gcig pa'i ngan pa 'ga' zhig gis bcom nas/ slar 'brog pa de rje'i zhabs drung du log byung nas smre sngags
du ma zhu yin 'dug pa la/ rje nyid thugs khros te gsung shugs chen pos chos skyong rnams kyi mtshan nas brjod cing / nga'i yon bdag 'di la gang min byed mkhan de tsho
la rtags dang mtshan ma da lta nyid du ston cig ces gsungs shing

phyag phreng brdabs pa mdzad byung bas/ zhabs drung na gnas pa rnams kyang 'jigs shing skrag nas skad mi thon pa tsam byung zhes thos la/ de nas yun ring ma lon par sngar gyi
chom po rnams gnas pa'i thod kyi brag don med du zhig nas phyugs ma rnams 'ur zhing sbra 'gyel ba dang / chom po byed mi la brag chen po zhig phog ste rtags mtshan drag
po mngon sum du byung zhes grags la/ yang gling dgar mus stong dpon dang dbon po kun dga' lhun grub sogs mched grogs 'ga' zhig la dpal sa skya pa'i chos skyong gi man ngag
phyi srung 'khor brag rdzong ma zhal shes dang bcas pa gnang dus ljang lung la sa lo thams cad mkhyen pas drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog gnang bas bran bdud pho mo'i gtor chog
gi thad du slebs pa dang rlung 'tshub chen po zhig langs ste bla brang yom yom byed pa tsam byung bas/ rje 'di nyid lta stangs kyi ngang la cung zad kyang mi g.yo bar
bzhugs 'dug pas/ de ma thag rlung zhi song ba

dang / rje 'di nyid rlung drag po gsum 'bud pa gnang rjes rje'i gsung las/ bran bdud 'di la rjes gnang zhig dgos pas/ de ma byas par 'di'i lung byas pas kho ma dga' zer ba
yin pa 'dug gsungs byung bas/ mus stong dpon sogs sku gzhogs na yod pa thams cad la mthun par lus zi bun byed pa byung zhes khong rang rnams las dngos su thos pas/ 'di ni
las kyi gshin rje nag po yab yum gyi gdug rtsub kyi cho 'phrul rje 'di'i ting nge 'dzin gyi zil gyis mnan nas bran du bkol ba la the tshom mi dgos par mngon zhing / yang
skabs shig gling dga' bla brang du rje dpon slob rnams mi bzhugs pa'i skabs shig na ngan pa zhig gis rkun ma tshabs chen byas pa la/ rje 'di shin tu thugs khros pa'i tshul
gyis chos skyong mthu rtsal can rnams kyi mtshan nas brjod cing / rkun ma ngan pa de da lta nyid du rtsad chod cig ces gsung shugs chen pos gsungs shing phyag brdabs pa
sogs mdzad

byung ba na de mtshams bla brangs kyi tshom gyi mthong gar bya rog gcig babs byung ba la/ khyod kyang chos skyong gi sprul pa zhig yin yong / rkun ma ngan pa'i rjes la rgyugs
shig ces gsung gin 'dug ces thos la/ de 'phral rje dbon zhabs drung na gnas pa rnams kyis rta bzang po dang bcas phyogs bzhir kha bkram nas btsal bas rkun ma de rta mo
shar gyi grog phug tu slebs pa na/ kho rang gi bsam pa la da nga do nub mtshan 'gros byas thag ring po zhig tu sleb pa 'gro snyam pa'i tshe/ glo bur du bya rog gcig byung
nas phyogs gang la phyin kyang gshog lcag kho na brgyab byung pas/ 'dir sdod zer ba yin nam snyam bsdad pas/ nam langs mtshams rje dbon rnams der slebs nas dngos po thams
cad gyar med du phyag tu 'byor 'dug pa 'di lta bu'i mthu rtsal ni sngon gyi rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras gong ma rnams dang sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po

yab sras sogs skyes bu dam pa 'ga' zhig la byung bar grags kyi/ gzhan tshe gang drag sngags kho na 'dren pa la nan tan du byas pa'i mthu rtsal chen por rlom zhing grags pa
phal cher la 'di lta bu byung ba mthong ba'am thos pa med/ yang snga gong gi dus shig rje nyid kyis/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho'i bka' bzhin thub bstan du rje byams
pa rab brtan pa'i drung du mgon po'i chos skor rnams gsan par phebs dus bar lam kun la chos skyong gi sprul pa bya nag gnyis kyis skyel bsu kho na byed pa yang byung zhes
thos la/ yang dus der chom po 'ga' zhig rje dpon slob rnams bsgugs sdod byas pa mkhyen nas/ rje 'di chos skyong la gtor 'bul 'phrin bcol mdzad nas byon pas/ chom po rnams
grog gting du bza' btung bya ba'i bar la rje dpon slob rnams nyes med du phebs pas phyis rje'i gsung gis/ nged la'ang gtor 'bul tsam byas pas/ chom po'i 'jigs pa las
dngos su

bskyabs pa sogs chos skyong 'di rnams byin rlabs dang mthu rtsal gzhan las mchog tu che ba yin no/ /zhes bstod bkur bsngags gsum du ma mdzad pa yin la/ gzhan yang bsam gtan
phur bzhugs pa'i dus shig chos skyong gi sprul pa a tsa ra'i cha lugs can 'ga' zhig bro byed pa mngon sum du gzigs nas/ rje nyid kyang thugs nyams 'ur te de rnams dang lhan
cig tu bro mdzad nas gzim phug tu byon te/ da res kyi chos skyong gi sprul pa de rnams e 'dug gzigs pas/ de nas kyang gzim phug gi 'gag de ka na 'dug ces gsungs shing
/ de rnams ye shes kyi mgon po phyag drug pa'i 'khor du 'dug gsungs la/ yang gsung las/ nged la lung bstan phal cher ye shes kyi mgon po 'dis byed kyin 'dug ces kyang dad
ldan gyi bu slob 'ga' zhig la gsungs pa las brgyud de thos so/ /tshul 'di ni rje bla ma 'di zab lam nai gu chos drug gi

yang nyams rtogs kyi mnga' bdag chen por bzhugs pas na/ de'i chos skyong gis 'phrin las bsgrubs pa'i mtshan mar snang la/ gzhan yang chos skyong rnams la bka' bsgo mdzad pa'i
nus pas 'byung po gdug pa can gnas spar ba'i tshul ni/ gdan sa chen por phebs pa'i skabs shig yab rje chos kyi rgyal po'i gsol dpon zhig la rkang pa na ba'i rkyen gyis
mkhas btsun bzang gsum sus kyang 'dul bar ma nus pa'i jo bo shar par grags pa'i stobs ldan gyi 'byung po de gnod pas shin tu nyen par gyur pa na/ sngags 'chang grags pa'i
mtshan can gyi gsung gis/ khyed rang rje mus pa 'di la gegs sel byin rlabs shig zhus na legs par 'dug pa'i lung bstan stsal par brten/ gsol dpon ma bu gnyis rje 'di'i drung
du byung ba'i tshe gdon gyi skyon yin pa mkhyen nas/ bla ma brgyud pa'i byin rlabs shig mdzad pa'i kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma zhes mtshan brjod pas/ ma chen nad pa de
dran

med du brgyal nas 'gyel song bas/ ma des shi song zer nas ngu yin 'dug pa la/ rje 'dis yon chab kyi chu zhig gdong la 'thor ba mdzad pas/ kho langs byung nas mchi ma gtong
zhing / nga mgo na nas ding sang bar dran pas ma zin 'dug da lta gang byas pa yin zer nas smre sngags du ma 'don zhing 'dug go zhes kun la grags so/ /skabs der rje 'dis phyag
mdud cig gnang nas/ da nad kyis gcig kyang skyon pa mi yong zhes lung bstan gnang bas/ de bzhin du nad las grol ba kun gyi mngon sum du gyur cing / de nas rje 'dis lan
cig mus su phebs nas/ slar gdan sar phebs skabs sngar nas rje nyid la shin tu mos pa'i gdan sa chen po'i chos las pa chos rje kun dga' rnam rgyal du grags pa de der skabs
kyang rje 'di la yang yang mjal du byung ba la/ chos rje khong sngar bas sku mdangs dang gsung dpang dma' ba sogs 'o brgyal nyams che ba

zhig 'dug pa la/ rje'i gsung gis/ chos rje las chen pa khyed da lam sngar las sku mdangs sogs lod pa 'dug pa snyung ba sogs ma byung ngam gsungs pas/ chos rje khong shin tu
ngo nag po'i rnam pas/ bdag na ba bzhin ma byung na'ang / bdag tsho la mthun rkyen sgrub pa'i pho lha zhig yod pa/ na ning bdag chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi ma chen la rje
rin po ches byin rlabs gnang bas/ skabs der ma chen dran med du brgyal 'dug pa de dus bdag tsho'i lha de tshe 'phos nas/ bdag tsho'i nye 'brel rnams dang gdul bya'i rgyun
sogs cung lod du song ba yin lags zhes zhus song ngo / /zhes rje'i zhabs drung du yun ring bsdad pa brdzun mi zer ba dag gi ngag las thos so/ /de ltar rje btsun mthu stobs
kyi dbang phyug 'dis gnas spor ma mdzad pa'i sngon du jo bo shar par grags pa'i 'byung po 'di gdug rtsub shin tu che bas/ gdan sa chen po'i skye bo drag zhan phal cher
gyis sku rten 'dzugs pa dang / mchod

'phrin sogs la 'bad dgos pa yin na'ang / deng sang ming tsam yang mi grags pa 'di ni shin tu yid ches shing ngo mtshar ba'i gnas rmad du byung ba yin no/ /chos las pa der 'byung
po 'dis mthun rkyen bsgrubs pa'i rgyu mtshan ni/ chos rje de'i yab ri khrod 'grims pa'i rnal 'byor pa zhig yin pa la/ lan gcig sa skya'i phu'i ri ldebs shig la phyin
pas/ mtshan mo'i ring la me 'od khrom khrom yong ba zhig 'dug pa ci yin bsams pa la/ nyin zhig de phyogs phyin pas sngar mthong ma myong ba'i btsun pa zhig dang 'phrad
byung ba/ khyed su yin dris pas/ nged jo bo shar ba zer ba zhig yin/ nged rgyal rtse sku gnyer yon tan can zhig yin pa la/ nged la gzhan gyis phra ma bcug ste sde srid kyi
btsun mo dang gtam cha zhig byung bas/ gong nas bka' bkyon phog pas/ nged kyis rgyal rtse pa'i sde pa rnams la smon lam log pa btab pa'i rkyen

byas 'drer skyes te jo bo shar par grags la/ de nas rgyal rtse pa'i sde pa'i gdung rabs rnams bcad rjes/ sa skyar 'phos nas yong pa yin pas/ da rang re gnyis kha dan byed pas/
nged la 'dir sdod gnas shig bzos rten gsol gyis shig khyod kyi mi rgyud la ngas phan chen po yong zer yal song bas/ khong gis de bzhin byas pas khong rang mi rgyud mi
nor dang bcas pa la phan thogs chen po byung bar grags so/ /dus phyis rje'i gsung gis/ nga'i bsam pa la gdan sa chen por nad pa ma bu la byin rlabs byas dus/ nad pa de dran
med la brgyal dus der sa skya pa'i chos skyong rnams kyi mthu rtsal dang byin rlabs la brten 'dre de tshe'i dus byas 'dug pa snying re rje bsam smon lam gang yong rang
byas zhes gsungs so/ /'di lta bu'i rnam thar la so skye dag yid gnyis skye bar srid kyang / de ltar dgos pa ma yin te/ de yang bsam yas chos skyong chen po sogs ngo bo
sar gnas yin kyang / rnam pa 'jig rten dregs pa'i tshul bzung ba rnams

ma gtogs/ gzhan smon lam log pa sogs kyi mtshams sbyor las byung ba'i 'byung po rnams ni stobs ji ltar che yang rang rang gi 'phen byed rdzogs byed kyi las ji tsam yod pa de
rdzogs pa dang / rkyen dge ba'i bshes gnyen sogs kyi byin rlabs la brten tshe 'phos te mtho ris kyi lus rten sogs su skye ba chos nyid yin pas/ des na jo bo shar par grags
pa de yang / rje 'di'i byin rlabs dang las 'brel smon lam gyi dbang zhig gis skabs der tshe 'phos par sems la/ ci ste der skabs kyi 'byung po de dngos ma yin yang / de'i
'khor du gtogs pa'i gdug pa can 'jig rten ma rungs par byed pa'i stobs ldan gyi 'byung po zhig yin par gdon mi za bas/ gang ltar shin tu ngo mtshar ba'i gnas su shes
par bya zhing / don du na bdag cag gi yongs 'dzin rje btsun mus pa chen po 'di ni/ dus gsum gyi rgyal ba kun gyi spyi gzugs dam pa 'khor 'das brtan g.yo kun gyi bdag por
gdod ma

nas bzhugs pa de'i phyir de nyid kyi ngo mtshar ba'i rnam thar gyi cha shas phyogs re tsam yang bskal brgya'i bar du brjod par ga la nus/ 'on kyang rang gi blo nus dang 'tshams
par spros pa'i rgyas pa'i phyogs rnams shes par 'dod na/ kho bos logs su byas pa'i rje 'di'i rnam par thar pa rnams su blta bar byos shig yang bdag gi 'dren pa rje btsun
dbang phyug rab brtan de nyid kyang / rgyun du thugs dam la shin tu brtson pas nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag tu gyur cing khyad par chos skyong rnams kyis zhal ston
pa dang / las mdzad par gdon mi za ste/ rje nyid sa skyar phebs pa'i tshe yang / gdan sa chen po gzigs pa nas bla brang sgo sper ma phebs kyi bar la dpal mgon bram ze'i
gzugs can sku mdog dkar po/ phyag g.yas na rtse gsum dang / g.yon na thod pa bsnams pa/ sku tshad thog dpang gsum tsam yod pa yum chen bzhi dang bcas pa zhig gar stabs
kyi ling ling 'byon pa spyan lam

du 'bral med du gzigs pa byung zhes rje nyid kyi gsung las dngos su thos pas mtshon te shes la/ gzhan yang rje 'di la gnyan mgon chen po shin tu 'ches pa'i mtshan ma 'ga' zhig
kho bo la yang shar mod kyis 'dir ma spros so/ /yang sprul pa'i sku lo nas spyan snga rin po che kun dga'i mtshan can la yang bka' srung rnams kyis zhal bstan cing 'phrin
las bsgrubs pa'i tshul ni/ rje nyid gdan sa chen por thog mar phebs dus/ bdag cag gis chos skyong gi chos skor rnams gsol ba btab pa'i tshe/ de'i nub mo mnal lam gyi
tshul du sprin nag rab tu 'khrugs pa'i dbus su gur gyi mgon po lha brgyad yongs rdzogs sprul pa'i pho nya rnams dang bcas pa yang yang du gzigs pa zhig byung bas/ nangs
par nyid kyi gsung las/ nged la rmi lam 'di bzhin byung bas gser kha bdag po'i dper 'dug pa bzhin/ da lam mgon po'i chos skor rnams cis kyang

phul bas thus pa 'dug ces zhal bzhes bka' drin bskyangs nas/ thog mar 'di skor gyi dbang dang rjes gnang rnams stsal dus/ phyi'i las mkhan gcer bu zangs gri can gyi rjes gnang
gi skabs/ nam mkha' shin tu dwangs shing gzim khang gi steng du chu pho ba sogs kyi rkyen gang yang med pa la/ rjes gnang gi mchod bshom gyi stegs kyi steng du gdung
mtshams nas brdol ba lta bu'i chu rgyun dri ma med pa bum gang tsam zhig rjes gnang gnang bar la babs byung bas der yod thams cad ngo mtshar du gyur cing / rang gi bsam pa
la rje 'di la chos skyong 'di skor gyi byin rlabs kyi chu rgyun khyad par can zhig bzhugs pa'i ngo mtshar ba'i rtags su 'dug snyam pa byung zhing / yang de dus nang so
pu tra khang du dmigs yul zhig la ched gtad las sbyor gyi sku mtshams zhag 'ga' mdzad pa na/ nub gcig mnal lam gyi tshul du las mkhan chen po nyid 'brog pa khyi ra ba'i tshul
du sprul nas byung ste/ de na re/ dmigs yul la rtags myur du 'byung ba dang / rje nyid rgyal sras thogs med pa'i sku'i skye ba yin tshul/

de'i bla ma rnams kyang zhing 'di dang 'di na bzhugs pa'i lo rgyus sogs dang / gzhan yang lung bstan ngo mtshar can mang du brnyes 'dug cing / yang skabs der sgo rum du gur
gyi mgon po lha lnga'i dbang bzhi yongs rdzogs sindhu ra'i dkyil 'khor la brten pa thun mong ma yin pa de gnang ba'i tshe/ gtor dbang bka' bsgo mdzad pa na/ bse mgon chen
po'i phyag g.yas pa dang / kho bo'i lag pa sbrel gsungs nas de bzhin du byas pa la/ rje nyid bskyed rim shin tu gsal ba'i ngang nas spyan gnyis nyi zla lta bu'i mig gis
'cham mgon dang bdag cag la yang yang gzigs shing / bstan par dgongs pa'i thugs bskyed drag po dang bcas gsung shugs mthon pos bla ma brgyud pa lugs srol mang po'i mtshan
nas brjod cing bka' bsgo drag tu

mdzad byung pas/ de'i byin rlabs kyi zil gyis rang gi lus skyi phung byed pa dang / sems la dga' bde khyad par can skyes shing / 'di lta bu'i snang tshul ni rang yang skal
ba bzang ba dang bla ma 'di yang sprul pa'i sku yin pa la the tshom mi dgos pa 'dug snyam pa'i bcos min gyi dad pa dung dung skye ba zhig byung zhing / yang dus der lha khang
rtse'i gsang ba'i mgon khang khyad par can de'i gnyan mgon bram ze'i gzugs can gyi sku brnyan 'bur sku'i drung du mchod bshams mdzad nas/ zhal bzhi pa bsgrub dus kyi
rjes gnang rgyas pa dang / bram ze'i sngags gtad gnang ba'i tshe/ cung zad rtsub 'gyur che ba dang bcas rtags ya mtshan che ba zhig rmi lam du shar bas blo bde bar byung
zhing / bla ma dang chos skyong la yid ches kyi dad pa thun mong ma yin pa zhig de dus skyes pa yin la/ yang ngos cag gi rnam 'dren dam pa mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa
ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa ni/ nges

pa'i don du lha mchog 'jam pa'i dbyangs sam sa skya pa'i rje btsun gong ma gcig gi ngo bor bzhugs pa gdon mi za yang / gdul bya'i snang ngo tsam du ston par mdzad pa ni gzhi
tshul khrims rnam par dag pa la gnas shing / mkhas grub kyi bla ma du mas rjes su bzung bas gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha mthar son cing / mdo sngags rig gnas kyis bsdus pa'i
shes bya'i yul mtha' dag la bslabs sbyangs mthar phyin pa mdzad pas/ 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gang mdzad kyang thogs med kyi mkhyen rab mnga' bas bstan pa ma lus yongs rdzogs
kyi gsal byed mchog tu gyur cing / rgyun du bsgom sgrub la rtse gcig tu gzhol bas/ so so'i rgyud dang man ngag nas bshad pa'i nyams rtogs thams cad thugs la 'khrungs
pas gzhan gyi gegs sel ba dang / ting nge 'dzin ma skyes pa bskyed pa/ skyes pa bogs 'byin pa sogs la byin rlabs kyi rgyun gzhan las ches che ba mnga'

zhing / che dgu kun gyis zhabs la gtugs kyang / khengs pa dang dregs pa thams cad rgyang ring du spangs te/ kun gyi 'bangs ltar gzhan gyi don la dgyes pa lhur mdzad pa sogs
mdor na sngon gyi skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi ngo mtshar ba'i rnam par thar pa rnams ma tshang pa med pa mnga' ba'i tshul gyis dus ding sang gi gangs ri'i khrod kyi bstan
'dzin kun gyi gtsug rgyan dam par gyur te/ da lta dgung lo bdun cu pa'i steng du phebs pa/ slar yang bskal brgya'i bar du seng ges bteg pa'i 'gyur med rdo rje'i khri la
zhabs zung brtan par bzhugs pa'i dge mtshan thams cad 'bad med lhun grub tu gyur pa'i ngang nas/ bdag cag lha dang bcas pa'i 'dren pa dam par sku lham me/ gsung lhang nge
/ thugs lhan ne ba'i tshul du bzhugs pa'i skyes chen dam pa 'di nyid kyi ngo mtshar ba'i rtogs pa brjod pa rgyas pa ni logs su 'chad par bdag spro la/ 'dir yang sku'i skye
ba dran pa dang / bla ma dang lhag pa'i lha'i zhal gzigs

shing byin gyis brlabs pa/ chos skyong rnams kyis 'phrin las bsgrubs pa sogs cung zad brjod na/ rje 'di sku gzhon nu'i dus thos bsam la bzhugs pa'i skabs shig tshes bco lnga'i
zla ba nya gang ba shar byung ba'i dus der rang gi skye ba snga ma rnams dran pa'i tshul ni/ sngon chos rgyal 'phags pa hor yul nas phebs dus rje nyid dad can gyi gang
zag cig tu gyur nas 'phags pa'i zhabs rjes su 'brangs te/ gdan sa chen po'i grol chu'i lho phyogs kyi grong 'dabs shig tu khyim pa mo zhig dang lhan cig tu bzhugs nas sras
kyang 'ga' byung zhing / de dus kyi thugs dam chos rgyal ma rang la mdzad pa gsal bar dran pa dang / de'i rjes su g.yag mi pham chos kyi bla ma sangs rgyas dpal bas/
sa skya'i dga' ldan du 'chad nyan mdzad pa'i tshe/ rje nyid de'i slob ma'i nang tshan sde snod 'dzin pa chen po bsod nams bzang po zhes bya bar gyur nas/ de dus mkhan chen

g.yag pa khri steng du phebs pa dang / rang nyid chos ra'i phyogs kyang 'di phyogs su bzhugs pa sogs thugs la gsal bar shar zhing / yang de'i rjes su rdo rje 'dzin pa chen
po sbas pa'i rnal 'byor zhig tu sku skye ba bzhes te/ de dus g.yas ru byang gi ldog gi sa cha zhig tu chos rje rdzong pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan la gshed dmar lha lnga'i dbang
gsan te/ dbang gral gyi rnam pa 'di bzhin yod sogs shin tu gsal bar dran pa byung gsungs te/ des mtshon nas sku'i skye ba mang por mkhas grub du ma'i tshul bzung nas
bstan 'gro'i don mtha' yas pa zhig mdzad par gdon mi za zhing / sku tshe 'dir yang chos gsan pa'i rje bla ma rnams la sangs rgyas dngos kyi 'du shes mnga' ba ni/ grub mchog
bsod nams chos 'phel gyi drung du 'jigs byed kyi ra khrid gsan pa'i tshe/ bla ma 'jam dbyangs su bsgoms nas gsol ba btab pas/ gsung rab kyi don la go blo khyad par can
zhig de dus na byung ba yin

gsungs shing / gzhan yang 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen dbang phyug dpal bzang / rje klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ mus chen rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/
rje 'gyur med bde chen/ rtse gdong bdag chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan sogs gtso bor gyur pa'i chos gsan pa'i bla ma thams cad la thugs dad
bcos min 'khrungs pas/ so so'i rnam thar gsung dus phyag thal mo sbyor ba dang / spyan chab g.yo ba sogs mdzad byung pa na/ gzhan rgyud la yang dad pa dbang med du skyes
pa myong bas grub cing / lhag par mus chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho la nged kyi rtsa ba'i bla ma yin gsungs nas thugs dad lhag par che bas/ rje de nyid kyi
sku 'dra phyag nas ma zhig kyang 'bral spangs du mdzad cing / rang gzhan gyi don gal che ba kun la yang rje mus chen kho na la

gsol ba rtse gcig tu btab nas lung bstan zhu ba mdzad de/ gang byung ba de bka' stsal pas kun la bslu med kyi gdeng khel kho na 'byung ba zhig yod 'dug cing / ding sang gi
dus 'dir bstan 'dzin kun gyi bla na bzhugs shing 'phrin las kyis phyogs med khyab pa 'di yang / mus chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs de nyid kyi byin rlabs thugs rgyud la 'phos pa'i
dge mtshan las byung bar nges te sngon rje 'di sku gzhon nu'i dus yangs pa can du bzhugs skabs/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho gnas der byon pa'i dus thams cad du zhabs drung
du yang yang byon gsungs nas/ phye mar rdag bcang ma phyag spar do gsum re dang rje de nyid rang gi gsol ba bzhes 'phro rnams rgyun par gnang nas/ 'di rnams gzhan la ma
ster bar rdzogs par zo gsungs pa'i bka' phebs rgyun du gnang ba zhig yod 'dug pa dang / chos ra dang phebs lam sogs gang du mjal yang / rje mus chen nyid spyan

cung zhig mi gsal ba'i tshul gyis/ pha gi de mdar pa 'tsho byed kyi bu yin 'dug gam gsungs shing mjal res bzhin dgyes dgyes kho na mdzad pa zhig yod gsungs pas/ des na rje
'di ma 'ongs ba'i dus su sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i gsal byed dam pa skye 'gro kun gyi rtsa lag mchog tu 'gyur ba la dgongs nas/ mus chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs de nyid kyi thugs
rje'i spyan ras kyis bu gcig pa ltar 'tsho zhing byin gyis brlabs par mdzad pa la the tshom dang yid gnyis mi dgos pa yin zhing / bla ma dang lhas zhal bstan tshul ni/ rje
nyid 'jigs byed kyi gsung bsnyen zhig la bzhugs skabs/ lan cig sku mdun gyi nam mkhar de'i dkyil 'khor yongs su rdzogs pa gsal la dwangs pa zhig yun ring du gzigs shing
/ de dang dus nye bar rje nyid sa skya'i mchod zhing bya khra ma na 'khor mang po dang bcas bzhugs 'dug pa la/ de'i lho phyogs kyi nam mkhar rje sa skya pa chen

po'i sku/ tshad thog dpang gcig tsam byas pa/ zhal shar phyogs su gzigs pa'i sku mdun du ting bdun cha che ba zhig yon chab dwangs mas bkang nas 'dzin mkhan sogs med pa bar
snang de kar bgrengs tshar du 'dug pa gzigs pas/ thugs dad lhag par g.yos nas gsol ba drag tu btab pa'i mnal lam shin tu gsal ba byung gsungs pa ni/ rje sa skya pa chen
pos rjes su bzung ba'i mtshan mar snang zhing / yang sa skyar phebs pa snga ma zhig la kho bos 'dod chos 'dra gsol ba btab pas/ re zhig zur khang gi rje btsun gyi sku 'dra
mdze thod ma'i drung du chos rnams ma dang / zhabs skor 'bum ther mdzad dgos pa 'dug gsungs nas de bzhin gnang bas/ nyin gcig gi mnal dang 'od gsal 'dres pa'i gzigs snang
la/ rje btsun gyi sku'i 'gram nas bud med cig dang / sngags pa 'dra ba'i khye'u gos dkar gyon pa zhig byung nas/ rje nyid kyi sku la phyag gis reg byung bas/

de ma thag thugs rgyud la bde chen gyi ye shes khyad par can 'khrungs pa snyam byed pa byung gsungs pa ni/ gsal bar ma gsungs pa ma gtogs/ don la dus der rje btsun gyi sku
de rje btsun dngos dang / de'i thugs ka nas sprul ba'i ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor gsal bar gzigs nas/ de'i gtso bo yab yum gyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i mod la/ thugs rgyud la
dbang gi ye shes khyad par can 'khrungs nges pa'i gsung du 'dug snyam pa kho bo la shar zhing / yang lan cig rje nyid kyi mnal lam du ri mthon po zhig la 'dzegs byon pas/
de'i rtse na brag phug chen po zhig 'dug par phebs pa na/ brag de la zhabs rjes gsal po gnyis 'dug pas/ sus yin gsungs pas/ mi zhig nas chos rgyal 'phags pa'i yin zhu ba
la/ de ma thag zhabs rjes las chu bo chen po brdol te rgya je cher song ba la/ rje nyid kyis thugs dad pa chen po dang bcas chu de nas zhal du gsol ba dang / sku khrus mdzad

pa sogs kyi snang ba byung gsungs ba ni/ chos rgyal 'phags pa rje 'di sku'i skye ba mang po'i bla mar 'dug pas thugs rjes 'bral med du skyong ba'i mtshan mar gsal zhing / mkha'
'gro chos skyong rnams kyis 'phrin las bsgrub pa'i tshul yang / sa skyar phebs res bzhin sgo rum sogs mgon khang rnams su ched gtad byon nas bstan pa rgyas pa/ bstan
'dzin sku tshe brtan pa/ 'jig rten bde ba sogs kyi 'phrin las bcol ba dang bcas thugs dam bskang gso rgyas par gnang ba zhig 'dug pas/ lan cig de rnams gnang nas yun ring
ma lon pa'i dus shig na/ sa skya pa'i bstan pa la log sgrub byed pa'i stobs ldan ma rungs pa zhig bstan srung rnams kyis tshar bcad pa'i tshul mnal lam du gsal bar shar
'dug pa dang / yang lan cig nang so pu tra khang du thugs dam mdzad pa'i nub las mkhan chen po nyid bande snum bag can zhig gi tshul du byung nas/ byang khog gi rje rang
gi

slob ma zhig la ma 'ongs pa 'byung tshul lung bstan pa bzhin thog tu khel ba byung gsungs shing / yang snga mo'i dus phru ma bsgrub gnas su thugs dam yun ring mdzad dus gnyan
mgon zhal bzhi pa kho bo cag gi yab rje grags pa'i mtshan can de nyid kyi rnam pas/ chu snod chen po chab kyis bkang ba phyag na bsnams nas 'byon pa sogs byung gsungs
pa ni/ rje nyid la zhing skyong chen pos tshe chu'i dngos grub phul bas sku tshe ring ba'i mthar thug pa'i rten 'brel de dus nas 'grig pa'i dge mtshan rmad du byung ba yin
par kho bo sems la/ yang lha sar zhabs skor 'bum ther mdzad dus mnal lam du gser mdog can pa'i mkhan chen shAkya bstan 'dzin pa dang rje nyid lhan cig pas ri mthon po zhig
la 'dzegs byon pa'i mod la/ lung bstan khyad par can zhig brnyes 'dug kyang 'dir bri bar ma nus la/ yang lan cig mnal lam du dpal ldan bla ma dam pa dang mjal ba sogs
ngo

mtshar du ma byung 'dug cing / der ma zad rje bla ma 'di byang chub snying po brnyes kyi bar du byang phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gser mdog can na bzhugs pa'i dpal ldan
grags pa'i zhabs kyis skad cig kyang 'bral ba med par thugs rje'i lcags kyus 'dzin par mdzad pa'i gtan tshigs yang dag pa zhig kho bos rtogs mod kyis/ 'dir ni de tsam mo/
/mdor na yongs 'dzin dam pa 'di nyid la gdul bya'i snang ngo tsam du bstan pa la yang / lung rtogs kyi yon tan gzhal du med pa zhig mnga' bar yid ches mod kyang / rje nyid
yon tan sba ba la gtso bor mdzad pas thugs rgyud la spangs rtogs kyi yon tan gang yang med pa skad mdzad cing thugs sgam pas thugs dam gsal ltas sogs ji ltar byung sus
kyang zhu mi nus shing / zhus kyang gsal po mi gsungs la/ cung zad thor bu gsungs pa rnams la yang gzhan la mi 'chad pa'i dam dog chen po mdzad pa zhig 'dug pas 'dir zhib
tu 'bri bar ma

nus la/ slar rje nyid kyi dgongs pa bkrol nas rnam thar rgyas pa spel ba'i tshe rim gyis gsal bar byed pa sha chags pa lags so/ /'dir smras pa/ 'gro ba kun la dga' bzhi'i lam
bstan nas/ /snying po'i 'bras bu ster mdzad bla chen dang / /bsod nams ye shes rtse mo mthar son zhabs/ /rab snyan grags pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin rnams bsngags/ /lnga rig
mkhas pa'i gtsug rgyan paN chen dang / /byang phyogs chos srid bdag po 'phags pa'i mtshan/ /de dag dbon dang chos rgyud 'dzin pa yi/ /skyes mchog rnams la su zhig dad
mi byed/ /khyad par dus ngan snyigs ma'i mthar thug 'dir/ /bstan pa'i me ro gso la bsam bzhin du/ /byon pa'i sngags 'chang chos rje yab sras kyi/ /bka' drin bsams na lan
brgyar phyag byar 'os/ /de ltar thub dbang rgyal tshab sa skya pa'i/ /chos kyi rgyud pa 'dzin pa'i slob ma

ru/ /ma gyur gangs ri'i khrod 'dir bstan 'dzin du/ /zhal gyis 'ches pa'i gang zag gcig yod min/ /de yang dwags po bka' brgyud par grags pa'i/ /bstan 'dzin gtso bo khams pa
mi gsum gyi/ /nang tshan phag mo grub pa'am mtha' tsa pa/ /khams pa rdor rgyal zhes pa'i mtshan gsum dang / /ldan pa de yis sa skya'i bla chen zhabs/ /bcu gnyis lor bsten
gdams pa phal cher gsan/ /slar yang rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan la/ /gtugs nas gsung gi bdud rtsi mang gsol bas/ /sa skya'i rgyud 'dzin slob ma grags pa can/ /yin zhing
de yi slob brgyud gling ras nas/ /brgyud de gtsang pa rgya ras zhes bya bas/ /'brug tu dgon pa btab pas deng sang dus/ /'brug pa zhes pa'i bka' srol chen po zhig /byung
ba 'di kun sa skya'i slob rgyud du/ /gtogs shing gzhan yang phag gru'i nye gnas che/ /ga zi rin chen dpal gyis stag lung thang / /btab pa nas bzung 'di pa'i srol

'dzin la/ /stag lung thang pa zhes grags de dag kyang / /sa skya pa yi slob mar bsnyon med du/ /grub cing phag gru'i sku tshe'i mjug tsam gyi/ /thugs sras skyu ra rin chen
dpal zhes pas/ /'bri khung thel btab 'bri khung pa zhes pa'i/ /srol chen gcig tu grags shing 'di kun kyang / /dpal ldan sa skya pa yis rje 'jug tu/ /nges pa yin la dus gsum
mkhyen pa'am/ /spre'u chos kyi grags pa zhes kyang bya/ /khams pa dbu se zhes pa'i mtshan gsum dang / /ldan pa'i skyes bu de yis sa chen gyi/ /dngos slob rga lo dang ni
a seng zhabs/ /shan pa rdor seng gsum las lam 'bras sogs/ /sa lugs chos kyi bdud rtsi mang gsol nas/ /gang des smar khams sgang zhes bya ba ru/ /karma lha sdings dgon pa
btab pa nas/ /karma kam tshangs zhes pa'i srol chen po/ /gcig tu grags te 'di dag thams cad kyang / /sa skya pa yi slob rgyun khongs su gtogs/

/gzhan yang grub thob khyung po rnal 'byor ram/ /shang pa du khu ba zhes bya ba des/ /legs par phye ba'i shangs pa bka' brgyud pa/ /zhes grags lugs srol bzang po 'di nyid la/
/rgyud pa rin chen sna bdun byung ba las/ /de yi rgyud pa bzhi pa rmog cog pa/ /rin chen brtson 'grus zhes bya sa chen gyi/ /dngos slob a seng zhabs las sa lugs kyi/ /gdams
pa mang du nos shing de nyid kyi/ /rgyud pa drug par gyur pa gnyan ston che/ /sbas pa'i sangs rgyas zhes byas dpal sa skyar/ /rje btsun grags pa'i zhabs pad lo bcu
