gnyis/ /bsten de rgyud dang man ngag phal cher gsan/ /rgyud pa bdun pa 'gro ba'i mgon po mchog /sangs rgyas ston pas chos rgyal 'phags pa la/ /smin grol zhal gyi bdud rtsi
mang nos pas/ /'di dag kyang ni rje btsun sa skya pa'i/ /slob rgyun yin zhing zhang ston g.yu brag par/ /grags pas sa skya'i bla chen sku dngos kyi/ /slob ma shan pa rdor
seng zhes bya

dang / /a seng zhabs la gtugs nas sa lugs kyi/ /chos skor mang gsan de yi rgyud 'dzin la/ /zhang gi bka' brgyud ces grags 'di rnams kyang / /sa skya'i rgyud 'dzin yin la su
yis bsnyon/ /phyis su byung ba bo dong par grags pa'i/ /rtsa ba gshong ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan zhes/ /chos rgyal 'phags pa'i thugs kyi sras mchog yin/ /de yi gcung po
gshong ston blo brtan dang / /dpang lo chen po blo gros brtan pa'i zhabs/ /de yi dbon po lo chen byang rtse ni/ /dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i dngos slob mchog /yin zhing lo
chen byang rtse'i dbon rgyud ni/ /lo chen grags pa zhes bya de nyid byon/ /de yi dbon po bo dong ka bcu pa/ /chos kyi rgyal mtshan dngos kyi mtshan yin te/ /ston ming phyogs
las rnam rgyal zhes grags pa/ /'di dag kyang ni dpal ldan sa skya pa'i/ /bstan 'dzin dge ba'i bshes gnyen ngo mtshar can/ /kho na yin zhing de yi rgyud

'dzin la/ /bo dong pa zhes grags 'di byung ba lags/ /deng sang dge ldan par grags srol 'di yang / /thog ma'i byung tshul shar phyogs tsong kha pa/ /blo bzang grags pas 'brog
gi ri bo che/ /dge ldan rnam par rgyal ba'i gling btab nas/ /de yi gdan sa dar ma rin chen dang / /gdan sa gnyis pa dge legs dpal bzang ste/ /de ltar gsum las snga ma gnyis
po ni/ /sa skya'i las chen gzhon nu blo gros kyi/ /slob ma rab 'byams smra ba'i bshes gnyen mchog /bdun gyi nang tshan yin zhing phyi ma ni/ /ka bcu legs par shes pa
bcu phrag gcig /byung ba'i nang du gtogs pas 'di kun gyis/ /mdo phyogs mtha' dag dpal ldan sa skya ru/ /legs par btugs shing de bzhin sngags phyogs kyang / /'gro mgon rje
dang de yi thugs kyi sras/ /spyan snga grags pa byang chub la sogs pa las/ /thog mar gsung ngag lam 'bras nas brtsams te/ /sa skya'i rje btsun gdams pa phal

che ba/ /gsan pas deng sang dus na dge lugs zhes/ /'phrin las shin tu che ba'i tsong kha pa/ /blo bzang grags pa brgyud par bcas 'di yang / /mtshungs med sa skya'i rje btsun
mchog rnams kyi/ /gsung la sbyangs pas dge bshes gnas thob cing / /rjes 'brangs yin pa'i rgyu mtshan de ltar lags/ /gzhan yang jo nang kun spangs thugs rje dpal/ /zhes
bya de yis chos rje khu dbon gyi/ /dngos slob nags phug shes rab 'od zer dang / /chos rgyal 'phags pa gnyis kyi slob bu'i mchog /shar pa 'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan
la/ /gtugs nas lam 'bras la sogs sa skya pa'i/ /gdams pa ma lus gsan nas skyes mchog des/ /sa skya'i dgon lag jo nang ri khrod btab/ /de yi dngos slob kun mkhyen dol bu
yis/ /sngon med gzhan stong lta ba'i srol btod pas/ /'di la mkhas mchog rnams kyis mgrin gcig tu/ /khyed

nyid sa skya'i grub mtha'i rjes 'jug tu/ /khas len bzhin du rje btsun gong ma yi/ /gsung dang 'gal ba'i lta ba 'di 'dod pa/ /'thad pa min zhes rtsod ngag mang du bsgrags/ /'on
kyang kun mkhyen de yis gzhan stong gi /lta ba ston byed gsung rab mang brtsams nas/ /sa skyar byon tshe chos rje sa paN gyi/ /na bza' bla gos sku dreg can zhig la/ /mjal
bas dad gus chen pos sku chos de/ /zhal du 'jibs shing gsol ba mang btab pas/ /gzhan stong lta ba la zhen thugs 'gyur te/ /de phyin gong ma'i gsung dang mthun pa yin/
/lta ba rang stong skyong la gus pa zhig /byung ba yin zhes bdag gi bla ma gsungs/ /de ltar kun spangs rje dang dol bu ba/ /gdan sa rim par byon la jo nang par/ /grags
shing dus phyis nag po spyod pa yi/ /rnam sprul dpal ldan kun dga' grol mchog zhabs/ /dngos slob brgyud par bcas rnams sa skya pa'i/ /rgyud 'dzin 'dres med yin par so so
yi/

/rnam thar bltas pas nges shes skye bar 'gyur/ /des na gangs khrod bstan 'dzin thams cad kyis/ /zhabs la gtugs shing dpal ldan sa skya pa/ /'di ni yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i bdag
po zhes/ /snyan grags rgya mtsho'i gos can khyab 'di yang / /skyes chen rnams kyi 'phrin las bstan srung gis/ /bsgrubs las byung bar kho bo nges shes rnyed/ /rnyed pa
de yang blo gros mthu las byung / /byung ba 'di la rjes 'jug skal bzang kun/ /kun kyang yid ches gus pa bskyed par rigs/ /gangs ljongs 'di na yongs 'dzin mang yang kun gyi
skyabs gnas sa skya pa/ /sa skya pa yi bstan 'dzin mang yang snyigs dus 'gran bral sngags 'chang rje/ /sngags 'chang rje yi rjes 'brangs yang yang brgyud pa zin pa kun
dga'i ming / /kun dga'i ming can spyod tshul mang yang kun kyang bstan pa'i bya ba lags/ /gnyis pa de las byung ba'i gdams pa dngos bshad pa la

bzhi ste/ byin rlabs chu bo'i rgyun dang 'dra ba'i bka' ma nub pa/ gdams ngag gser 'gyur gyi rtsi dang 'dra ba'i sarga ma log pa/ bsnyen bkur lha 'dod yon la longs spyod pa
lta bu'i dpal 'byor gyi rgyun ma nyams pa/ mos gus gzhon nu'i dga' ba dang 'dra ba'i bsam pa tshim pa'o/ /dang po la dbang gi bka' ma nub pa dang / rjes gnang gi bka' ma
nub pa gnyis las/ dang po dbang gi bka' ma nub pa ni/ theg chen chos rje dang / rdzong pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan pas lha brgyad ma bcu gnyis ma/ bcu bdun ma sogs la thun
mong du dbang gi cho ga'i yig sna mgon po rnam rol zhes bya ba mdzad cing / phyag len gyi sgo nas kyang dar rgyas su mdzad pa yin la/ ding sang yang dbang de gsum gyi rgyun
dang gzhan yang gri gug lha lnga la dbang gnyis dang bcas pas mgon po'i dkyil 'khor lnga'i dbang rgyun ma nub par yod pa yin no/ /de dag gi khungs kyang gri gug lha lnga
pa

la ni dkyil chog rgya gzhung bram zes mdzad pa yod cing / bcu bdun ma'i dbang ni rgyud dur khrod nag po'i lha bskyed pa'i le'us bcu bdun ma'i dkyil 'khor dang / dbang gi le'us
dbang bstan pa yin la/ lha brgyad ma dang bcu gnyis ma'i dbang la yig sna rje btsun gong mas mdzad pa mi snang zhing / gsan yig sogs na theb ma theb ci rigs pa 'byung
yang / gang ltar dam pas mdzad pa'i bris sku dang / ka pA la'i shog ril las rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po 'di nyid bram ze mchog sred kyi zhal gzigs ltar lha gsum
ma dang / rgya gzhung ltar lha lnga ma'am/ bla ma brag steng pa'i khyad chos lha bcu gnyis ma'am/ bla ma mal lo'i khyad chos lha brgyad ma'am/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang
po'i bzhed pa ltar lcam dral gnyis yum dang bcas pa la gtso bor mdzad pa'i lugs gang yang rung ba gcig gi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi mtha'

rten dang bcas pa thob pa zhes gsungs pas na dbang de dag rtsod bral tshad mas grub pa yin no/ /des na gur gyi mgon po gri gug lha lnga/ mgon po lha brgyad/ lha bcu gnyis ma
rnams kyi dbang thun mong ba rgya gzhung lugs/ rig pa'i dbang lnga/ sku gsung thugs kyi rjes gnang / sngags kyi bzlas lung gtor dbang dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje
'chang / mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur/ slob dpon bram ze mchog sred/ nor bu gling pa bde ba'i rdo rje/ shrA dha kA ra warma/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon
tan tshul khrims/ mal lo tsA ba blo gros grags pa/ rje sa chen/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ bkras lung pa nam mkha'
bsod nams/ dge sding pa chen po/ sangs rgyas dpal/ rin chen gling pa/ bla ma rin chen rdo rje pa/ theg chen

chos kyi rgyal po/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun bzang pa/ brag thog pa dpal 'dzin bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ rig 'dzin kun
dga' rgyal po/ drin can tshe dbang bkra shis/ rje tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ rje bod mkhar ba don grub rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga chos rgya mtsho/ lo nas spyan snga
chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang lha brgyad ma dang bcu gnyis ma'i brgyud pa lugs gcig
ni/ 'phags pa'i rjes su dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ 'gro mgon bsod nams/ nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal/ ye shes dpal bzang / blo bzang dpal
'byor/ chag lo rin chos/ sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa/ rje dkon mchog lhun

grub sogs las brgyud de da lta ma chad pa bzhugs so/ /yang gur gyi mgon po lha lnga ma 'am lha brgyad ma'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa dbang gong ma gsum sindhu
ra dang ting nge 'dzin gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba zhal nas snyan du brgyud pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i dbang gi brgyud rim ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi DA
ki ma/ slob dpon yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ mtsho skyes rdo rje/ indra bhu ti/ phun tshogs byed pa/ nag po spyod pa/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ ga ya dhA ra/ bla chen 'brog mi shAkya
ye shes/ se ston kun rig zhang ston chos 'bar/ sa chen/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ gcung rdo rje 'od
zer/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ rong mi ye shes/ pre bo rdo rje grags/ bag ston gzhon tshul/ bla ma tshul rgyal ba/ bla ma ngag dbang pa/ mkhan

chen dbang phyug seng ge theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun bzang / de man chad gong gi brgyud tshul dang 'dra'o/ /skabs
'dir theg chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i dkyil chog las/ 'di la dbang bzhi rdzogs kyi zin bris gcig 'dug na'ang / kho bos ma thob cing / rgya gzhung ma mthong bas yi
ger bkod ma nus so zhes gsungs pa'i don ni/ bla ma rin chen rdo rje pa la rgya gzhung lugs kyi dbang thun mong ba rnams las ma gsan/ de mtshams su dkyil chog 'di thugs rtsom
gnang / phyis su mkhan chen byang seng ba la snyan brgyud lugs kyi dbang bzhi yongs rdzogs gsan pa yin pas/ rgyus med kyi log rtog mi bya'o/ /don gyi dbang de dag la
dgongs nas/ rje tshar chen gyi mgon po'i dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ snyan brgyud dang po byin rlabs chu bo'i skabs/ /

theg chen chos rje man chad yig cha dang / /phyag len lha brgyad bcu gnyis bcu bdun la/ /dkyil 'khor la brten dbang rdzogs mdzad 'dug pa/ /de yan rje btsun gong ma'i yig cha
dang / /gsan yig sogs su gsal ba ji ltar gzigs/ /khyad par sindhur la brten gong ma gsum/ /bskur ba'i brgyud pa da lta su la mchis/ /zhes gsungs pa'i dgongs pa'i don yang
gsal bar byas pa yin la/ yang bcu bdun ma'i dbang dang / gcer bu dang / bran bdud kyi rjes gnang gyi ljang gi lugs yin par grags shing / don la yang de nas brgyud pa yod
pa la/ brgyud pa gyi ljang nas 'dren tshul yod med ci rigs 'dug pas/ gzhan dag la ci 'dra yod dam snyam du dgongs nas yang dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ 'di yi bcu bdun
gshin rjes bskor ba dang / /las kyi mgon po zangs gri rnam gnyis kyi/ /rjes gnang gyi ljang lugs zhes kha cig smra/ /de nas rim

bzhin brgyud pa ji ltar yod/ /ces gsungs nas/ dri ba po rang gi dgongs bzhed ni/ nyid kyis mdzad pa'i snyan brgyud rin chen lde mig tu/ gyi ljang yongs grags kyi brgyud pa
'dren par mdzad pa'i rjes su/ de nas ma brgyud pa'i bcu bdun ma'i dbang gi brgyud pa zhig kyang 'dren par mdzad 'dug pa bzhin/ kho bos bstan bcos 'dir yang gong du bkod pa
ltar yin pas/ des na gyi ljang las ma brgyud pa'i bcu bdun ma zhig ni rje tshar chen rang yang yod par bzhed rgyur snang zhing / gcer bu zangs gri can dang / bran bdud
kyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ gyi ljang / mal lo/ sa chen/ yar bsgom se bo/ rgyal tsha lung mang po/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen seng ge bzang po/ yar lung pa seng
rgyal/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN

chen 'bum phrag gsum pa/ chos rje gong dkar tshul khrims pa/ rje tshar ba/ rje mkhyen brtse ba/ rje bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ spyan snga chos
kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na mkhyen brtse ba'i rjes su/ rje byams pa rab brtan/ chos rje snying rje bzang po/ rje spyan snga ba man 'dra'o/ /yang
na tshar chen gyi rjes su/ rje mai tri pa/ spyan snga ba chos rgya mtsho/ lo nas kun dga' don grub man 'dra/ de dag ni gyi ljang nas brgyud tshul bkod pa yin la/ las
mkhan de dag gi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa lugs gzhan ni 'og tu 'chad do/ /gnyis pa rjes gnang gi bka' ma nub pa ni/ ding sang lcam dral du grags pa lha gsum gyi rjes gnang
/ mkha' 'gro sbags sgrub tu grags pa lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang / lha brgyad kyi steng du gdong brnyan sgo ma

bzhi bsnan pa lha bcu gnyis ma'i rjes gnang / las mgon pu tra ming sring gi rjes gnang ste/ bzhi po 'di la bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan pa'i gsung gis rjes gnang 'di bzhi
yongs su grags shing med mi rung yin pas gces par bya zhing / de bzhi thob nas man ngag mtha' dag nyams su len rung ba yin pas/ rnam grangs mang po chos kyi zab khyad tsam
yin no zhes gsungs par grags shing / gzhan yang rgyas pa'i yan lag tu khro bcu'i rjes gnang / bran bdud gshin rje nag po'i bka' gtad/ zangs gri can gnyis kyi rjes gnang
yang yod pa yin la/ de lta bu'i lcam dral gsum gyi rjes gnang 'di la thog ma'i yi ge tho tsam zhig mal los mdzad cing / de'i rjes su 'phags pa dang / chos rje bla ma sogs
kyis mdzad pa yang yod cing / da lta chos rje bla ma'i de'i steng nas gtso bor gnang ba yin la/ lha brgyad la

rjes gnang thun mong ba dang / thun mong ma yin pa gnyis las/ 'di la yi ge a gnyan dam pas mdzad pa dang / yar lung pas nag po 'gro shes dang / rje tshar pa dang sngags 'chang
chen pos mdzad pa yod pa las/ da lta phyi ma gnyis po gang rung gi steng nas gnang ba yin zhing / 'di'i zhal ngo nang brgyud kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i rim pa ni gong du
brjod pas rtogs nus pa yin la/ ngor lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ dam pa kun dga' grags yan gzhan dang 'dra ba las/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ 'gro mgon bsod nams
pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ grub chen dkon blo/ rje sangs rin/ rje dkon
mchog lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/

des sa skya pa la'o/ /yang na 'phags pa'i rjes su/ rgyal tsha chos kyi dbang phyug mkhas pa yon tan khri/ drin can seng ge bzang po/ bla ma dam pa/ yar lung seng rgyal/ mkhan
chen rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs nam rgyal/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ mkhas btsun dpal ldan rgyal po/ rje sangs rin man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen mus chen/ rgyal tshab
rje/ kun mkhyen/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel man gong dang 'dra/ lcam dral gyi brgyud pa ni/ dam pa kun grags kyi rjes su/ bdag nyid chen po/ 'gro mgon rje/ bla chen
kun rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs nam rgyal/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje rdo ring pa/ rje blo gsal rgya mtsho/ rje bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ rje bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhan chen
thams cad mkhyen pa/

des bdag la'o/ /lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang rdzong lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ chos rje bla ma yan 'dra/ de nas sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal ba/ bla ma dge legs bzang po/ zur ban
shAkya dpal/ bla ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ yang na bla ma dam pa/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ rdzong pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun bzang / mus srad
pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ yang na 'phags pa/ mkhan chen byang chub dpal/ 'dzim chen rgyal mtshan dpal/ paN chen ma ti/ theg chen chos rgyal/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/
khrom yon pa/ mus srad pa/ bla ma shes rab rin chen/ tshar chen chos rje man gong gi lcam dral dang 'dra/ gsang khrid kyi sngon du 'gro ba lha brgyad kyi steng du ber
nag bsnan pa lha dgu'i rjes gnang shin tu zab pa gcig 'byung ba 'di la yig cha mkhan /

chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis mdzad pa yod la/ yang brag rdzong ma dang gtso bor 'brel ba mgon po 'di nyid la 'khor mgon po bcus bskor ba khro bcu'i rjes gnang du grags pa yod
cing / 'di'i brgyud pa bdag chen yab sras gnyis la ma byung bas/ phyis rje tshar pas lcags mo bkra shis seng ge la gsan pa yin zhing / 'di la yi ge rje tshar pas mdzad
pa dang / zur 'debs rje mkhyen brtses mdzad pa yod la/ da lta de gnyis gung bsgrigs pa'i steng nas gnang ba yin zhing / phyis kho bas kyang gsal ba zhig byas yod do/ /'di'i
brgyud pa 'og tu 'chad la/ lha brgyad kyi steng du seng gdong ma/ gzig gdong ma/ dom gdong ma/ dred gdong ma bzhi bsnan pas lha bcu gnyis ma'i rjes gnang 'di la yi ge
rje tshar pas mdzad pa yod la/ 'di'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po yan lha /

brgyad dang 'dra ba las/ mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang
/ rje btsun rdo ring pa/ rje btsun sgo rum pa/ de gnyis la rje tshar chen/ rje mkhyen brtse/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa la'o/ /yang na bla ma dam pa'i
rjes su/ bzhi thog pa kun dga' rin chen/ bdag po grags pa blo gros/ bdag po blo gros dbang phyug sngags 'chang rin chen rnam rgyal/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa
lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ chos rje dkon mchog grags pa/ shes rab rgyal mtshan/ mus pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / grub mchog rdo rje'i mtshan can/ bla ma nam mkha' chos dar/ spyan
snga kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun /

dga' bsod nams la'o/ /'khor rkyang pu tra ming sring gi rjes gnang zur bka' 'di la yi ge dam pas mdzad pa dang / yar lung pas rgyas bsdus gnyis dang / de dang 'dra ba sngags
'chang chen pos mdzad pa yang yod pas/ ding sang de dag gi steng nas mdzad cing / 'di la bzlas lung gi skabs su bod rbad bsad gsum ga yod pas/ las sbyor gang byed kyang
'di sngon du nges par thob dgos pa yin la/ 'di'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'phags pa klu sgrub/ slob dpon padma 'byung gnas/ paNDi ta dharma pa la/ lo chen rin chen
bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/ bla ma mal lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po
che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags /

pa/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ rdo
rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/
grub chen dpal ldan bkra shis/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ des bdag sa
skya pa a nanda la'o/ /yang na sa lo'i rjes su/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang
chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa la'o/ /'di la yar lung pas mdzad pa'i yi ge las/ bod /

rbad bsad gsum gyi bzlas lung bka' bsgo dang bcas pa/ rje pa'i drung du/ chos rje pa dang / bla ma yar bsgom gnyis kas gsan/ de gnyis la rgyal tsha lung mang po dang / mkhas
pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen seng bzang / de la yar lung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyis gsan par bshad pas/ sngon gyi dus su bzlas lung la bod pa gnyis tsam mdzad pa'i 'khor
rkyang gi rjes gnang zhig dang / ding sang yongs grags kyi sngags gsum ga bzlas lung gi dus mdzad pa'i phyag len gnyis shig byung ba 'dra zhing / sngags 'chang chos kyi
rgyal pos kyang / ming sring gsum gyi rjes gnang gi yi ge dang / zur bka'i yi ge so sor mdzad pa'i/ snga ma de la bzlas lung la bod pa gnyis tsam gyis chog pa kho bo sems
shing / 'on kyang dpe rnams su bzlas lung la sngags gsum ga byed pa bshad snang bas/ yi ge pas ma dag gam /

snyam pas dpyad par bya'o/ /gzhan yang zangs gri skor gsum la yang rjes gnang zur bka' re re yod pa ni/ yig rnying gung bsgrigs nas mdzad pa'i phyi'i las mkhan gcer bu zangs
gri can dang / nang gi las mkhan ber nag zangs gri can gyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje gur/ bram ze mchog sred/ nor bu gling pa/ dad byed go cha/
lo chen rin bzang / brag steng pa/ mal lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ 'gos ston tshar sgang ba/ dge bshes mi g.yo ba/ gshen bsgom bla ma dpal/ slob dpon shes rab bla ma/
dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa/ yar lung pa khu dbon/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan/
paN chen 'bum phrag gsum pa/ gong dkar chos rje tshul khrims/ rje tshar chen/ rje /

mkhyen brtse ba/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na tshar chen gyi rjes su/ rje bod
dkar ba/ spyan snga chos rgya mtsho/ bdag gi bla ma lo nas chos kyi spyan ldan no/ /bran bdud kyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ chos rje sa paN yan chad mal lo nas brgyud
pa'i mgon po lha brgyad dang 'dra ba las/ do ba ston tshul/ rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug mkhas pa yon tan khri/ drin can seng ge bzang po/ yar lung seng
ge rgyal mtshan/ tshem bu pa dpal ldan blo gros/ dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer/ bla ma kun bzang rtse ba/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sngags 'chang
chos kyi rgyal po/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas/ des /

bdag la'o/ /yang bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan dang / rje rdo ring pa las ma brgyud kyang bla ma gong ma gzhan las 'ongs pa'i mgon po khro bcu'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/
dam pa kun dga' grags yan lha brgyad dang 'dra zhing / de nas bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ sngags 'chang gzungs pa/
bzang po rgyal mtshan/ dge rgyal ba/ sangs rgyas mchog pa/ skyes mchog rgyal mtshan/ bkra shis seng ge rje blo gsal rgya mtsho/ rje bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ rje byams pa
rab brtan/ mus chen rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa rigs sngags 'chang ba ngag dbang kun dga'i ming can la dgyes bzhin du gnang nas/ yig cha
de yang 'phral du brtsams nas gzigs phul bas/ rje bla ma nyid thugs rab tu dgyes pa'i gsung du /

ma stsol bar mdzad pa lags so/ /mal lo nas brgyud pa la pho rkyang dang / mo rkyang gnyis kyi rjes gnang ni med do/ /'o na khro bcu'i rjes gnang 'di pho rkyang du song snyam
na/ 'di gtso 'khor sbags sgrub yin pas pho rkyang du mi 'gyur ba yin zhes rje blo gsal rgya mtsho bzhed cing / bla ma gong ma 'ga' zhig ni/ gri gug lha lnga dang / mgon
po khro bcu yang pho rkyang gi nang du 'du bar 'dod pa dag byung mod kyi/ 'di ni gtso 'khor sbags sgrub tu bzhed pa nyid don la gnas pa yin no zhes bdag gi rje bla ma dag
gsungs pa shin tu 'thad par mthong ngo / /de dag gis ni rje tshar chen gyi mgon po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ mal lo nas brgyud pho rkyang mo rkyang
la/ /rjes gnang thog ma nyid nas med pa'am/ /'on te bar skabs ji tsam dag nas chad/ /khro bcu'i rjes gnang /

byed pa dag gam ci/ /zhes dri ba mdzad pa'i don yang gsal bar byas pa yin no/ /yang zhing skyong chen po tsa turmu kha'i rjes gnang gi skor la/ bsnyen dus/ sgrub dus/ las sbyor/
spogs chog shi sa bstan pa sogs kyi mgon po'i mngon rtogs mi 'dra ba tha dad pa'i/ rjes gnang mi 'dra ba du ma yod pa las/ de dag gi yig sna'i rnam grangs kyang / bla
ma gnyan los mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge rjes gnang kha'u pas mdzad pa sa chen gyis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge rjes gnang gsal ba rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa/
rjes gnang shin tu rgyas pa'i nag po 'gro shes yar lung pa ldong ston seng ge rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ de nyid las brgyud pa'i gri snying bla rdo srog 'khor phyag mtshan
rnams kyi rjes gnang gi yi ge sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po dang / rje tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i /

rjes gnang yi ge sogs dang / las bzhi'i mgon po'i skor la/ dkar po tshe 'phel gyi sgrub thabs/ rjes gnang gi yig chung / ser po rgyas pa'i yi ge nag po dgra bgegs sgrol ba'i
yi ge dmar po dbang sdud kyi yi ge las bzhi'i mgon po'i mngon rtogs kyi gsal byed/ mgon po ser po'i rjes gnang gi yig chung / de dag gi gsal byed rje mkhyen brtse ba dang
/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pas mdzad pa sogs yod pa'i/ ding sang bla ma phyi ma rnams kyi yi ge'i steng nas phyag len mdzad de/ gnang ba'i thog mar bsnyen dus kyi mgon
po'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / klu sgrub/ ba ling ta/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ dpal bde ba/ bi ma la gupta/ ratna kirti/ ratna
badzra/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma/ gnyan lo dar ma grags/ gnam kha'u pa//

rje sa chen/ slob dpon rin po che/ sa paN/ 'phags pa/ dam pa kun grags/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/
'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin
chen/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ des bdag sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la gnang ba'o/ /sgrub dus thun mong ma
yin pa'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ kha che rin chen rdo rje yan sngar bzhin/ de nas ta thA ga ta rakShi ta/ gnyan lo/ kha'u pa yan sngar bzhin/ yang na bla ma dam pa
nas/ bzhi thog pa kun rin/ bzhi thog pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ /

mtshungs med shes rab zla ba/ rje rdo ring pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ mkhan chen gzhon nu blo gros/ grub mchog bsod nams dbang po/ des sa skya pa a nanda la'o/ /bram
ze mngags gtad kyi brgyud pa ni/ bla ma dam pa yan sngar ltar/ de nas bzhi thog pa kun rin/ bzhi thog pa bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan nas/
rje tshar chen bar sngar bzhin/ de nas rje mkhyen brtse ba/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag la'o/ /yang bram ze mngags gtad rdzong lugs nas brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa
yan sngar bzhin las/ de nas zhang ston/ brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa/ sngags 'chang gzungs/ dge legs bzang po/ a nanda ma ti bzang po/ mus srad pa/ rje shes rin pa/ mkhan
chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ rdo ring kun rgyal/ mkhan /

chen byams pa bzang po/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ des bdag sa skya pa rigs sngags 'chang ba ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la dge sdings su gnang ba yin/ dpal mgon gyi
gsang khrid sngon 'gro rjes gnang dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma dam pa yan bsnyen dus kyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa dang 'dra ba las/ de nas sngags 'chang gzungs ba/
chos rje bzang po rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub dge ba rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sangs rgyas mchog pa/ mtshungs med skyes mchog rgyal mtshan/ lcags mo bkra shis seng ge rje tshar
chen/ rje mkhan chen pa/ chos rje nam mkha' chos dar/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag a nanda la gnang ba'o/ /sngon 'gro'i rjes gnang kho na'i
brgyud pa ni/ rje tshar chen yan gong bzhin la/ de nas rje bon dkar ba don grub rgyal /

mtshan/ spyan snga chos rgya mtsho/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa a nanda la gnang ba yin/
dpal mgon khyung zhal can gyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / mahA de wa/ paNDi ta shi la singha/ a tsa ra gnyan chen dpal dbyangs/ ka ma ru pa/ gnyan lo/ glang
ban ngag ro/ rtogs ldan mtsho dkar ba/ spyan snga bsod nams grags/ chos rje bsod nams bzang po/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ grwa thang shes
rab zla ba/ rje btsun rdo ring pa/ grub mchog sbyin pa rgya mtsho/ drin can tshar pa chos rje/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rje dbang phyug rab brtan man 'dra/
dpal mgon gdong brnyan can gyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni//

kha che rin chen rdo rje man dkyus bzhin/ de nas paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa/ gnyan lo/ kha'u pa/ gong ma lnga/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge dharmA kirti/
blo bzang pa/ nya dbon pa/ bla ma lung rigs rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ pha brag thog pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ thugs sras kun dga' rgyal po/ rje
tshe bkras pa/ rje tshar chen/ rje mai tri pa/ spyan snga chos rgya mtsho man 'dra/ dpal mgon brtsegs zhal can gyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang nas/ ri sul
gyi rnal 'byor ma/ gnyan lo/ kha'u pa/ dkar po rnam gsum/ sa paN/ rong pa sga lo/ sras shes rab seng ge bla ma bsod nams lhun grub/ bla ma ngag dbang grags pa/ bla ma dpal
ldan legs dbang / chos sgo ba chos dpal shes /

rab/ pha brag thog pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa man 'dra/ dpal mgon dkar po tshe 'phel/ ser po bsod nams sgrub pa/ dmar po dbang bsdud/ sngon po bgegs 'joms te las
bzhi mgon po so so'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang nas/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma'i bar dkyus bzhin/ de nas sa lo/ kha'u pa/ gong ma lnga/ lo tsA ba mchog
ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge chos rje dharmA kirti/ chos rje blo bzang / nya dbon kun dga' dpal ba/ bla ma lung rigs rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ pha brag thog
pa bsod nams bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ mus chen rnam rgyal bzang po/ klu dbang gling pa kun dga' rgyal po/ rje tshe dbang bkra shis/ drin can
tshar pa chos rje/ rje /

mai tri pa/ spyan snga chos rgya mtsho man 'dra/ dpal mgon bram nag bshan pa drug bskor nag po dom mchong gi rjes gnang dang chos skor gyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / klu
sgrub/ dzu ki ka ma ru pa/ zhang mdo sde dpal/ 'jam skya nam mkha' dpal ldan/ brang mo che ba/ rje btsun re mda' ba/ grub chen thang stong rgyal po/ ras chen dpal 'byor
bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ rgya ston byang chub dbang rgyal/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog bstan 'dzin ngag dbang nyi zla bzang po/ rje btsun dbang phyug
rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa a nanda la gnang ba'o/ /gong gi
brgyud pa de dag la mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi rjes su/ rje snying rje bzang po bcug kyang chog pa 'ga' zhig /

snang ngo / /bla ma gnyan lo tsA ba chen po rgya gar nas bod du 'byon khar/ kharsa pa Ni'i ri sul gyi rnal 'byor mas gnang ba'i stobs 'phrog nag po chen po'i thun mong ma yin
pa'i shog ril nyer gcig gi gtso bor gyur pa srung 'khor/ tshe sgrub dang bcas pa'i man ngag zab mo/ gnyan lo chen po dgung lo phyed dang nyis brgya thub par grags pa'i
mgon po 'di'i man ngag gi nying khu zab mo'i mthar thug khrid rgyas bsdus gnyis kyi brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa yan gzhan dang 'dra ba las/ de nas zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag
phug pa bsod nams dpal ba/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug
kun mkhyen mkhas pa'i dbang po bsod nams seng ge 'dren mchog chos rje/ 'jam /

dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ gling dpon chen chos sku 'od zer/ rje byams pa shes rab bzang po/ chos kyi rje bsam gtan rin chen/ rje 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus
chen 'khor lo sdom pa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa zhing skyong dgyes pa'i rnal 'byor pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la gnang ba yin no/ /dpal dur khrod
bdag po yab yum gyi rjes gnang gi yi ge rje sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen dang / sngags 'chang chen pos mdzad pa sogs 'byung ba'i/ ding sang phyi
ma'i steng nas phyag len mdzad cing de'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ padma badzra/ ra hu la/ sgeg pa'i rdo rje/ dznyA na siddhi/ dpal dam tshig
gi rdo rje/ 'chi med blo gros bzang po/ mkhas pa bai ro tsA na/ dpal chen rga lo/ bla ma sa skya

pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bla chen yarmar sgom/ rgyal tsha lung mang po/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ drin can seng ge bzang po/ yar lung
pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ bla ma bsod nams rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs sangs
rgyas rin chen/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sbas pa'i rnal 'byor dpal ldan bkra shis/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas grags pa blo
gros/ des bdag sa skya pa la'o/ /de'i rgyud dang man ngag gi skor la/ rten bca' ba/ bsnyen pa bskyal ba/ dngos grub sgrub pa/ bdag bsrung ba/ gzhan bsrung ba/ grong khyer
gyi rims dang / dgra kun bsrung ba/

shes rab bskyed pa/ rang gzhan gyi gdug pa gzhom pa/ sngags la gsham bu gdags pa/ rigs sngags bzlog pa/ las spyi'i sgrub thabs/ 'bru spel ba/ mar spel ba/ zhing gi lo spel
ba/ thab gter 'dzugs pa/ kha zas bsdu ba/ mi byams par bya ba/ bdag gi dmag bsrung ba/ gzhan gyi dmag bzlog pa/ spyir bsam pa thams cad sgrub pa/ nang gtsang gi yams bsrung
ba/ dus min 'chi ba bzlog pa/ phyogs kyi don sgrub pa/ sri'u gso ba/ dbang sdud bya ba/ zhing la gnod pa bsrung ba/ phyugs nad bcad pa/ lam bsrung ba/ 'di la las sna sum
cu tsam 'dug pa bai ro tsa na'i zhal gdams sa chen pas bsgrigs pa/ yab yum gyi rten sku sba ba sa chen pas mdzad pa/ mchod gtor 'bul ba'i las sgrig seng ge rgyal mtshan
gyis mdzad pa/ gsham na jag bcings

dang bcas pa de dag gi brgyud pa ni/ dpal ldan rgyal po yan rjes gnang dang 'dra ba las/ de nas mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ 'khor lo
sdom pa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag la'o/ /yang lugs gcig la/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje rdo ring pa/ rje tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rje mkhyen brtse ba/ rje
bsod nams chos 'phel/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' la'o/ /yang lugs gcig la/ rje kun dga' grol mchog rje zhe dgon pa bsod nams rtse
mo/ de gnyis ka la ngag dbang nyi zla bzang po/ de'i drung du rje lo phu ba a nanda'i mtshan can/ des sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /sa skya
pa'i yab chos yang phur gnyis kyi srung ma dkar bdud lcam dral gyi rjes gnang gi

brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang po/ longs sku rdo rje sems dpa'/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ 'khon klu'i dbang po/ 'khon rdo rje rin chen/ 'khon shes rab yon tan/ 'khon
tshul khrims rgyal po/ 'khon rdo rje gtsug tor/ 'khor dge skyabs/ 'khon dge mthong / 'khon bal po/ 'khon shAkya blo gros/ 'khon rog shes rab tshul khrims/ 'khon dkon mchog
rgyal po/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal
'phags pa/ kha'u pa 'od ldan dpal/ bu lung pa kun dga' rdo rje/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla chen
kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ theg chen chos kyi

rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang
kun dga' rin chen/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ des 'khon a nanda la'o/ /'di'i sgrub skor bdud rgyal thod phreng can gyi rgyud man
ngag dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan yan gong dang 'dra ba la/ de nas bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ kun spangs chos kyi nyi ma/ rje blo
gsal rgya mtsho/ rje bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ de'i drung du bdag a nandas thos so/ /de ltar dbang dang rjes gnang gi bka' ma nub pa de nyid chu
bo'i rgyun dang 'dra ba'i rgyu mtshan ni/ chu bo ganggA de nyid bar ma chad du mthud nas 'bab pa de bzhin du/ ya mtha' rdo rje 'chang dang bram ze mchog sred sogs nas/
ma mtha' rang gi rtsa ba'i bla ma'i bar du dbang dang rjes gnang gi bka' yod la lhag chad med pa/ byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ma nyams shing 'phrin las kyi nus mthur ldan pa
phyag len phra mo tshun gyi srol ma nyams pa/ mkha' 'gro'i kha rlangs thul le ba zhig dgos pa'i don yin par gsungs so/ /rdo rje slob dpon mchog gi bka' drin las/ /rdo rje
chos skyong rnams kyi dbang rjes gnang / /rdo rje slob mar byin pa'i byin rlabs kyis/ /rdo rje 'dzin par sgyur byed 'di ngo mtshar/ /bar skabs kyi tshigs su bcad pa'o/
/gnyis pa gdam ngag gser 'gyur gyi rtsi dang 'dra bas sarga ma log pa la gsum ste/ phyi rten dang dkyil 'khor la brten nas sgrub pa/ nang rtsa gsum 'khor lo la brten nas
sgrub pa/ gsang ba yang gsang sems kyi gnad la brten nas sgrub pa'o/ /dang po la rnam grangs spyir bstan pa dang / de'i

nang nas mchog tu zab pa ngos bzung ba/ de nyams su len pa'i gdams pa bstan pa'o/ /dang po la gnyis te/ rkyang sgrub dang / sbags sgrub bo/ /rkyang sgrub la gsum ste/ pho rkyang
/ mo rkyang / 'khor rkyang du sgrub pa'o/ /pho rkyang la/ bka' sdod/ tshogs bdag gnod sbyin/ gshin rje ltar sgrub pa ste yongs su grags pa'i sgrub chen bzhi/ gzhan
yang bdud dang mon pa ltar sgrub pa'i tha snyad kyang dam pa kun dga' grags kyi sgrub yig las bshad do/ /'di la bsgrub bya lha'i rnam 'gyur dang / sngags kyi dbye bas bzhir
bshad pa ni/ brag steng pa'i sgrub lugs bzhi'i yi ge dang / bla chen bsod blo ba'i man ngag tshigs bcad du gsal zhing / sgrub tshul gyi sgo nas bdag nyid mgon por bskyed
pa tshogs bdag dang / rang yi dam du gsal ba'i mdun du mgon po bka' nyan du bskyed pa bka' sdod de/ bsdus na 'di gnyis su 'dus pa gnyan phul chung pa'i sgrub yig sogs
su bshad pas/ de dag gi tshul cung zad bshad na/ dang po pho rkyang bka' sdod ltar sgrub pa ni/ mgon po gcer bu la gaNDe mchan khung na bsnams pa/ gri thod 'dzin pa/ sngags
ni/ oM shrI mahA kA la ye hU~M hU~M phaTa? phaTa? swAhA/ zhes pa'o/ /gnyis pa ni rtsa ba'i mgon po de nyid de/ phyag gnyis gri thod 'dzin pa'i steng na gaNDe bsnams pa/
dar nag gi gos 'khyud lhab lhub dang bcas pa'o/ /gsum pa ni mgon po nyid shin tu rngams pa'i cha byad zhal cung zad gdangs pa'o/ /bzhi pa ni sku shin tu brjid cing rgyas
pa'i rnam pa can no/ /dang po gnyis la ni rim bzhin bka' sdod kyi mgon po dang / tshogs bdag gi mgon po zhes pa'i tha snyad kyang bshad/ gsum pa ni drag po'i las la bsngags
shing gshin rje'i rnam pa 'dra bas na/ gshin rje ltar sgrub pa zhes bya/ bzhi

pa ni rgyas pa'i las la bsngags shing gnod sbyin gyi rnam pa 'dra bas na/ gnod sbyin ltar sgrub pa zhes bya zhing / gnod sbyin lta bu'i mgon po byas kyang chog go /des na 'di
bzhi'i khyad par ni/ bsgrub bya lha'i rnam pa mi 'dra ba nyid kyi sgo nas 'byed cing / so so'i nges tshig kyang de ltar yin la/ bdag mdun sogs sgrub tshul gyi sgo nas
kyang cung zad 'byed de/ tshogs bdag ltar sgrub pa 'di la/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum yod pa'i/ bsnyen pa'i skabs su rang yi dam du gsal ba'i mdun du mgon po bskyed nas/ dam bzhag
mna' chu blud pa/ sngags bzla ba sogs byas nas/ sgrub pa'i skabs su rang nyid mgon por bskyed pa yig rnying las bshad la/ gzhan gsum ni bsnyen sgrub gang byed kyang
/ mdun bskyed gtso che ba yin no/ /mgon po mdun du bskyed na bka' sdod yin pas ma

khyab pa yang shes par bya'o/ /gzhan yang bdud dang mon pa ltar sgrub pa sogs ni/ snga ma de bzhir ma 'dus pa'i sgrub tshul gyi dbye ba phra mo gzhan yin no/ /don de dag la
dgongs nas mgon po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ snyan brgyud gnyis pa gdams pa'i rnam grangs skabs/ /pho rkyang sgrub lugs rnam bzhi'i khyad par 'di/ /bsgrub
bya lha yi rnam 'gyur gyis dbye bam/ /bdag mdun la sogs sgrub tshul sgo nas 'byed/ /so sor 'dogs pa'i nges tshig gang yin dang / /gzhan yang bdud dang mon pa ltar
bsgrub sogs/ /dam pas mdzad par grags pa'i gshin rje ltar/ /bsgrub pa'i yi ger bshad pa ji ltar lags/ /zhes gsungs pa'i dgongs don yang gsal bar byas pa yin no/ /gnyis pa
mo rkyang du bsgrub pa la/ nang pa ltar bsgrub pa dang / phyi pa mu stegs pa ltar bsgrub pa gnyis/ dang po la 'jam rtsub gnyis yod de/ e ka dza Ti'i lto bar sa bon

bhyoHlas bskyed pa 'jam lugs dang / de'i snying khar sa bon ma~M las bskyed pa rtsub lugs so/ /gnyis pa phyi pa la yang 'jam rtsub gnyis yod par bshad/ dam pas mo rkyang sgrub
lugs bzhi'i dbye ba zhes bshad pa yang / phyi nang la 'jam rtsub gnyis gnyis te bzhi po 'di tsam yin par sems so/ /yum 'khor dang bcas pa zhes bshad pa ni/ lha mo nyid
bka' nyan gyi 'khor tshogs ma mo bcu dgu dang bcas te bsgrub pa la zer ba yin no/ /'on kyang 'di ni mo rkyang du 'khrul par mi bya ste/ mo rkyang gi don ni gnya' gnon du
mgon po yang med/ rang gi bka' nyan gyi 'khor yang med par lha mo rkyang pa bsgrub pa la bya'o/ /phyi pa dang nang pa'i don la kha cig yum chen gyi sku'i phyi ru lha mo
bskyed pa la phyi pa dang / nang du bskyed pa la nang pa zhes pa'i tha snyad zer ba ni mi 'thad de/ dam pa

gcung gi yi ge dang / gzungs pas mdzad pa'i yar lung pa seng rgyal gyi dris lan las/ phyi pa dang nang pa zhes tshig gsal dngos su gsungs pa dang 'gal bas so/ /des na lha mo
la mu stegs pa'i lugs kyi bskyed chog dang sngags sbyar ba ni phyi pa ltar bsgrub pa yin la/ dgos pa ni rno zhing myur ba'i phyir yin zhing / 'di la yum chen gnya' gnon
du med do/ /yum chen gnya' gnon du byas shing / rgyud dang gzungs nas bshad pa'i bskyed chog dang sngags sbyar ba ni nang pa ltar bsgrub pa yin no/ /phyi pa ltar bsgrub
pa la rgya gzhung mchog sred kyis mdzad pa yod cing / 'di nyid paNDi ta lo ka shrIs bsgyur pa yin la/ khong la mu stegs kyi ston par yang grags/ 'on kyang mu stegs kyi grub
mtha' 'dzin mkhan ni ma yin par bla ma dag bzhed do/ /de dag gis ni rje tshar chen gyi mgon po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ mo rkyang skabs

su e ka dza Ti yi/ /sku yi phyi nang bskyed pas de bzhin no/ /des na dam pa gcung gi sgrub yig dang / /gzungs pas yar lung sing ha'i dris lan du/ /phyi pa nang pa zhes bya
gsal ba yi/ /tshig de'i nus pa ji bzhin gang las thon/ /mu stegs pa ltar bsgrub pa sogs 'dod na/ /de yi dgos pa ci yin lo ka shrI/ /mu stegs ston pa yin pa'i rgyu mtshan
gang / /dam pas mo rkyang bsgrub lugs bzhir bshad dang / /yum 'khor bcas pa'i ngos 'dzin gang la byed/ /ces gsungs pa'i dgongs don yang gsal bar byas pa yin no/ /gsum pa
'khor rkyang du sgrub pa la gnyis te/ thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'o/ /dang po ni/ srid pa gsum na che bar gyur pa ni mgon po lcam dral 'di yin pas/ dregs pa pho rgyud
mo rgyud thams cad 'khor du gtogs pa yin no/ /gtso bor gyur pa

ni dbang phyug 'dod pa'i dbang phyug lha'i dbang po/ tshogs bdag tshangs pa/ gzhon nu karti ka khyab 'jug bhring gi ri ti ste lha chen brgyad dang / stobs kyi rgyu/ dung skyong
/ mtha' yas/ nor rgyas/ 'jog po/ rigs ldan/ padma/ padma chen po ste klu chen po brgyad dang / tshangs pa chen po dang / dbang phyug chen po dang / khyab 'jug chen po
