zhang dbon rdo rje bdud 'dul/

sgrol gying / 'dzam ser/ 'dzam nag khyab pa chen po ste gnod sbyin brgyad dang / brgya byin/ gshin rje/ chu lha/ gnod sbyin/ dbang ldan/ me lha/ srin po/ rlung lha/ tshangs
pa/ sa bdag ste phyogs skyong bcu dang / dmu/ klu/ rgyal po/ btsan/ bdud/ gnod sbyin/ ma mo/ ging ste lha srin sde brgyad dang / gzhan yang 'jigs byed dgu/ gza' brgyad/
rgyu skar nyi shu rtsa brgyad la sogs pa rnams so/ /'di rnams la'ang klu brgyad kyis bskor bas char 'bab pa dang / gza' brgyad kyis bskor bas thog ser 'bebs pa sogs man ngag
ci rigs pa snang ngo / /gnyis pa ni/ phyi'i las mkhan gcer bu zangs gri can/ nang gi las mkhan ser nag zangs gri can/ gsang ba'i las mkhan pu tra ming sring la/ ru mtshon

gyi las mkhan bran bdud gshin rje nag po/ sbas pa'i las mkhan sgo ma rnam pa bzhi/ gaNDe'i las mkhan khro tshogs 'bar ba/ srog gi las mkhan bshan pa dmar nag rnams so/ /dang
po 'di la brten nas seng ldeng gi dbyug pa'i mgul du sre mong gi blud bu dang / thod pa sngar can gyi sgo nas phyi'i rdzas dang / yo byad bsrung pa la gtso cher bsngags
pas sam/ yang na phyi'i dur khrod kyi khor yug la gnas pa'i gnod sbyin klu bdag ces bya ba de yin pas phyi'i las mkhan du bzhag pa yin gsungs shing / ber nag can ni nang
bsad pa'i las sbyor kho na la bsngags pa'am/ nang sgrub thun mong min pa'i skabs las mkhan gyi gtso bo yin pas de ltar du bzhag pa yin te/ gcer bu'i sgrub thabs yig rnying
bla ma la la las brgyud pa las de dag kyang las mkhan zangs gri can gnyis yod pa las ber nag ni nang dang 'di phyi'i

las la bsngags pa'i lugs yin/ gzhan gnod sbyin yab yum dang las mkhan ming sring ni nang ngam/ gsang sgrub yin no zhes gsungs pa yin zhing / ber nag la sgrub thabs rgyas bsdus
gnyis mal gyi dbon po blo gros seng ges mdzad pa yod la/ pu tra rnams ni mgon po'i las mkhan gyi nang nas sbas shing gsang ba zab pa'i mthar thug tu byed pa'am/ yang
na 'di'i sgo nas dgra bgegs kyi lus rtsa mdud kyi gnad gsum la/ pu tra ming sring gsum srog bdud kyi tshul du gnas pa la gnad du bsnun pas dmigs yul de mi snang bar byed
pa'i gsang ba'i las sbyor zab mo 'di la ma gtogs gzhan rnams la med pas de ltar bzhag go gsungs so/ /'di la phyi nor srung gnod sbyin pho mo'i tshul du bsgrub pa/ nang bsad
pa gshin rje pho mo'i tshul du bsgrub pa/ gsang ba las mkhan pho mo'i tshul du

bsgrub pa/ 'di rnams la sku mdog phyag mtshan sgrub tshul mi 'dra ba'i khyad par du ma zhig yod cing / sgrub tshul rgyas pa 'di dag ni don gyi mkha' 'gro sbags sgrub dang 'dra
bar snang ngo / /pu tra'i sgrub thabs bsam yas kyi ka ba nas spyan drangs pa'i gter ma/ dam pas mdzad pa'i rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum/ sa chen gyis mdzad pa gcig ste lnga
yod pa rnams ni me 'bar ma'i nang na bzhugs pa yin la/ sgrub thabs bka' khol ma'i dngos bstan slob dpon padma nas brgyud pa'i pu tra'i khol sgrub ni/ dam pas mdzad pa'i
shan pa lcam dral gyi sgrub thabs su grags pa 'di yin gsungs thugs rtsis su mdzad de/ gzhan bdud pu tra dang / mon chung pu tra'i man ngag ni 'di dang mi gcig pa'i rgyu
mtshan zhib tu yod pas bsre bar mi bya'o/ /'di la bdag gi bla ma mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsung gis/ pu tra la gsang ba'i las mkhan pu

tra/ bdud pu tra/ rkyal 'bud mon chung pu tra dang gsum yod pas ma nor ba gal che/ dang po ni/ ming sring gsum gyi nang tshan pu tra yongs grags 'di'o/ /gnyis pa la bdud pu
tra'i sgrub thabs bshan pa ro khur zhes bya ba yod/ gsum pa rkyal 'bud kyi rtsa ba'i yi ge lag len gyi zhal gdams/ las sbyor gyi zhal gdams lo rgyus dang bzhi yod pa snyan
brgyud po ti na bzhugs pa'o/ /zhes gsungs so/ /de dag gis ni rje tshar chen gyi mgon po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ 'khor rkyang skabs su zangs gri
rnam gnyis dang / /pu tra rnams la phyi nang gsang gsum gyi/ /las mkhan dag tu 'dogs pa'i rgyu mtshan ci/ /rkyang 'bud mon chung pu tra 'di yin nam/ /zhes pa'i don yang gsal
bar byas pa yin la/ bran bdud ni mal lo tsA ba la rje sa chen gyis zhus pa/ do pa ston

tshul la gnang ba'i myur cing rtsub par byed cing / 'di'i sgo nas rnga mdung gi ru mtshon la brten pa sogs mngon spyod kyi las mkhan du 'jog ces rje bla ma dag bzhed cing /
kha cig gsang ba'i las mkhan du 'dod pa ni rgyu mtshan med pa yin no/ /'di dang gyi ljang lugs kyi las mgon chen po gnyis 'dra bar snang yang / 'dir med pa gyi ljang lugs
las blangs pa ni ma yin te/ dper na mgon po nyid bzhin no/ /'di'i yig skor la bran bdud gshin rje nag po'i sgrub thabs gong mas do pa la gnang ba/ bran bdud kyi lung sbyin
pa'i tshul yar lung pas mdzad pa sogs yod cing / sgo ma bzhi ni mkha' 'gro bye ba 'bum sde'i nang na sbas pa'i ma mo bzhi yod pa de yin zer/ 'di la 'jam dbyangs nam mkha'
rgyal mtshan pas mdzad pa'i sgo ma bzhi bran mor sgrub pa'i man ngag ces pa'i yi ge zhig kyang yod la/ gaNDe'i khro bo

la ni/ dam pas mdzad pa'i rnam sprul gaNDe sgrub pa'i yi ger/ sku gsung thugs kyi sgo gsum las spro tshul/ de'i sgo nas las la sbyor tshul sogs zhib par bzhugs/ ding sang shog
ril bcu par grags pa'i nang na yod pa'i gaNDe sgrub pa'i shog ril zhes pa 'di dang ye mi gcig pas 'khrul par mi bya'o/ /bshan pa dmar nag ni mgon po 'di'i mngon spyod
kyi las mkhan med mi rung lta bu yin zhing / 'di'i sgrub tshul gyi yi ge sbas pa'i rnal 'byor pa bar sding pa badzra dhwa dzas mdzad pa yod do/ /gnyis pa sbags sgrub la/
rje rtse mos lo rgyus kyi yi ger/ lcam dral du bsgrub pa man ngag gi lugs yin/ zhes gsungs pa ltar/ dper na rje btsun bi ru pa nas rje sa chen gyi bar snyan brgyud du byon
pa la kyai rdo rje man ngag lugs su 'jog pa ltar/ 'di yang bram ze chen pos

bhe dan gyi yul du mgon po zhal gzigs pa yan chod du sbags sgrub kyi ming tsam yang med pa la/ de'i tshe mgon po rang gis sbags sgrub rnams bye brag tu gsungs/ bram ze mchog
sred nas mal lo'i bar du yi ge med pa'i snyan brgyud du byon pas/ 'dir yang sbags sgrub rnams la man ngag gi lugs zhes gdags su rung bar bla ma rnams bzhed pa yin no/ /de
la sgrub tshul gyi sgo nas dbye na/ yab yum sbags te sgrub pa/ lcam sring sbags te bsgrub pa/ lcam dral sbags te sgrub pa/ gtso 'khor sbags te sgrub pa dang bzhi/ dang
po ni/ 'jig rten pa'i bza' tsho ltar byas nas bsgrub pa mgon po dang lha mo gnyis sku tshad mnyam pa'o/ /gnyis pa ni yum chen gyi lto bar gnyis ka bskyed cing sku tshad
mnyam pa'o/ /'di ni 'jig rten pa'i ming sring dang go ba cung mi gcig go /gnad 'di nyid thugs la bzhag nas ngor chen rdo rje 'chang

chen pos kyang / rgyud nas bshad pa'i mgon po dang / gzungs nas bshad pa'i lha mo gnyis dgos pa'i dbang gis lhan cig tu bsgrubs pa las/ 'jig rten pa lta bu'i ming sring ma
yin no gsungs pa yin pas na/ gong mas lcam sring sbags sgrub gsungs pa dang 'gal ba med cing dgongs pa gcig pa yin la/ 'o na lha mo yang rgyud nas bstan yod pa las ched du
gzungs las bsngags pa ci zhe na/ de nas rgyud kyi tshig ris gsar ma ba rang gi yin pa de 'dra gsal po da lta 'dren rgyu mi snang la/ gzungs nas gsal bar bstan pa thos tshod
tsam ma yin pa mngon sum du grub pas dgongs gzhi de ltar yin no/ /gsum pa lcam dral ni/ lha mos mgon po'i sku'i phyed tsam du slebs pa che chung yod pa 'di'o/ /de yang
lcam dral ni che chung gi brda rnying dag yin par sems so/ /bzhi pa gtso 'khor sbags sgrub la/ thun mong ba'i

gtso 'khor dang / thun mong ma yin pa'i gtso 'khor gnyis/ dang po ni/ gong du bshad pa ltar mgon po la 'khor lha chen brgyad la sogs pa brgyad brgyad drug cu rtsa bzhis bskor
ba'o/ /gnyis pa ni gtso bo mgon po lcam dral la sngar smos pa'i phyi nang gsang gsum gyi las mkhan dag gis bskor ba'o/ /gsang ba'i las mkhan lngas bskor ba'i tshe na lha
brgyad ma dang / sgo ma bzhi yang bsnan pas na bcu gnyis mar 'gyur ro/ /sa chen gyi lcam dral sbags sgrub lha brgyad ma la bshad/ ding sang lcam dral sbags sgrub lha gsum
ma la ngos 'dzin grags so/ /'on kyang sa chen dang mi 'gal te/ de ni lcam dral 'khor bcas sbags sgrub la dgongs pa'o/ /'di lta bu'i lcam dral sbags sgrub kyi dbye ba
shes na/ rje sa chen gyis sbags sgrub kyi yi ge chen mor/ yab yum du bsgrub pa dang / lcam dral du bsgrub pa gnyis las/ 'dir lcam dral du

bsgrub pa'i lugs kyi gdam ngag go /zhes lha brgyad la lcam dral du gsungs pa'i dgongs pa sogs rang grol du shes pa yin zhes bla ma dag gsung ngo / /de dag gis ni rje tshar
chen gyi mgon po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ sbags sgrub skabs su ngor chen a nandas/ /rgyud dang gzungs nas bshad pa'i ma mgon gnyis/ /dgos pa'i dbang
gis lhan cig bsgrub pa las/ /'di gnyis ming sring lta bu min gsungs pa/ /gong mas lcam sring yab yum sbags sgrub ces/ /gsungs dang dgongs pa gcig pa'i rgyu mtshan gang /
/lha mo rgyud nas gsal bar bstan bzhin du/ /ched du gzungs las bsngags pa'i bzhed pa'ang ci/ /brtse ba chen pos sbags sgrub rgyas pa ru/ /yab yum dag dang lcam dral sbags
sgrub ces/ /phyi ma lha brgyad dag la bzhed bzhin du/ /phyis byon rnams kyis lha gsum lcam dral du/ /ngos bzung

mdzad pa gong dang mi 'gal lam/ /des na yab yum lcam sring lcam dral dang / /gtso 'khor sbags sgrub so sor dbye ba dang / /nges tshig gzhung dang mthun pa ji 'dra mchis/ /zhes
gsungs pa'i dgongs pa'i don yang gsal bar byas pa yin no/ /de lta bu'i gong gi sbags sgrub de rnams kyi nang nas/ lo chen gyis lcam dral lha gsum la gtso bor mdzad/ brag
steng pas bcu gnyis ma la gtso bor mdzad/ bla chen mal los mkha' 'gro lha brgyad sbags sgrub la gtso bor mdzad/ rje sa chen gyis lha bcu gnyis ma 'di bsgrubs na byin
rlabs che ba la dge sbyor gzhan la gnod par 'dug gsungs so zhes grags so/ /gnyis pa ni/ mchog tu zab pa ngos bzung ba la/ gong gi sgrub tshul de thams cad kyang khyad par
'phags pa yin mod na'ang / 'di dag rang la ltos te zab khyad 'jog pa'i dbang du byas na/ spyir pho rkyang du sgrub pa nus pa che

yang rtsub/ mo rkyang du sgrub pa myur te bsten pa dka'/ de gnyis la'ang bka' sdod ltar sgrub pa 'jam ste chun dka'o/ /tshogs bdag ltar sgrub pa tshan che ste bul bas 'khul
dka'/ yab yum du sgrub pa dang / lcam sring du sgrub pa tsam tshan che ste/ rnal 'byor pa chung ma can yin na bud med la gzan/ 'khor rkyang rno la myur te 'khu ldog che
zhing mthar mi shis/ des na lcam dral 'khor dang bcas pa'i sbags sgrub ni tshan che ba dang myur zhing shis la/ des na sgrub thabs kyi snying po lcam dral 'khor dang bcas
pa'i sbags sgrub 'di nyams su blang bar bya ba yin no/ /de lta bu'i sgrub thabs rnams las sbags sgrub zab/ sbags sgrub la'ang lcam dral tsam las lha brgyad du sgrub pa zab/
bcu gnyis sogs rgyas kyang bsnyen pa tsam ma gtogs las sbyor sogs thams cad lha brgyad kho na la 'brel chags/ bram ze mchog sred/ slob

dpon padma ste brgyud pa'i srol gnyis kyi man ngag gtso bo thun mong ma yin pa'i gsang ba'i sbags sgrub mkha' 'gro lha brgyad 'di/ rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras kyi thugs dam
gyi nying khu zab pa'i yang tig rtags 'phral du mngon sum ston pa'i lag len rgyun ma chad pa yin no zhes bla ma rnams gsungs so/ /de lta bu'i sbags sgrub kyi yig sna la/
sa chen gyi sbags sgrub che chung dang / kha'u pa 'od ldan dpal gyis mdzad pa shin tu legs pa dang / gzhan yang yig rnying mal los mdzad pa'i lha brgyad kyi bsnyen thabs
dang / de la mkho ba'i bsgrub pa dang / las sbyor gyi yi ge mal gyi dbon po blo gros seng ges mdzad pa sogs yod la/ mus srad pa sogs kha cig 'od ldan dpal gyi sbags sgrub
'di dam pas mdzad pa yin zer ba sogs ni mi 'thad de/ mgon po'i man ngag tshigs bcad ma bla chen bsod blos mdzad pa las/ rkyang sgrub rnam gnyis

dam pas mdzad par gsal/ /sbags sgrub sa chen mdzad par gsal ba yin/ /zhes dam pas rkyang sgrub mdzad par bshad kyis/ sbags sgrub mdzad par ma bshad pas so/ /rang lugs ni bdag
chen kun dbang ba'i gsung rgyun du me 'bar ma'i nang gi sbags sgrub shin tu legs pa 'di 'od ldan dpal gyis mdzad par bdag chen rdo rje 'chang bzhed pa yin no/ /yang kha
cig mal lo'i bsgrub yig 'di bu lung kun rdor gyis mdzad pa yin zer ba ni gzhi med kyi 'khrul pa kho na'o/ /gong du bshad pa ltar lha bcu gnyis ma'i sbags sgrub la sa chen
gyi 'di 'grub na legs mod/ 'on kyang dge sbyor la gnod/ tshig pa za zhes gsungs pa'i sgo ma bzhi po 'di 'dod pa la chags pa'i rnam pa 'jig rten pa'i tshul 'dzin pa yin
pas/ de'i rten 'brel gyis sgrub pa po la tshul khrims 'chal lo zhes pa'i gleng gzhi phran tshegs kyi

nyes dmigs 'byung ba la dgongs pa yin zhes rje bsod nams chos 'phel sogs gsung bar grags shing / bdag gi bla ma mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi bzhed pa ni/ sgo ma bzhi po
'phrin las bsgrub pa la myur bas/ 'gro ba dbang du 'du ba dang / zang zing gi dpal 'byor rgyas par byung tshe/ rnam g.yengs che bas dge sbyor la gnod par 'gyur ba la dgongs
pa yin zhes gsungs shing / legs bshad 'di ni mkhas pa'i gsung rmad du byung ba yin pa blo gsal rnams kyis snying la 'chang bar rigs so/ /de dag gis ni rje tshar chen
gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ bdag chen kun dga' dbang phyug gsung rgyun las/ /'od ldan dpal gyis mdzad ces sgrub yig 'di/ /kha cig a gnyan dam pas mdzad ces gleng /
/phyis byon 'ga' dag gzungs pas mdzad ces smra/ /dang po ltar na dam pas sbags sgrub kyi/ /yi ge mdzad na bla chen bsod blo bas/ /

rkyang sgrub rnam gnyis dam pas mdzad par gsal/ /sbags sgrub sa chen mdzad par gsal zhes pa/ /de las 'di nyid ches cher gsal bzhin du/ /rkyang sgrub kho na ched du brjod pa
ci/ /dam pa tshad mar byas phyin 'di sbed dam/ /mal los mdzad pa'i bsgrub yig chen mo 'di/ /kha cig bu lung kun rdor gyis mdzad ces/ /smra mod de lta'i log rtog gang la
'khrul/ /dgongs sam kyi hud snyigs ma'i tshul 'di skyo/ /bcu gnyis sbags sgrub dag la sa chen gyis/ /'grub na legs mod 'on kyang dge sbyor gnod/ /gsungs pa'i tshig rigs de
tsam yang snang bas/ /'di yi dgongs gzhi gang la dgongs pa yin/ /zhes gsungs pa'i dgongs pa'i don yang gsal bar byas pa yin no/ /gsum pa ngos zin pa'i gdams pa nyams su
len pa'i tshul bye brag tu bshad pa la bzhi ste/ gang du nyams su len pa'i gnas/ gang gis nyams su len pa'i

gang zag nyams su blang pa'i gdams pa dngos/ ji ltar nyams su len pa'i tshul lo/ /dang po ni/ bsod snyoms pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs su/ yid dang mthun pa'i gnas su/ zhes dang
/ dregs pa zil gnon du/ dben pa'i gnas su bca' gzhi byas la zhes dang / srog gi spu grir/ gnas ni dur khrod la sogs su/ /zhes dang / bram ze chen pos lha mo'i gzhung
du/ gnas ni dur khrod dam/ shing drung ngam/ gcong rong ngam/ khang stong ngam/ dben pa'i gnas su phyin la zhes sogs gsungs shing / mdor na sgrub khang la sogs pa dben zhing
yid dang mthun pa/ khyad par dam nyams dang grib can gnas pa'i sa ma yin pa zhig gal che'o/ /gnyis pa gang gis nyams su len pa'i gang zag ni/ bram ze chen pos/ bla ma
la gus snying rjer ldan/ /tshul khrims sogs ldan bsdu dngos bzhi/ /sems can don

ldan brtson 'grus ldan/ /rtag tu bsgrub la dga' ba yi/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ gzhi dam tshig dang sdom par ldan zhing / bla ma dang chos skyong gdam ngag la yid ches shing the
tshom gyi rtog pa cung zad kyang med pa/ bcos ma ma yin pa snying nas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rin po che srog ltar gces par 'dzin pa/ brtson 'grus dang snying stobs mchog
tu gyur pa/ thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes su gnang ba mtha' dag thob cing / phyi nang gsang ba'i man ngag la sgro 'dogs legs par chod pa'i gang zag cig go
/de ltar na rdo rje theg pa nas bshad pa'i dam tshig dang sdom pa mtha' dag rgyab tu bskyur nas/ bsnyen sgrub mthar phyin par mi byed pa gtor tshogs che ba tsam dang /
dbyangs dang rol mo'i 'ur chem gyis bstan srung khol du 'dod pa rnams ni blun spyod kho na ste/ srung ma ye shes pa 'di rnams kyis ni gdul bya'i snang ngor/

sngon rdo rje 'chang dang bla ma gong ma rnams kyi spyan sngar sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa srung zhing / dam tshig can skyong bar khas blangs pas/ dam tshig dang ldan pa'i rnal
'byor pas bstan pa dang sems can gyi don du dam rdzas kyis mchod cing / bskul ba na sngon gyi thugs bskyed kyi dbang gis 'phrin las rnams 'bad med du bsgrub pa yin gyi/
gzhan ma dag pa sha chang la sred pa'i rtogs nyams kyi snang ba cung zad kyang med pas/ sangs rgyas la sems can gyi rgyas bkab byed pa rgod bro bar gda'/ des na chos ma
yin pa'i bya ba thams cad la 'dzem med du zhugs shing / gtor chog gi bshar sbyangs tsam re byas pa'i sdug yus kyis ming bstan pa dang sems can gyi don du btags nas/ rang
re'i nye du'am khang gzhis phra mo tsam re'i phyir du zhe sdang chos brgyad drag pos kun nas bslangs te nyam thag pa'i nga ro dang bcas pas/ sha dang zan gyi ri bo/ khrag
dang chang gi rgya mtsho bskyil/ stong gsum

rnga dang bse chal gyis bkang ste bos kyang / 'di dag la ye shes kyi spyan yod pa'i phyir thogs med du mkhyen nas thugs kyis gtan nas khrel bar 'gyur zhing / dam tshig dang
sdom par mi ldan pas mchod gtor phul kyang mi bzhes par bshad do/ /'jig rten pa dag gi 'byung bo mgo bskor ba'i phyir gyi mchod pa dang mi 'dra bas legs par bsam pa gal
che'o/ /gsum pa nyams su blang pa'i gdam ngag dngos ni/ rdo rje gur las/ slob dpon la rtag sdang ba dang / /dkon mchog gsum la 'khrug ldan dang / /sems can du ma gsod pa
rnams/ /rang gi yan lag sha bcad de/ /nag po chen pos za bar 'gyur/ /zhes dang / sgrub thabs kyi rgya gzhung las/ slob dpon la smod bstan la sdang / /dam tshig la 'chal mtshams
med byed/ /de rnams bsgral bar bya ba yin/ /gzhan du dam tshig nyams par

'gyur/ /zhes dang / dregs pa zil gnon du/ 'di'i phan yon ni/ tshe 'dir dgos pa 'grub/ phyi mar lam sna 'dren gnod byed dgra bgegs 'dul/ gsol ba ci btab 'grub par 'gyur/ zhes
dang / de sogs nag po chen po yi/ /sbyor ba'i yon tan bsam mi khyab/ /ces gsungs pas spyir mgon po 'di la brten nas thun mong gi dngos grub thams cad 'grub par nus shing
/ lhag par snyigs ma lnga bsdo ba'i dus 'dir nag phyogs la dga' ba'i mi ma yin pa dag gis/ spyir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rin po che 'di nyid ma rungs par byed pa dang
/ sems can rnams kyang log pa'i lam la sbyor zhing phan bde'i rtsa lag 'phrog pa dang / bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu dam pa rnams kyi 'tsho ba rkyen med du 'joms par byed cing
rang gi bka' drin nos pa'i rdo rje slob dpon gyi sku la bsdo ba sogs dang / mtshams med kyi las byung rgyal du spyod pa/

de'i dbang gis 'gro ba de dag kyang mnar med la sogs pa'i gnas su yun ring zhing dos drag pa'i sdug bsngal myong ba'i gnas tshul legs par bsam ste/ las 'jam po gsum gyis bzlog
pa'i thabs la 'bad/ de dag gang gis kyang bzlog par ma nus na/ snying rje chen pos kun nas bslangs te/ 'di'i bsnyen bsgrub mthar phyin pas mngon spyod kyi las la brtson
par bya'o/ /de ltar bsgrubs pas bsgrub bya de dag ngan song gi rgyu 'bras las bsgral te thar lam la bkod pa dang / bstan pa dang sems can la phan bde 'byung bas/ de'i
stobs kyis rang rgyud la'ang bsod nams kyi tshogs rlabs po che bde blag tu rdzogs par 'gyur ba'o/ /yul de lta bu min pa la rang 'dod kyis kun nas bslangs te drag po'i las
sbyor brtsams na dam tshig nyams pas nag po chen po khros te rang nyid la chad pas gcod cing / rdo rje dmyal ba mi zad pa'i gnas su skye bar gdon mi za bar gsungs pas/ tshul
'di la

bag yod cing rang nyid la brtse bas mi 'dor ba cis kyang gal che'o/ /bzhi pa ji ltar nyams su len pa'i tshul la gsum ste bsnyen pa/ sgrub pa/ las la sbyor ba'o/ /'di gsum la
bod pa/ rbad pa/ bsad pa zhes pa'i tha snyad kyang mdzad cing / dper na skyes bu dpa' bo g.yul 'gyed pa'i dgra thabs dang tshul mtshungs pa yin te/ skyes bu des thog mar
de 'dra'i g.yul 'gyed par nus pa'i mi dag la mgu ba'i gtam smra/ zas gos khang gzhis sogs dpag med byin nas dga' ba ru ma gyur gyi bar de srid du 'bad rtsol drag pos 'gugs
par byed pa ltar/ 'dir yang dam tshig dang sdom pa legs par bsrung zhing / lha'i rnal 'byor dang sngags kyi bzlas brjod dang mchod gtor la rtse gcig tu 'bad pas/ zla
ba drug la sogs pa'i tshe mgon po 'khor bcas bdag nyid la nye bar gyur pa'i rtags 'byung ba ni bsnyen pa'o/ /de nas dpung gi tshogs bsdus te go khrab bskon/ mtshon cha

rnams brdar/ rta dang glang po sogs zhon nas chas pa la dgra che ge mo 'di'o/ /yul che ge mo 'di zhes ngo sprad pas de rnams thogs med du g.yul ngor zhugs pa ltar/ 'brub khung
dang / thun rdzas dang / 'khrul 'khor dang / ming rus bla btags te de dag dang ldan pa'i lingga sogs bca' zhing / sgrub pa'i dmigs pa dang sngags bzlas pas de'i rtags
'byung ba ni bsgrub pa'o/ /de ltar g.yul bskyed cing 'khrug pa'i tshe/ rta glang rgyug cing mchongs pa dang / gri mtshon 'debs pa dang / zhags pa 'phen pa sogs drag tu byas
pas pha rol po bsad pa dang / bcings pa dang / yul 'phrog pa sogs rang phyogs yid tshim par 'gyur ba ltar/ bsad pa'i sngags dang / dmigs pa dang / thun brabs pa dang
/ sbyin sreg sogs byas pas/ phyi rol tu dgra bgegs la nad dug mtshon dang khrag skyug pa sogs kyis btab ste/

mi snang bar gyur pas sgrub pa'i 'bras bu mngon sum du thon pa'i rmi lam du chos skyong rnams zhal pho 'don pa sogs 'byung ste/ de 'dra'i las grub pa'i g.yul ston dang 'dra
bar/ srung ma rnams la gtang rag mnga' gsol byed pa dang / de dag gi skabs su 'phral dpes kyi 'gro mtshams gzab dgos pa ltar/ bogs 'don gegs sel gnad la mkhas pa ni med
kha med kyi man ngag dam pa'o/ /bsnyen pa las su rung ba'i gang zag gis/ /bsgrubs pa'i rtags dang mtshan ma nges byas nas/ /las sbyor nyams su len 'di sarga 'am/ /go rim
'khrul pa med pa'i man ngag gnad/ /bar skabs kyi tshigs su bcad pa'o/ /gsum pa rnyed bkur lha 'dod yon la longs spyod pa lta bu'i dpal 'byor gyi rgyun ma nub pa ni/ de yang
lha rnams 'dod yon che zhing dpal 'byor gyi bde bas rang gzhan kun 'tsho ba ltar/ sgrub pa pos kyang rang gi chos skyong la tshogs dang /

mchod pa dang / gtor ma rnams bzang zhing rgya che ba rgyun ma chad par phul nas/ man ngag nyams len la brtson par byas na chos skyong rnams mnyes te las bzhi'i 'phrin las
lhun grub tu 'byung ba ni rten 'brel gyi chos nyid yin pas na de skad ces bya'o/ /'di la gsum ste/ sngon 'gro rten dang mchod gtor bshams pa/ dngos gzhi bsnyen bsgrub las
gsum gyi rim pa/ zhar byung thor bu'i man ngag bstan pa'o/ /dang po la gsum ste rten bshams pa/ gtor ma bshams pa/ mchod pa bshams pa'o/ /dang po la bzhi ste/ phyi'i rten
dang / nang gi rten dang / gsang ba'i rten dang / de kho na nyid kyi rten no/ /'di dag kyang mkhas grub singha dhwa dzas/ ru mtshon rta nag g.yag nag dang / /lug nag khyi
nag bya nag rnams/ /man ngag bzhin du bcas pa ni/ /phyi rten yin gyis 'bad par bya/ /

nang rten tshogs gtor mchod rdzas rnams/ /mtshan nyid ldan pa'i bris sku'am/ /rten gyi dkyil 'khor drung du bshams/ /mkhas shing brtson 'grus ldan pas bca'/ /gri snying la
brten sngags 'khor lo/ /gsang rten rtsa gsum 'khor lo lnga/ /rlung sbyor bla ma yi dam dang / /lta bas rgyas btab de kho na/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar yin zhing / lag tu blang
ba'i rim pa 'di rnams re re la'ang / thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i bca' tshul re re so sor yod pas gong ma'i man ngag dang bla ma'i snyan brgyud las shes par bya'o/
/gnyis pa la gsum ste/ rtag gtor dang / 'dzin gtor dang / rgyun gtor ro/ /dang po ni dus rtag tu 'jog pa'i gtor ma lhar bskyed pa'o/ /gnyis pa ni/ lo zla ba'i bar dus
gsum du 'bul zhing / nyi shu dgu lta bu la phul nas gsar pa bca' ba'o/ /'di la brten gtor yang zer/ gsum

pa ni/ thun bzhi la sogs par gsar du bcas shing thun re'i mthar 'bul ba'o/ /'di la ming gi rnam grangs thun gtor/ mgyogs gtor/ las gtor/ 'phral gtor rnams so/ /'di la rnam
grangs kyi sgo nas dbye na/ dam rdzas rgyan gyi gtor ma/ dpal gyi zhal zas/ 'dzam bu tri pa'i zhal zas/ dmar chen bshos bu dang bzhi'o/ /gzhan dam tshig gi rten dang / las
sgrub pa'i gteng par 'dzin pa'i gta' gtor zhes pa zhig kyang bshad cing / 'di rnams la snod dang / rgyu dang / dbyibs dang / kha dog dang / mtheb kyu'i grangs dang / rtsig
tshul dang / gzungs 'jug tshul dang / rgyan dang / bskyed tshul dang / byin gyis brlabs te 'bul ba dang / mthar gtong tshul la sogs pa dang / zhar byung gtor bsngos/
gtor sgrub/ gtor 'bul rnams kyi khyad par zhi rgyas dbang drag gi mi 'dra ba'i tshul/

gtor ma lhar sgrub pa/ dam rdzas su sgrub pa/ dgra bgegs su sgrub pa sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig yod cing / rje sa chen yab sras dang / dam pa sogs tshad ldan gyi yi ge
dang / man ngag dang ldan pa'i bla ma'i phyag len dang gsung las 'byung ba ltar ston shes pa'i sngags 'chang zhig la ltos dgos pa de kho nar yod do/ /de ltar mgon po'i bsnyen
bsgrub las gsum thams cad gtor ma la brten pa kho nar snang bas/ 'di'i man ngag mtha' chod par ma shes na/ ci tsam bsgrubs kyang mi 'grub cing / 'grub pa ltar snang
yang / mthar mi shis pa'i rgyur 'gyur bar dam pas gtor ma'i yi ge las gsal bar bshad pas skal ldan dag gis go bar mdzod/ ding sang ni kha cig yi dam 'ga' zhig gi gtor ma
zlum por bshad pa'i rtags la brten nas de ltar byed/ kha cig mthu che zhing 'jigs par yong snyam nas gru gsum kho nar byed/ mdor na bla ma gong ma tshad ldan dag gi man
ngag gi yi ge

dang / snyan brgyud ldan pa'i bla ma'i man ngag dang bral zhing / phyag len mthong yang tshad mar mi 'dzin pa rang bzo kho na la longs spyod cing / rang nyid kyi blo bzo byas
pa de dang ma mthun na lung rigs kyi sgrub byed gcig kyang med par zhe thag pa nas ngan smras kyi smre sngags phyogs bcur bsgrags te/ rang gzhan kun gyi dge rtsa gcod
pa la brtson pa'i gcan gzan gtum po'i rnam thar skyong ba lta bu'ang 'ga' mthong ngo / /'di lta bu la dgra bgegs zhi zhing dngos grub 'byung ba nam mkha'i padmo'i zlos gar
yin pas legs par bsam zhing / gzu bor gnas pa'i blos spang bar rigs so/ /des na 'dir rjes 'jug rnams rnam dbye shes pa'i phyir/ gtor ma gsum sogs kyi rnam gzhag 'phros
don dang bcas pa cung zad bshad na/ gong du bstan pa ltar/ gtor ma la rtag gtor/ brten gtor/ rgyun gtor dang gsum/ dang po ni/ gtor ma chos skyong du bskyed

nas bskal pa chags 'jig gi bar du bzhugs su gsol ba'o/ /de yang gtor ma dngos gzhi gzungs dang bcas pa lhar bskyed pa yin gyi mtheb kyu rnams ni dus bzhir gso zhing bdud rtsir
byin gyis brlabs nas bsngo ba'o/ /gnyis pa ni chos skyong lcam dral nyid la gtor ma lag len ltar bshams nas/ de'i steng du lcam dral bskyed nas gtor ma de la 'bral med
du bzhugs par gsol ba gdab/ dus bzhir gsol zhing / dus bzhir bsngo'o/ /mthar gtong ba'i tshe/ gtor ma tshab bshams grub nas khang pa'i yang thog la sogs par spyi stabs
byas nas 'bul ba'o/ /'di ni dam tshig gi rten du 'dzin pa'i gtor ma yin pas 'dzin gtor zhes kyang bya'o/ /'di la yi ge slob dpon padmas mdzad pa yod cing / de nyid las/ bzhed
dgu 'byung bar byin gyis brlabs/ /de steng padma nyi ma'i steng / /lhag pa'i lha ni bzhi rdzogs bskyed/ /de 'og lcam dral bskyed gzhug cing / /

gdan 'bul dam bzhag gtor ma bsngo/ /gtor ma de la 'bral med du/ /bzhugs par bsam la gsol ba gdab/ /rten 'brel snying pos rab gnas bya/ /zhes bshad pa dang / dam pas/ rtag tu
mi 'bral 'grogs pa'i phyir/ /brten gtor chen pos thugs dam bskang / /zhes pa rnams dgongs pa'i gnad gcig tu 'grig pa yin no/ /gta' gtor ni/ pu tra sogs la gta' gtor zur
brgyad pa bshams nas/ las 'di zhes bgyi ba sgrub par gyis shig da bzod ster ro zhes go bar byas nas/ dus gsum la sogs par kha gso zhing byin gyis brlabs nas mi bsngo bar
bzhag las grub pa dang / cho ga bzhin bsngos nas 'bul ba de'o/ /'di ni gtor ma gta' mar bzung nas las myur du bsgrub tu 'jug pas na gta' gtor ro/ /'di la yi ge rje sa chen
gyis mdzad pa me 'bar ma'i nang na bzhugs shing / rgyun gtor ni/ thun gsum

la sogs par gsar ba bca' zhing bsngos nas de 'phral 'bul ba ste/ dam pas rtag tu 'phrin las mdzad pa'i phyir/ /rgyun gyi gtor mas thugs dam bskang / /zhes pa 'di yin no/ /'di
la thun gtor dang / 'phral gtor dang / mgyogs gtor zhes kyang bya/ kha cig 'bul gtor zhes kyang zer ro/ /dus deng sang gi sa skya pa'i sngags 'chang dag gtor ma gsum gyi
rnam dbye 'di bzhin phyed par gyis shig gtor bsngos kyi cho ga'i go rim la rje rdo rje 'chang gi phyag len la gdong bzhi pa'i rjes su las mgon gyi bskyed chog byas nas/
gtor ma 'bul bar mdzad/ zhal ngo nang brgyud las 'ongs pa'i brgyud pa 'di pa dag gdong bzhi pa'i rjes su pu tra la bskyed chog logs su byas na 'khor rkyang du bsgrub par
song bas cung mi shis pas/ lcam dral dang lhan cig tu bskyed cing dpon 'gro g.yog 'gro'i tshul du spyan 'dren dam bzhag byas la/ 'bul ba'i tshe gtor ma'i go rim dang mthun

par gdong bzhi pa'i rjes su 'bul ba'am/ yang na lcam dral gyi gtor sngags kyi rjes la a li a li ma sogs kyis phul kyang shin tu legs shing thun mong ma yin pa'i phyag len yin
no/ /pu tra sogs lcam dral dang lhan cig tu bskyed nas/ lcam dral gyi rjes la gtor ma phul bas chog pa ni/ yar lung pa'i gtor chog yi ge las kyang gsal bar bshad pas phyag
len 'khrul pa med do/ /sa paN yan chad du lcam dral gnyis kyi mtshams nas pu tra'i gtor ma 'bul yang / ding sang gdong bzhi pa'i 'og tu 'byung ba ni 'phags pa rin po
che nas byung ba yin te/ de nyid rgya nag tu bzhugs dus skabs shig pu tra la las shig bcol bas yun ring ma 'grub/ de nas gdong bzhi pa la bcol bas 'phral du 'grub pa byung
bas/ de man chad du las mgon gyi sngon la gdong bzhi pa la 'bul bar mdzad pa yin no zhes

pa'i gtam rgyud las shes so/ /de dag gis ni rje tshar chen gyi mgon po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ gtor chog skabs su rje btsun e waM pas/ /lcam dral las
mgon bar du gdong bzhi pa'i/ /gtor chog mdzad pas 'og ma 'khor rkyang du/ /bsgrub par song ngam min na 'khor rkyang gi /sgrub thabs ngos bzung ci yin gong ma yis/ /'phral
rtsub mthar mi shis par bshad pa ci/ /arYa'i gtam rgyud 'og tu gtor ma tsam/ /yang na gzhi bdag yan chad sbags sgrub 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa'i dgongs don yang gsal bar byas
pa yin no/ /de ltar gtor ma gsum gyi rnam gzhag mdo tsam bshad nas/ 'phros don la gtor ma'i dbyibs dang / byin rlabs sogs ji ltar bya ba'i tshul/ bskang bshags kyi go
rim dang / gtor sgrub kyi don bshad pa/ gtor bzlog gi rnam gzhag la dogs pa dpyad pa/ gtor ma spyi stabs mdzad tshul la phyag

len mi 'dra ba'i rnam gzhag bshad pa'o/ /dang po gtor ma dbyibs ji ltar bya ba'i tshul ni/ ding sang rgyun gtor du grags pa/ don la brten gtor du 'gro ba 'di la phyag len thun
mong ba la rdo rje chu'i dam tshig nas bshad pa ltar gtor ma zlum po lnga tshar ram bdun tshar sogs dang / yang dam rdzas glang ru ma zhes pa glang gi rwa rtse bcad pa
lta bu'i dbyibs can du mdzad pa yang skabs 'gar snang zhing / phyag len thun mong ma yin pa dam pa kun dga' grags sogs kyi rgyun/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang dang / sa lo
chen po/ sngags 'chang yab sras rnams la bka' babs pa brgyud pa 'di pa'i srol la/ yi dam mkha' 'gro spyi gtor gzhi bdag gsum po la zlum po/ mgon chen la dpal bshos zur gsum
pa/ lha mo la de dang 'dra ba/ zhal la stod zur gsum che ba gcig la/ chung ba bzhis bskor ba/ pu tra la zur

brgyad pa/ gzhan yang bskang gtor la rgyas par byed na/ gtor ma zur gsum pa khrag dang smug rtsi sogs kyis dmar nag spel nas byugs pa mgon po/ lha zhal/ pu tra/ dkar bdud sogs
lha grangs dang mnyam pa'am/ bla ma 'ga' zhig bco lnga mdzad par yang grags shing / thams cad mar gyis brgyan phyag mtshan me ris sogs kyis spras pa/ rgyun gtor ram thun
gtor ni/ lcam dral 'khor bcas la rgyas par na snying gzugs byas pa gnyis/ gdong bzhi pa la yang gnyis te bzhi/ bsdu na zur gsum pa bzhi 'am bdun/ de dag thams cad mthong
ba brgyud pa'i phyag len ltar ro/ /mdos bskang sngags drug dang phyag rgya drug gis byin gyis brlabs pa ni dam pas bshad de/ bskang gso chos nyid ma las/ mdos yod na
sngags drug dang phyag rgya drug gis byin gyis brlabs zhes gsungs pa yin la/ gtor mdos gnyis ka yang sngags

drug sogs kyis byin gyis rlob pa ni/ sangs rgyas spyan nas brgyud pa'i mdos kyi bskang bzlog las bshad de/ de nyid las/ gtor mdos sngags drug dang phyag rgya drug gis 'dod
yon lngar byin gyis brlabs te/ zhes gsungs pa'o/ /'di'i phyag len ni chab gtor klu gtor sogs na gsal bar yod cing / ngor e wa~M chos ldan na bskang gso'i tshe yang phyag
len la yod par snang ngo / /sngags drug 'di dag ni gtso bor rgyud sde 'og ma'i sngags yin kyang / bla med du yang sbyor ba'i rgyu mtshan ni/ sngags 'di dag sbyangs sgyur
sogs la ched du bsngags pas so/ /de dag gis ni rje tshar chen gyi mgon po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ rgyun gtor bskang gso'i gtor ma la sogs la/ /rang
dga'i 'dod rigs sna tshogs bzo mod kyi/ /gong ma rnam lnga a gnyan sku mched dang / /chos rje bla ma sogs kyis gsal ba ci/ /mdos bskang sngags drug

sogs kyi byin gyis rlob/ /gtor bskang de ltar byed pa'i khu rnying dang / /'di dag rgyud sde 'og ma'i gsang sngags dag /gong du sbyor ba'i dgongs pa mkhyen lags sam/ /zhes
gsungs pa'i dgongs pa'i don yang gsal bar byas pa yin no/ /gnyis pa bskang bshags kyi go rim dang gtor sgrub kyi don bshad pa ni/ bskang ba sngon la byas nas bshags pa rjes
la byas kyang rung zhing / bshags pa sngon la byas nas bskang ba rjes la byas kyang chog mod/ 'phags pas mdzad pa'i bshags pa tshig lhug ma 'di bya na/ bskang gso'i sngon
la byed rigs pa yin te/ 'di nyid rang gi tshig gi go rim la yang / nongs par spyad pa dang / de'i las kyi 'bras bu thams cad zhi bar gyur cig ces pa yan gyis bshags pa
byas nas/ sngags dang phyag rgya dang ting nge 'dzin gyi byin gyis brlabs pa'i mchod sbyin gyi gtor ma zhes sogs man chad kyis bskang ba byas pa yin no zhes bla mas gsungs
la/

yar lung pa seng rgyal gyi gtor sgrub zhag sbrel gyi yi ge las kyang / bshags pa 'di nyid sngon la byas nas/ de'i rjes su bskang ba bshad/ de bzhin du sa skya pa'i zhal ngo
nang brgyud sogs phyag len tshad ldan kun la 'di kho na gnang zhing / de yang bshags pa byed pa'i tshe chos skyong rnams mdun du bsam zhing / rang nyid tha mal par byas
nas byed pa chos rje bla ma'i phyag len yin gsungs pa dang / yang rang yang yi dam chos skyong rnams kyang yi dam du mos nas bshags pa dang / mchod bstod sogs byed pa/ chos
rje sa paN gyi gsung bgros/ na bza' brag phug pa'i phyag len yin gsungs pa'i lugs gnyis snang ba las/ phyi ma 'di nyid legs par gong ma dag bzhed cing / gtor sgrub kyi
go don la bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi slob rgyud rje rdo ring pa dpon slob rnams kyi dgongs bzhed kyi gtso bo ni/ gtor sgrub ces pa gtor ma sgrub cing mchod pa'i

don yin te/ rtag gtor dang 'dzin gtor gang rung chos skyong du bskyed nas gtor ma bsngo ba dang / mchod pa dang / bskang ba dang / bstod pa rnams grub na thams cad dang / bsdu
na gtor bsngo'i rjes su bshags pa dang mchod pa sogs ci rigs pa byas pa ni gtor ma sgrub mchod du 'gyur ba yin/ de skad du yar lung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyi gtor sgrub
kyi yi ge las/ sngon 'gro gtor ma nas dkon mchog dang gtor ma la tshogs phud 'bul ba'i bar sgrub mchod rgyas bsdus gang rung byas la zhes gsungs pa'i dgongs pa dang
mthun pa'i dbang du mdzad nas/ rje tshar pa'i gtor ma gsum gyi rnam gzhag las kyang / zhi rgyas dbang gsum gyi gtor sgrub kyi lag len zhal shes ni/ rtag gtor yod na rab/
med na 'dzin gtor lhar bskyed ces gsungs so/ /don 'di nyid rdzong pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa yang bzhed do/ /khong gis mdzad pa'i

sgrub thabs bdud las rnam rgyal na yang bshad pa snang bas/ des na gtor ma lhar bskyed pa dang ma 'brel na bskang gso dang bstod pa sogs ci rgyas kyang gtor sgrub kyi tha snyad
mi thob ste/ dper na rdul tshon dang ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor gang rung dkyil 'khor du bskyed pa dang ma 'brel na/ mdun bskyed mchod bstod rgyas bsdus gang yin kyang
dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod kyi tha snyad mi thob pa bzhin no/ /gnad 'di ni snying gi dkyil du chongs shig des na bskang bshags dang gtor sgrub la mu bzhi las/ bskang bshags
yin la/ gtor sgrub ma yin pa ni bshad ma thag pa ltar yin zhing / gtor sgrub yin la bskang bshags ma yin pa ni/ gtor ma lhar bskyed pa la gtor bsngo dang / bdud rtsi lnga
mchod dang / bstod pa tsam byed pa'o/ /gnyis ka yin pa ni gtor ma lhar bskyed pa la bskang bshags rgyas pa byed pa'o/ /gnyis ka ma

yin pa ni/ gtor ma lhar bskyed pa dang yang ma 'brel zhing gtor bsngo tsam byed pa'o/ /de lta bu'i gtor sgrub kyi go don 'di rnams ni rje dbang phyug rab brtan dang / mkhan
chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsung las ji ltar 'byung ba bzhin bkod pa yin la/ yang bla ma de dag gi bzhed pas gtor sgrub zhag mang po sbrel nas brgya tshar sogs byed na/
gtor ma lhar bskyed pa dang 'brel ba'i tshar dang po la mchod pa dang bskang ba sogs thams cad rgyas pa/ de nas tshar gzhan la rgyas bsdus byed na/ bskang ba dang bstod pa
gnyis kyis chog cing / de bas bsdu na bshags pa dang bstod pa/ de bas kyang bsdu na bstod pa tsam gyis kyang chog pa yar lung pa'i yi ge las bshad do zhes gsungs shing
/ tshul 'di la dpag na gtor sgrub la bstod pa nges par ma chad pa gcig dgos par bzhed rgyur snang la/ yang bla ma gong ma'i phyag len lugs gcig la/ chos skyong gang la gtor
sgrub brgya

tshar byed pa'i de'i gtor ma yang brgya rtsa bshams/ bskang ba rgyas bsdus gang rigs la grangs bzung bas kyang chog par bzhed cing / de gnyis ka phyag len 'khrul med tshad
thub re re yin par sems so/ /de dag gis rje tshar chen gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ spyir gyi bskang bshags go rim ma nges kyang / /'phags pas bshags pa tshig lhug
mdzad pa 'di/ /'di nyid rang gi go rim bzhugs tshul dang / /brag ngag dbang grags pa/nag pa dang sing yar lung pa seng rgyal/ha'i yi ge dang / /sa lugs ngor rdzong kun gyi
phyag len dang / /mi mthun bzhin du'ang bshags pa rjes su byed/ /'di 'dra'ang rmongs pa'i bskang bshags zhes pa yi/ /tshig tsam dag la zhen pa ma lags sam/ /gtor bsngo
tsam dang gtor sgrub khyad par ci/ /zhes gsungs pa'i dgongs pa'i don yang gsal bar byas pa yin no/ /'dir dam pas mdzad pa'i bskang gso che chung gi ngos 'dzin la bla ma gong
ma rnams

bzhed tshul mi 'dra ba cung zad brjod na/ de yang dam pas mdzad pa'i mdos bskang rgyas pa/ mdos bskang gtor ma thun mong bas bskang ba chos nyid mar grags pa/ bskang gso nag
po mchod rten ma/ dam pa'i bskang gso chung bar grags pa rnams yod pa las/ 'di'i skabs su bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i gsung las/ mdos bskang rgyas pa dang / chos
nyid ma gnyis la dam pas mdzad pa'i bskang gso che chung gi tha snyad byed pa yin gsungs shing / nag po mchod rten ni dam pa'i mdos bskang chen mo las sngags 'chang gzungs
kyi dpal bas zur du phyung ba yin no zhes bzhed la/ rdo rje gdan pa chen po'ang don gyis de ltar zhal gyis bzhes par snang ste/ mdos bskang chen mo dang chos nyid ma'i
lung rgyun bzhugs shing / nag po mchod rten gyi lung tsam yang mi bzhugs par bla ma dag bzhed cing / mus srad pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan pa ni/ mdos bskang

chen mo/ nag po mchod rten/ gzhan bskang gso chung ngu zhig dang gsum la dam pa'i bskang gso rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyi tha snyad mdzad nas them yig sogs gces spras che bar
mdzad do/ /ding sang phal cher ni chos de sus byas dang / rang gi brgyud pa'i phyag srol la gang byed sogs rtog dpyod ci yang mi byed par/ byed mkhan su mang dang / lag
tu dpe cha gang byung dang 'jigs rngams gang che ba zhig nyams su len par snang / bar skabs su 'phros pa'i gtam mo/ /gsum pa gtor bzlog gi rnam gzhag la dogs pa dpyad pa
ni/ rje tshar chen gyi bzhed pas/ spyir sangs rgyas spyan nas brgyud pa'i mdos kyi bskang bzlog sogs yi ge tshad ldan la brten nas bla ma'i man ngag gis brgyan te/ bdag
chen rin po ches mdzad pa'i mdos kyi bskang bzlog gi nang du/ de yang mgon po'i mdos kyis bzlog ces pa rnams/ de yang

mgon po'i gtor mas bzlog /ces 'don pa bsgyur bar gsungs shing / khyad par gyi bskul rnams ni slob dpon padmas mdzad pa dang / mkhas pa yon tan khris mdzad pa rnams yin pas/
de dag gi phyag len rgyas pa rje tshar pa rang gis bsgrigs pa'i rang lugs kyi dmar chen gtor bzlog 'di la ni 'khrul pa med cing / ming yang drag po gtor ma'i man ngag ces
'dogs pa yin la/ gzhan dag gi gtor bzlog la ni khams kyi phyogs na dgra chos zhes bya ba'i gtor bzlog gi lag len/ dbus gtsang 'di na drug cu pa zhes pa'i ming 'dogs pa'i
phyag len rnams la ni khungs dgos te/ dgra chos ni bon la grags pa yin gyis/ lugs 'di la med cing / drug cu pa ni gshin rje pa rnams la grags pa yin gyis/ lugs 'di'i yi
ge gang na yang bshad pa sngar tshar chen rang gis ma gzigs pas/ des na khungs btsal bar bya dgos pa'i gnas yin la/ shol ril drug pa'i nang tshan gyi

gtor ma la brten nas dgra bsad pa ni/ gtor ma dgra bgegs su bskyed nas bsad las byed pa yin pa la/ de ma rtogs pa kha cig gtor ma lhar bskyed pa la 'di'i nyams len byed pa
yang gad mo'i gnas yin no snyam du thugs la bzhag nas/ don gyi dbang de dag la dgongs nas rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i mgon po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/
gtor bzlog ces bya ding sang rlung ltar grags/ /'di nyid tshad ldan yi ge gang la brten/ /de dang mthun pa'i phyag len yod lags sam/ /khams kyi phyogs na dgra chos zhes bya
dar/ /dbus gtsang phyogs 'dir drug cu pa la sogs/ /rngams brjid spros pa shin tu che bar snang / /'di dag rnams la khungs thub ji ltar mchis/ /shog ril drug gi nang tshan
gtor ma 'di/ /dgra bgegs dag tu bsgrub pa'i bsad las yin/ /gzhan dag gtor ma lha ru bskyed bzhin du/ /'di yi nyams len dag tu bzhed

pa ci/ /zhes gsungs pa yin la/ de lta bu'i dri ba'i tshig de dag las/ gtor bzlog ces bya ding sang rlung ltar grags/ /zhes sogs tshig rkang gsum po 'di ni sa skya pa'i chos
skyong gi chos brgyud 'dzin pa'i gtor bzlog mdzad pa po thams cad la dris par snang bas/ so so nas lan 'debs mdzad par 'os pa las/ bdag kho nas 'dir 'bri bar ma nus la/
de bzhin du/ khams kyi phyogs na dgra chos zhes bya dar/ /zhes pa 'di'i lan yang byed pa po dag gis smra bar rigs pas na/ 'dir ni ma bris so/ /des na 'dir ched du bya ba/
'dzam gling bstan pa'i mnga' bdag sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje dang / sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen yab sras rnams kyi rjes su zhugs par khas 'che
ba kho bo cag rnams kyis ni mgon po'i man ngag drug cu pa'i phyag len 'di nyid tshad ldan gyi yi ge rnying ma'i khungs dang 'brel ba zhig ci nas kyang bsgrub dgos rgyur
snang yang / rang re rjes 'jug rnams za

chog tsam don du gnyer ba las/ gsung rab kyi rtog dpyod shin tu chung bar brten/ gong du bkod pa'i dri ba'i tshig rnams la rang lugs kyi rjes 'jug phal cher ni ji snyam du
yang mi sems par btang snyoms su bzhugs par gyur cing / la la ni khungs med par ma 'dod cing / rang gis yang ma rnyed pas/ dri ba mdzad pa por skur pa 'debs par brtson par
gyur la/ mkhas rlom kha cig ni/ mgon po 'di la gshin rje ltar bsgrub pa'i tshul bshad pas/ man ngag de yang 'jigs byed drug cu pa'i rgyas bkab par 'dod pa sogs long ba
'khar 'dzugs kyi rnam thar skyong ba las rgyu mtshan yod par ma mthong na/ kho bo cag gi bsam pa la mgon po'i man ngag drug cu pa 'di'i khungs rnam dag cig rnyed na ci ma
rung snyam pa'i dwangs 'dod kyi dad pa chen po'i ngang nas rang lo nyer gcig lon pa me mo sbrul gyi lo/ dpal sa skya'i gnas mchog chu mig rdzing ga'i bla brang bde mchog
pho

brang zhes bya ba'i skyed mos tshal ga la ba der chos skor gyi yig cha mang po la lta rtog bgyis skabs/ mgon po'i man ngag dpe rnying ma brabs gcig bzhugs pa'i glegs bam zhig
gi khrod na/ shog bu ser mdangs can la yi ge lcags smyug gis bris pa'i las tshogs gtor ma la brten nas dgra bsad pa'i man ngag gi yig chung zhig 'dug pa la bltas pas/
mgon pod me 'bar ma sogs na bzhugs pa'i shog ril drug gi nang tshan de yang ma yin zhing / de las gzhan pa'i gtor ma la brten nas dgra bsad pa'i man ngag gzhan du'ang mi
'dug pas slar zhib tu dpyad cing brtags pas/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i mgon po'i man ngag drug cu pa'i cho ga dgra bgegs gnad gcod kyi spu gri'i rten gzhir gyur
pa'i yi ge rnying ma rje btsun gong ma'am/ dam pa kun dga' grags sogs kyis mdzad pa'i khungs thub cig dgos rgyur 'dug pa las/ kho bos rnyed pa'i yi ge 'di ni

dam pas mdzad pa'i man ngag drug cu pa'i yig chung yin nges par snang bas/ des na sa lo chen po'i gsung rab kyi rten gzhi 'di kho na yin pa'i nges shes khyad par can rnyed
de/ mgon po'i man ngag drug cu pa'i yi ge rnying ma'i khungs tshad ldan 'di lta bu rnyed pa ni/ bla ma dang chos skyong gi thugs rje dang byin rlabs kho nar nges so snyam
pa'i dad pa bcos min rang dbang med par skyes shing / yid dga' bde tshad las 'das pa'i rab dga'i sa thob pa ltar gyur pa lags so/ /de ltar gtor bzlog drug cu pa'i khungs
kyi yig rnying tshad thub de nyid rnyed pa la brten/ rje tshar chen gyi dri ba'i gsung gi lan 'debs byed pa'i spobs pa rnyed de/ dpal sa skya pa'i chos skyong rdo rje gur
gyi mgon po'i las tshogs gtor ma la brten nas dgra bsad pa'i man ngag drug cu pa'i cho ga dgra bgegs gnad gcod kyi spu gri'i rten gzhi'i yi ge rnying ma'i don rnams dris
lan gyi sgo nas legs

par bshad pa log rtog 'joms pa'i lha dbang rdo rje zhes bya ba brtsams nas de'i nang gi brjod don la/ mkhas pa'i dbang po mchog gi dri ba'i gsung bkod pa/ de'i lan btab ste
skal bzang dpyod ldan gzur gnas rnams yid ches bskyed pa/ rgyu mtshan des na rang gi rjes 'jug rnams legs bshad 'di la gces par gzung bar gdams pa ste/ don tshan gsum du
bsdus nas/ de'i gnyis pa la yi ge rnying ma'i khungs bkod pa de dang da ltar gyi phyag len sbyar te bshad pa dogs pa'i gnas gzhan dpyad pa dang gsum du phye nas/ rang re
sa skya pa'i zhal ngo brgyud pa dang bcas pa rnams phyag len mdzad pa'i drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog 'di nyid yi ge rnying ma'i khungs dang 'brel tshul zhib cing mtha' chod par
bshad yod pas/ blo gsal rtog dpyod can rnams tshul 'di skor la nges shes rnyed par 'dod na kho bos byas pa'i dris lan gyi yi ge de nyid la blta bar gyis shig bzhi pa gtor
ma spyi stabs mdzad tshul la

phyag len mi 'dra ba'i rnam gzhag bshad pa ni/ mgron gshegs pa'i rjes su byed pa dang / mgron gshegs pa'i gong du byed pa'i lugs gnyis snang ba las/ dang po ni chos rje bla
ma'i kyai rdor mngon rtogs sogs las bshad cing / gnyis pa ni/ yar lung pa sogs kyi phyag len yin pas gnyis ka yang lugs tshad ldan re yin par gsungs shing / da lta phyag
len la snga phyi gnyis ka mdzad pa 'di yin la/ gtor ma phyir 'bul ba'i dgos pa la/ thun gtor phyir 'bul ba ni thun gcig gi bya ba rdzogs pas/ thun gsham bsdud pa'i ched
yin par snang la/ bskang gtor dang brten gtor rnams phyir 'bul ba ni ched du gtad pa'i dmigs pa gsal ba'i ched dang / gtang rag gi tshul du yin par bzhed cing / de yang gtor
ma rnams khang pa'i yang thog la sogs par khyer te dgra phyogs su kha bstan nas 'bul ba ni/ gtor ma 'di

snoms la dgra bo bsad pa'i las gyis shig ces pa'i don yin zhing / sa skya la sogs pa mgon po bzhugs pa'i phyogs la dmigs nas 'bul ba ni mgron bzhugs pa'i phyogs su dmigs nas
'bul bas thugs mnyes par byed pa'i dgos pa khyad par can yod pa yin no zhes brgyud ldan gyi bla ma rnams gsungs so/ /de dag gis ni mgon po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam
rab dkar las/ chos rje bla ma'i kyai rdor mngon rtogs sogs/ /yig cha phal las mgron gshegs spyi btab bye/ /gzhan dag de yi gong du byed par snang / /'di nyid 'bul yul
phyir 'bul dgos pa gang / /zhes gsungs pa'i dgongs pa'i don yang gsal bar byas pa yin no/ /de ltar gtor ma'i rim pa 'phros don dang bcas pa bshad zin nas/ gsum pa mchod
pa'i rnam gzhag la gsum ste/ las 'jam po gsum gyi mchod pa/ drag po'i mchod pa'o/ /de re re la'ang

phyi nang gsang gsum gyi mchod pa gsum gsum yod do/ /gnyis pa dngos gzhi la bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi rim pa la gsum ste/ gzhi bsnyen nam rgyun gyi bsnyen pa/ sgrub bsnyen
nam kha gso'i bsnyen pa'o/ /de la gnyis te/ thun mong ba dang / thun mong ma yin pa'o/ /dang po la bzlas pa'i grangs/ bzlas pa'i go rim/ bzlas pa'i dmigs pa/ ma 'grub na
spogs pa'i cho ga'o/ /phyi ma 'di la bzhi ste/ bsnyen pa'i bzlas pa/ mi 'khu ba'i bzlas pa/ srog 'phrog gi bzlas pa/ srog gi yang tig blang ba'i bzlas pa'o/ /gnyis pa thun
mong ma yin pa la gnyis te/ sngon 'gro dang / dngos gzhi'o/ /dang po sngon 'gro la brgyad de/ bsgral ba'i zhing gsal btab pa/ sa bon bskyed pa/ dam tshig bsre ba/ dam tshig
bsgrags pa/ srog dbang du bya ba/ snying po bsdu ba/ thig le bsdus te nye bar bya ba/ gzi mdangs

dbang du bya'o/ /gnyis pa dngos gzhi la bzhi ste/ bzlas pa'i grangs/ bzlas pa'i go rim/ bzlas pa'i dmigs pa/ ma grub na spogs pa'i cho ga'o/ /phyi ma 'di la bsnyen pa'i bzlas
pa/ mi 'khu ba'i bzlas pa/ srog 'phrog pa'i bzlas pa/ srog gi yang tig blang ba'i bzlas pa'o/ /'di'i dang po la hU~M 'khor tshul du bzlas pa/ hU~M 'pho tshul du bzlas
pa/ hU~M phyed bcad du bzlas pa/ dngos grub 'byin pa'i tshul du bzlas pa'o/ /gnyis pa rgyun gyi bzlas pa la gnyis te/ bdag don lha nye ba'i tshul gyi bzlas pas/ gnas skabs
las bzhi sgrub pa'i bzlas pa'o/ /'dir bsnyen pa'i dogs dpyod cung zad brjod na/ spyir mgon po 'di nyid kyi bsnyen pa la/ gzhi'i bsnyen pa/ dus rgyun gyi bsnyen pa/ sgrub
pa'i bsnyen pa/ kha gso'i bsnyen pa dang bzhi'am/ bsdu lugs kyi gnyis sogs su yod pa'i dang po gzhi

bsnyen la/ yi dam gyi bsnyen pa sngon du song na rab/ ma song yang mgon po yi dam ltar bsgrub pa zhes bya ba bdag bskyed la brten pa nyid la gtso bor phyag len mdzad pas na
skyon med de/ rang sha rang gis mi za ba'i dpes 'khu ldog kyang chung ba yin no/ /mgon po yi dam ltar bsgrub pa'i khungs kyang yod de/ byung lugs gtor ma dang bcas pa'i
khrigs gong mas mdzad pa las/ yi dam ltar bsgrub pa dang / bka' bsgo'i tshul du bsgrub pa gnyis zhes dang / yi dam ltar bsgrub na bdag mgon por bskyed pa yin gsungs/ zhes
gsal bar gsungs pas so/ /chos rgyus chung pa kha cig mgon po la bdag bskyed med zer ba yod kyang / de dag ni yig rnying rnams las mgon po la bdag bskyed mang du bshad pa
dang / las sbyor gyi skabs su rang nyid lha mo sogs su yang bskyed par bshad pa dang /

khyad par rjes gnang gi yi ge phal cher las/ rjes gnang gi gzhi lus sprul pa'i skabs su slob ma mgon por bskyed par bshad pa rnams ma mthong bar bab col du smra bar zad do/
/rang gis cung zad shes shing rgyus yod nas smras na 'os yin mod/ rgyus med la mchu'i rnam 'gyur mang na rang gi de nyid ston pas gzab 'tshal lo zhes kyang gdams so/ /bsnyen
pa'i grangs la rje bla ma 'ga' zhig gi zhal rgyun las/ rab yi ge bdun ma la 'bum phrag drug cu re bzhi bzla dgos par gsungs la/ de'i dgongs pa yang tha mas 'bum phrag
bcu drug bzla dgos pas/ 'bring la de nyis 'gyur brtsis pas 'bum phrag so gnyis/ rab la 'bring gi de yang nyis 'gyur brtsis pas drug cu re bzhir 'gyur ba yin no zhes bzhed
cing / yang sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i gsung las/ rab 'bum phrag brgya'am lnga bcu/ 'bring nyi shu rtsa gcig gam bcu/ tha ma bdun dang

kha skong gcig dang brgyad bzla bar gsungs pas/ lugs gnyis ka 'khrul med kyi phyag len re re yin no/ /de dag gis ni rje tshar chen gyi mgon po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam
rab dkar las/ bsnyen pa'i skabs su yi dam bsnyen pa ni/ /ma song na'ang byas pas chog lags sam/ /chog na de yi gsal kha tshad ldan ci/ /mi chog na ni mgon po yi dam ltar/
/bsgrub pa zhes bya bdag bskyed la brten pa/ /'di yi tshig gi nus pa 'chad tshul dang / /don gyi dgos pa gang yin de ltar na/ /yi dam la yang gong bsnyen bzhed lags
sam/ /zhes gsungs pa'i dgongs pa'i don yang gsal bar byas pa yin la/ gnyis pa bsgrub pa la gsum ste/ phyi nor bsrung ba gnod sbyin pho mo'i tshul du bsgrub pa/ nang bsad
pa gshin rje pho mo'i tshul du bsgrub pa/ gsang ba las mkhan pho mo'i tshul du bsgrub pa'o/ /

dang po la sngon 'gro dang / dngos gzhi'o/ /dang po la gsum ste/ phyi rten phyi ru bcas te phyi'i nor rdzas dang yo byad bsrung ba/ nang rten nang du bcas te las kyi dngos
grub sgrub pa/ gsang rten gsang bar bcas te gsang ba mkha' 'gro'i 'khu ldog spong ba'o/ /bar pa 'di la gnyis te/ bskyed pa rten gyi 'khor lo yan lag bzhi dang bcas pa'i bca'
thabs/ bsad pa las kyi 'khrul 'khor 'brub khung lingga dang bcas pa'i bca' thabs so/ /gnyis pa dngos gzhi la gnyis te dkyus kyi sgrub pa dang / 'khu ldog spong ba'o/
/dang po la brgyad/ bdag bskyed/ mdun bskyed/ mchod bstod/ mkhyen gsol/ dgug 'dren/ kha sbyor dbye ba/ bcings mnan/ 'dzab 'dren pa las la sbyar ba'o/ /kha sbyor dbye ba la
brgyad de/ rang bzhin gyi gnas pa'i ye shes sems pa'i kha sbyor dbye ba/ bsgoms pa'i ye shes sems dpa'i kha sbyor dbye ba/ bla ma'i

byin rlabs dbang bskur gyis/ tshogs kyis/ sngags pa nang 'khrug gis/ 'go ba'i lha'i/ 'byung ba'i kha sbyor dbye ba/ srog gis kha sbyor dbye ba'o/ /gnyis pa la bzhi ste/ 'khu
ldog 'byung ba'i rgyu/ byung ba'i rtags/ byung ba'i nyes dmigs/ mi 'byung ba'i thabs so/ /phyi ma 'di la bzhi ste/ phyi rol lha sogs gnad drug gi man ngag la brten nas/
'khu ldog spangs te grogs ltar du 'khol ba/ nang sngags tshogs lha drug gi man ngag la brten nas bzlog rdugs ldang sogs kyi skyon drug spangs te 'khor 'bangs ltar 'khol
ba/ gsang ba sems kyi gnad lnga la brten nas bzlog rdugs ldang sogs skyon drug spangs te/ ji ltar bcol ba'i las thams cad sgrub pa'i bran g.yog ltar 'khol ba/ bsgrubs kyang
rtags med na ji ltar bya'o/ /dang po la drug ste/ sgrub pa'i bca' thabs

kyi gnad/ gnyan po lha'i gnad/ gnyen po sngags kyi gnad/ rdzas kyi rdo rjes dam la gzhag pa'i gnad/ las mkhan mya ngan las 'da' ba'i gnad/ drag sngags go bzlog gi gnad do/
/gnyis pa la drug ste/ chos skyong rang la bzlog na ji ltar bya ba/ dgra la rdugs na ji ltar bya ba/ bar du ldang na ji ltar bya ba/ 'khyams na ji ltar bya ba/ las ma btub
na ji ltar bya ba/ rbod ka 'dom na ji ltar bya ba'o/ /gsum pa la lnga ste/ mal 'og rdzas kyi gnad la brten nas ma mgon gyi srog snying ltar bzung ba'i man ngag rno zhing
myur ba'i ngar 'don pa spu gri so 'debs kyi man ngag btsan po'i mkhar du zhugs shing byin rlabs dang nus mthu'i stobs 'don pa'i ched du ga'u kha sbyor gyi man ngag gzi
brjid dang nus mthu'i rtsal 'don pa'i ched du ngan sngags kyi dug mda' khong du 'phangs pa'i man ngag chos skyong gi srog snying

dbang du bya ba gsang ba yang tig gi man ngag go /'di la gnyis te/ ngo bo la brten nas srog gi yang thig blang ba dang / rnam pa la brten nas srog gi yang tig blang ba'o/ /bzhi
pa la gnyis te/ rtags mang na ji ltar bya ba/ nang rtags byung yang phyi rtags ma byung na ji ltar bya ba'o/ /dang po la gnyis te/ tshogs bsags shing bsnyen pa skyar
ba/ dam tshig gsos te bsnyen pa bskyar ba'o/ /gnyis pa la gnyis te/ srog phur gyi lha gnad la dbab pa dang / las byas nas lha slar gso ba'i cho ga'o/ /dang po la bzhi ste/
ar la gtad pa/ ur la mnan pa/ bcud la bor ba/ shi sa bstan pa'o/ /gsum pa las sbyor la dgu ste/ 'khor los bsad pa/ tsha ba dug nad kyis bsad pa/ phur bus bsad pa/ thun
gyis bsad pa/ dam shing gis/ ba dan gyis/ sbyin sreg gis/ mnan pas/ zor gyis bsad pa dang dgu'o/ /gsum pa/ thor bu'i

man ngag bshad pa ni spyir bsam gyis mi khyab pa yod kyang / 'dir skabs su bab pa thun mong ba'i shog ril bcu dang / thun mong ma yin pa'i shog ril drug ste bcu drug las/ dang
po ni/ sngon 'gro bshom gyi shog ril/ bris sku sgrub pa'i shog ril/ gri gug/ thod pa/ gaNDe/ ral gri/ thug chen/ rnga chen/ kha TwaM kA/ pho nya'i las rim gyi shog ril
dang bcu'o/ /skabs 'dir bris sku shog ril gyi dogs pa'i gnas cung zad dpyad na/ dam pas mdzad pa'i bris sku'i shog ril 'di la gzhal yas khang med pas/ zhing khams tsam
yin gyi dkyil 'khor ma yin la/ 'on kyang shar sgor/ lho sgor/ nub sgor/ byang sgor zhes pa'i tshig rnams ni dkyil 'khor gyi dkyus cung zad shor ba ste/ 'di 'dra'i rigs can
mang du mthong ngo / /'di nas lha gsum ma la dbang bshad pa ni sngon du byung bar bla ma dag bzhed cing / 'on kyang da lta phyag len

gyi rgyun chad par snang ngo / /de dag gis ni rje tshar chen gyi mgon po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ shog ril bcu par grags pa'i bris sku'i skabs/ /bshad
pa 'di nyid zhing khams dkyil 'khor gang / /'di nas lha gsum dag la'ang dbang bshad pa/ /dag gam 'on te rdzun mar bzhed pa lags/ /zhes gsungs pa'i dgongs pa'i don yang gsal
bar byas pa yin zhing / gnyis pa thun mong ma yin pa'i shog ril drug ni/ gtor ma la brten nas dgra bo gsod pa'i shog ril/ gtor ma med pa kha zas la/ dgra bgegs tshogs
su za ba'i/ byad sha lpags pa'i/ rmi lam ngan pa dang ltas ngan pa bzlog pa'i/ gzhan gyi rig sngags dang rbod gtong bzlog pa'i shog ril dang drug go /gnyis pa nang rtsa
gsum 'khor lo brten nas sgrub pa la bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi/ dang po la lnga ste/ snying ga chos kyi 'khor

lo la brten nas thun mong ba'i bzlas pa/ mgrin pa longs spyod kyi 'khor lo la brten nas thun mong ma yin pa'i bzlas pa/ spyi bo bde chen gyi 'khor lo la brten nas dgra bo gsod
pa'i mi 'khu ba'i bzlas pa/ lte ba sprul pa'i 'khor lo la brten nas srog 'phrog pa'i bzlas pa/ gsang gnas bde skyong 'khor lo la brten nas srog gi yang tig blang ba'i
bzlas pa'o/ /gnyis pa bsgrub pa la gsum ste/ dregs pa pho rgyud du bsgrub pa/ dregs pa mo rgyud du bsgrub pa/ dregs pa gnyis med rgyud du bsgrub pa'o/ /de re re la dbang
du bya ba dang byin gyis brlab pa gnyis gnyis yod do/ /gsum pa las sbyar la gnyis te/ thun mong gi dmigs pas spyi'i las la sbyar ba dang / khyad par gyi dmigs pas bye brag
tu las la sbyar ba'o/ /phyi ma 'di la drug ste/ spyi bo bde chen gyi 'khor lo la brten nas zhi ba'i las sgrub pa/ mgrin pa longs spyod kyi 'khor lo la brten nas dbang
dang tshe bsgrub

pa/ snying kha chos kyi 'khor lo la brten nas mngon spyod kyi las bsgrub pa/ lte ba sprul pa'i 'khor lo la brten nas rgyas pa'i las bsgrub pa/ gsang gnas bde skyong gi 'khor
lo la brten nas las sna tshogs bsgrub pa/ 'khor lo thog mtha' gnyis la brten nas 'gal rkyen sel zhing mthun rkyen bsgrub pa'o/ /skabs 'dir nang sgrub la brten pa'i khungs
sogs kyi dogs pa'i gnas cung zad dpyad pa ni/ nang sgrub kyi man ngag zab mo 'di'i khungs ni/ rdo rje gur dang / las gsang ba'i rgyud gnyis la brten par nang sgrub kyi
yig rnying las bshad la/ de yang rdo rje gur las/ de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las nag po chen po 'di nyid rab tu
phyung ngo / /zhes pa'i rgyud tshig 'di nyid spyi don du bshad pas phyi sgrub bstan/ sba sa don du bshad pas nang sgrub bstan par snyan brgyud 'dzin pa'i bla ma gong ma
rnams bzhed cing /

las gsang ba'i rgyud kyis bstan tshul nges pa can zhig sngar ma mthong bas smra bar ma spobs la/ nang sgrub 'di la rtsa gsum la brten pa'i yi ge nyung ngu gong mas mdzad pa
dang / de'i rjes su de nyid cung zad rgyas su btang ba dang / gsang rten lus la bcangs pa'i yig chung dam pas mdzad pa yod pa la/ gzhan yang mahA ka la'i spu gri so 'debs
kyi man ngag ces bya ba ha cang mi nyung tsam zhig kyang 'byung zhing / des na 'di ni nang gi man ngag bsnyen sgrub las gsum cha tshang ba zhig yin par bzhed la/ khyad
par snying ga chos 'khor la brten pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i las sbyor ni/ rdo rje gur las/ de yi spyi bor 'dug nas ni/ /til tsam du ni za bar byed/ /ces pa'i don yin par
bla ma dag gsung ngo / /gzhan yang 'di nyid yig rnying tshad ldan mang po las zur tsam bshad de/ lcam dral gyi rjes gnang gi tho mal los mdzad pa las kyang / yon tan sgrub
pa'i lung sbyin

pa'i skabs su bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi man ngag phyi sgrub dang / nang lus la brten pa rnams sbyin zhes dang / byung lugs gtor ma dang bcas pa'i khrigs las kyang / nang gi
rnal 'byor yin na thun gyi rjes su mgon po 'khor bcas bdag nyid kyi lte bar chos 'byung gru gsum gyi nang du bsdus la gzhag par gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang de 'dra'i rigs
can mang du yod pas/ khungs de dag la brten nas yar lung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyis nang khrid kyi yi ge rgyas pa 'di mdzad cing / kha cig 'di la bka' brgyud pa'i chos
skyong phyag bzhi pa'i man ngag nas rgyas bkab pa yin gyi/ rang lugs la nang gi man ngag las sbyor thor bu ma gtogs khrid rim du byed rgyu med gsungs pa ni/ gong du drangs
pa'i yig rnying de dag kyang ma gzigs par snang zhing / rang nyid la 'di skor gyi rgyus med pa'i de nyid ston par zad do/ /des na nang sgrub 'di la bsnyen sgrub las gsum
gyi

man ngag cha tshang par yod pa mal lo sogs kyis bshad cing / de yod phyin bla mas kyang khrid rim du byas nas bstan/ slob mas kyang dmigs thun du bcad nas bsgom pa la skyon
ci yod soms shig des na zhal ngo nang brgyud las 'ongs pa'i gsang khrid thob pa dag gis bltas na/ yar lung pa'i 'di nang khrid thun mong ba tsam du mthong ste/ 'di las rtsa
nang tsam du lha bskyed par bshad la/ zhal ngo nang brgyud las 'ongs pa la ni rtsa thig rlung gsum dang dbyer med du lha bskyed pa yin zhing / gzhan yang gzhi skye med
dngos po'i gnas tshul la mkhas pa zhes bya ba/ phyi nang gsang gsum gyi dregs pa rgyud gsum ngos bzung nas/ chos thams cad sems nyid gsal stong zung 'jug gi cho 'phrul
du ston pa zab pa las kyang ches zab pa yod do/ /rtsa dang dbyer med du lha bskyed pa ni yig rnying las kyang bshad de/ ro ma'i rtsa mdud dang dbyer med du mgon po rkyang
ma'i rtsa mdud dang dbyer med du lha mo sogs bskyed

par bshad pa'i phyir ro/ /des na zhal ngo nang brgyud kyi khrid 'di ni nang sgrub thun mong ma yin pa yin zhing / phyi sgrub sogs gsum du phye ba'i gsang sgrub yin par bla
ma brgyud pa rnams bzhed pa yin no/ /yang 'di'i las sbyor gyi dmigs pa'i skabs su/ rang dang bsgrub bya'i rtsa rnams la lha bkod nas/ gzhan la gcod pa'i dmigs pa bsgom pa'i
tshe/ phan tshun mtshungs par 'dra ba'i rten 'brel gyi dbang gis gzhan la gnod pa bzhin/ rang gi tshe srog la'ang gnod pa ma yin nam snyam na/ 'di la gnad kyi zhal gdams
'di yod de/ bsgrub bya pha rol po'i rtsa la lha bkod pa ni/ phyag mtshan gyi gri gug la sogs pa'i so nang la bkug nas gcod pa'i stangs ka byed pas gzhan la gnod pa yin
zhing / rnal 'byor pa rang gi rtsa la lha bkod pa na/ nang la gcod pa'i stangs ka mi byed par/ phyi la 'phyar stabs su 'dzin pas bar chad bsrung zhing rang gi tshe srog
la

mi gnod pa yin zhes bla ma gong ma rnams kyi gsung rgyun bzhin/ bdag gi rje bla ma rnams yang yang du bka' stsol ba zhig 'dug pas/ zhal gdams 'di ni snying gi dkyil du bcang
bar bya'o/ /de dag gis ni rje tshar chen gyi mgon po'i dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar las/ nang sgrub skabs su gong ma'i tho yig las/ /rdo rje gur dang las gsang gis bstan zhes/
/'byung ba de gnyis dag las ji skad bshad/ /lhag par phyi ma'i ngos 'dzin ji ltar lags/ /rtsa gsum la brten nang gi bsgrub pa'i skabs/ /kha rje kun dga' grol mchog cig
las sbyor skabs su thor bu las/ /'chad pa las gzhan khrid rim med ces gleng / /des na yar lung khrid yig dag min nam/ /zhes dang / nang sgrub 'di ka gsang sgrub yin pa'am/
/gsang sgrub ces bya zur na yod pa yin/ /dang po ltar na so sor dbye ba ci/ /phyi ma ltar na ngos 'dzin ci la byed/ /'di yi thun mong ma yin las sbyor skabs/ /rang dang
bsgrub bya'i rtsa la lha

bkod nas/ /gzhan la gcod tshe phan tshun mtshungs 'dra yi/ /rten 'brel dbang gis gzhan la gnod pa bzhin/ /de bzhin rang gi tshe srog la gnod par/ /bshad cing de 'dra'i gtam
rgyud mang snang ba/ /'di la gnad kyi gdams pa ji ltar yod/ /bla mar thos sam yi ge gzigs lags sam/ /zhes gsungs pa de dag gi dgongs pa'i don yang gsal bar byas pa yin no/
/de lta bu'i nang khrid dam gsang khrid 'di 'chad dam nyams su len pa sogs gang byed kyang / gong du bshad pa'i gong ma'i yi ge thor bu ba de dag sogs dang / gzhan yang
yar lung seng rgyal/ rje tshul khrims bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rin/ rje rdo ring pa/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ rje tshar chen rnams kyis mdzad pa'i khrid yig
dngos dang / de la phan pa'i yig sna che chung du ma yod pa rnams dang / lhag par rje tshar pa'i gsung ma nyams pa'i rgyun mkhyen brtse

chos rjes zin bris su btab pa'i khrid yig chen mo dang / de'i snying po bsdus pa bdag gi bla ma mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis mdzad pa sogs de dag la thos bsam mthar phyin
par bgyis na/ lugs 'di la mi 'jigs pa'i spobs pa thob pa ni kho bos nges pa thob pa yin la/ de bzhin du srung 'khor brag rdzong ma'i man ngag la mkhas par 'dod pa rnams
kyis/ thog mar rje btsun gyi dngos slob dkar gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge nas bzung / bar skabs kyi bstan 'dzin so sos mdzad pa'i srung 'khor gyi yig sna du ma 'byung ba de rnams
dang / khyad par rje rdo ring pa'i yi ge rgyas pa/ tshar chen gyi sa bcad/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i srung 'khor bar chad kun sel/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi
gsung rgyun snyan brgyud ma nyams pa/ rje blo gsal rgya mtsho la bka' bab pa bzhin/ slob ma rnams la ji ltar gsungs pa ltar zin bris su btab pa'i khrid yig rje mkhyen brtse
ba dang /

rje bod mkhar ba gnyis kyis mdzad pa sogs dang / de dag gi gsal byed snying por gyur pa bdag gi bla ma mus chen rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan dang / mkhan chen thams
cad mkhyen pas mdzad pa'i gsung rab de rnams la lta rtog zhib tu bgyis na/ srung 'khor brag rdzong ma'i man ngag gi skor la bshad sgrub gang byed kyang thogs med kyi
blo gros rgyas par 'gyur ba ni kho bos nyams su myong ba lags so/ /gsum pa yang gsang sems kyi gnad la brten nas bsgrub pa la gsum ste/ thog mar gzhi skye med dngos po'i
gnas lugs la mkhas pa/ bar du lam dbri bskyed nyams len gyi gnad la mkhas pa/ mthar thug sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa srung ba'i mtshon char gtad pas mngon spyod mchog gi dngos
grub tu bsgyur ba la mkhas pa'o/ /'di dag ni brgyud ldan gyi bla ma rnams kyi zhal las byung ba'i man ngag gi tho tsam bkod pa yin la

zhib tu ni snyan brgyud dang ldan pa'i yongs 'dzin dag gi zhabs pad yun ring du bsten zhing / lus longs spyod kyi sgo nas dka' ba rgya chen po spyad de gsol ba nan tan du btab
nas thugs dgyes pa chen pos zhal gyi sgo nas 'byung ba kho na la rag las pa yin pas/ skal bzang don gnyer can rnams kyis dgongs par mdzod cig cir snang dregs pa rgyud
gsum rnam rol la/ /gang shar rnyed dang bkur bsti'i mchod sprin gyi/ /dbyings nyid gdod nas yod ma myong bzhin du/ /snang ba gzhi nas 'gag med 'di ngo mtshar/ /bar skabs
kyi tshigs su bcad pa'o/ /bzhi pa mos gus gzhon nu'i dga' ba dang 'dra bas bsam pa tshim pa ni/ de ltar chos skyong gi rjes gnang ci rigs pa thob pa'i rjes su/ phyi sgrub
dang nang sgrub kyi man ngag la brtson pas nyams su blang zhing / thun mtshams su yang tshogs dang gtor ma la sogs pas bla ma yi dam chos skyong rnams mnyes par byas pas
rang gzhan

gyi gnas skabs dang mthar thug gi bzhed don rnams lhun grub tu 'byung ba rten 'brel gyi chos nyid yin la/ de'i tshe bla ma dang chos skyong dang gdam ngag rnams la yid ches
pa'i dad pa dang mos gus gsha' ma rkyen gyis 'phrog par mi nus pa'i gting tshugs pa ni mos gus kyis bsam pa tshim pa zhes bya ba yin par gsungs so/ /mtshan ldan bla mar
man ngag drin nos nas/ /nyams su blangs pas don gnyis lhun grub ste/ /lam 'dir bslu ba med pa'i mos gus kyis/ /bsam pa tshim pa chos 'di'i zab khyad lags/ /bar skabs kyi
tshigs su bcad pa'o/ /de ltar de dag gis ni dpal rdo rje nag po chen po'i zab mo'i chos skor rnams byung ba'i tshul legs par bshad pa bstan srung chos kun gsal ba'i nyin
byed ces bya ba ma tshang pa med pa bstan zin to// //'dir smras pa/ gangs can ljongs 'dir 'gran zla kun bral sa skya'i bla chen gong ma lnga/ /brgyud par bcas

dang sa skya paN chen dri med dpal du sangs rgyas te/ /slar yang byon pa sprul pa'i skyes mchog sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun rin zhes/ /ci mdzad bstan 'gro'i don du gyur pa'i
skyes chen de la slar yang 'dud/ /mgon de'i rigs sras padma'i rnam sprul mthu stobs rdzu 'phrul bsam yas gter/ /gang gi zhal dkyil mthong ba tsam gyis 'gro kun dbang sdud
bsod nams dbang / /zhi zhing des pa'i ngang tshul bzang pos rmu rgod kun kyang 'dul mdzad pa'i/ /'gro mgon chos rje'i rnam 'phrul grags pa'i mtshan te sku mched zhabs
la dad/ /brtan g.yo 'di kun khyed kyi rnal rol khyed ni brtan g.yo kun gyi bdag /gdod ma'i mgon po rang sems bla ma rang ngo sprod pa'i bka' drin can/ /'khor 'das kun khyab
rgyal ba'i gong bu rgyal ba mus pa chen po zhes/ /da lta 'bras bu'i sa la bzhugs pa'i sa gsum bla mas da dung skyobs/ /chos tshul bye ba'i spyan zung dang ldan 'gro

kun dga' mdzad don grub zhabs/ /sa skya'i gser chos kun la dbang phyug nyams rtogs rab brtan chos rje dang / /gang gi mkhyen rab ngag dbang lha mtshungs chos kyi don kun gzigs
pa yi/ /grags pa gsal ldan yongs 'dzin rnams kyi bka' drin bsam bzhin dad pa 'phel/ /rnam snang pho brang rdo rje gdan la sogs/ /rgya bod mkha' 'gro 'du ba'i gnas rnams
su/ /bzhugs nas bstan dgra'i srog dbugs la dgyes pa'i/ /phyi yi chos skyong rnams kyis bdag srungs shig /rtsa gsum 'khor lo byang sems rlung gi dngos/ /gzung 'dzin dgra
bo'i gshed ma lhan skyes kyi/ /ye shes bde chen mgon po'i sar 'khrid pa'i/ /nang gi srung mas rtag tu dge legs mdzod/ /phyi nang sgyu 'phrul dregs pa'i zlos gar kun/ /rang
sems gsal stong brjod bral blo 'das kyi/ /rol par shes pas snang srid rgyud gsum gyi/ /rang zhal

mthong ba'i gsang ba'i mgon pos skyongs/ /de ltar phyi yi dregs pa rgyud gsum la/ /rnam drug rten dang gtor ma gsum la sogs/ /bshams nas bzlas brjod bskang bshags bstod bskul
gyis/ /mnyes par byas pas las bzhi'i don kun 'grub/ /lus la grub pa'i nang gi rgyud gsum po/ /dmigs rim zab mo'i byang sems dbab bzlog dang / /rlung sbyor bzlas pa'i sngags
kyis rgyud bskul bas/ /bde chen mgon pos 'dzum zhal ston par nges/ /gsal stong zung 'jug gsang ba'i rgyud gsum de/ /brjod bral blo 'das mchod pas dgyes byas na/ /tshe
'dir sems nyid rtog med chos sku dang / /lus nyid 'ja' lus rdo rje'i sku 'grub gyur/ /de 'dra'i 'bras bu tshe 'dir ma thob na/ /'chi ba 'od gsal zhes bya'i sgra bo che/
/yang yang 'phrad pa'i mdza' bo de mthong bas/ /ngo shes nang gi 'pho bas dus der grol/ /der yang 'khrul nas bar dor 'khyams gyur na/ /bla ma bstan srung

rnam sprul bgrang yas kyis/ /gdugs dang rgyal mtshan la sogs mchod sprin bcas/ /ming nas lung ston mkha' spyod 'khrid par nges/ /ci ste las kyis mngal sgo 'grims srid kyang
/ /lus rten bla ma chos sogs mthun rkyen kun/ /bka' srung rnams kyis 'bad med legs bsgrubs nas/ /ring por mi thogs rnam grol mchog thob pas/ /lam bzang 'di dang mjal kun
skal ba bzang / /de ltar brtan g.yo kun khyab srung ma'i gtso/ /dpal ldan gur gyi mgon po lcam dral dang / /mthu ldan gnyan gyi mgon po gdong bzhi pa/ /bstan dgra'i srog
bdag las mkhan pho nyar bcas/ /u rgyan mkha' 'gro'i gling gi nor skyong zung / /dpal chen thugs kyi sprul pa dkar mo dang / /bdud kyi rgyal po dam can bcu gnyis sogs/ /bstan
srung dbang po rnams kyi zab rgyas kyi/ /chos tshul sngon tshe rgya gar 'phags yul dang / /phyis

rabs gangs ri'i ljongs 'dir dar ba'i tshul/ /legs par bshad pa'i sngon med bstan bcos kyi/ /nyi ma gsar du shar ba'i dge mtshan 'dis/ /blo gsal rnams kyis bstan srung chos
tshul kun/ /gsal bar mthong zhing rtogs pa'i rgyur gyur te/ /sa skya'i bka' srung man ngag chu rgyun gyis/ /rgya mtsho'i gos can ma lus khyab gyur nas/ /de dang lhan cig
yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i bdag /dpal ldan sa skya'i rje btsun mchog rnams kyi/ /bzhed gzhung zab dang rgya che'i bstan pa'i rgyun/ /kun kyang 'phel zhing srid mthar rgyas gyur
cig /'di sbyar dge dang dus gsum legs byas kyi/ /mthu las byung ba'i gzi brjid me 'od kyis/ /bdag cag dpon slob gdul byar bcas pa yi/ /sdig sgrib nyes ltung mun pa kun
bcom nas/ /dus 'dir tshe ring nad med bsam don rnams/ /sngar bzhin 'bad med yid bzhin lhun grub ste/ /spyi dang bye brag bstan pa cher rgyas shing / /de rgyun bskal par
rigs

rgyud dri med kyis/ /rgyun du bskyangs nas dpal ldan sa skya yi/ /chos srid dpal 'byor yar ngo'i zla ba ltar/ /gong 'phel gyur te sngags 'chang yab sras kyi/ /bstan pa'i rgyun
'di nam yang mi nub cing / /bdag dang bdag la yid gtad slob bu rnams/ /nam zhig tshe 'di'i snang ba nub ma thag /bde ba can du snang ba mtha' yas kyi/ /drung du skyes
nas sa lam mthar phyin te/ /slar yang bsam bzhin srid pa'i zlos gar gyi/ /sna tshogs thabs mkhas du mas bstan pa dang / /'gro ba'i don mang yid la re ba bzhin/ /'grub nas
kun kyang dag pa'i zhing bsgrod shog /bdag cag so skye rang stobs bral yang bla ma bstan srung dbang po rnams/ /dbyer med thugs rje'i gzhan stobs dbang las 'di dang phyi
ma'i don mtha' dag /yid la bsam pa ji bzhin 'grub ste sa skya'i rje btsun bstan pa'i rgyun/ /phyogs dus kun tu mi nub dar ba'i mthu dang nus pa'i stobs ldan shog /nges
pa'i

don du bden pa'i dngos po phra rab rdul gyis ma gos kyang / /ye shes gsal snang cir yang 'char ba gdod ma nyid nas 'gag ma myong / /yod ma myong ba'i dbyings dang 'bral med
brjod bral cir yang ma grub pa/ /zung 'jug gnas lugs myur du rtogs nas rang gzhan don gnyis lhun grub shog /ces dpal rdo rje nag po chen po'i zab mo'i chos skor rnams byung
ba'i tshul legs par bshad pa bstan srung chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba 'di yang / snyigs dus kyi bstan pa'i gsal byed chen po sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po
ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyi thugs sras dam pa gcen 'jam mgon grub pa'i dpa' bo padma'i rnam sprul bsod nams dbang po'i zhal snga nas dang / de'i gcung byang chub sems
dpa' zhi ba 'tsho'i sku'i skye ba dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan nyid slar yang bsam bzhin du byon pa yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags
pa blo gros/ rigs thams cad dang dkyil 'khor thams cad

kyi khyab bdag drug pa rdo rje sems dpa' dang rnam dbyer med pa'i dus gsum sgrib med du gzigs pa rgyal ba mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ sprul pa'i sku lo nas spyan
snga rin po che kun dga' don grub/ nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag chos kyi rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhas shing btsun pa'i yon tan gzhal du med pa mnga' ba rje nags
dgon pa chen po sbyin pa grags pa/ shes bya'i dkyil 'khor mtha' dag la mi 'jigs pa'i spobs pa brnyes pa mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa la sogs
te yongs 'dzin bslu med dam pa du ma'i zhabs sen rin po che dbang gi rgyal po spyi bo'i rgyan du bkod cing / gsung gi bdud rtsi'i skal ba bzang por gyur pa shrI sa skya
pa shAkya'i dge bsnyen paNDi ta mkhas pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos/ sa skya pa'i bka' srung khyad par can 'di dag
gi man ngag gi chos tshul

rnams bshad pa'i gzhi che zhing / zab cing rgya che ba 'ba' zhig tu bzhugs pas 'di rnams kyi chos skor rnams byung tshul gyi yi ge zhib pa zhig bgyis te/ lugs 'di'i bstan pa'i
zhabs 'degs su 'gyur ba zhig byung na ci ma rung snyam pa'i rang nyid kyis kyang lhag bsam rnam par dag pas kun nas bslangs shing / don gnyer can gyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen
du mas kyang 'phral yun du bskul ba dang / lhag par rigs kyi bu ngag dbang bsod nams dbang phyug la sogs te rigs dang chos las skyes pa'i slob ma'i tshogs rang dang
skal ba mnyam pa rnams la phan par bsams nas/ lugs 'di la mkho ba'i mgon pod me 'bar ma sogs na bzhugs pa'i chos skyong gi bla ma brgyud pa'i lo rgyus kyi yi ge gong mas
mdzad pa'i gsung rab rjes 'brangs kyi zin bris du ma dang bcas pa rnams/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan gyi mgon po'i man ngag gi khog khrigs kyi yi ge khyad par rje btsun
blo gsal rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i mgon po'i chos skor byung

tshul man ngag gi khog phub rnam bshad/ snyan brgyud rin chen lde mig dang / snyan brgyud rol mtsho ste gsung rtsom 'phro can de gnyis la gtso bor brten zhing / gzhan yang
sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i gsung rgyun dri ma med pa la brten nas/ 'jam mgon grub pa'i khyu mchog bsod nams dbang pos mdzad pa'i 'di skor la mkho ba'i gsung rab 'ga'
zhig dang / yab rje sbas pa'i rnal 'byor sangs rgyas mi gzugs can grags pa'i mtshan can/ de nyid kyis mdzad pa'i bse 'bag nag po 'phur shes kyi lo rgyus kyi yi ge mkhan
chen thams cad mkhyen pa sogs kyis mdzad pa'i mgon po'i chos skor gyi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar gyi don 'grel bla ma'i gsung rgyun ma sogs tshad thub kyi yig cha du ma
la gzhi byas shing / dngos brgyud kyi bla ma rnams kyi gsung rgyun khyad par can blo la zin pa rnams kyis kyang mdzes par byas te/ rang gi bgrang gzhi bcu phrag bzhi dang
nyag ma lngar slebs pa 'phags pa'i

yul na br-i ShaHste khyu mchog ces grags shing / rgya nag lugs la lcags mo sbrul gyi lo me tog can gyi zla ba'i dkar phyogs dga' ba dang po'i tshes la/ gza' dang skar ma dang
sbyor ba dang byed pa bzang po 'dzoms pa'i nyin/ bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal sa skya'i chos grwa chen po'i bzhi thog bla brang gi yang rtse ngo mtshar 'chi med rdo rje'i
pho brang e waM byang chub 'byung ba'i gnas su bla ma dang mkha' 'gro chos skyong khyad par can rnams la gsol ba rtse gcig tu 'debs bzhin pa'i ngang nas legs par sbyar ba'i
yi ge pa ni/ gso ba rig pa la mkhas shing / yi ge'i 'du byed la byang chub pa gdong ga ba bsam pa don chen dang / A kSha ra'i bya ba la phul du phyin cing dpal dus kyi
'khor lo'i rtsis gzhung rgya mtsho la legs par sbyangs pa shab stod pa bkra shis don grub gnyis kyi sor mo'i 'du byed las bskrun pa'o/ /'di bgyis dge bas bdag cag dpon
slob kyi sdig sgrib thams cad byang zhing dag ste/ dus 'dir tshe ring nad med bsam don yid bzhin du

'grub cing / phyi ma lhan cig bde ba can du padmo las brdzus te skyes nas/ rgyal ba 'od dpag med las theg chen chos kyi bdud rtsi'i bka' drin nos nas sa lam rnams skad cig
gis bsgrod de/ rang nyid grol ba mthar phyin cing / phyin chad las nyon gyi skye sgo spangs pa'i gang 'dul gyi sprul pas 'gro kun smin grol la 'god cing / spyi dang bye brag
gi bstan pa rab tu gsal zhing yun ring du gnas par bya nus pa'i mthu stobs dang ldan pa'i smon gnas yid bzhin du 'grub pa'i rgyur gyur cig de de bzhin du gyur cig de
las gzhan du nam yang ma gyur cig na mo shrI badzra mahA kA la sa pa ri wa ra ye ma ma pa ti sa pa ri wa ra sya a yu puNya dhan shtsa wartA ni bista ra bha wantu/ bA hya
mudhya yoH dpal rdo rje nag po chen po 'khor dang bcas pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bdag 'khor dang bcas pa'i tshe bsod nams nor longs spyod 'phel zhing rnam par rgyas par mdzad
du gsol/ phyi dang nang gi mi mthun phyogs thams cad nye bar zhi bar mdzad du gsol/ sarba a pakSha u pa shintaM

kurbantu/ dngos grub thams cad bdag la rab tu stsal du gsol/ sarba siddhi mme pra yatstshantu/ thams cad bkra shis/ sarba mangga laM/ dharme u da ya mastu/chos 'di rab tu dar
bar gyur cig skabs 'dir yi ge pa bzang ldan nor bus zhus/ ye dharmmA he tu pra bha bA he tunte Shanta tha ga to hya ba datre te Shanytsa yo ni ro dhA e baM bA di mahA
shra ma NaH sarba mangga laM//
